dhātoreva vicaraṇābhidhāyakatvam । upasargāstu dyotakāḥ na vācakāḥ । ata eva sūtre caraṇābhidhānāt ityevoktam। bhāṣye tu avicaraṇābhidhānāt'; iti spaṣṭārthamuktam । ata eva tattvapradīpe aspaṣṭatvāya vicaraṇābhidhānāt ityuktam'; ityuktam। ame'; ityasmacchabdena mantradraṣṭā ṛṣirucyate । adūra ādhīḥ'; ityasya ekapadatve api avagrahadarśanena dvikhaṇḍatvādvibhajyānvayaḥ । āṅ īṣadabhivyāptyubhayārthakaḥ । vartata iti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca yato me karṇau jyotiṣo viruddhaṃ patayataḥ patataḥ । svārthe ṇic । cakṣuśca viruddhaṃ patatīti vipariṇāmenānvayaḥ । yathā karṇāderjyotirvidūratvaṃ evaṃ jyotiṣo api karṇādividūratvamityāha - vīdamiti । kampo atyantamityarthe । tathā ca yadidaṃ hṛdaye aāhitam'; ā samantāt sthitaṃ jyotistadatyantaṃ karṇādiviruddhaṃ vartate । evaṃ me manaḥ jyotiṣo dūre vicarati atīva taddarśanaviruddhaṃ vartate । manaścaraṇasya tattvaniṣṭhāvirodhitvaṃ acañcalaṃ hi manaḥ kṛṣṇa'; iti gītāyāmuktam । ataḥ kāraṇāt aādhīḥ'; īṣadbuddhirahaṃ vyāptabuddhirapīti vā akiṃ svit'; kiṃ nu vakṣyāmi । kimu kiṃ vā nu idānīṃ amaniṣye'; cintayāmīti mantrārthaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu - ā samantāddūrasthabuddhirahamityekānvayena vyākhyātam ।

tacca jyotiragnisūktatvātprasiddheścāgnireveti prāptam ।

atha sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣayati - tacceti । agniśabdo bhūtataddevatāparaḥ। dvitīyacaśabdo bhinnakramaḥ । tathā ca tajjyotirguhānihitaṃ cāgnireva bhavediti prāptaṃ, kutaḥ? aprasiddheḥ'; jyotiśśrutestasyāśca tasminnagnāveva prasiddheḥ rūḍhatvāt । na kevalaṃ śruterevedaṃ jyotiragniḥ, kintu tasya jyotiṣaḥ aagnisūktatvāt'; agniprakaraṇagatatvācceti yojanā । ata eva pūrvapakṣopasaṃhāraṭīkāyāṃ śrutiprakaraṇayorbalavatvāditi prasiddhapadalakṣitāyāḥ śruteḥ prathamamuktiḥ । ata eva candrikāyāṃ bhāṣye agnisūktasthatvācceti caśabdaprayogādityuktam । tathā ca śrutiprakaraṇābhyāṃ guhānihitatvaliṅgamātrasya bādhāt agnirevedaṃ jyotirguhānihitaṃ ceti bhāvaḥ ।

ata āha -
jyotiś caraṇābhidhānāt । karṇādīnāṃ vicaraṇābhidhānāt ।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati - ata iti ।। yataḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ prāpto ataḥ uttaraṃ sūtramāha bhagavānbādarāyaṇa ityarthaḥ । tadeva sūtraṃ paṭhati jyotiriti । sūtre tattvityasya anuvṛttiṃ vipariṇāmaṃ cābhipretya pratijñāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - viṣṇureveti । ajyotiḥ'; tacchabdavācyo viṣṇureva bhavediti yojanā । kuta ityataḥ prāptaṃ acaraṇābhidhānāt'; iti hetvaṃśaṃ caraṇaśabdasya vicaraṇārthatvaṃ karṇādīnāmityasya adhyāhāraṃ cābhipretya vyācaṣṭe - karṇādīnāmiti । atra vākye karṇādīnāmetajjyotiḥprati viruddhacaraṇokteḥ karṇādividūratvaliṅgaśravaṇādityarthaḥ । atra karṇādividūratvaṃ nāma tairiyaditi paricchedāyogyavaibhavatvaṃ, na tu karṇādividūratvamātram । tadviṣaye tasyāsambhavāt । abhidhānaparyantadhāvanaṃ hetvasiddhiparihārāyeti draṣṭavyam ।

sa hi aparo mātrayā tanvā vṛdhāna'; ityādinā karṇādividūraḥ ।।

nanvastu jyotiṣaḥ karṇādividūratvoktiḥ, tāvatā tasya viṣṇutvaṃ kuta ityataḥ karṇādividūratvasya viṣṇvekaliṅgatve śrutimudāharan tatpratijānīte - sa hīti ।। evetyanuṣajyate । ādiśabdena ana te viṣṇo'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । tathā ca ahi'; yasmāt asaḥ'; viṣṇureva aparo mātrayā'; ityādivākyena karṇādividūra iti pramitaḥ tasmānnāprayojakatā, na vā hetuviśeṣaṇāsiddhirityadhyāhāreṇa yojanā । anena ajyotiḥ'; tacchabdavācyaṃ brahmaiva । kutaḥ? atra karṇādīnāmetajjyotiḥ prati sākalyena tadaviṣayīkaraṇarūpaviruddha acaraṇābhidhānāt'; karṇādividūratvaliṅgaśravaṇāt ittyāvṛttyadhyāhārābhyāṃ sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । māpayati jñāpayati viṣayāniti vā mīyante viṣayā aneneti vā mātrā indriyagaṇaḥ tayā tatastvaṃ aparo'; dūro asīti he viṣṇo anyamahimnaḥ paramantaṃ sīmānaṃ te mahimānaṃ ko api śrotrādinā nāpeti ca prakṛtānuguṇyena śrutirvyākhyeyā । atra tattvapradīpasannyāyaratnāvalīkārayoḥ jyotirityādicatussūcī ekamevāntarbhedādhikaraṇamityabhipretam । agnisūktacchāndogyagataviṣayavākyabhedādanayorbhedaḥ । ṭīkākṛtastujyotissūtramekamadhikaraṇaṃ achandaḥ'; ityāditrisūtrī adhikaraṇāntaramiti jñātavyam ।।

।। iti jyotiradhikaraṇam ।।

।। chando abhidhānādhikaraṇam ।।

chando abhidhānān neti cen na tathā ceto'rpaṇanigadāt tathā hi darśanam ।

atrādhikaraṇe adhivedagatagāyatryādyaśeṣaśabdasamanvayaḥ kriyate । saṅgatyādijijñāsājananāya sūtramevādau paṭhati - chanda iti ।। atra chanda ityāvartate । tacca vyastaṃ samastaṃ ca । tathā ca achando abhidhānāt'; agāyatrī vā idam'; iti vākyasthagāyatrīśabdena caturviṃśatyakṣaramantraviśeṣātmakachandasaḥ pratipādanāt, tacchabdasya tatra rūḍhatvāt, gāyatrīśabdavācyo na viṣṇuḥ, kintu chanda eva । yato gāyatrī na viṣṇuḥ, api tu chandaḥ, ato jyotirapi na viṣṇuḥ kintu chandaḥ । kutaḥ? achando abhidhānāt'; chandasā gāyatryā tadaikyābhiprāyeṇa jyotiṣo abhidhānāt upakramāditi cet - na, viṣṇureva jyotiḥ । kutaḥ? anigadāt'; gāyatrīpadena viṣṇorevābhidhānāt । gāyatryādipadairviṣṇorevābhidhānaṃ ca tadabhedavidhānārthaṃ kintu tathopāsanārthamevetyāha - tatheti । atathā'; gāyatryādiśabdārthaguṇasvarūpatvena acetaso'; manasaḥ aarpaṇāya'; brahmaṇyādhānāyopāsanārthameva viṣṇornigadādityarthaḥ । upāsanetyanuktvā

cetorpaṇetyuktirupāsanāsvarūpakathanārthā । anena prasiddhagāyatryādipadena viṣṇorabhidhānaṃ vyarthamiti śaṅkā parihṛtā। nanu bhavedgāyatrīśabdavācyatvena viṣṇorjyotiśśabdavācyatvasādhanam, yadi gāyatrīśabdavācyatvaṃ viṣṇoḥ pramitaṃ syāt । tadeva kuta ityata āha - tathā hīti । ahi'; yasmāt atathā'; gānatrāṇakartṛtvanimittena viṣṇorgāyatrīśabdavācyatvasādhakaṃ adarśanaṃ'; dṛśyate jñāyate artho yayeti vyupattyā agāyati ca trāyati ca'; ityādirūpā śrutirasti tasmāditi sūtrārthaḥ ।

aatha yadataḥ paro divo jyotirdīpyate'; 
ityuktasya jyotiṣo agāyatrī vā idaṃ sarvam'; 
iti gāyatryā samārambhaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।

tasmānna viṣṇuriti cet - na, tathā cetor'paṇārthaṃ hi nigadyate । agnigāyatryādiśabdārtharūpo asāviti cetor'paṇārthaṃ hi nigadyate ।

śrutyādisaṅgativiṣayavākyaviṣayasaṃśayapūrvapakṣatatphalāni sūcayan sūtre pūrvapakṣāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - atheti ।। uktasyetyāvartyate । tathā ca ahṛdaya āhitaṃ yat'; iti guhānihitatvena yaduktaṃ tasyaiva ajyotiṣaḥ'; punaḥ aatha yadataḥ paro divo jyotirdīpyate viśvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu sarvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu anuttameṣūttameṣu lokeṣu । idaṃ vāva tadyadidamasminnantaḥpuruṣe jyotiḥ'; iti chāndogye apyuktasya agāyatryā'; itthaṃbhūtalakṣaṇe tṛtīyā । gāyatrītvena tadrūpatayā asamārambhaḥ'; pāṭhaḥ kṛtaḥ । kuto ayaṃ vijñāyate? yato agāyatrī vā idaṃ sarvaṃ vāgvai gāyatrī vāgvā idaṃ sarvam'; iti vākye agāyatryā'; gāyatrīśabdena tadaikyatātparyeṇa asamārambhaḥ'; upakramaḥ kṛtaḥ ata iti yojanā । tataḥ kimityata āha - tasmāditi। idaṃ cāvartate । jyotirgāyatrīti ca śeṣaḥ । chanda iti cānuṣajyate । tathā ca yasmādgāyatryā samārambhaḥ kṛtaḥ, sa ca yasmādanupasañjātavirodhitvena balavān, tasmādidaṃ jyotirgāyatryeva bhavet । sā ca gāyatrī virṇasamāveśalakṣaṇamantrātmakachanda eva bhavet, na viṣṇuḥ । kutaḥ? tasmāt gāyatrīśabdasya chandasyeva rūḍhatvādvāktvābhidhānācceti yojanā । anena agāyatrī vā idaṃ sarvam'; iti pūrvavākyasthagāyatrīśabdasya viṣṇvanyaparatve tata evottaravākyasthajyotiṣo viṣṇvanyatvāpattyā tata eva agnisūktagatajyotiṣo api tadanyatvameva bhavet । ata evānandamayatvamapi anyasyaiva bhavenna viṣṇoriti pūrvoktākṣepeṇa etadadhikaraṇotthānātpūrveṇāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiḥ । evaṃ gāyatrī viṣayaḥ । kiṃ chandoviśeṣaḥ uta viṣṇuriti sandehaḥ । tathā gāyatrī chandoviśeṣa eva bhavet; tacchabdasya tatra rūḍhatvāditi sayuktikaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ । tathā tasmāt jyotirapi chanda eveti tasyaiva guhānihitatvamāndamayatvaṃ ceti pūrvapakṣaphalaṃ ca sūcitaṃ bhavati । atra pūrvapakṣe gāyatryādiśabdāḥ mantraparāḥ, sarvamapi vākyaṃ tanmāhātmyaparatayā yojanīyam। siddhānte tu aatha'; ityāderayamarthaḥ - bhagavanmāhātmyāntarārambhe athaśabdaḥ ayat'; śvetadvīpānantāsanavaikuṇṭhagataṃ nārāyaṇavāsudevavaikuṇṭhākhyaṃ rūpatrayaṃ tat aataḥ'; etasmādvivakṣitādbuddhisthāt adivaḥ paraḥ'; paraṃ tadapekṣayoccasthānasthitamityarthaḥ । ajyotiḥ'; tejomayaṃ evaṃbhūtaṃ tat aviśvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu'

pṛthivyāṃ brahmaṇo merau vaijayante antarikṣagam ।

tṛtīyaṃ satyaloke ca sadanaṃ trividhaṃ matam ।।

iti vacanādantarikṣagavaijayantamerusatyalokagatebhyo brahmasadanebhyaḥ krameṇocceṣu asarvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu'; antarikṣapṛthivīsvarātmakalokebhyaḥ krameṇocceṣu aanuttameṣu'; na vidyate uttamo loko yebhyasteṣu pratyavareṣviti vā । auttameṣu'; svayamevottameṣu alokeṣu'; śvetadvīpānantāsanavaikuṇṭheṣu adīpyate'; prakāśate

atat'; dīpyamānaṃ tejaḥ aidaṃ vāva'; idaṃ khalu। idaṃ ca kim? ayadidamasmin puruṣe'; hṛdaye aantarjyotiḥ'; tacchabditaṃ brahmāsti tattenaikībhūtamityarthaḥ । yo gāyatrīnāmā gāyatrīsaṃsthaḥ strīrūpo hayaśīrṣākhyo bhagavān tadidaṃ prathamaṃ rūpamityāśayena tasya dvitīyaṃ rūpaṃ vaktuṃ gāyatrītyādivākyaṃ pravṛttam । ayadidaṃ kiñca bhūtaṃ'; pūrṇaṃ matsyādyavatārarūpaṃ yacca asarvaṃ'; sarvāntaḥsthitaṃ rūpaṃ tatsarvaṃ agāyatrī'; gāyatrīnāmā bhagavāneva । vai prasiddham । tasyaiva tṛtīyaṃ rūpamāha - vāgiti । gāyatrīnāmā bhagavān avāgvai'; vāṅnāmako viṣṇureva । kuto asya viṣṇutvamityatastallakṣaṇayogādityāha - vāgvā iti । aidaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ'; prāṇijātaṃ avāgvai'; vāṅnāmakabhagavadadhīnameva । ataḥ sarvasvāmitvādvāco viṣṇutvamiti । siddhāntasūtrāṃśamanukaroti - neti । nigadyata ityatrāpi sambadhyate । tathā ca jyotiḥśabdena viṣṇureva nigadyata ityarthaḥ । kuta ityato nigadāditi hetuṃ yojayati - hi nigadyata iti । gāyatrīśabdeneti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca ahi'; yasmādgāyatrīśabdenāpi viṣṇureva anigadyate'; abhīdhīyate tasmādityarthaḥ । viṣṇorgāyatryādiśabdairabhidhānaṃ ca na tadabhedavidhānārthaṃ, kintu tathopāsanārthamevetyāha - tatheti । ceto arpaṇetyuktiprayojanaṃ pūrvavat । bhāṣyatvajñāpanāya tathetyādisvapadāni tathāśabdārthakathanena vivṛṇoti - agnīti । atra jyotiśśabdopalakṣakāgnipadaṃ jyotissūtrasya bhinnādhikaraṇatvapakṣe anyatra prasiddhasya gāyatrīpadasya viṣṇau prayoge prayojanamatra vadatā sūtrakṛtā pūrvatrottaratra cāgnyādipadasya viṣṇau prayoge prayojanaṃ sūcitamiti darśayitum । na ca gāyatryādipadābhyāmeva gāyatrīpadasamanvayaphalasya pūrvatrottaratra coktasamanvayaphalasya ca sūcanasambhavādagnipadaṃ vyarthamiti vācyam । phalībhūtasamanvayaviṣayatvenāsyāpi avaśyopādeyatvāt । samānaprakaraṇasthavāgādigrāhakatvena ādiśabdasyāpyāvaśyakatvāt । avaśyāpekṣitābhyāmubhābhyāmapyānandamayādyadhikaraṇeṣu uttaratra coktaprayojanasyāpi sūcanasambhavādubhayamapyāvaśyakam । jyotirityādicatuḥsūtryā ekādhikaraṇatvapakṣe tu sākṣātsamanvetavyapaśabdatvenaiva śabdadvayopādānaṃ, na tu phalatvenāgniśabdasyādhikaraṇāntare apyetannyāyasūcanaṃ tu ādiśabdenaiva, na tūbhābhyām । bhinnajātīyānekaśabdagrahaṇārthaṃ śabdadvayottarādipadam । ata eva tattvapradīpe ādiśabdasyobhayatrānvayaṃ prathamādiśabdena tejaḥśabdānāṃ dvitīyena chandaśśabdānāṃ ca grahaṇamabhipretya aagnyāditejaḥśabdānāṃ gāyatryādichandaśśabdānāṃ ca'; ityuktam। kecittu bhāṣyagatahiśabdo jñānārthamatha dhyānārthamiti pramāṇaprasiddhidyotakaḥ, adhikaraṇāntare apyasya nyāyasyānusandheyatvajñāpakaścetyāhuḥ । ceto arpaṇārthamiti sāvadhāraṇam । tathā ca aasau'; bhagavānagnigāyatryādiśabdairagnigāyatryādiśabdārthaguṇasvarūpa iti । tatra aceto arpaṇārthaṃ'; budhyavatāraṇārtham upāsanārthameva nigadyate, na tadabhedavidhānārthamityarthaḥ । itītyantena tathāśabdārtha uktaḥ। anenāprasiddhagāyatryādipadena viṣṇorabhidhānasya vaiyarthyaśaṅkā parihṛtā ।

tathā hi darśanaṃ agāyati trāyati ca'; ityādi ।

nanu bhavedgāyatryādiśabdavācyatvena viṣṇorjyotiśśabdavācyatāsādhanaṃ yadīyaṃ gāyatrī viṣṇuḥ syāttadeva kuta ityato gānatrāṇakartṛtvaliṅgādityāśayena tasyāsiddhiparihārāya pravṛttaṃ tathāhīti sūtraśeṣam

anukṛtya darśanapadoktāṃ śrutiṃ darśayati - tatheti ।। ahi'; yasmāt aityādi darśanaṃ'; śrutirastītyanvayaḥ । yadyapi agāyati trāyate ca'; iti pāṭhaḥ chandogānam, tathāpi śākhāntaramevedamityadoṣaḥ । ādipadena ayā vai sā gāyatrī iyaṃ vāva sā yeyaṃ pṛthivyasyāṃ hīdaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ pratiṣṭhitametāmeva nātiśīyate'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । śrutyarthastu - yato gāyatrīvācyo bhagavān vedān agāyati'; mukhānnissārayati prathamo vakteti yāvat । yasmācca atrāyate'; akhilamiti śeṣaḥ। ato gāyatrīśabdenocyate । ayā'; prasiddhā gāyatrī tannāmā viṣṇuḥ asā iyaṃ vai'; iyaṃ khalu । kimiyam? ayeyaṃ pṛthivī'; tannāmā bhagavān । kathaṃ pṛthivī viṣṇurityataḥ tallakṣaṇayogādityāha - asyāṃ hīdamiti । aasyāṃ'; pṛthivyāṃ abhūtaṃ'; prāṇijātamāśritamiti । sudhāyāṃ tu pūrvapakṣānuguṇatayā gāyatrī agāyati'; arthaṃ pratipādayati, adhyetṛn atrāyate'; pālayati pāpāt rakṣatītyartha uktaḥ ।

sarvachando abhidho hyeṣaḥ sarvadevābhidho hyasau ।
sarvalokābhidho hyeṣasteṣāṃ tadupacārataḥ ।।

iti vāmane ।।

nanu gāyatryādiśabdasya anyatra rūḍhatvātkathaṃ liṅgamātreṇa viṣṇutvaniścaya ityato gāyatryādiśruteḥ sāvakāśatvāditi bhāvena gāyatryagnipṛthivyādiśabdāḥ na kevalaṃ śrutyuktayogena viṣṇau sāvakāśāḥ, api tu paurāṇikarūḍhyā gāyatryāḥ bhagavadadhīnatvādapītyāśayena tatra smṛtimāha - sarveti । aeṣaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ asarvachando abhidhaḥ'; sarvachandasām abhidhevābhidhā yasyeti bahuvrīhiḥ । chandovācakagāyatryādisarvaśabdavācyaḥ ।

aevamasau'; viṣṇuḥ sarvadevatāvācakāgnyādiśabdavācyaḥ । tathā aeṣaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ sarvalokavācakapṛthivyādiśabdavācya ityarthaḥ । kuta ityataḥ chanda ādīnāṃ bhagavadadhīnatvāditi pratyekaṃ hetutrayasūcanāya hiśabdatrayaṃ, vedaprasiddhijñāpānāya vā । chandasāṃ lokānāṃ ca pratyakṣatvāt devānāṃ ca parokṣatvādeṣo asāviti vicitroktiḥ । kathaṃ tarhyanyatra vyavahāra ityata āha - teṣāmiti । chandodevalokānāmityarthaḥ । atat'; tacchabdabodhyatvam aupacārato'; viṣṇusamīpe caraṇāttadadhīnatvādamukhyata evetyarthaḥ। vāmana ityasya ahi'; yato vāmane iti adarśanaṃ'; pratipādanamastyataḥ śrutermukhyavṛtyā viṣṇāveva sāvakāśatvāt liṅgasyāmukhyato apyanyatrānavakāśatvāttena tadbādhopapatterbhavatyeva gānatrāṇakartṛtvaliṅgamātreṇāyaṃ nirṇaya ityupaskareṇānvayaḥ ।

bhūtādipādavyapadeśopapatteś caivam ।

hetvantareṇāpi gāyatryāḥ viṣṇutvaṃ sādhayatsūtramupanyasya tadgṛhītāṃ śrutimudāharati - bhūtādīti। itiśabdasya bhūtādītyanenānvayaḥ । sūtre bhūtaṃ viśvamādiḥ prathamoddiṣṭaṃ yeṣu te bhūtādayaḥ, te pādāḥ yasya gāyatrīpadārthasya sa bhūtādipādaḥ, tasya vyapadeśaḥ tatpratipādakaṃ vākyaṃ tasyopapatteḥ yuktatvāditi vigrahaḥ । pādaśabdo bhāvapradhānaḥ । ata eva bhūtādipādatvasyetyuktaṃ ṭīkāyām । evamityasya cobhayatrānvayaḥ । tathā ca apādo asya sarvā bhūtāni । tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi'; ityevaṃ gāyatryāḥ

bhūtādiśabdagṛhītāmṛtākhyāṃśacatuṣṭavattvopadeśāt tasya ca viṣṇāvevopapatteranyatrānupapattereva gāyatrīśabdavācyo viṣṇureva bhavedityarthaḥ । caśabdasya vyapadeśapadenānvaye gāyatryā viṣṇutve sādhye pūrvasūtre darśanapadoktahetoḥ etatsūtroktahetudvayasya ca samuccaye saḥ । yathāśrutānvaye tu bhūtādipādatvasya viṣṇuliṅgatvaṃ na kevalaṃ viṣṇorevopapatteḥ siddham, kintu puruṣasūktoktatvācceti hetusamuccaye sa iti jñeyam । chāndogye hi asaiṣā catuṣpadā ṣaḍvidhā gāyatrī'; iti vākyena yaiṣā ṣaḍvidhā gāyatrī sā catuṣpadetyevaṃ gāyatrīnāmakasya bhagavataḥ prāguktagāyatrībhūtavākpṛthivīśarīrahṛdayalakṣaṇaṣaḍvidhatvamanūdya aṃśacatuṣṭayavattvarūpaṃ catuṣpādatvaṃ vidhāya svoktārtha eva puruṣasūktamantraḥ samākhyārūpatvenodāhṛto brāhmaṇena atadetadṛcābhyanūktam'; iti atadetat'; bhagavataścatuṣpādatvaṃ aṛcā'; ṛṅmantreṇa aabhi'; niśśaṅkaṃ spaṣṭam aanu'; ānukūlyenoktamityarthaḥ ।

atāvānasya mahimā tato jyāyāṃśca puruṣaḥ । pādo asya sarvā bhūtāni tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi'; iti ।

kimuktamityatastanmantraṃ paṭhati - tāvāniti ।। yadyapi ṛci aetāvān'; iti aviśvā'; iti ca pāṭhaḥ । tathāpi śākhāntarapāṭho ayamityadoṣaḥ । aasya'; puruṣasya apuruṣa evedaṃ sarvam'; ityṛcā yassarveśānatvādirūpaḥ tāvānmahimoktaḥ, na kevalametāvān, kintu, puruṣaḥ atataḥ'; pūrvoktadapi mahimno ajyāyān'; adhikamāhātmyopeta ityarthaḥ । jyāyastvameva darśayati - pādo asyetyādinā । asarvā bhūtāni'; sarvaṃ viśvam aasya'; viṣṇorekaḥ apādaḥ'; pādavatpādo bhinnāṃśaḥ । yadyapi tattvapradīpe - viśvabhūvidhirbhāti । tathāpi ṭīkāyāṃ sarvāṇi bhūtānyasyaikaḥ pāda iti pādavidhānadarśanāt; candrikāyāṃ apaśvekatvavat vidheyagatatvātpādaikatvaṃ vivakṣitam'; ityuktatvācca, tattvapradīpo apyevameva vyākhyeyaḥ । asya aamṛtaṃ'; nāśarahitam ata eva svarūpabhūtaṃ atripāt'; trayāṇāṃ pādānām aṃśānāṃ samudāyo nārāyaṇavāsudevavaikuṇṭhasaṃjñaṃ triṣu rūḍhyā dyotamānatvācca dyuśabdavācyeṣu śvetadvīpānantāsanavaikuṇṭheṣu tiṣṭhatīti ṛcoktamityarthaḥ । yadyapi bhūtaśabdo abhinnapādassarvajīvāḥ'; iti chāndogyabhāṣye jīvaparatayā vyākhyātaḥ । tathāpi asuvarṇam'; iti śrutyanusāreṇa atra viśvārthatayā vyākhyātavyaḥ ।

suvarṇaṃ kośaṃ rajasā parīvṛtam । devānāṃ vasudhānīṃ virājam । amṛtasya pūrṇāṃ tāmu kalāṃ vicakṣate । pādaṃ ṣaḍḍhoturna kilā vivitse iti śruteḥ । pāda iti ekadeśaparimitaṃ caturbhāgabala itivadbhinnaṃ ca ।

nanu gāyatryāmiva viṣṇāvapi bhūtādipādatvoktiranupapannā । tasya bhūtabhinnatvādityata āha - suvarṇamityādi ।। asuvarṇam'; ityārabhya abhinnaṃ ca'; ityantamekavākyatayārthakrameṇa vyākhyeyam । yajñadattasya, devadattaḥ, ityucyate, viśvamiti ca śeṣaḥ । pāda iti cāvartate । caśabdaevārthe hetau ca । ekadeśaparimitamiti hetugarbhamāvartanīyam । tathā ca aco'; yataḥ śrutisthena pāda iti śabdena na bhūtānāmityamṛtapādatrayavatsvarūpāṃśatvamucyate। yenānupapattiḥ syāt । kintu, yajñadattasya caturbhāgabalo devadatta iti vadbhinnameva viśvam । yataḥ aparimitam'; viṣṇupādaparimitasāmarthyam ataḥ pāda iti viṣṇupādatvenocyate ityarthaḥ । asyāto viṣṇau bhūtādipādavyapadeśopapatteścaivamiti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । tarhi viśvacatuṣṭayasamo harirityāgatamityato apyāha - pāda itīti। tathā ca yataḥ śrautapāda iti padena caturbhāgabala itivat na viśvaṃ viṣṇusāmarthyasya caturthāṃśaparimitamityucyate । kintu, aekadeśaparimitaṃ'; viṣṇusāmarthyaikadeśaparimitamiti ato noktadoṣa ityarthaḥ । kuta etat jñāyata ityata āha - suvarṇaṃ kośamiti । aśruteḥ'; taittirīyaśruteḥ । śrutau tṛtīyārthe ṣaṣṭhī, samudāyaikavacanaṃ caitat । ata eva amuktaiḥ pūrṇām'; ityuktaṃ ṭīkāyām । evaṃ ca tattpradīpaṭīkayorekavākyatayā । tatraikaṃ bhāvasādhanam । na kileti dīrghaḥ sāṃhitikaḥ । tathā ca ekasmin kapāle asuvarṇaṃ'; tanmayaṃ arajasā parīvṛtaṃ'; rajoguṇopalakṣitabagnīranabho ahaṃkṛnmahattattvaguṇatrayaiḥ parivṛtaṃ avirājaṃ'; brahmaṇaḥ śarīraṃ, tattvapradīparītyā viśeṣeṇa rājantamiva akośaṃ'; liṅgavyatyayaḥ, brahmāṇḍākhyaṃ yadasti । devānāṃ avasudhānīṃ'; dravyanidhānamañjūṣām aamṛtaiḥ'; muktaiḥ pūrṇāṃ tāṃ aṣaḍḍhotuḥ'; ṣaḍindriyeṣu viṣayān juhvataḥ, ṣaḍindriyāṇi viṣayeṣu jīvena juhvato vā, ṣaḍindriyaiḥ sārādanakarturvā, viṣṇoḥ akalāmu'; ekadeśaparimitāmeva apādaṃ vicakṣate'; pādaśabdenācakṣate vadanti puruṣasūktādyāgamā iti śeṣaḥ । na kila atra pādaśabdenāṅghri vadanti, nāpi caturthāṃśamityevārthaḥ । kutaḥ? yataḥ sā mañjūṣā apādaṃ'; pādatvaṃ caturthabhāgasāmyaṃ ana vivitse'; na lebhe kileti śrutyarthaḥ । sattarkadīpāvalyām - pādaṃ na vivitse iti । pādasāmyaṃ na lebhe ityuktam । atra pakṣadvaye api puruṣavyatyayastulyaḥ । ṭīkākṛtpakṣe lakāravyatyayaśca । yadvā - liṅgavyatyayasya chāndasatvaṃ kośamityasya dvitīyāntatvaṃ copetya strīliṅgapadānāmapi kośaviśeṣaṇatvenaika evānvayaḥ।

sa hi puruṣasūktābhidheyaḥ । ayajñena yajñamayajanta'; iti yajñaśabdāt । ayajño viṣṇurdevatā'; iti hi śrutiḥ ।

syādetadevaṃ yadi atāvān'; ityasyāmṛci viṣṇurabhidhīyate ityatra pramāṇaṃ syāt, tadeva nāsti, ato liṅgamanyaniṣṭhaṃ bhaviṣyatītyataḥ sautracaśabdena bhūtādipādatvasya viṣṇuliṅgatve sādhye puruṣasūktoktatvāditi yadanumānaṃ sūcitaṃ tasyāprayojakatvamāśaṅkya pariharati - sa hīti ।। ahi'; yasmāt asaḥ'; viṣṇureva apuruṣasūktābhidheyaḥ'; tatpratipādyaḥ tasmātsa eva puruṣasūktoktabhūtādipādo apīti yojanā । anyathā bhūtādipādatvasya viṣṇudharmatvābhāve puruṣasūktapratipādyatvaṃ na syāditi bhāvaḥ । yadvā - gāyatryā viṣṇutve sādhye sūtre bhinnakrameṇānvitacaśabdasūcitayuktyantaramāha - sa hīti । asya tasmādgāyātrī viṣṇureveti pradhānapratijñāvākyenānvayaḥ । catuṣpadetyuktagāyatrīcatuṣpādatvasya puruṣasūktamantreṇopapādanāt tatpratipādyatve tadupapādyagāyatrīśabdārthatāpi tasyaiva prāpnotīti bhāvaḥ । puruṣasūktoktasya viṣṇutvaṃ kuta ityata āha - yajñeneti । devāḥ ayajñena'; jñānakarmātmakena rudrākhyapaśunā vā ayajñaṃ'; viṣṇum aayajanta'; apūjayanniti śrutyarthaḥ । iti yajñaśabdāditi । iti vākye yajñaśabdaśravaṇādityarthaḥ । yajñaśabdaḥ kathaṃ viṣṇutvaniścāyaka ityato vidvadrūḍhyetyāha - yajña iti । ahi'; yataḥ yajña iti padena viṣṇvākhyā devatācyata ityarthaḥ । yadyapi ayajño vai viṣṇuḥ'; ityadhvaryūṇāṃ śrutiḥ । tathāpi śrutyantaramidamityadoṣaḥ ।

tasmin kāle mahārāja rāma evābhidhīyate । yathā hi pauruṣe sūkte viṣṇurevābhidhīyate । iti ca skānde ।।

nanu puruṣasūktaṃ na viṣṇuprakaraṇaṃ, kintvanyaprakaraṇameva । na ca yajñaśrutivirodhaḥ । paśurūpānyaprakaraṇe tadanyaviṣṇuśruteḥ ayogāditivācyam । tasyāḥ prāsaṅgikatvasambhavāt । na ca tata eva bhūtādipādatvasya viṣṇuliṅgatvaniścayaḥ । apādo asya viśvā bhūtāni'; iti śruterbhūtādipāde yajñaśruterabhāvādtyataḥ puruṣasūktoktasya viṣṇutve smṛtiñcāha - tasminniti ।। mahārājeti kasyacitsambodhanaṃ rāmaviśeṣaṇaṃ vā । tathātve dīrghassyāt । tathā ca he mahārāja atasmin'; tretāyuge sarvaiḥ puruṣanāmabhī rāma evābhidhīyate ityarthaḥ । ata evāṃśādhikaraṇe -

nakṣatramānagaṇitaṃ trayodaśasahasrakam ।

brahmalokasamaṃ cakre samastaṃ sarveṣāmabhavattadā ।।

rāmorāma iti hyākhyā sarveṣāmabhavattadā ।

sarvo rāmamayo loko yadā rāmastvapālayat ।।

iti skānde ityuktaṃ tattvapradīpe । atra dṛṣṭāntamāha - yatheti । yathā kṛtsne pauruṣe sūkte viṣṇureva na tvanyaḥ । paśuḥ naraḥ prāsaṅgikatayābhidhīyate ityarthaḥ । anena siddhasyaiva dṛṣṭāntatvātpuruṣasūktasya viṣṇuparatvaṃ siddhamiti bhāvaḥ । skānda ityantaraṃ etaduktamiti śeṣaḥ । asya sa hīti purvavākyenānvayaḥ।

upadeśabhedān neti cen nobhayasminn apy avirodhāt । atripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi'; iti pūrvopadeśaḥ । aparo divaḥ'; iti pañcamyantaḥ paścimaḥ । tasmānnekaṃ vastvatrocyate iti cet - na, trisaptalokāpekṣayā ubhayasminnapyavirodhāt ।।

uktamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasyati - upadeśeti ।। aupadeśayoḥ'; saptamīpañcamīyutavākyayoḥ aupadeśena'; gāyatrījyotiṣoḥ dyusthatvadivaḥparatvarūpaviruddhadharmoktyā abhedāt'; virodhāt na dvayorviṣṇvākhyam ekaṃ vastu pratipādyaṃ, kintu bhinnameveti cet - na, kintu aubhayasmin'; ubhayatrāpyupadeśe ekameva pratipādyaṃ, katham? avirodhāt । trisaptalokāpekṣayā saptamīpañcamyoḥ ekārthatvena virodhābhāvāditi sūtrayojanāmabhiprayannākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - tripāditi । apūrvopadeśaḥ'; pūrvoktiḥ । apaścimaḥ'; paścāttanaḥ uttara upadeśastadbhinno astīti śeṣaḥ। virodhasphoraṇāya pañcamyanta ityādyuktiḥ । upakramagatasya prābalyopapādanāya pūrva ityuktiḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha - tasmāditi । yasmādevaṃ bhinnopadeśadvayamasti tasmādatropadeśadvaye gāyatrījyotiśśabdābhyāṃ naikaṃ vastu viṣṇvākhyamucyate । kutaḥ? yato atra anaikam'; anekaṃ vastu dyusthatvadivaḥparatvarūpaṃ dharmadvayamucyate । kintvatra anaikam'; anekaṃ vastudvayamucyate iti yojanā । siddhāntayatsūtrāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - neti । nātra vastudvayamucyate ityarthaḥ । kiṃ tvitiśeṣaḥ, ekaṃ vastūcyate iti anuṣajyate । ubhayasminniti sādhyāntargatam । apiśabdo na kevalamekatra, kintūbhayatrāpīti samuccaye । tathā ca kintūbhayasmin apyupadeśe ekameva viṣṇvākhyaṃ vastūcyate iti yojanā । virodhātkathametadyujyate ityata āha - trisaptalokāpekṣayeti । trilokavivakṣayā saptalokavivakṣayā ca aavirodhāt'; ubhayatrāpyekavastvabhidhāne virodhābhāvādityarthaḥ । ayaṃ bhāvaḥ - yadā bhūrbhuvassvariti lokatrayavivakṣā, tadā lakṣayojanocchritāntarikṣākhyabhuva uparitanasya sarvasyāpi dyutvāt śvetadvīpānantasanavaikuṇṭhānāṃ cāntarikṣāduparitanatvāttatratyaṃ nārāyaṇavāsudevavaikuṇṭhākhyaṃ tripācchabdoktaṃ rūpatrayaṃ divitiṣṭhatītyucyate iti na saptamyantopadeśavirodhaḥ । na ca

pṛthivīstheṣu sarvocco loko anantāsanātmakaḥ ।
antarikṣātmakebhyaśca śvetadvīpasthito hariḥ ।।

ityukteranantāsanasya nāntarikṣāduparitanateti śaṅkyam । tasya pṛthivīsthatve api bahulakṣayojanocchritatvenaikalakṣayojanocchritāntarikṣāduparitanatvopapatteḥ । sarvapṛthivīsthoccatvoktyā tu na pṛthivīsthānyoccatvayogovyāvartyate । kintu pṛthivīsthoccatvāyogaḥ । yadā tu bhūrbhuvassvarmaharjanaspassatyamiti saptalokavivakṣā । tadendrasadanasya dyutvāt taduccasyāpyuparisthitatvena tatsajātīyasyavaikuṇṭhasya divaḥ paratvam ।

pṛthivyāṃ dyaurmahāmerurākāśe sūryamaṇḍalam ।
divīndrasadanaṃ caiva tatpare tu divaḥ pare ।।

iti smṛtermerorapi dyutvāttaduccasya bhūspṛṣṭatvena tatsajātīyasyānantāsanasyāpi divaḥ paratā । evaṃ sūryamaṇḍalasyāpi dyutvāttaduccasyoparisthatvena tatsajātīyasya bhūmeḥ kiñcidantaritasya sarvargasamonnatasya śvetadvīpasyāpi divaḥ paratvamastīti na pañcamyantopadeśavirodho apīti । dyuparatvaṃ ca sambhāvitasajātīyadyuparatvamiti na yāvattvayatkiñcittvamukhena dūṣaṇāvakāśaḥ । vaikuṇṭhasya svargalokātparatvenaiva divaḥ paratvasiddhāvapi tasya asarvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu'; ityanenaiva uktatvāt svargatyāgenendrasadanasya dyutvoktiḥ । na ca lokatrayavivakṣayaivānantāsanādīnāmapi mervādiparatvena divaḥ paratvasyāpi siddheḥ saptalokavivakṣā vyartheti vācyam । tathā sati vaikuṇṭhasyāpi dyuśabdārthaniviṣṭatvena tasya sarvadyuparatvāsiddhyāpatyā advyātmakebhyaśca sarvebhyo vaikuṇṭhaścocca ucyate'; iti pramāṇavirodhāpātāt । chāndogyabhāṣye tu -

anantaśayanaṃ caiva tathānantāsanaṃ hareḥ ।
bahulakṣocchrite nitye vimāne saṃsthitaṃ yataḥ ।।

citprakṛtyātmani yato divīti kathitaṃ śrutau ।
iti pramāṇabalena citprakṛtyātmakānantāsanaśvetadvīpavaikuṇṭhākhyasthānatraye saptamyanto dyuśabdo dyotamānatvanimittena yaugikaḥ, svargādau tu rūḍha iti upadeśayoravirodha iti prakārāntareṇa virodhaparihāraḥ kṛtaḥ ।।
।। iti chando abhidhānādhikaraṇam ।।

।। pādāntyaprāṇādhikaraṇam ।।

prāṇo viṣṇurityuktam । tatra atā vā etāḥ śīrṣan chriyaḥ śritāścakṣuḥ śrotraṃ mano vākprāṇaḥ'; ityatra prāṇasya viṣṇutvaṃ na vidyate । indriyaissahābhidhānāditi । ata āha -

atrādhikaraṇe lokato anyatra prasiddhaprāṇanāmno viṣṇau samanvayaḥ pratipādyate । śrutyādisaṅgativiṣayavākyaviṣayasaṃśayasayuktikapūrvapakṣān darśayati - prāṇa iti ।। ādyaprāṇādhikaraṇe atadvai tvam'; iti vākyoktaprāṇo viṣṇurityuktamityarthaḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha - tatreti । uktamityanuṣajyate । tasyāvṛttivipariṇāmau । evaṃ tatretyapyāvartanīyam । tathā ca atatra'; tadvai tvamiti vākye uktasya prāṇasya viṣṇutvaṃ na vidyate na yujyate । kutaḥ? yatastatra atadvai tvam'; iti vākyoktaprāṇaviṣaye aukte'; śrute atā vā etāḥ'; ityaitareyavākye uktasya śrutasya prāṇasya viṣṇutvaṃ na vidyata iti yojanā । kuto na vidyate ityata āha - indriyaissahābhidhānāditi । indriyaissaha paṭhitatvāt indriyagaṇe gaṇitatvāt ityarthaḥ । anenaitareyaprāṇasya viṣṇvanyatvākṣepamukhena prācīnataittirīyoktaprāṇasyāpyanyatvākṣepāttenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । aitareyaprāṇākhyo viṣayaḥ । prāṇo anya uta viṣṇuriti saṃśayaśca sūcitaḥ । tathā vāyvādiranya eveti pūrvapakṣaḥ । indriyagaṇe gaṇitatvākhyatatsādhakaliṅgaṃ ca sūcitam । atā vā etāḥ'; ityetacca caturmukhaśirasi śiraśśabdapravṛttinimittakathanāya pravṛttam । vaiśabdaḥ prasiddhau । tathā ca yataḥ atā etāḥ'; cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ manovākprāṇa ityetacchabdavācyāstadabhimāninyo devatāḥ । aśīrṣan'; śīrṣṇi śiraḥsaṃjñikamūrdhni śritāḥ । ata eva śrayaṇācchriya iti siddhānte śrutyarthaḥ । anena cakṣurādibhiḥ śritatvaṃ śiraḥpadapravṛttinimittamityuktaṃ bhavati । pūrvapakṣī tu prāṇaśabdamanyamātraparaṃ manyate । siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati - ata iti । yataḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ prāptaḥ ata uttaraṃ sūtramāha bhagavān bādarāyaṇa ityarthaḥ ।

prāṇas tathānugamāt । ataṃ devāḥ prāṇayanta'; asa eṣo asuḥ sa eṣa prāṇaḥ'; aprāṇa ṛca ityeva vidyāt'; atadayaṃ prāṇo adhitiṣṭhati'; ityādyānugamāt ।

sūtraṃ paṭhitvā tatrānugamāditi hetvaṃśaṃ śrutyudāharaṇena vyācaṣṭe - prāṇa iti ।। ityādīti । evamādivākyoktānāṃ devatopadeśyatvādiliṅgānāmatrāsmin prakaraṇe bahuṣu sthaleṣu aanugamāt'; anuvṛtterabhyāsādityarthaḥ । ādipadena aprāṇo hyevaiṣa ya eṣa tapati'; iti sūryamaṇḍalasthatvapratipādakavākyaṃ gṛhyate । tathā asarvāṇi bhūtānyāpipīlikābhyaḥ prāṇena bṛhatyā viṣṭabdhāni'; ityādi vākyaṃ ca gṛhyate ।

atrāpi prāṇo viṣṇureva ।

sautraṃ tathāśabdaṃ vyācaṣṭe - atrāpīti ।। śruta iti śeṣaḥ । na kevalaṃ atadvai tvam'; ityatra, kintvaitareye apīti samuccaye apiśabdaḥ । sūtre anuvṛttasya tattvityasyārthamāha - viṣṇureveti । anena yathā

atadvaitvam'; iti śrutyuktaprāṇo viṣṇuḥ tathaitareyokto api viṣṇureva, na tvanyaḥ । kutaḥ? viṣṇuliṅgānāṃ devatopadeśyatvādīnāmasmin prakaraṇe aanugamāt'; anuvṛtterabhyāsāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

aitareye ataṃ devāḥ prāṇayanta'; iti ekakhaṇḍasthavākyam । ataṃ'; nārāyaṇaṃ vāyuṃ ca devāḥ aprāṇayanta'; prakarṣeṇa śiṣyapraśiṣyadiṣu nītavantaḥ upadidiśurityarthaḥ । anena viṣṇoḥ sarvadevopāsyatvamuktaṃ bhavati ।

asa eṣo asuḥ sa eṣa prāṇaḥ sa eṣa bhūtiḥ'; ityādyanyakhaṇḍagataṃ vākyam । anena bhūtitvādinā devādyupāsyatvamucyate । asa eṣaḥ'; bhagavān duṣṭanirasanādasuḥ prakṛṣṭānandarūpatvātprāṇaḥ devānāṃ bhūtiśabditajñānādyaiśvaryapradatvādasurāṇām ajñānādyanaiśvaryahetutvācca bhūtyabhūtiśabdavācya ityarthaḥ ।

tatraiva atā vā etāḥ sarvā ṛcaḥ sarve vedāḥ sarve ghoṣā ekaiva vyāhṛtiḥ । prāṇa eva prāṇa ṛca ityeva vidyāt'; iti anyadvākyam । atra prāṇasyasarvavedoktatvamucyate । yāstāḥ etāḥ sarvā ṛcastāsāṃ aekaiva vyāhṛtiḥ'; ekameva vyāhartavyaṃ pratipādyam । tacca kim? prāṇo viṣṇureva । kiñca ye sarve vedāḥ teṣāmapi prāṇa eva pratipādyaḥ। api ca ye samudrādighoṣāḥ teṣāmapi, kimu vedānām । tatra ṛcastu viśeṣata indrādināmavato viṣṇorguṇān alpajñānāmapi prakāśayantīti, prāṇe nārāyaṇe tadviṣayā eva avidyāt'; tatpratipādikā eveti jānīyādityarthaḥ । aitareyabhāṣye tu - prathamaprāṇapadamapi viṣayasaptamyantatayā vyāhṛtiśabdaṃ ca vyāharaṇaparatayā vyākhyāya ekameva vyāharaṇaṃ nirdeṣaguṇapūrtivācakatvādekaprakārameva nāmetyarthaḥ uktaḥ । tattvapradīpe apyayamevoktaḥ ।

atha devarathaḥ atasya vāguddhiḥ śrotre pakṣasī cakṣuṣī yukte manaḥ saṅgṛhītā tadayaṃ prāṇo adhitiṣṭhati'; iti vākyāntaraṃ atra prāṇasya deharathatvamucyate । prameyāntarakathanārambhārtho athaśabdaḥ । ucyata iti śeṣaḥ। tathā ca devasya viṣṇoḥ vāyoḥ adhyātmamadhidaivataṃ ca ratha ucyate ityarthaḥ । tasyādhyātmaṃ dehākhyarathasya avāk'; vāgākhyā umā uddhiḥ dhāraṇarajjurūpā adhidaivaṃ viṣṇurathasya prasiddhasyandanasya ca nāgākāromā uddhiḥ aśrotre'; dakṣavāmapārśvagatacandratadbhārye apakṣasī'; pārśvayuktāśvau anyatrāśvarūpau pārśvayoryuktau acakṣuṣī'; ubhayapārśvagatasūryatadbhārye ca ayukte'; agrato niyuktāśvau amano'; mano abhimānī rudraḥ asaṅgṛhītā'; sārathiḥ evam adhidaivaṃ prasiddhasyandanasyāpi rudraḥ sārathiḥ । sa cāsāvayaṃ ca tadayamityekaṃ padam । tattvapradīparītyā

bhinnapadatve api taditi rathatayoktaṃ śarīraṃ parāmṛśyate । liṅgavyatyayena taṃ rathamiti vā । ayaṃ prāṇo viṣṇuḥ vāyuścādhitiṣṭhatītyarthaḥ । liṅgena pūrvapakṣite kathaṃ tenaiva siddhānta ityāśaṅkānudayāya liṅgabāhulyoktiḥ ।

viṣṇumevānayan devā viṣṇuṃ bhūtimupāsate ।
sa eva sarvavedoktastadratho deha ucyate ।।

iti skānde ।

nanu bāhulyena balavataḥ saiddhāntikaliṅgādapi pūrvavādyuktaliṅgameva balavat । niravakāśatvena svabhāvato balavattvāt । na cāviśeṣeṇanirṇayaḥ, bāhulyena balavato api svābāvabalinaḥ prābalyāt । yadāhuḥ - 
dvividhaṃ balavattvaṃ ca bahutvācca svabhāvataḥ ।
tayossvabhāvo balavān upajīvyadikaśca saḥ ।।

iti । ataḥ kathaṃ tairviṣṇutvaniścaya ityato devatopadeśyatvādiliṅgānāṃ niravakāśatvamapi smṛtyā sādhayati

- viṣṇumiti । devāḥ viṣṇumeva prādhānyena śiṣyādiṣu jñānasampradāyapravartanena aānayan'; upādiśan । bhūtimuddiśya viṣṇumevopāsate । bhūtimiti vidheyaviśeṣaṇaṃ vā । tathā ca viṣṇuṃ bhūtiṃ bhūtirjñānādyaiśvaryarūpa ityupāsate ityarthaḥ । asaḥ'; viṣṇurmukhyavācyatayeti śeṣaḥ, tenaivakāropapattiḥ । atadratho'; viṣṇoreva rathaḥ । atraivakārasya dvirgrahaṇātsarvatrānuṣaṅgaḥ sūcitaḥ । tena sarvaliṅgānāmapi niravagakāśatvamuktaṃ bhavati । skānde ityanantaraṃ liṅgānāmananyathāsiddhatvamuktamiti vākyaśeṣaḥ । tathā caikaprakāreṇa prabalātpūrvapakṣiliṅgātprakāradvayenāpi prabalasya saiddhāntikaliṅgasyādhikyena nirṇayopapattiriti bhāvaḥ । abhyupetya cedamuditam । vastustu pūrvapakṣiliṅgasya na niravakāśatvenāpi prābalyamasti, prāṇaiḥ sahagaṇitatvasyāntaryāminiṣṭhatāsambhavāt ।

brahmaśabdānugamācca ।।

yadā bahutvaniravakāśatvākhyaprakāradvayenāpi durbalaliṅgasyobhayathāprabalaliṅgato bādhasambhavena tainaiva prāṇasya viṣṇutvasiddhiḥ, tadā kimu vācyaṃ niravakāśabrahmaśabdābhyāsāditi bhāvenānugamapadaṃ prakārāntareṇa vyācaṣṭe - brahmeti ।। asmin prakaraṇe aetadbrahma'; abrahmaṇo lokaḥ'; abrahmemaṃ puruṣam'; audaraṃ brahmetyācakṣate'; aa iti brahma'; ityādi niravakāśabrahmaśabdābhyāsāccetyarthaḥ । etadviṣṇusvarūpaṃ brahma guṇapūrṇam । ayaṃ jīvo brahmaṇaḥ parasyāśrayaḥ । imaṃ puruṣaṃ caturmukhaṃ parabrahma prāpadyata । vāyuryatra sthita urveva garaṇaṃ stavanaṃ cakre tatsthānamudaraṃ tadgatamityarthaḥ ।

na vaktur ātmopadeśād iti ced adhyātmasaṃbandhabhūmā hy asmin । aprāṇo vā ahamasmyṛṣe'; iti vakturātmo- padeśādindra eveti cet - na, aprāṇastvaṃ prāṇaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni' iti bahvadhyātmasambandho hyatra vidyate ।।

uktamākṣipya samādadhatsūtraṃ paṭhitvākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - neti ।। prāṇa ityanuvartate । tathā ca prāṇo viṣṇuriti na yuktam । kutaḥ? aprāṇo vā ahamasmyṛṣe'; iti vākyena bṛhatīsahasravakturviśvāmitrasyendreṇa prāṇatayā ātmanaḥ svasyaivopadeśādityarthaḥ । prāṇa indra eveti phaloktiḥ । na tūktahetoḥ sādhyoktiḥ । aprāṇo vāhamasmyṛṣe'; iti vākyaṃ tu atamindra uvāca ṛṣe priyaṃ vai me dhāmopāgāḥ varaṃ te dadāmīti । sa hovāca tvāmeva jānīyāmiti । tamindra uvāca'; iti pūrvavākyena saha vyākhyeyam। tatprakārastu - ataṃ'; viśvāmitraṃ aindraḥ'; tadantaḥstho bhagavānuvāca । kimiti? he ṛṣe me priyaṃ dhāmopāgāḥ prāpnuhi । te varaṃ dadāmīti । vaiśabdo avadhāraṇe prasiddhau vā। evaṃ trivāraṃ śaṃsanena dhāmaśabditasālokyaprāptibhagavatpuraprāptisādhanabhagavatprasādaṃ prāptaḥ asaḥ'; viśvāmitraḥ indrāviṣṭena hariṇā varaṃ te dadānīti punaruktassan uvāca । kimiti? tvāṃ sāmānyataḥ pūrvam ahaṃ jāne । adhunā kīdṛśastvamiti viśeṣato jānīyāmiti । evamuktaḥ aindraḥ'; tadantargato hariḥ ṛṣiṃ pratyuvāca । kimiti? he ṛṣe ahaṃ prakṛṣṭānandarūpatvātprāṇaśabdavācyo asmīti । atra vākyasamanvayapakṣe asmadādiṣūpapadeṣu vihitānāmasmītyāditiṅantapadānāṃ tadvṛtteḥ sulabhatvāditi tattvanirṇayaṭīkārītyā ahamitīndrāntaḥsthena hariṇā svātmano nirdeśādasmīti uttamapuruṣopapattiḥ । pūrvapakṣirītyā śrutyarthastu spaṣṭaḥ । ahaṃ prāṇo asmīti padānāṃ aheyatvaprakṛṣṭānandatvasaṃhartṛtvajñātṛtvanimittaiḥ bhagavati samanvayapakṣe tu na tadanupapattiriti dhyeyam । nañadhyāhāreṇa siddāntāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - neti । anugamādityanuvartate । netyāvartate । hiśabdo yata ityarthe । asyoktamiti śeṣaḥ । tathā cetthaṃ tattvapradīpaṭīkoktā yojanā - nāyaṃ prāṇa indraḥ, kintu viṣṇureva । kutaḥ? aanugamāt'; prāguktaprabalatamaliṅgādeḥ । tathā satyupadeśavirodha iti

cet - na, kutaḥ? yato atra prakaraṇe svasthitasyaiva prathamaṃ aprāṇo vā ahamasmyṛṣe'; iti vākyena paramātmatvamuktamindreṇa । tarhyaikyoktivirodha ityapi na । yato atra tasyaiva prāṇākhyaparamātmanaḥ aprāṇastvaṃ prāṇaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni'; ityevamādivākyena abahvadhyātmasambandhaḥ'; indrādijīvarūpabahudehasambandhaḥ sarvagatatvameva ṛṣiṃ prati indreṇoktaṃ avidyate'; asti natvaikyamata iti । sūtroktasambandhabāhulyaṃ sambandhini paryavasyatītyāśayena

bahvityuktam । bhūmaśabdasya bhāvavācitve api bhāvabhavitrorabhedāt bhavitari prayogaḥ । sūtre tu paranipāta ārṣaḥ । athavā - adhikaścāsāvātmā cādhyātmā tasya sambandhaḥ bahuścāsāvadhyātmasambandhaśceti vigrahaḥ । tathā ca ahi'; yataḥ aatra'; indre abahuḥ'; bahulaḥ paramātmasambandhaḥ sannidhiviśeṣo vidyata ityarthaḥ । vidyata ityanantaraṃ tadapekṣayāyam upadeśo na svāpekṣayeti śeṣaḥ । tathācendre tātkālikeśvarasannidhānaviśeṣābhiprāyā aprāṇo vā aham'; ityuktiḥ, na svāpekṣayeti nopadeśavirodha iti bhāvaḥ । kuto na svāpekṣayetyataḥ prāṇastavamityādyāha । yojanā tu - hi yasmāt aprāṇastvam'; ityādi vākyenāsya prāṇasya abahvadhyātmasambandhaḥ'; adhyātmatvenāntaryāmitvena indrādirūpabahudehasambandhaḥ sarvagatatvamuktaṃ vidyate na caitadatra jīvaviśeṣendre vidyate yujyate tasmāditi । prathamapakṣe ayasyātmā śarīram'; iti śruterindrādīnāṃ viṣṇudehatvādaikyavyapadeśaḥ śarīraśarīribhāvanibandhana iti jñāpanāyādhyātmetyuktiḥ । anena bṛhatīsahasravakturviśvāmitrasya taṃ pratīndreṇa prāṇatayātmopadeśādayaṃ prāṇo na viṣṇuḥ, kintu indra eveti cet - nendro ayaṃ prāṇaḥ, kintu viṣṇureva । kutaḥ? anugamāt prāguktabalatamaliṅgādeḥ । na copadeśavirodhaḥ । yato ayamindragatādhyātmaviṣaya eva । kutaḥ? hi yasmādasmin prakaraṇe adhyātmasambandhabhūmā । atrādhyātmasambandhaśabdenātmādhikāre vartamānamiti । adhiścāsau ātmā ceti dehaḥ paramātmā cocyate । tathā ca yasmādadhyātmano viṣṇorindraviśvāmitrādidehasambandha ukto asti tasmāt । athavā - hi yasmāt asminnindre adhyātmasambandhabhūmā - adhirīśvare - adhikasyātmanaḥ paramātmanaḥ sambandhasyāveśasya bhūmā bāhulyaṃ vidyate tasmādupadeśasya sannihitaparamātmaviṣayatvopapteriti bhāvaḥ । tadapi kutaḥ? hi yasmāt asmin prakaraṇe adhyātmasambandhabhūmoktaḥ tasmāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

śāstradṛṣṭyā tūpadeśo vāmadevavat ।

nanu yadi prāṇaśabdenendreṇāpi viṣṇureva svātmādisarvagatatayocyate tarhi mayi prāṇa iti nirdeśaḥ syāt । viṣṇāvahamityādirūpopadeśāyogādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtraṃ paṭhati - śāstreti ।। turevārtho apyarthaḥ, yatha ityarthe smṛtisūcakaśca । tathā ca yato api prāṇasya viṣṇutve apyupadeśaḥ prāṇo vāham ityevaṃrūpo yujyate, ato na tadanupapattiḥ । kathamayaṃ yujyate? yato ayamupadeśaḥ aśāstradṛṣṭyā'; śāsti sarvamiti śāstraṃ antaryāmī bhagavān, taddṛṣṭyā tadapekṣayaiva pravṛtto na tvaikyena । na cāntaryāmiṇi ahamādiprayogādarśanāt tadayogaḥ । yato avāmadevavat'; tatkartṛkaprayogavat । yathā vāmadevo nāma ṛṣiḥ antaryāmivivakṣayā aahaṃ manurabhavam'; iti svasmin ahaṃmanvādiśabdān prayuyuje । tathā ayamapyupadeśo yujyate ata iti sūtrayojanāmabhiprayan sautraśāstrapadaṃ vyācaṣṭe - śāstramiti । viṣṇuriti śeṣaḥ । tathācāntaryāmī viṣṇariha śāstrapadenokta ityarthaḥ । antaryāmīti prakṛtābhiprāyeṇa । yadvā - śāsti prerayati sarvāniti vyutapattyā antaryāmītyetadeva śāstramityasya vyākhyānaṃ bhavatīti

nāpadārthatvaśaṅkāvakāśaḥ । ata eva bhāgavate dhyeye antaryāmiṇyeva śāstraśabdaprayogaḥ। aitareyabhāṣye aśāsturantaryāmiṇaḥ'; iti śāstṛśabdaṃ mūlīkṛtya vyākhyāne api, tadanusāreṇa ca tattvapradīpe śāsturantaryāmiṇo viṣṇoriti vyākhyānepi nāsya tadvirodhaḥ śaṅkyaḥ, yatastatparyāyaśabdavyākhyānenaiva śāstraśabdo vyākhyāto bhavatītyāśayena śāstraśabdaparyāyaśāstṛśabdo vyākhyāyate । yadvā - śāstraśabde śāstṛ a ityavayavavibhāgamabhipretya śāstrityaṃśasyāntaryāmiṇa ityanena aśabdasya viṣṇorityanena ca vyākhyātattvāt, atra tu avayavavibhāgamavivakṣitvā śāstramityakhaṇḍapadasyāntaryāmiti vyākhyānāt tadanukūlatayā asaṃvicchāstram'; iti vacanopanyāsācca na virodhaḥ ।

asaṃvicchāstraṃ paraṃ padam'; iti hi bhāgavate ।

antaryāmiṇo viṣṇoḥ śāstrapadavācyatve pramāṇamāha - saṃviditi ।। prathamaskandhe vyāsaṃ prati nāradavākyamidam ।

svapno māyāgrahaḥ śayyā jāgradābhāsa ātmanaḥ । nāmarūpakriyāvṛttiḥ saṃvicchāstraṃ paraṃ padam ।।

asyārthaḥ - ātmano jīvasya māyāvāsanākhyasaṃskāropādānakavastujñānarūpaḥ svapnaḥ । agrahaḥ jāgratsvapnaviṣayajñānarahitā śayyā suṣuptiḥ nāmarūpakriyāsu śabdārthakarmasu vṛttirvyāvṛttiryanyāḥ sā । ābhāsaḥ pratyayaḥ saṃjñādiviṣayajñānarūpo jāgracca । āhatyaitadavasthātrayaṃ yasmādātmanaḥ parabrahmaṇo bhavati, tatsaṃvit sarvaviṣayaka-

yathārthajñānarūpaṃ sarvajñaṃ vā । śāstraṃ sarvaniyantṛ, paraṃ uttamaṃ padaṃ sadbhiḥ prāpyaṃ brahma aham acintayamiti । bhāgavata ityanantaraṃ aprayogāt'; iti śeṣaḥ । asyāntaryāmītyanenānvayaḥ ।

tattannāmnocyate viṣṇuḥ sarvaśāstṛtvahetutaḥ ।
na kvāpi kiñcinnāmāsti tamṛte puruṣottamam ।।

iti pādme ।।

nanvantaryāmiṇi ahamādiprayogaḥ kathaṃ sambhavatītyāśaṅkyāṃ tatra tuśabdasūcitāṃ smṛtimevāha - tattaditi। viṣṇuḥ atattannātmā'; anyaparatvena prasiddhāhamādināmnocyate iti । anena tasyāntaryāmiṇi viṣṇau vidvadrūḍhirdarśitā । asarvaśāstṛtvahetutaḥ'; sarvaniyantṛtvanimitteneti । anena mahāyogo darśitaḥ । tatra tasya svātantryanimittokteḥ । anena paramata ivāsmanmate api lākṣaṇikatvaṃ parihṛtam apuruṣottamam'; antaryāmiṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ aṛte'; vinā, anyatra akvāpi'; jīvādau akiṃ cit'; ahamādirūpaṃ anāma'; vācakatayā nāstīti । anena harau paramamukhyatā anyatra kevalamukhyatā coktā । anyathā na kvāpīti sāmānyaniṣedhāyogāt । atrāhamādiśabdāḥ pratyagādivācitvena prasiddhāḥ, pratyagādayaśca sarvadā piṇḍībhūtāḥ, tānavivekenājñāḥ kevalajīvādau prayuñjate dahati śabdamiva kāṣṭhe । prājñāstu mukhyāmukhyavivekavanto hyamukhmarthamanādṛtya mukhyārthe harau prayuñjataiti tattvanirṇaṭīkoktamanusandheyam । apādme'; ityanantaram aantaryāmiṇyahamādipadānāṃ mukhyatvokteḥ śāstradṛṣṭyā ahamādyupadeśo yukta eva'; iti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

aahaṃ manurabhavaṃ sūryaśca'; ityādivat ।।

nanvantaryāmiṇi ahamādiprayogādarśanāt tadayoga ityāśaṅkāṃ sūtroktadṛṣṭāntavivaraṇena pariharati - ahamiti ।। aahaṃ'; vāmadevasaṃjñakaṛṣyantaryāmī tattadantaryāmitayā manuḥ sūryaścābhavamiti ṛṅmantrārthaḥ । ādipadena aahaṃ kakṣīvānṛṣirasmi vipro ahaṃ kutsam'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । aityādivat'; evamādiprayogavadityasya aśāstradṛṣṭyopadeśaḥ'; ityanenānvayaḥ ।

jīvamukhyaprāṇaliṅgān neti cen nopāsātraividhyādāśritatvād iha tadyogāt । atāvanti śatasaṃvatsarasyāhnāṃ sahasrāṇi bhavanti'; iti jīvaliṅgaṃ prāṇasaṃvādādimukhyaprāṇaliṅgaṃ tasmāt neti cet -

punaruktamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasya ākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - jīveti ।। anusandhīyate

uktamiti ca śeṣaḥ । saṃvādo vivādaḥ kalahaḥ prāṇasya prāṇaissaha saṃvāda iti vigrahaḥ । tathā ca yasmādatra prakaraṇe ataṃ śataṃ varṣāṇyabhyārcat tasmācchataṃ varṣāṇi puruṣāyuṣo bhavanti'; ityanena yacchatasaṃvatsaraparyantaṃ prāṇasya jīvadehe avastānahetukaṃ śatāyuṣṭvarūpaṃ jīvaliṅgamuktaṃ tat atāvanti śatasaṃvatsarasyāhnāṃ sahasrāṇi bhavanti'; ityādinā bahuṣu sthaleṣu anusandhīyate । yasmācca atā ahiṃsantāhamukthamahamukthamasmi'; iti vākyena prāṇasya prāṇairindriyaiḥ saha saṃvādarūpamukhyaprāṇaliṅgamuktam । yasmāccādipadagṛhītaṃ aprāṇo vaṃśa iti sthaviraḥ śākalyastadyathā śālāvaṃśe sarve anye vaṃśāḥ samāhitāssyuḥ evamasmin prāṇe cakṣuśśrotraṃ mano vāgindriyāṇi śarīraṃ sarva ātmā samāhitaḥ'; iti vākyena sarvajīvendriyadehadhārakatvarūpaliṅgaṃ coktamasti tasmādayaṃ prāṇo na viṣṇuḥ, kintu jīvamukhyaprāṇāveveti yojanā । yadyapi atasmācchataṃ varṣāṇi puruṣāyuṣo bhavanti'; iti śatāyuṣṭvaliṅgapratipādakavākyamevodāharaṇīyaṃ, na tu atāvanti'; iti vākyam । tathāpi liṅgasya bahuṣu sthaleṣu anugamo astīti jñāpanāyopaniṣado jīvaliṅge tātparyamastīti jñāpayitum anusandhivākyamevodāhṛtam । siddhānte śrutyarthastu - puruṣāyuṣaḥ śatasaṃvatsarasyāhnāṃ sahasrāṇi śatasaṃvatsarāntaḥpraviṣṭāharniyāmakasūryagatabhagavatpuruṣarūpāṇi tāvanti sahasrāṇi । kiyanti? bṛhatīsahasragatākṣarāṇāṃ vācyāni puṃrūpāṇi yāvanti sahasrāṇi tāvanti । tathā ca tāni ṣaṭtriṃśatsahasrāṇi sampannāni bhavanti । atāḥ'; cakṣurādidevatāḥ aahiṃsanta'; vivādamakurvan । kinviti? ahamasya caturmukhadehasyoktho asmi utthāpako asmīti ।

na, antarbahissarvagatatvenetyupāsātraividhyādihāśritatvācca ।

parihārāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - neti ।। prāṇo viṣṇurneti na, kintu viṣṇurevāyaṃ, na jīvādirityarthaḥ । kuto netyatastatra prāguktānugamahetvanuṣaṅgaṃ, na coktajīvamukhyaprāṇaliṅgavirodha ityatastatrahetutvena yataḥ śāstradṛṣṭyā tvayamupadeśaḥ ityasyānuṣaṅgaṃ, kimarthamantaryāmīti praśnasyāntarupāstyarthamiti parihāraṃ cābhipretya na copāsane avāntarabhedābhāva iti codyottaratvena pravṛttam aupāsā'; iti sūtrāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - antariti । gatatvenetyasyāntarbahissarvaśabdaiḥ pratyekaṃ sambandhaḥ । itiśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ । tathā ca dehāntargatatvena tadbahirgatatvena sarvagatatveneti prakāreṇa aupāsātraividhyāt'; bhagavadupāsanasya trividhatvādityarthaḥ। nanu tathāpi kathanaṃ vyarthaṃ vastuta upāsanātraividhyasyehānuktasyāntaryāmikathanāprayojakatvādityataḥ pravṛttam aāśritatvāt'; ityaṃśaṃ caśabdādhyāhāreṇa vyācaṣṭe - iheti । etatprakaraṇe uktatvādityarthaḥ । upāsātraividhyasyeti vipariṇāmenātrānvīyate । co

hetūpapādakahetusamuccaye । tathā ca atroktatraividhyāntargatāntaropāsanārthamantaryāmikathanaṃ yuktamiti bhāvaḥ ।

asa etameva sīmānaṃ vidāryaitayā dvārā prāpadyata'; asa etameva puruṣaṃ brahma tatamamapaśyat'; aetaddha sma vai tadvidvānāha mahidāsa aitareyaḥ'; ityādinā ।

atropāsanātraividhyamucyata ityatrāpi kiṃ liṅgamityata āha - sa iti । asaḥ'; vāsudevo bhagavān aetameva sīmānaṃ'; śiromadhyaṃ vidāryaiva aetayā dvārā'; suṣumnānāḍyā aprāpadyata'; prāptaḥ । caturmukhahṛdayamiti śeṣaḥ । anena bhagavato dehāntaḥpraveśokteḥ ukteścopāsanārthatvāt antarupāstiruktā bhavati । asaḥ'; caturmukhadehe prākprapadābhyāmantaḥ praviṣṭo nārāyaṇaḥ aetameva puruṣaṃ'; vyāsakṛṣṇakapilādirūpamātmānam ātataguṇaṃ svasvarūpabhūtamādānādikartāraṃ vā । tatamaṃ alopaḥ samāne'; iti sūtrāttalopaḥ । tamabarthe mapratyayo vā । tathā ca tatamaṃ atiśayena vyāptaṃ niravadhikavyāptimantaṃ abrahma'

guṇapūrṇam aapaśyat'; tadguṇakatayā tadrūpaṃ dadarśetyarthaḥ । kecittu - takāra eva vyāptyabhidhāyaka ityāhuḥ । anena sarvagatatvaṃ tathopāsanārthamuktam । atadetat'; prakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ avidvān'; jānannaitareyaḥ itarāyā apatyaṃ pumān viśālasaṃjñāt ṛṣeḥ utpannaḥ aitareyaḥ । amahidāso'; mahino mahātmāno devāḥ dāsabhūtāḥ yasyāsau bhagavānāhetyarthaḥ । hasmavaiśabdāḥ prasiddhidyotakāḥ । atra bahirupāstyarthaṃ mahidāsa āheti bahirupāstiruktā bhavati । na ca vācyamatra svarūpamātramucyate, nopāsanārthamiti । upāsanāṃ vinoktiprayojanābhāvāt । ityādinetyasyetyādināvākyenopāsanātraividhyasyāśritatvādarthāduktatvādityanvayaḥ । ādiśabdena ataṃ prapadābhyāṃ prāpadyata brahmemaṃ puruṣametasyāmetam'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । nanu aetaddhasmavai tadvidvānāha hiraṇyadanvaidaḥ'; itivanmahidāso api ṛṣitvenocyatāmiti cenna । asyāḥ upaniṣadaḥ aitareyasaṃjñayaivetarāputrasya mahidāsasya ṛṣitvasiddhyā taduktervyarthatvāt ।

mahidāsābhidho jajñe itarāyāstapobalāt ।
sākṣātsa bhagavānviṣṇuryastantraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ vyadhāt ।।

iti brahmāṇḍe ।

tathāpi mahidāsasya viṣṇutvaṃ kuto jñāyata ityata āha - mahidāseti ।। ajajñe'; vyakto babhūva । asa ca'; mahidāsaḥ -

mahidāsastvaitareyo bahvṛcopaniṣadgataḥ ।
sākṣātsa bhagavānviṣṇustannāmaiko munirhyabhūt ।।

iti chāndogyabhāṣye anantaroktabhagavadanyaḥ tatsaṃjñaketarāputraḥ ṛṣiratra na vivakṣitaḥ, kintu । yo avaiṣṇavaṃ'; viṣṇuviṣayaṃ atantraṃ'; granthaṃ avyadhāt'; nirmame । yadvā - atantraṃ'; pañcarātraṃ vyadhāt nāradādibhyo vyācakhyau । yaśca asākṣāt'; svayaṃ abhagavān'; pūrṇajñānādimān aviṣṇuḥ'; tadavatārabhūtaḥ pūrvoktaḥ sa evātra vivakṣita ityāha - sākṣāditi। brahmāṇḍe purāṇa ityasyāśritatvādityanenānvayaḥ । mahidāsasya viṣṇutvoktiriti tadarthaḥ । tena caśabdānvayaḥ ।

tattadupāsanāyogyatayā ca puruṣāṇām ।

nanvekavidhopāsanayā sarveṣāṃ brahmāparokṣasambhavātkimupāsātraividhyena ityataḥ pravṛttaṃ atadyogāt'; iti sūtraśeṣaṃ vyācaṣṭe - tattaditi ।। upāsanetyanena puruṣāṇāmityanena ca tadityasyāvṛttiḥ sūcitā । tathā ca teṣāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ manuṣyarṣigandharvadevākhyādhikāriṇāṃ teṣu trividhopāsaneṣu madhye tattadupāsane yathākramaṃ bahirantarvyāptirūpaikaikopāsana eva yogyatayā yogyatvena hetunetyarthaḥ । asyopāsātraividhyādityanenānvayaḥ । tathā cānekavidhopāstiyogyatāvatāmadhikāriṇāṃ naikavidhopāsanayā brahmajñānamiti tattraividhyamāvaśyakamiti bhāvaḥ ।

keṣāṃcitsarvagatvena keṣāṃciddhṛdaye hariḥ । keṣāñcidbahirevāsau upāsyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ । iti brāhme ।

puruṣāṇāmuktānekavidhopāsanayogyatā kuto jñāyata ityataḥ kartṛviśeṣānanupādāya sāmānyataḥ upāsakatraividhyapratipādikāṃ smṛtiṃ paṭhati - keṣāñciditi ।। apuruṣottamo'; hariḥ akeṣāñcit'; devānāṃ devaiḥ sarvagatatvena prakāreṇopāsyaḥ । akeṣāñcit'; ṛṣigandharvādīnāṃ ahṛdaye'; svasvahṛdayākāśe upāsyaḥ । akeṣāñcit'; manuṣyottamānāṃ tu bahirevopāsya ityarthaḥ । prācuryādevamuktiḥ । iti brāhma ityasya tattadupāsanayogyatayā tadviśiṣṭatvena puruṣāṇāmāśritatvāduktatvāditi pūrveṇānvayaḥ ।

agnau kriyāvatāṃ viṣṇuryogināṃ hṛdaye hariḥ ।
pratimāsvaprabuddhānāṃ sarvatra viditātmanām ।।
iti ca ।।
।। iti pādāntyaprāṇādhikaraṇam ।।

iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite brahmasūtrabhāṣye prathamādhyāyasya prathama pādaḥ

atraivādhikaraṇe kartṛviśeṣapratipādakaṃ viśeṣapramāṇamāha - agnāviti ।। viṣṇuḥ akriyāvatāṃ'

yajñādikriyānuṣṭhātṛṇām aagnau'; gārhapatyādau upāsyaḥ hariḥ । ayoginām'; ṛṣīṇāṃ hṛdaye upāsyaḥ । aaprabuddhānāṃ'; mandamatīnāṃ atyalpapratibhānāṃ manuṣyottamānāṃ apratimāsu'; kṛṣṇarāmādivigraheṣu upāsyaḥ । aviditātmanāṃ'; viśeṣato jñātabhagavadrūpāṇām aśrutapratibhānāṃ devānāṃ tu asarvatra'; sarvasthāneṣūpāsya ityarthaḥ । atrāgnau pratimāsviti vākyadvayena bahirmātropāsanopalakṣyate । ata eva sthānadvayoktiḥ । yathāśruteḥ sūryādau

viṣṇūpāsterbahirupāstitvaṃ na syāt । yogināmityanenāntarupāstiruktā । aṛṣayo antaḥprakāśāḥ'; iti śruteḥ । sarvatreti sarvagatopāstiriti jñātavyam । na cātra "yeṣāṃ bahirupāsanena mokṣasteṣāmapi hṛdyupāsanaṃ kiñcitkāryameva"iti bṛhadbhāṣyeṇa "bhagavān bimbadarśanenainaṃ mocayati"iti nyāyavivaraṇena ca virodhaśśaṅkyaḥ । agnāviti vākye anyaniṣedhābhāvena bimbaśabditasvasvayogyātmāparokṣārthaṃ hṛdyupāsanasyāpi sarvaiḥ kāryatvābhyupagamāt । mocakayogyāparokṣadvārābhūtāvatārādyaparokṣasādhanopāsanāya eva taistaiḥ prācuryeṇa prakaraṇasyāgnāviti vākyena vyavasthayā pratipādanācca । vacanadvayasyāpyekārthasādhakatvādasyāpi brāhme āśritatvāditi pūrveṇānvayaḥ । tattadupāsanayogyatāvattvena puruṣaviśeṣāṇāmuktatvāditi tadarthaḥ । ato na tadyogāditi hetvasiddhiḥ śaṅkyeti bhāva ।

anena nātroktaprāṇo viṣṇuḥ, kintu jīvamukhyaprāṇāveva । kutaḥ? ajīvamukhyaprāṇaliṅgāt'; śatāyuṣṭvarūpajīvaliṅgasyaprāṇasaṃvādādirūpamukhyaprāṇaliṅgasya ceha śravaṇāditi cet - na, viṣṇurevāyaṃ prāṇaḥ, na jīvādiḥ । kutaḥ? aanugamāt'; hetoreva, na cānyaśrutiliṅgavirodhaḥ । uktarītyā atadyogāt'; teṣāmantaryāmiviṣayatvopapatteḥ । yataśśāstradṛṣṭyāyam upadeśa iti vā । kimarthamatrāntaryāmikathanamiti cet, antarupāstyarthamiti brūmaḥ । na copāsane avāntarabhedābhāvaḥ । aupāsātraividhyāt'; antarādibhedena bhagavadupāsanasya trividhatvāt । na ca tathāpi kathanamayuktam । vāstavatraividhyasyehānuktasya kathanāprayojakatvāditi vācyam । aiha'; prakaraṇe tatraividhyasyāśritatvāduktatvāt । na caikavidhopāsanayā sarveṣāṃ brahmāparokṣasambhavāt kimupāsātraividhyeneti vācyam । atadyogāt'; teṣāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ tasmin tadupāsana eva yogyatvāt । anekavidhopāstiyogyatāvatāṃ ca puruṣāṇāṃ ekavidhapāsanayāparokṣāsambhavena yogyatābhedādupāsātraividhyasyāvaśyakatvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । na ca vivādakartṛtvaliṅgasyāntaryāmiviṣayatve audāsīnau ca tāvāstāṃ keśavaścābjasambhavaḥ'; iti vacanavirodhaḥ śaṅkyaḥ । tasyāntaryāmiviṣayabhinnabāhyarūpaviṣayatvāt । ato anyaliṅgānāṃ tattadantaryāmiviṣayatvopapatteḥ tadvirodhābhāvāt । viṣṇurevāyaṃ prāṇaḥ ānandamayaśceti yuktā tajjijñāseti siddham ।

।। iti pādāntyaprāṇādhikaraṇam ।।

iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryāṇāṃ sarvatantrasvatantrāṇāṃ

śrīmadraghunāthatīrthapūjyapādānāṃ śiṣyeṇa

śrīmajjagannāthayatinā kṛtāyāṃ

śrīmadbrahmasūtrabhāṣyadīpikāyāṃ

prathamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ

।।

tataḥ saptadaśe jātaḥ satyavatyāṃ parāśarāt ।
cakre vedataroḥ śākhā dṛṣṭvā puṃso alpamedhasaḥ ।। śrīmadbhāgavatam, 
taduktam īśāvāsyabhāṣyaṭīkāyāṃ - abrahmādīnām aprāptajñānamutpadyate śriyastu sarvadā vidyata iti vivekaḥ'; iti।

atha dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

sarvagatatvādhikaraṇam ।।

liṅgātmakānāṃ śabdānāṃ viṣṇau pravṛttiṃ darśayatyasmin pāde prādhānyena।

pūrvottarapādabhedasya svasminnekavākyatāyāśca siddhaye etatpādapratipādyaṃ darśayati - liṅgeti ।। liṅgānumāpako dharmaḥ । saḥ ātmevātmā pravṛttinimittaṃ yeṣāṃ te tathoktāḥ । animittanimittinorabhedopacārāt'; iti sudhokteḥ । svarūpārtho vā ātmaśabdaḥ । pūrvayojanāyāmātmapratipādake gauṇī vṛttiḥ । dvitīyāyāṃ tu sāmānādhikaraṇyamiti bhedaḥ । svārthe kaḥ । tathā ca vyāpyadharmadvārā dharmibodhakānāmāpātato yaugikānāmityarthaḥ । viṣṇoranyatra prasiddhānāmiti ca saṃyojyam aśabdānāmiti'; ekaprātipadikarūpāṇāmanekapadasamabhivyāhārarūpāṇāṃ cetyarthaḥ । aviṣṇau pravṛttiṃ'; prakarṣeṇa vṛttiṃ mahāyogavidvadrūḍhibhyāṃ viṣṇuparatvamiti yāvat । apradarśayati'; prakarṣeṇa sādhayati sūtrakāra ityarthaḥ । vaiśvānarādhikaraṇe nāmasamanvayakaraṇādavyāptinirāsāya prādhānyena ityuktam । tathā ca tatrāpi nāmasamanvayamukhena prādhānyena phalato bahuliṅgasamanvayasyaiva karaṇānnāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ ।

abrahma tatamam'; iti sarvagatatvamuktaṃ viṣṇoḥ । tacca atasyaitasyāsāvādityo rasaḥ'; ityādinā'dityasya pratīyate ।

yadyapi pūrvapādāntyadhikaraṇenaitatpādādyasya nāvāntarasaṅgatyapakṣeti na sā pradarśanīyā । tathāpi iha tasyāḥ sambhavātphalasyāvaśyavaktavyatvācca sā pradarśyata ityāśayena pūrvādhikaraṇasaṅgatiṃ viṣayādikaṃ ca darśayati brahmeti ।। iti vākye viṣṇoḥ nivadhikasarvagatatvamuktamityarthaḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha - tacceti ।। tadityāvartate, uktamiti ca vartate । tathā ca abrahma tatamam'; iti yattatamatvamuktaṃ prāṇākhyaviṣṇostattadekadeśabhūtaṃ sarvagatatvāntargataṃ sarvaprāṇihṛdayasthatvaṃ tatraivaitareyake aetaṃ hyeva bahvṛcāmahatyukte mīmāṃsanta etamagnāvadhvaryava etaṃ mahāvrate chandogāḥ etamasyāmetaṃ divyetaṃ vāyāvetamākāśa etamapsu etamoṣadhīṣvetaṃ vanaspatiṣvetaṃ candramasyetaṃ nakṣatreṣvetaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣvetameva brahmetyācakṣate'; ityādau etamityuttaravākyena uktamityarthaḥ । tato api kimityataḥ sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣamāha - tacceti ।। co avadhāraṇe । ādiśabdena asa yaścāyamaśarīraḥ prajñātmā yaścāsāvāditya ekametaditi vidyāt tasmāt puruṣaṃ puruṣaṃ pratyādityo bhavati sūrya ātmā jagatastasthuṣaśca etaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu'; ityādivākyaṃ gṛhyate । atra tasyetyāderupanyāsaḥ etamiti parāmaraśanīyasamarpakatayāvaśyakatvātpūrvapakṣayuktipradarśanārthaṃ ca kṛtaḥ । tathā ca yatha etamityuttaravākyenoktaṃ sarvaprāṇihṛdayasthatvaṃ tasyetyādinā pūrvavākyena prakṛtatvāttasyādityasyaiva pratīyate, atastasyaiva tatpūrvoktaṃ tatamatvamapi bhavet । na viṣṇoriti yojanā । atra pūrvapakṣe tatamatvaṃ saṅkucitaṃ sarvabhūtagatatvarūpaṃ vivakṣitam । na caivaṃ siddhāntyabhimataniravadhikasarvagatatvākṣepāprāptiriti vācyam । pūrvapakṣe aetameva'; iti avadhāraṇena viṣṇoranyatrākṣepāt tenāsyākṣepikīsaṅgatiḥ, viṣayasaṃśayau, viṣṇoranyasyaiva sarvaprāṇigatatvamiti sayuktikapūrvapakṣaśca darśito bhavati । siddhānete śrutyarthastu - atasya'; prakṛtasya aetasya'; saṃvatsaranāmakasya caturmukhasya sarvāditvatatamatvaniyāmakatvanimittairādityanāmā pradyumno rasaḥ sārabhūtaḥ । sa yaścāyaṃ puruṣadehagataḥ prākṛtadehavarjanādaśarīraḥ aprajñātmā'; jñānarūpo aniruddhaḥ । yaścāsāvāditye sthitaḥ pradyumna etatsthānadvayagataṃ rūpamekamiti vidyāt । tasmātpuruṣādityagatāniruddhapradyumnayoraikyādādityaḥ apuruṣaṃ puruṣaṃ prati'; pratipuruṣaṃ abhavati'; abhimukho bhavati । pratigṛhaṃ kūpa itivatsarvapuruṣagato bhavatīti ceti । ajagato'; jaṅgamasya atasthuṣaḥ'; sthāvarasya aātmā'; ādānādikartā asūryaḥ'; sūriprāpyo viṣṇurdivaṃ pṛthivīmantarikṣaṃ ca aāprāḥ'; āsamantādapūrayadityarthaḥ । etamityādīnāṃ saptamyantapadaiḥ pratyekaṃ sambandhaḥ । tathā ca abahvṛcāḥ'; ṛgvedinaḥ aetaṃ hyeva'; etameva puruṣādityagatameva hi viṣṇuṃ amahatyukthe'; mahadukthanāmakabṛhatīsahasre taddevatāviṣaye taddevatāmiti yāvat amīmāṃsante'; jānanti । aadhvaryavo'; yajurvedinaḥ aagnau'; cayanasādhaneṣṭakādevatāviṣaye taddevatāṃ mīmāṃsante । achandogāḥ'; sāmavedino amahāvrate'; tadākhyastotrasya devatāṃ stotre mīmāṃsante । aasyāṃ'; pṛthivyāṃ etaṃ adivi'; antarikṣe vāyvādau caivaṃ etameva asarveṣu bhūteṣu'; sarvaprāṇiṣu antaḥ vyāptamācakṣate vidvāṃśa ityarthaḥ । sarveṣvityeva pūrteḥ punarbhūteṣvityuktiratra bhūtavṛttitvamātraṃ pratipādyatayābhipretamiti jñāpayitum । etaṃ sarvabhūtagatameva viṣṇuṃ guṇapūrṇatvādvyāptatvācca etaṃ mukhyato brahmetyācakṣate iti vākyaśeṣārthaḥ । na sthānādhikaraṇaṭīkāyāṃ tu - sarveṣu bhūteṣu cakṣurādisthāneṣu etamekameva brahma guṇapūrṇamācakṣate iti vyākhyātam । pūrvapakṣī tu tasyaitasya prakṛtaprasiddhasaṃvatsarasyāsau prasiddha ādityaḥ sūryo rasaḥ sārabhūto adhipatirityarthaṃ manyate ।

ato abravīt - sū - oṃ।। 
sarvatra prasiddhopadeśāt ।।
atha siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati - ata iti ।। iti saṅgatisambhavādākṣepasadbhāvācca atastatparihārāyottaramabravīdbādarāyaṇa ityarthaḥ । tadeva sūtraṃ paṭhati - sarvatreti ।

asa yaścāyamaśarīraḥ prajñātmā'; ityādinā sarvatrocyamāno nārāyaṇa eva ।

atra samanvayasūtrāttattvityasyānuvṛttiṃ liṅgavyatyayam aucyamānam'; ityadhyāhāraṃ cābhipretya pratijñāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - sa yaśceti ।। vākyeneti śeṣaḥ । yadyapi atasyaitasyāsau'; ityādineti vaktavyam । pūrvavākyatvāt । tathāpi tasya pūrvapakṣayuktipradarśanārthatvenopanyastatvāttadvihāya siddhāntayuktipradarśakavākyajñāpanāya asa yaścāyamaśarīraḥ prajñātmā'; ityādinetyevoktam । vastutastu - na atasyaitasyāsau'; ityasyeva asa yaśca'; ityasya yuktipradarśanamātratātparyeṇopanyāsaḥ, nāpi viṣayamātrapradarśanatātparyeṇa । api tu pūrvaṃ viṣayavākyasya anudāhṛtatvāttadarthatayā tadgataitacchabdaparāmarśanayasamarpaṇārthamananyasādhāraṇasvato aśarīratvayuktipradarśanārthaṃ ceti dhyeyam । asarvatra'; sarvaprāṇihṛdayeṣvantargatatayocyamāno nārāyaṇa eveti । nārāyaṇaśabdaprayegena - 
yacca kiñcijjagatsarvaṃ dṛśyate śrūyate api vā ।
antarbahiśca tatsarvaṃ vyāpya nārāyaṇassthitaḥ ।।

iti vākyamapi saṅgṛhītaṃ bhavati । tena ca sūtre saṅkucitavṛttinā sarvatretyanena sarvabhūtahṛdgatatvasyaivābhipretatvenānyatra bahirneti prāptaśaṅkā nirastā bhavati ।

atadeva brahma paramaṃ kavīnām'; aparamaṃ yo mahadbrahma'

hetvaṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - tadeveti ।। vyākhyātametajjijñāsānayer । iśvarabrahmaṇorabhedabodhanārthaṃ pravṛttasya aparamaṃ yo mahadbrahma paramaṃ yaḥ parāyaṇam'; iti bhāratavākyasya yaḥ paramaṃ mahadbrahma yaḥ paramaṃ parāyaṇaṃ tasya lokapradhānasya jagannāthasya nāmnāmityuttaravākyenānvayaḥ ।

vāsudevātparaḥ ko nu brahmaśabdodito bhavat । sa hi sarvaguṇaiḥ pūrṇaḥ tadanye tūpacārataḥ ।। tasminneva prasiddhabrahmaśabdopadeśāt ।।

vāsudevādityaparā smṛtiḥ । avāsudevāt'; kṛṣṇādanyaḥ ko vā brahmaśabdamukhyavācyo bhavet, na ko api । kintu sa eva mukhyavācyaḥ । kutaḥ? ahi'; yasmāt asaḥ'; vāsudevaḥ sarvaguṇaiḥ pūrṇastadanye tvapūrṇāḥ tasmāt । tarhi abrahmāṇi jīvāḥ sarve api'; ityādi kathamityata āha tadanya iti ।। vāsudevādanye jīvāḥ aupacārataḥ'; amukhyata eva brahmaśabdoditāḥ, na tu mukhyata ityarthaḥ । anena sarvatretyasya hetāvapyanvayo darśitaḥ । tathā ca sarvatrodāhṛtavākyeṣu atasminneva'; viṣṇāveva aprasiddhasya'; rūḍhatvenāvagatasya abrahmaśabdasyopadeśāt'; sarvagate vastuni śravaṇādityarthaḥ । tasminnevetyanena śruterniravakāśatvamuktaṃ bhavati । anena asa yaścāyamaśarīraḥ prajñātmā'; ityādinā asarveṣu bhūteṣvetameva brahmetyācakṣate'; iti śākhāśeṣeṇa sarvatra sarveṣu bhūteṣu antargatatayocyamāno nārāyaṇa eva na tvādityādiḥ । kutaḥ? aetameva brahmetyācakṣate'; iti sarvabhūtagate vastuni nārāyaṇaikaniṣṭhatvena śrutyādiprasiddhabrahmaśabdopadeśācchruteriti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sū - oṃ।। vivakṣitaguṇopapatteśca ।।

asa yo ato aśrutaḥ'; ityādi ।

yuktyantareṇa viṣṇorevātroktasarvagatatvaṃ pratipādayatsūtramupanyasya tadupāttaśrutimevodāharati - vivakṣiteti। ādipadena aagato amato anato adṛṣṭo avijñāto anādiṣṭaḥ । śrotā mantā draṣṭādeṣṭā ghoṣṭā vijñātā prajñātā sarveṣāṃ bhūtānāmantarapuruṣaḥ sama ātmeti vidyāt'; iti vākyaśeṣo gṛhyate । ityādīti luptatṛtīyavibhaktikaṃ padam । asya vivakṣiteti sūtrapadenānvayaḥ । ata eva sūtrabhāṣyayorekībhāva iti tattvapradīpoktiḥ । anena sūtre śrutyeti śeṣaḥ sūcitaḥ । caḥ pūrvoktahetusamuccaye avadhāraṇe ca । yato vaktuṃ yogye vivakṣā bhavati । ato vivakṣitāḥ vaktuṃ yogyāḥ vakṣyamāṇā iti vā । ye tu śrutīnāṃ brahmaguṇeṣu tātparyābhāvaṃ vadanti, tannirāsāya vivakṣitapadamupanibabandha sūtrakṛditi tattvapradīpokteḥ śrutitātparyaviṣayabhūtā iti vā । sarvatretyanuvartate । gate iti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca sarvatra gate vivakṣitānāṃ śrutyā sarvatra gataniṣṭhatayā vaktuṃ yogyānāṃ itaḥparaṃ śrutyā sarvagataniṣṭhatayā vakṣyamāṇānāṃ śrutitātparyaviṣayībhūtānāṃ vā guṇānāmupasaṃhāragatāśrutatvādīnāṃ viṣṇoreva yogyatvena tasminnevopapatteḥ anyatrānupapatteśca sarvatrocyamāno nārāyaṇa eva iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । yaḥ prakṛto viṣṇuḥ saḥ aataḥ'; deśakālaguṇairvyāptaḥ । ata sātatyagamane iti dhātuvyākhyānāt asantato hyata ucyate'; iti vacanācca । yadvā - ato atistṛtīye atiśaye adhika ityarthaḥ । aaśrutaḥ'; sarvātmanā śrotumaśakyaḥ । svayameva svātmānaṃ svātantryeṇa śṛṇoti । anarte tvat'; iti śruteḥ । aagataḥ'; aprāptaḥ pūrṇatvātsarvātmanājñāta iti vā । sarvātmanā mananaviṣayo na bhavatītyamataḥ । anato netṛrahitaḥ svatantra iti yāvat । aadṛṣṭaḥ'; pratyakṣeṇa kenacit, sarvātmanā pūrṇatvāt । ata eva sarvātmanā aavijñātaḥ'; viśeṣato na jñātaḥ । aanādiṣṭaḥ'; niyojakaśūnyo anyairanājñapta iti vā । yathānyaiḥ svayamaśrutādirna tathānye, sarvātmanā śrutyādyā ityāha - śroteti । aśrotā'; yugapatsvātantryeṇa śravaṇakartā । amantā'; svātantryeṇa sarvamananakartā । svātantryeṇa sarvadraṣṭā । aādeṣṭā'; niyojanakartā । aāghoṣṭā'; samyagvaktā । avijñātā'; viśeṣeṇa jñātā । asarveṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ'; jīvānām aantaraḥ'; antasthaḥ apuruṣaḥ'; pūrṇaḥ asamaḥ'; samānaḥ, sarvarūpeṇa aātmā'; ādānādikarteti vidyādityaitareyabhāṣyatattvapradīpaviśveśvaratīrthīyadiśā śrutyarthaḥ ।

sa hi ana te viṣṇoḥ jāyamāno na jāto devaḥ'; ityādināśrutatvādiguṇakaḥ ।

nanvetacchrutyuktānām aśrutatvādiguṇānāṃ kuto viṣṇuniṣṭhatvamityata āha - sa hīti ।। hiśabdaḥ prasiddhau । asaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ ana te'; ityādinā vākyenāśrutatvādiguṇaḥ tadvattayā prasiddha ityarthaḥ । śrutau aśrotrādinā'; iti padādhyāhāreṇeti bhāvaḥ । yadyapi śrutāvatatvasya prathamoktatvādatatvādiguṇa iti vaktavyam । tathāpi tasya sarvagatatvarūpatvena viṣṇuniṣṭhatayā sādhyatvāt asiddhatvāt sa viṣṇuratatvādiguṇakaḥ prasiddha iti siddhanirdeśāyogāt aśrutatvādītyuktam । yadvā - viṣṇuratatvādiguṇakaḥ ana te viṣṇo'; ityādiśruteriti prayoge sarvagatatvarūpasyātatvasya sāodhyatvāttasya ca ana te viṣṇo'; ityādāvanukterhetvananvayādaśrutatvādītyuktam ।

asa savitā sa vāyuḥ sa indraḥ so aśrutaḥ so adṛṣṭo yo hariryaḥ paramo yo viṣṇuryo anantaḥ'; ityādicaturvedaśikhāyām ।।

ana te'; ityādiśrutau mukhato aśrutatvādikaṃ viṣṇorna pratīyate ityato atraivārthe spaṣṭaśrutiṃ cāha - sa iti । yaḥ asavitā'; jagadutpādakaḥ sa harireva । yo avāyuḥ'; balajñānarūpo devaḥ sa paramaḥ paramātmaiva । yaḥ aindraḥ'; paramaiśvaryavān sa viṣṇureva, na prasiddhādiḥ । yo aśruto adṛṣṭaḥ so ananto aparimito harireva nānya ityarthaḥ । yadvā - yo haryādiśabdavācyaḥ prasiddhaḥ, sa eva savitṛtvādiguṇavāciśabdavācya ityarthaḥ । ityādīti । yataḥ caturvedaśikhāyāmityādyuktamato api sa evāśrutatvādiguṇa ityanvayaḥ ।

na cādityaśabdāccakṣurmayatvādeva jīva iti vācyam ।

nanu yathā brahmaśabdādaśrutatvādiliṅgaiśca viṣṇuḥ sarvagata ityucyate । tathādityādiśabdātsarvajīvaliṅgāccādityaḥ sarvajīvā vā sarvagatāḥ kiṃ na syurityata āha - na ceti ।। aādityo rasaḥ'; ityādityaśabdāt sarvagatatvaprakaraṇe acakṣurmayaḥ śrotramayaḥ chandomayo manomayo vāṅmaya ātmā'; iti śrutau jñānakaraṇacakṣurādyātmakadehābhimānitvena jīve prasiddhāccakṣurmayatvādeścetyarthaḥ । hetusamuccaye caśabdaḥ। ajīvaḥ'; ityanena sūtragataṃ śārīrapadaṃ vyākhyātam । aśārīrau tāvubhau proktau jīvaśca paramastathā'; iti smṛteḥ । śarīrābhimānitvācca jīvasya śārītvaṃ yuktam । jīva ityekavacanaṃ samudāyābhiprāyam । jīvaścetyapi caśabdānvayaḥ । tenādityapratijñā samuccīyate । sarvatra gata iti śeṣaḥ । iti na vācyamiti sambandhaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। anupapattestu na śārīraḥ । 
।।
ekasya sarvaśarīrasthatvānupapattereva ।।

kuto na vācyamityatra hetvākāṅkṣāyāṃ sūtramupanyasya pratijñābhāgasyāvatārikābhāṣyeṇaiva vyākhyātatvāddhetvaṃśameva vyācaṣṭe - anupapatteriti ।। ekasyaikaikasya jīvasyeti vipariṇāmenānuvartate । sarvaśarīrasthatvasyānupapatteḥ sarvajīvasya samānabhogaprāptirūpopapattiviruddhatvādevetyarthaḥ । na tvanyaprāpakābhāvāditi hetvantaramanveṣaṇīyamityevaśabdārthaḥ । evetyanena sautratuśabdo vyākhyātaḥ । anupapattistu ṭīkāyāmeva sahetukamupapāditā ।

sū - oṃ।। karmakartṛvyapadeśācca । 
।।
aātmānaṃ parasmai śaṃsati'; ityādi ।।

yuktyantareṇa śārīrasya sarvagatatvaṃ nirākurvatsūtramupanyasya tadupāttaśrutimevodāharati - karmeti ।। bhāvapradhāno ayaṃ, caḥ samuccaye । asarvatroktaḥ śārīraḥ'; iti padatrayaṃ vipariṇāmenānuvartate । tathā ca sarvatroktasya sarvagatasya prakṛtasya aetamātmānaṃ parasmai śaṃsati'; ityaitareyaśrutau śaṃsanakriyāyāṃ sa etamātmānamiti karmatvena śārīrasya jīvasya ca tasyāmeva kartṛtvena vyapadeśāt ekasyāṃ kriyāyāṃ tayorutsargato bhinnatvaniyamāt apavādakāraṇābhāvācca na sarvatrocyamānaḥ śārīra ityarthaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu - cakārāt aparasmai'; iti sampradānavyapadeśāccetyabhiprāya ityuktam । yaḥ aetamātmānaṃ'; cakṣurmayatvādiguṇakaṃ paramātmānam aanyasmai'; ayogyāya aśaṃsati'; upadiśati tasya vedāḥ adugdhadohāḥ'; phalavidhurā bhavantītyarthaḥ । ityādītyasya pūrvavatsūtreṇānvayaḥ । ādipadena aātmānaṃ veda'; iti ṭīkoktaṃ ayastityāja sacividaṃ sakhāyaṃ na tasya vācyapi bhāgo asti'; iti tattvapradīpodāhṛtavākyaṃ ca gṛhyate । asacividaṃ'; karmasañcayavettāraṃ prītyā ekadeśasthatvāt sakhāyaṃ hariṃ ayastityāja'; tatyāja anyathā veda, tasya avāci'; vedādhyayanādau tasmāt abhāgaḥ'; phalaṃ nāsti narakaṃ ca syādityarthaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। oṃ।।

aetameva brahmetyācakṣate'; iti ।

yaduktaṃ brahmaśabdāt viṣṇureva sarvagata iti । tadayuktam, brahmaśabdasya jīve api vṛtteḥ । na cāsau jīve amukhya iti tadagrahaḥ । cakṣurmayatvādibādhakabalenāmukhyārthasyāpi grahaṇopapatteḥ । na ca dvitīyasūtroktabādhakānna jīvaḥ aśrutvāpyenaṃ veda na caiva kaścit'; iti gītāyāṃ jīvasyāśrutatvādiśravaṇāt, tṛtīyoktasya ca viṣṇāvapi sāmyāt । nāpi turīyoktacakṣurmayatvādibādhakena, ekasyaiva karmatvakartṛtvayoḥ upapatterityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya tadupāttaśrutimevodāharati - śabdeti ।। bhāṣyasya sūtreṇānvayaḥ । tathā ca aetameva brahmetyācakṣate'; iti vākye hetutvena prakṛtabrahmaśabdasya aviśeṣāt'; sāvadhāraṇatvarūpaviśeṣavattvādityarthaḥ । asya nānena brahmaśabdena śārīra ucyate iti labdhasādhyenānvayaḥ। anenaivakāro vidheyapadasaṅgataḥ, tacchiraskabrahmaśabdaśca mukhyabrahmatvārthakaḥ। sa ca jīve na yukta ityuktaṃ bhavati । yadvā - evakāra emityuddeśyavācipadenaiva saṅgato anyayogavyavacchedārthakaḥ । na caivaṃ brahmaśabdasya sāvadhāraṇatvāprāptiriti vācyam । evakārārthāvadhāraṇasyānyayogavyavacchedasyānyasmin brahmatvayogavyavaccheda iti vivaraṇe brahmaśabdārthabrahmatvasambandhāt brahmaśabdasya sāvadhāraṇatvaprāpteḥ । yadyapi na śārīra etacchabdārthaḥ । kutaḥ? tasya evakārārthapratiyogivācakabrahmaśabdenaiva viśeṣitatvāditi sūtravṛttissambhavati । tathāpi na sā ṭīkokteti na kairapi pradarśitā ।

na hi jīvameva brahmetyācakṣate ।

sāvadhāraṇatve api brahmaśabdasya kuto na jīve vṛttirityata āha - na hīti। hiśabdaḥ prasiddhau hetau ca। kavaya iti śeṣaḥ । kuta iti cet evakāraśiraskabrahmaśabdavācyatve jīvasya mukhyabrahmatvaṃ syāt, tacca nopapadyate । tasyāmukhyabrahmatvena prasiddhatvāditi bhāvaḥ । evamevakārasyoddeśyasambandhonānyayogavyavacchedakatve api pūrvapakṣe etacchabdārthatvena abhimatajīvādanyasya brahmatvaṃ niṣiddhaṃ syāt । tacca nopapadyate । jīvādanyasya paramātmāno mukhyabrahmaṇo jātyāderamukhyabrahmaṇaśca sattvenānyasya brahmatvasambandhaniṣedhāyogādityapi draṣṭavyam । tattvapradīpe tu - jīvasya brahmatve tasya bhūtatvena bhūteṣvityuktaṃ bhūtasthatvaṃ na yujyata ityuktam ।

aeṣa u eva brahmaiṣa u evātmaiṣa u eva savitaiṣa u evendra eṣa u eva harirharati paraḥ parānandaḥ'; iti cendradyumnaśākhāyām ।।

viṣṇāvapi sāvadhāraṇabrahmaśabdasya vṛttiḥ kuta ityata āha - eṣa iti ।। u eva । yadvā - uśabdo viṣṇuparaḥ । tathā caiṣa viṣṇureva brahmetyarthaḥ । aātmānam'; ityuktamātmatvaṃ asa savitā'; ityuktasavitṛtvādikamapi viṣṇorevetyāha - eṣa u evātmetyādinā । ya u yo viṣṇureva hariḥ । tatra nimittamāha - haratīti । yajñagṛheṣviḍopahūtaṃ bhāgaṃ svīkarotītyarthaḥ । yadvā - satāṃ pāpaṃ haratītyarthaḥ । evameṣa eva para uttamaḥ pūrṇānandaśceti yojanā । indradyumnaśākhāyāmityasya aya etaṃ sarvabhūtasthaṃ viṣṇumeva brahmetyācakṣate indradyumnāḥ'; ityupaskṛtenānvayaḥ । asya ca hetoravatārikāgatasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।।
ahamātmā guḍākeśa sarvabhūtāśayasthitaḥ । gāmāviśya ca bhūtāni dhārayāmyahamojasā । 
ityādi ।

smṛtisamākhyayāpi viṣṇoratroktasarvagatatvaṃ sādhayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā tāṃ smṛtimudāharati - smṛteśceti ।। ityādismṛteśca sarvatrocyamāno nārāyaṇa evetyanvayaḥ । na kevalamuktahetubhya iti cakārārthaḥ । smṛteḥ svavacanatve api paroktānuvādarūpatvāt taduktiryuktā । he aguḍākeśa'; guḍākā nidrā tadīśastadrahita iti yāvat । guḍavadāsamantātkeśā yasya saḥ ślakṣṇakeśeti vā । ahamantaryāmitayā sarvahṛdayasthita ityarthaḥ agāṃ'; bhūmiṃ āviśya tatrāvatīrya abhūtāni'; jīvān aojasā'; sāmarthyena dhārayāmītyanyavākyasyārthaḥ । ime ca gītāyāmarjunaṃ prati kṛṣṇavākye । pūrvavākye sarvabhūtāśayastho ya ātmā jīvaḥ so ahamityabhedapratītinirāsāya dvitīyavākyodāharaṇam । tadgatatvenaiva taddhārakatvamabhipretam । ādipadātsmṛtyantarasaṅgrahaḥ ।

na cāprāmāṇikaṃ kalpyam ।।

anye tu amanomayaḥ prāṇaśarīro bhārūpaḥ satyasaṅkalpaḥ'; iti vākye manomayatvādiguṇar iśvara eva, na jīva iti siddhāntite jīveśayoraikyāt kathametadityāśaṅkya asti bhedaḥ । na cāpasiddhāntaḥ, yato ayaṃ na pāramārthikaḥ, kintu, mithyābhūta eva sūtrakṛtā vivakṣita iti samādhāya bhedamithyātve sūtratātparyaṃ varṇayanti । teṣāṃ matamāśaṅkya dūṣayati - na ceti ।। castvarthe । nañ ca tadviruddhatadabhāvārthaḥ । tathā ca aaprāmāṇikaṃ'; bhedamithyātvaṃ ana kalpyaṃ'; sūtrakṛdvivakṣāviṣayatvena na kalpanīyam । kutaḥ? yatastadaprāmāṇikaṃ pramāṇaśūnyaṃ advā suparṇā'; ityādipramāṇaviruddhaṃ ca ata iti yojanā ।

sū - oṃ।। arbhakaukastvāttadvyapadeśācca neti cenna nicāyyatvādevaṃ vyomavacca ।।

sarveṣu bhūteṣvityalpaukastvāt cakṣurmayatvādinā jīvavyapadeśācca neti cenna ।

uktārthamākṣipya samādadhatsūtraṃ paṭhitvākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - arbhaketi ।। vākya iti śeṣaḥ । arbhaketyasya vyākhyālpeti । alpamokaḥ sthānaṃ yasya tasya bhāvastattvaṃ tasmāt । tathācālpasthānasthitatvokterityarthaḥ । sarvajīvahṛdayasuṣirāṇāmalpatvāditi bhāvaḥ । sūtragatatacchabdasya prakāraprakāryubhayārthatvaṃ matvāha - cakṣuriti, jīva iti ca । ādipadena śrotramayatvādi gṛhyate । cakārādādiśabdādvā ādityaśrutirapi gahyate । ata eva jīvapadamādityasādhāraṇaṃ prāyoji । jīvasya vyapadeśo vacanaṃ jīvavyapadeśaḥ acakṣurmayaśśrotramayaḥ'; iti śrutāviti śeṣaḥ । co hetusamuccaye । sarvatrocyamāno nārāyaṇa eveti yaduktaṃ tannetyarthaḥ । paramātmapakṣe api jīvapakṣa iva bādhakasadbhāvāditi bhāvaḥ ।। parihārāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - neti । uktabādhakādviṣṇoḥ sarvatrocyamānatvābhāvo netyarthaḥ ।

arbhakaukastvena cakṣurmayatvādirūpeṇa ca tasyaiva viṣṇornicāyyatvāt ।

kuto netyato atra bādhakābhāvāditi hetum arbhakaukastvādīnāṃ ca viṣṇāvevopapannatvenābādhakatvāditi tadupapādakahetuṃ copaskṛtya tarhi viṣṇāvarbhakaukastvādikathanavaiyarthyamityāśaṅkya tatparihāratvenoktamevaṃnicāyyatvādityaṃśaṃ vyākhyāti - arbhakaukastveneti । ādiśabdenmanomayatvena ityāha । anena sautraivaṃśabdaḥ prakārārthatayā vyākhyātaḥ । siddhāntāṃśe api viṣṇvarthakasya vyatyastatacchabdasya sāvadhāraṇasyānvayamabhipretyāha - tasyaiveti । yadvā - pradhānasūtre anuvṛttasya tadityasyeha vipariṇatasyāvṛttiṃ matvāha - tasyaiva viṣṇoriti । tathā ca sarvagatasyāpi jīvavilakṣaṇasyāpītyarthaḥ । na tu jīvasya, ityanyaniṣedhārtho vā evakāraḥ । anicāyyatvāt'; upāsyatvāt । anenāparichinne alpaukastvoktiḥ jīvavilakṣaṇe cakṣurmayatvādyuktivyartheti śaṅkā nistā bhavati ।

sarvagatatve apyalpaukastvaṃ ca yujyate vyomavat ।

idānīṃ sarvagatasyālpaukastvamayuktamiti śaṅkānirāsāya sūtragṛhītaṃ dṛṣṭāntāṃśaṃ evamityasya caśabdenāpyanvayaṃ vyatyastatatpadasya āvṛttasya ayujyate'; iti adhyāhṛtenāpi sambandhamabhipretya vyākhyāti - sarvagatatva iti ।। apīti dvitīyacaśabdavyākhyānam ।

sarvendriyamayo viṣṇuḥ sarvaprāṇiṣu ca sthitaḥ ।
sarvanāmābhidheyaśca sarvavedoditaśca saḥ ।।

yadapi jīvavilakṣaṇasya nityajñānavato jñānakaraṇacakṣurādiprācuryarūpacakṣurmayatvādikathanamayuktamiti codyaṃ, tat caśabdasūcitasmṛtyā nirāha - sarvendriyamaya iti ।। viṣṇuryataḥ sarvaprāṇiṣu saṃsthitaḥ । prāṇā indriyāṇi tadvantaḥ prāṇinaḥ teṣvindriyaniyāmakatvena sthitaḥ । sarvendriyasvāmīti yāvat । ataḥ sarvendriyamaya ityukta ityarthaḥ। svāmitvaṃ mayaḍartha iti bhāvaḥ । caśabdaḥ prathamapādārthe dvitīyapādārthaṃ hetumāha । evaṃ dvitīyatṛtīyapādadvayamapi ādityādisarvaprāṇisthitatvādādityādisarvanāmābhidheya iti hetuhetumadbhāvena vyākhyeyam । ata eva caśabdaḥ dvitīyatṛtīyacaśabdavat viśeṣaṇāntarasamuccayepyanveyaḥ । anena prathamapādena acakṣurmayaḥ śrotramayo manomayo vāṅmayaḥ'; ityādikaṃ brahmaṇi tatsvāmitvena nimittena prayuktamiti vyākhyātaṃ bhavati । evaṃ dvitīyatṛtīyapādābhyāṃ tattadgatatvenādityāditattannāmavācyatvakathanamukhenādityaśruterīśvaravācitvamuktaṃ bhavati । anenaivāditye anuktiyuktivirodhaśca parihṛtaḥ । caturthapādena chandaḥpadoktavedamukhyārthatvācchandomayatvaṃ ca viṣṇoryuktamitiyuktaṃ bhavati । aitareyabhāṣye - asampūrṇadarśanaśakteḥ cakṣurmayaḥ sampūrṇaśravaṇaśakteḥ śrotramayaḥ satyakāmatvāt chandomayaḥ sarvamantṛtvānmanomayaḥ sarvavaktṛtvādvāṅmayaḥ pūrṇaphalarūpatvādātmā'; iti । tathā bṛhadbhāṣye - amayaṭprāyuryārthaḥ svarūpe ca'; iti pratijñāya - sarvadraṣṭṛsvarūpatvāccakṣurmaya itīryate । sarvaśrotṛsvarūpatvātsa śrotramayar iritaḥ ।। iti । tathā bhāgavatatātparye - sarve viṣṇau sthitā yasmādatassarvamayo hyasau । iti prakārāntareṇa bhagavati cakṣurmayatvādikaṃ vyākhyātam । skānde ityanantaraṃ uktvāditi śeṣaḥ । asya jīvavilakṣaṇasyāpi indriyasvāmitvādinā cakṣurmayatvādi yujyate iti na tadayoga ityupaskṛtasādhyenānvayaḥ । anena asarveṣu bhūteṣu'; ityātrārbhakaukastvokteḥ acakṣurmayaḥ'; ityādau ca tasya jīvasya tena cakṣurmayatvādinā prakāreṇoktatvāt ādityavyapadeśācca asmādeva bādhakānna sarvatrokto nārāyaṇa iti cet - na, kutaḥ? atra bādhakābhāvāt, arbhakaukastvādeśca viṣṇāvevopapatteḥ । na cāparicchinnasyārbhakaukastvoktiḥ jīvavilakṣaṇasya cakṣurmayatvādyuktiśca vyartheti vācyam । cāyṛ pūjāniśāmanayoḥ । tasyaiva tasyāparicchinnasyāpi viṣṇoḥ alpaukastvacakṣurmayatvādinā prakāreṇopāsyatvena upāsanārthaṃ taduktisārthakyāt । na cāparicchinne jīvavilakṣaṇe ca brahmāṇi arbhakaukastvādyuktirna yujyata iti vācyam। yataḥ aevaṃ ca'; evamapi sarvagatatve api avyomavat'; tadalpaukastvaṃ cakṣurmayatvādi yujyate । yathā vyāptasyāpi vyomno avyākṛtākāśasya maṭhādyekadeśāvasthitiḥ tathā brahmaṇo bhūtāśayādau sthitiryuktā । yataścaivaṃ viṣṇorjīvavilakṣaṇatve api indriyasvāmitvādinā cakṣurmayatvādyuktiryuktāta iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sū - oṃ।। sambhogaprāptiriti cenna vaiśeṣyāt ।।

jīvaparayorekaśarīrasthatve samānabhogaprāptiriti cenna ।

punaruktamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasyati - sambhogeti । atra pūrvasūtrādevaṃśabdamanuvartya tadbodhitamāpādakaṃ darśayan pūrvapakṣāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - jīveti ।। jīvaparamātmanorityarthaḥ । eketi ।। viṣṇoḥ sarvaśarīrasthatve jīvena sahaikaśarīrasthatvaprāpteriti bhāvaḥ । saṃśabdasya avyavahṛpaṇossamarthayoḥ'; ityatreva samānārthatvamāśrityāha - samāneti । iveśvarapakṣe api bādhakasāmyānnāyaṃ sarvagata iti vākyaśeṣaḥ । parihārāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - neti। neśvarasya samānabhogaprāptirityarthaḥ ।

sāmarthyavaiśeṣyāt ।

kuto netyastatra hetutvena vaiśeṣyādityaṃśaṃ yojayati - sāmarthyeti ।। svārthe ṣyañ । viśeṣiṇo bhāva iti vā । tathā ca parasya samānabhogāprāptau jīvādapi sāmarthyavaiśeṣyādityarthaḥ ।

uktaṃ ca gāruḍe - sarvajñālpajñatābhedātsarvaśaktyalpaśaktitaḥ । svātantryapāratantryābhyāṃ sambhogo neśajīvayoḥ ।।

।। iti sarvagatatvādhikaraṇam ।।

kiṃ tatsāmarthyavaiśeṣyaṃ, yena samānabhogāprāptirityata āha - uktamiti ।। na kevalaṃ sūtre jīveśayorbhogasāmyābhāvaḥ, tatra hetutvena sāmarthyavaiśeṣyaṃ coktam, kintu gāruḍe ceti samuccayārthaścaḥ । kimuktamityatastatpaṭhati - sarvajñeti ।। sarvajñatvālpajñatvarūpabhedakadharmābhyāmityarthaḥ । prāptasya bādhakasya parihārāya viṣṇoḥ sāmarthye satyapi prathamaṃ prāptistāvatsyādeva agnistambhavato dāhaprāptivat । sāpi bhagavati na sambhavati । tasya sārvajñenaiṣyadbādhakaparihartṛtvasambhavāditi bhāveneha sārvajñoktiḥ, na jīvena sahekaśarīrasthatve api duḥkhaparityāgena sukhamātrabhoge svātantrayaṃ hetuḥ । jīvasya cobhayānubhave pāratantryaṃ heturiti vivektavyam । sambhogaḥ samānabhogaḥ । aiti ca'; iti caśabdapāṭhe tatra pūrvoktena samuccayārthaścakāraḥ। anena yato yathā ekasya jīvasya sarvaśarīrasthatve sarvasamānabhogaprāptiḥ bādhikānupapattiḥ sūtroktāsti । tathā evamīśasya sarvabhūtagatatvamaṅgīkṛtya jīveśvarayorekaśarīrasthatve parasya jīvasamānabhogaprāptirbādhikāsti । ato neśvaraḥ sarvabhūtagata iti cenna, kutaḥ tasya tadaprāptau jīvādapi sāmarthyavaiśeṣyāt agnistambhavato dāhābhāvavaditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।।

।। iti sarvagatatvādhikaraṇam ।।

।। attṛtvādhikaraṇam ।।

ajanmādyasya yataḥ'; ityuktam । tatrāttṛtvaṃ asa yadyadevāsṛjata tattadattumadhriyata sarvaṃ vā attīti tadaditeradititvam'; ityaditeḥ pratīyate ।

atrādhikaraṇe lokato anyatra prasiddhāditiśabdena sahoktāttṛtvaliṅgasya harau samanvayaḥ kriyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiḥ viṣayavākyamudāhṛtya viṣayasaṃśayau sayuktikapūrvapakṣaṃ ca sūcayati - janmeti ।। janmādisūtre janmādikartṛtvaṃ viṣṇoruktamityarthaḥ । tatreti । uktalakṣaṇeṣu madhya ityarthaḥ । praviṣṭamiti śeṣaḥ ।।

sa sargakāle ca karoti sarvaṃ saṃhārakāle tu tadatti bhūyaḥ । sraṣṭā pātā tathaivāttā ityādāvadidhātuprakṛtikānekaśabdavācyaṃ saṃhartṛtvāparaparyāyaśabdabodhyaṃ ūrṇanābhyādivadattṛtvaṃ tadityarthaḥ । anena aderbhakṣaṇārthatvādaditerattṛtve api na saṃhartṛtvalakṣaṇasyātivyāptiriti śaṅkā nirastā । prathametiśabdaḥ śrutigataḥ । dvitīyastu bhāṣyakārīyaḥ । tatraikaṃ bhāvapradhānam । tathā ca iti bṛhadāraṇyakavākye yadattṛtvaṃ pratīyate tat aditeḥ devamātureva bhavet । kutaḥ? aaditeḥ'; aditiśruteḥ । tathā adititvaliṅgācceti yojanā । adititvaṃ ca gotvādivadaditimātradhramo, na viṣṇau sāvakāśam । anena janmādisūtroktalakṣaṇasyātivyāptyasambhavākṣepāttenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiḥ । śrutyuktamattṛtvaṃ viṣayaḥ । viṣṇoranyasya veti sandehaḥ । devamāturaditereveti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । aditiśrutiradititvayuktiśca sūcitā bhavati । pūrvapakṣe śrutyarthastu - asaḥ'; aditirdevamātā saṃvatsaranāmnā caturmukhena ayadyadasṛjata tattadattumadhriyata'; manaḥ । kutaḥ sarvāttṛtvamaditeḥ? yasmātsarvātrī sā sarvamattīti yat tadeva hyaditerdevamātuḥ aadititvam'; aditiśabdavācyatve nimittam, anyathā tanna syāditi । asmin pakṣe api sthalāntarasthāditiśabdasya nirvacanamidam । atra sarvaśabdaḥ sudhārītyā adityadanayogyasarvaparaḥ । ṭīkārītyā saṅkucitasarvaparo vā। siddhānte śrutyarthastu - asaḥ'; saṃvatsaranāmakaḥ caturmukho ayadyadevāsṛjata tattatsarvamattuṃ'; sa mṛtyunāmā janārdano adhriyata । kutaḥ sarvasaṃhartṛtvaṃ viṣṇoḥ? aaditeḥ'; aditiśabdāt । aditirhi aidaṃ sarvaṃyadidaṃ kiñca'; aaditirdevatāmayī'; iti śrutyantare brahmaṇyaditiśabdaprayogāditi yāvat । tāvatāpi kutaḥ sarvāttṛtvaṃ viṣṇoḥ? sarvamattīti yattadeva hi aaditeḥ'; strīliṅgāditiśabdavācyasya aadititvam'; aditiśabdavācyatvaṃ anyathā sa nirnimittakaḥ syāditi bhāvaḥ । anena viṣṇoḥ sarvāttṛtāyāṃ tannimittakaśrutyantaragatāditiśabdo heturityuktaṃ bhavati । uktaṃ hi candrikāyām । atattadattumiti pūrvapratijñātasarvāttṛtāyāṃ śrutyantare brahmaṇi prayuktasya sarvāttṛtvanimittakasyāditiśabdahetūkaraṇe sambhavati'; iti । ata eva ṛgbhāṣye aatti viśvaṃ tena caivāditiriti viṣṇuḥ'; ityuktam । tatraiva aguṇataḥ kālataścānantyarūpamakhaṇḍitatvaṃ cāditiśabdapravṛttinimittam'; iti coktam ।

asa yadyadevāsṛjata'; iti pulliṅgaṃ ca akūṭastho akṣara ucyate'; ityādivat ।।

nanvetadattṛtvamaditeścetkathaṃ tarhi tasyāṃ sa iti pulliṅgaṃ yuktaṃ syāt । atastena śrutyādibādha ityata āha - sa iti ।। iti vākye śrutamityarthaḥ । ityādivadityānantaraṃ adityāṃ yujyata iti śeṣaḥ । ādipadena aso ahaṃ vāyuṃ diśāṃ vatsaṃ veda'; iti chandogavākyaṃ gṛhyate । kūṭamākāśaṃ tadvannirvikāratayā tiṣṭhatīti kūṭasthaḥ । prakṛtiḥ aakṣaro'; dehato avināśitvāducyate iti gītāvākyasyārthaḥ । dikśabditānāṃ pūrvādi caturdigavasthitabhagavadbāhūnāṃ avatsaṃ'; tato jātaṃ avāyuṃ'; mukhyaprāṇamahaṃ aveda'; jānāmītyarthaḥ ।

atrocyate - sū - oṃ।।
attā carācaragrahaṇāt ।।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati - atreti ।। iti codye samādhānamucyate sūtrakṛtā iti śeṣaḥ । anena sūtre atrocyate iti śeṣo darśitaḥ । tatsūtraṃ paṭhati - atteti । tattvityanuvartate, vipariṇamyate ca । tathā cātra vākye yaḥ aattā'; saṃhartocyate sa viṣṇureva । kutaḥ? asarvaṃ vā atti'; iti acarācarasya'; cetanācetanarūpasya viśvasyādyatayā saṃhāryatayā agrahaṇāt'; carācarāttṛtvaliṅgāditi yāvaditi sūtrārthaḥ ।

na hi carācarasya sarvasyāttṛtvamaditeḥ ।

carācarasyādyatayā grahaṇe api kuto nāditestadattṛtvamiti liṅgasya sāvakāśatvaśaṅkāṃ nirāha - na hīti।। hiśabdaḥ prasiddhau । carācarasyeti sūtrākṣarāṇyanūdya śrutyanusāreṇa sarvasyeti vyākhyānam । na ca sāmānyapadena vyākhyānaṃ vyarthamiti vācyam । sūtrasya śrutivisaṃvādapratītinirāsārthatvāt । aaditeḥ'; devamātuḥ ।

sraṣṭā pātā tathaivāttā nikhilasyaika eva tu । vāsudevaḥ paraḥ puṃsāmitare alpasya vā na vā ।।

carācarāttṛtvaṃ viṣṇorapi kutaḥ siddhamityata āha - sraṣṭeti ।। apuṃsāṃ paraḥ'; tebhyaḥ uttamo avāsudevaḥ'; kṛṣṇaḥ aeka eva'; nikhilajagataḥ ekaḥ svatantraḥ asraṣṭā'; sṛṣṭikartā tathā apātā'; rakṣitā tuścārthaḥ । avasudevetare'; brahmādyāstu aalpasya'; jagadekadeśasyāsvātantryeṇa sṛṣṭyādi kartāro bhavanti। svātantryāpekṣayā netyarthaḥ। iti skānde ityanantaram uktatvāditi vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

ekaḥ purastādya idaṃ babhūva yato babhūva bhavanasya gopā ।
yamapyeti bhuvanaṃ sāmparāye sa no harirghṛtamihāyuṣe attudevaḥ ।।

spaṣṭārthatvātprathamaṃ smṛtimudāhṛtyātraivārthe śrutimapyāha - eka iti ।। eka ityasyāvṛttiḥ, idamityasyāpyāvṛttipariṇāmau । tathā ca ya ekaḥ aidam'; asya jagataḥ apurastāt'; pralaye babhūva । yataśca sṛṣṭau aidaṃ'; jagat ababhūva'; jātam । atha yaścaiko bhavanasya agopāḥ'; goptā babhūva । yaṃ ca asāmparāye'; muktipralayayoḥ bhuvanaṃ praviśati nigīrṇaudanavat । asaḥ devo'; hariḥ naḥ aāyuṣe'; āyurarthe aiha'; yajñasthāne āgatya aghṛtam'; āhutirūpam aattu'; svīkarotviti taittirīyaśrutyarthaḥ । mantradraṣṭṛṛṣivākyametat । iti śrutyanantaraṃ yata iti śeṣaḥ । asyāto api viṣṇoścarācarāttṛtvaṃ siddhamityanvayaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। oṃ।।
