yadā niravakāśasarvāttṛtvaliṅgamātrātsāvakāśāditiśrutyadititvaliṅgayorbādhena attā viṣṇureveti siddhyati । tadā kimu vācyaṃ niravakāśaprakaraṇasamuccitālliṅgādityarthaṃ pratipādayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe - prakaraṇācceti ।। anaivehaṃ kiñcana'; iti niravakāśaviṣṇuprakaraṇabalāccāttā viṣṇureveti sūtrārthaḥ ।

apsaṃvatsarasṛṣṭyādinā tatprakaraṇatvācca ।

prakaraṇasya vaiṣṇavatvāsiddhimāśaṅkyāha - apsaṃvatsarasṛṣṭyādineti ।। apsṛṣṭiḥ saṃvatsaranāmakacaturmukhasṛṣṭiśca te ādī yasya tat tathoktam । ādipadena saṃvatsarādanodyamādiliṅgaṃ gṛhyate । atatprakaraṇatvāt'; viṣṇuprakaraṇatvādityarthaḥ । etatprakaraṇasyeti śeṣaḥ । avagamopalakṣakametat । asyātaḥ prakaraṇādviṣṇureva atrocyate iti prakṛtasādhyenānvayaḥ । co hetusamuccaye । prakaraṇaṃ nāmaikaprameyapratipādakānekavākyāni । bṛhadāraṇyake hi - anaiveha kiñcanāgra āsīt । mṛtyunaivedamāvṛtamāsīt । aśanāyayāśanāyā hi mṛtyustanmano akurutātmanvī syāmiti। so arcannacaratatasyārcata āpo ajāyantatadyadapāṃ śara āsīttatsamahanyata sā pṛthivyabhavat tasyāmaśrāmyat so akāmayata dvitīyo ma ātmā jāyeteti sa manasā vācā mithunaṃ samabhavadaśanāyā hi mṛtyustadreta āsīttatsaṃvatso abhavat taṃ jātamabhivyādadātsa bhāṇamakarotsaiva vāgabhavatsa aikṣata yadi ha vā imamabhimaṃsye kanīyo annaṃ kariṣya iti sa tayā vācā tenātmanā idaṃ sarvamasṛjata'; iti viṣṇuviṣayāṇyanekavākyāni śrūyante । aagre'; pralaye aiha'; asvatantravarge, gagana iti vā । akiñcana'; jīvajaḍarūpaṃ vastu naivāsīditi । 
nanu - sarvasaṃhārakaṃ viṣṇuṃ devīṃ jīvāṃstathaiva ca ।
kālaṃ triguṇasāmyaṃ ca karmāṇi prāṇamindriyam ।
saṃskāraṃ caiva vedāṃśca narte kiñcillaye tvabhūt ।।

iti bṛhadbhāṣyodāhṛtavacanānnityānāṃ jīvānāmapi sattvātkathamiyamuktirityata uktaṃ - mṛtyunaiveti । aidaṃ'; jīvādikaṃ amṛtyunā'; tannāmakena janārdanena aāvṛtam'; ācchāditamāsīt । mṛtyorāvarakatve hetuḥ - aśanāyayeti । aśaṃ jagattannetryetyarthaḥ । mṛtyoraśanāyātvaṃ śrutiprasiddhamityāha - aśanāyā hīti । atat'; tasmādekākitvānmṛtyuḥ aātmanvī'; jagadrūpaśarīravān syāmityaicchat । evaṃ sa mṛtyuḥ aarcan'; svātmānaṃ pūjayan sañcacāra tasyārcata āpo ajāyanta । tā eva tāsāmarcanasādhanamiti bhāvaḥ । tatrāpsu yo apāṃ aśaraḥ'; phenarūpo maṇḍa āsīttaccharaḥ । sa śaro mṛtyunāsvaretasā asamahanyata'; saṅghātatvaṃ prāpitaḥ । yassaṅghātaḥ sā apṛthivī'; brahmāṇḍarūpābhavat atasyāṃ'; pṛthivyāṃ śvetadvīpe aaśrāmyat'; śiśye mṛtyuḥ । sa mṛtyuḥ ame'; mama aātmā'; brahmā dvitīyo vāyvapekṣayā jāyeteti akāmayata । atha aaśanāyā'; sa mṛtyuḥ amanasā'; svecchayā avācā'; vedābhimāniśriyā amithunaṃ'; dvandvībhāvaṃ asamabhavat'; prāpat । tena mithunībhāvena yadreta āsīt atatsaṃvatsaraḥ'; tupādānakadehavān saṃvatsaranāmakaścaturmukho abhavat । atha jātaṃ saṃvatsaramabhilakṣya attuṃ avyādadāt'; vidadāra svamukhaṃ mṛtyuḥ । sa saṃvatsaro bhayāt viṣṇudīptyānandabodhakabhāṇiti śabdamakarot । yadbhāṇiti vacastadabhimāninī saiva vāṅnāmnī sarasvatyabhavat । sa mṛtyuḥ aikṣata ālocitavān । kimiti? ayadīmaṃ'; saṃvatsaram aabhimaṃsye'; līnaṃ kariṣye tattadā me akanīyaḥ'; alpamannaṃ kariṣye । tato bahvannaṃ bhavatvityālocya sa mṛtyuḥ atayā vācā'; sarasvatyā atenātmanā'; caturmukhenedaṃ sarvamasṛjata । janayāmāseti śrutyarthaḥ ।

nehāsītkiñcanāpyādau mṛtyurāsīddharistadā ।
so ātmano manasāsrā kṣīdapa eva janārdanaḥ ।।

śayānastāsu bhagavānnirmame aṇḍaṃ mahattaram ।
tatra saṃvatsaraṃ nāma brahmāṇamasṛjatprabhuḥ ।।

tamattuṃ vyādadādāsyaṃ tadāsau virurāva ha ।
atha tatkṛpayā viṣṇuḥ sṛṣṭikarmaṇyayojayat ।।

so asṛjadbhuvanaṃ viśvamadyārthaṃ haraye vibhuḥ ।।
iti brahmavaivarte ।।
।। iti attṛtvādhikaraṇam ।।

nanvapsaṃvatsasṛṣṭyādinātrocyamānenāpi kathamasya viṣṇuprakaraṇatvaniścaya ityato apsaṃvatsarasṛṣṭyāderviṣṇuliṅgatvāditi bhāvena tasya talliṅgatve smṛtimāha - nehāsīditi ।। aādau'; pralaye aiha'; asvatantravarge akiñcināpi'; jīvo jaḍaṃ vā nāsīt । nanvidamayuktaṃ, jīvādeḥ nityasya sattvādityata āha - mṛtyuriti । pralaye mṛtyunāmā hariḥ jīvādyāvarakatvenāsīt । ata āvṛtatvānnāsīdityuktamiti nānupapattiriti bhāvaḥ । asaḥ ātmanaḥ'; iti padacchedaḥ । amantreṣvāṅyāderātmanaḥ'; ityāllopaḥ । tathā ca asaḥ'; prabhurviṣṇurātmano amanasā'; svecchayaivāpo asrākṣīt । atāsu'; apsu amahattaraṃ'; svārthe tarap । mahat sthūlam aaṇḍaṃ'; brahmāṇḍaṃ nirmame । atatra'; aṇḍe saṃvatsarākhyaṃ brahmāṇamasṛjadityanvayaḥ nāmetyanena samyagvatsabhūtān ramayatīti vyutpattyā saṃvatsaraśabdaścaturmukhe prasiddha ityucyate । atrāsāmarthyaparihārāya - prabhuriti । ataṃ'; caturmukham aattuṃ'; bhakṣayituṃ avyādadāt'; vyāvṛtat viṣṇuḥ । tadā brahmā avirurāva'; bhāṇitiśabdamakarodityarthaḥ । heti asyārthasya śrutiprasiddhatāṃ sūcayati । atha ārāvakaraṇānantaraṃ atatkṛpayā'; tasmin caturmukhe kṛpayā viṣṇustamajagdhvā sṛṣṭikriyāyāmayojayat । asa vibhuḥ'; caturmukho haraye hareradyārthaṃ bhuvanamasṛjat । yadvā - bhuvanamasṛjat, sṛṣṭaṃ taddharaye arpitavāniti śeṣeṇa yojanā brahmavaivarta ityanantaraṃ yata uktamiti śeṣaḥ । asyāto apsaṃvatsarasṛṣṭyāderviṣṇuliṅgatvasiddhirityadhyāhṛtasādhyenānvayaḥ । ।। iti attṛtvādhikaraṇam ।।

।।

sarvāttaikaḥ para uktaḥ । ṛtaṃ pibantau sukṛtasya loke guhāṃ praviṣṭau parame parārdhe । chāyātapau brahmavido vadanti pañcāgnayo ye ca trināciketāḥ iti pibantau pratīyate tau kāviti ।।

atrādhikaraṇe lokato anyatra prasiddhakarmaphalabhoktṛtvaliṅgasya viṣṇau samanvayaḥ pratipādyate । pūrvādhikaraṇaśrutisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyodāharaṇapūrvakaṃ viṣayaṃ sūcayati - sarveti ।। yasmāt aparaḥ'; paramātmā aekaḥ'; ekatvasaṅkhyāyuktaḥ asarvāttā'; sarvasaṃhartā ca, tasmātprakṛtipratyayārthayostatra yogāt sarvāttetyādikriyāliṅgabodhakaśabdavācyatvenokta ityarthaḥ । sarvāttetyuktyaiva arthātpātetyapyukta iti bhāvaḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha - ṛtamiti । tatretyādau saṃyojyam । tathā ca atatra'; sarvāttṛtvamadhye praviṣṭaṃ tadviśeṣabhūtaṃ pātṛtvaṃ yatroktaṃ tatra kāṭhake aṛtaṃ pibantau'; ityatra apibantau'; karmaphalasārabhoktārau dvau pratīyete iti yojanā । dvivacanena dvitvabodhāditi bhāvaḥ । anena yuktamattṛtvaṃ bhagavatastatra prakṛtipratyayārthayorupapatteḥ । iha tu karmabandhavidhure paramātmani prakṛtyarthasya nirbhede pratyayārthasya cāyogānna tasya dvivacanāntapibacchandavācyateti pūrvavaiṣamyeṇa pratyavasthānādvā pūrvamarthāduktasya pātṛtvasyānyamātraniṣṭhatve asambhavasyānyasminnapi sattve ativyāptervā ākṣepādvā pūrvādhikaraṇenāsya saṅgatiḥ, pātṛtvākhyaviṣayaśca sūcito bhavati । viṣayavākye janyajanakabhāvaḥ ṣaṣṭhyarthaḥ tathā ca asukṛtasya loke'; sukṛtanirmite puṇyakārye tattvapradīparītyā sukṛtanimitte śarīre hṛdayaguhāṃ praviṣṭau guhāyāmapi aparame'; sarvajīvottame ā ṛddha ārdhaḥ parebhyo rudrādibhya ārdhaḥ parārdhaḥ । tasminnatipūrṇe vāyāviti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca tatra praviṣṭau hṛdayaguhāśritavāyvadhiṣṭhānāviti yāvat । asa hāyastaḥ piturardhameyāya'; iti tattvapradīpodāhṛtaśruteḥ parabrahmāvāsatvāttadanyajīvābhimanyamānatvātparārdhaṃ śarīramiti vā । ṛtaṃ satyaṃ tathā dharmaḥ sukṛtaṃ cābhidhīyate । ṛtaṃ tu mānaso dharmaḥ iti gītābhāṣyodāhṛtasmṛteḥ śāstravihitakarmabhirāgataṃ phalamupalakṣaṇayā ṛtamityucyate । tathā ca aṛtaṃ pibantau'; bhuñjānau yāvātmāntarātmākhyabhagavadrūpaviśeṣau vartete tau abrahmavido'; brahmajñāninaḥ apañcāgnayo'; devapitṛbhūtamanuṣyabrahmayajñākhyapañcamahāyajñavantaḥ । asa eṣa yajñaḥ pañcavidho agnihotraṃ darśapūrṇamāsau cāturmāsyāni paśuḥ somaḥ'; ityaitareyoktapañcamahāyajñā vā । dyuparjanyadharāpuṃstryākhyapañcāgnividyāniṣṭhā vā । naciketā nāma ṛṣiḥ naciketasa idaṃ nāciketamagnicayanaviśeṣaḥ । trināciketāstrivāramanuṣṭhitanāciketeṣṭakācayanavanto ye vartante viduṣāṃ pāpināṃ ca krameṇa achāyātapau'; sukhaduḥkhakāraṇabhūtau vadantītyarthaḥ । sukhaduḥkhahetutvarūpaṃ gauṇaṃ chāyātapatvaṃ ca pratiyogibhedādaviruddham । yathoktaṃ tattvapradīpe amarāṇāmāhlādakāvasurāṇāṃ tāpakāvityartha iti । praśnarūpakāryadvārā tanmūlasandehaprakāraṃ darśayati - atau'; śrutyuktapibantāviti । iti vākye pibantau yau pratīyete tau kāvityanvayaḥ । anena pibantau kiṃ jīvaparau uta pararūpe eveti saṃśayaḥ sūcito bhavati । itītyanantaraṃ iti saṃśaye jīvasahitar iśvaraḥ pāteti pūrvapakṣe ca satīti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

ucyate - sū - oṃ।।
guhāṃ praviṣṭāvātmānau hi taddarśanāt ।
।।

guhāṃ praviṣṭau pibantau viṣṇurūpe eva ।

atha siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe - ucyate iti ।। sūtrātparata itiśabdo adhyāhāryaḥ । guhāṃ praviṣṭāviti hetugarbhaṃ viśeṣaṇam । pibantāvityātmapadavyākhyānam । ṛtamityādāvadhyāhāryam । viṣṇurūpe ityātmānāvityasya vyākhyānāntaram । tathā ca - yāvātmānau ṛtaṃ pibantau tāvātmānau viṣṇurūpe eva । kutaḥ? yato guhāṃ praviṣṭāviti yojanā । evetyanenānuvṛttatuśabdārtha uktaḥ । viṣṇū iti vaktavye viṣṇurūpe evetyuktiḥ dvivacanasya rūpadvayavivakṣayā sāvakāśatoktyarthā ।

agharmā samantā trivṛtaṃ vyāpatustayorjuṣṭiṃ mātariśvā jagāma'; ityādinā taddarśanāt ।।

nanu viṣṇossarvaśarīreṣvekaikarūpeṇaiva praveśātkathaṃ rūpadvayābhiprāyeṇāpi dvivacanopapattirityataḥ taddarśanāditi sūtrāṃśasūcitaśrutimudāharati - gharmeti ।। bhagavantāviti, kartumiti ca śeṣaḥ । trivṛtamityāvartate । tathā ca agharmā'; gharmau dīptau gharṣakau saṅkocakāviti vā । agharṣaṇātsarvalokasya nṛsiṃho gharma ucyate'; ityaitareyabhāṣyokteḥ, ghṛṣṭatvena ca mitāviti tattvapradīpokteśca । asamantā'; samantau vyāptau prakṛtipuruṣakālavyāpinau । deśataḥ kālataḥ śaktitaśca sampūrṇau yau bhagavantau trivṛtaṃ tejobannātmakaṃ śarīraṃ avyāpatuḥ'; viśeṣeṇāpatuḥ dehahṛdayaguhāsthānaṃ prāptau । tayoḥ ajuṣṭiṃ'; sevāṃ kartuṃ amātariśvā'; mukhyavāyurapi trivṛtaṃ jagāma । adivo'; devyā vāyupatnyāḥ stanyaṃ apayoḥ'; adidhiṣāṇāḥ'; pipāsanto devāḥ dvirūpaṃ tamekam aaveṣan'; anvaicchan । tam aarkam'; aram alaṃ kaṃ sukharūpaṃ asahasāmānaṃ'; sahavāyuṃ viduriti śrutyarthaḥ । gurvarthadīpikāyāṃ tu samantāditi padacchedaṃ kṛtvā vidyamānāviti cādhyāhṛtya samantādvidyamānau vyāptāviti vyākhyātam। taccintyam। ādipadena adivaspayaḥ'; ityuttarārdhaṃ, tathā - 
ekaḥ suparṇaḥ sa samudramāviveśa sa idaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ vicaṣṭe ।
taṃ pākena manasāpaśyamantitastaṃ mātā relhi sa u relhi mātaram ।।

suparṇaṃ viprāḥ kavayo vacobhirekaṃ santaṃ bahudhā kalpayanti । 
ityādikaṃ ca gṛhyate । aekaḥ suparṇaḥ'; suṣṭhu paramānandarūpo bhagavān samudramāviveśa । sa idaṃ sarvaṃ jagat avicaṣṭe'; paśyati । ataṃ'; paramātmānaṃ pakvena manasā ahamapaśyam । ataṃ mātā'; vyañjakatvādvāk sarasvatī arelhi'; lihyata iva । sa paramātmā mātaraṃ relhi । tāvanyonyaṃ sambaddhau bhavataḥ । tathā ca - bhagavadvyañjakavāco api taddhyaṅgyatvamiti bhāvaḥ । tameva suparṇamekaṃ santaṃ aviprāḥ'; viśeṣeṇa prakṛṣṭāḥ kavayo avacobhiḥ'; śabdaiḥ abahudhā'; keśavādidvādaśadhā sthitaṃ kalpayanti cintayanti ityarthaḥ । tasya viṣṇoḥ dvirūpatayā sarvaśarīrapraveśasya uktatvādityarthaḥ । tathā ca - ekasminnapi viṣṇau yuktaṃ rūpadvayābhiprāyeṇa dvivacanamiti bhāvaḥ । evaṃ taddarśanāt ityetat tattvapradīparītyā uktaviśeṣaṇe nirṇīte viṣṇau dvivacanadarśanāt aekaḥ suparṇaḥ'; ityādinā tacchabdenaikavacanena parāmarśadarśanāt tasyaiva samudraniveśino nikhilabhuvanadarśinaḥ aapaśyamantitaḥ'; iti guhāpraviṣṭatvadarśanādekasyaiva bahunāmarūpadarśanāt ityapi vyākhyeyam ।।

ātmāntarātmeti harireka eva dvidhā sthitaḥ ।
niviṣṭo hṛdaye nityaṃ rasaṃ pibati karmajam ।।

iti ca bṛhatsaṃhitāyām ।

nanu viṣṇau rūpadvayavivakṣayā pratyayārthopapattāvapi prātipadikārthakarmaphalabhoktṛtvāyogāt na aṛtam'; iti vākyapratipādyatvaṃ tasyetyata āha - ātmeti ।। eka eva hariḥ dehajīvarūpopādhibhedāt ātmāntarātmeti rūpabhedena advidhā sthito'; dvidhā bhūtaḥ । dehajīvayorhṛdaye niviṣṭaḥ । yaddhā - ṭīkārītyā upādhibhedavivakṣāmantareṇaiva dvirūpatayā dehaniviṣṭaḥ akarmajaṃ rasaṃ'; phalaṃ anityaṃ'; niyamena apibati'; bhuṅkte ityarthaḥ । smṛta iti pāṭhe kīrtitaḥ ityarthaḥ । rasaśabdena jīvābhogyaguṇabhoktaiveśvaraḥ, na tu tadbhogyadravyabhokteti prameyaṃ sūcitam । bṛhatsaṃhitāyāmityasya taddarśanādityanuvṛttavākyenānvayaḥ । karmaphalabhogasyoktatvāditi tadarthaḥ । tathā ca - na tadanupapattiriti bhāvaḥ । na kevalaṃ bṛhatsaṃhitāyām । kintu - 
śrotraṃ cakṣuḥ sparśanaṃ ca rasanaṃ ghrāṇameva ca ।
adhiṣṭhāya manaścāyaṃ viṣayānupasevate ।। 
iti gītāsvapīti cārthaḥ ।

śubhaṃ pibatyasau nityaṃ nāśubhaṃ sa hariḥ pibet ।
pūrṇānandamayasyāsya ceṣṭā na jñāyate kvacit ।।

nanu kimīśvaro duḥkhaṃ pāpakarmaphalaṃ bhuṅkte? puṇyajaṃ sukhaṃ vā? nādyadvitīyau, pūrṇānandatvādityata āha - śubhamiti ।। aasau'; sarvaśarīragataprāṇe sthito ahariḥ'; yajñe havissvīkartā pāpahartā bhagavān anityaṃ'; niyamena śubhakarmaphalameva apibati'; bhuṅkte । hariḥ aśubhakarmaphalaṃ ana pibet'; na bhuṅkte ityarthaḥ । apuṇyamevāmuṃ gacchati parame parārdhe'; iti śruteḥ । pibatīti ṛtapānakartari advitīyatvamabhyupaiti । anenārthena dvitīyapakṣamaṅgīkṛtya ādyapakṣo anabhyupagamena parihṛtaḥ । pūrṇānandasya sukhabhogāyoga iti dvitīyaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ pariharati - pūrṇānandamayasyeti । tādātmyārthe mayaṭ । atādātmyārthe vikārārthe prācuryārthe mayaṭ tridhā'; iti gītābhāṣyokteḥ । tathā ca - pūrṇānandarūpasyāsya viṣṇoḥ aceṣṭā'; aiśvaryaṃ kvacitkāle deśe kenāpi sākalyena ana jñāyate'; na cintyate ityarthaḥ । tathā ca - aiśvaryabalena pūrṇānandasyāpi sukhabhogo yukta iti bhāvaḥ । yadvā - viṣṇorbhoktṛtvābhyupagame aanaśnannanyaḥ'; iti śrutivirodha ityata āha - śubhamiti ।। parādhīnabhogābhāvaviṣayam aśubhabhogābhāvaviṣayaṃ vā tadvākyamiti bhāvaḥ । na ca anīcoccataiva duḥkhāderbhoga ityabhidhīyate । nāsau nīcoccatāṃ yāti'; iti vākyavirodhaḥ, sukhabhogasyoccatārūpatvāditi vācyam । viṣṇau jīvasamavete bhoge svīkārāmātrābhyupagamena uccatāsampādakavikriyāviśeṣānabhyupagamāt । uktaṃ hi tattvapradīpe - na ca aanaśnannanyaḥ'; iti śrutivirodhaḥ । na hi parādhīnatayā bhogo, nāpyapriyabhogo na ca tannimittoccanīcatā viṣṇoḥ, kintu - jīvasamavete bhoge svīkāramātramucyata iti । yadvā - nīcoccatāsampādako bhogaḥ svīyatayā sākṣātkāraḥ, sa cābhimānayuto vivakṣitaḥ, na cāsāvīśvare iti na virodhaḥ । pādma ityanantaraṃ uktatvāditi śeṣaḥ । tathā ca - na śrutiyuktivirodha iti bhāvaḥ ।

yo veda nihitaṃ guhāyām ityādinā prasiddhaṃ hiśabdena darśayati ।।

nanu kathaṃ guhāniviṣṭatvaliṅgātpibato viṣṇutvaniścayaḥ, tasya jīve api yogādityata āha - yo vedeti । viṣṇoreva guhānihitatvamatra grāhyamiti copaskartavyam । ādiśabdena aātmāntarātmā'; iti aśrotraṃ cakṣuḥ'; iti aahaṃ vaiśvānaro bhūtvā'; ityādismṛtirgṛhyate । tathā ca ityādinā viṣṇoreva prasiddhaṃ guhānihitatvamatra grāhyamiti imamarthaṃ sūtrakāro hiśabdena darśayatītyarthaḥ । tathā ca - hṛdayaguhāsthatvamātrasya jīve sambhave api na tadiha hetutvena gṛhyate । kintu - śrutyādiprasiddhaṃ mokṣajanakajñānaprakārībhūtaṃ prādhānyena guhānihitatvameva । tacca jīve niravakāśamiti bhāvaḥ। sūtre samanvayasūtrāttuśabdamātramanuvartate । ātmānāvityāvartate । tathā ca aātmānau'; ādeyaṃ sukhaṃ mātyanubhavatīti vyutpattyā ātmaśabdoktaśubhakarmaphalabhoktārau aātmānāveva'; ātmāntarātmākhye viṣṇurūpe eva, na tu jīveśvarau । kutaḥ? hi yasmāttau hṛdayaguhāṃ praviṣṭau tasmāt । na hi jīve api guhāniviṣṭatvaliṅgaṃ sambhavatīti vācyam । tasya śrutyādyaprasiddhatvāt । tatra prasiddhasyaiva grāhyatvāt । viṣṇostu ayo veda'; iti śrutyādyaprasiddhatvāditi hiśabdārthaḥ । nanu viṣṇau pibantāviti dvivacanānapapattiḥ । na ca rūpapraveśena dvirūpeṇa praveśasyāsiddhatvādityāśaṅkyāha - taddarśanāditi । tasya harerdvirūpatayā śarīrahṛdayaguhāsthatvasya liṅgasya darśanāt agharmā'; iti śrutyuktatvāditi sūtrārthaḥ । atra tattvityasyānuvṛtyā śrautapadānuvṛttyā ca ānandamayastadbrahmetyādivadihāpi pratijñāsiddheḥ ātmānāvityuktiḥ । śrautadvivacanasya gatimāha - ātmeti ।। smṛtisamākhyāṃ śrautapadānuvṛttiṃ vinā ādeyaṃ mātīti vyutpattyā śubhakarmaphalabhoktṛtvarūpaliṅgaṃ ca vaktum । uktaṃ hi candrikāyām - ādeyaṃ mātīti vyutpattyā ātmaśabdoktaṃ śubhabhoktṛtvaṃ mūlayuktiriti । na caivamṛtapātṛtvasamānādhikaraṇaguhāpraviṣṭatvoktidvārā taduktiriti tadvākyāntaravirodhaḥ śaṅkyaḥ । tasya sūtre avaśyavaktavyaguhāpraviṣṭatvaliṅgāpakadvivacanāntarapadānvayayogyatādṛśaviśeṣyoktimukhenetyarthābhyupagamāt । tathā - yadyapi samanvetavyamṛtapātṛtvaṃ sākṣādeva vaktavyamiti tadvākyāntarasyāpyādeyaṃ mātīti vyutpattimantareṇāntaryāmītivat ṛtaṃ pibantāviti spaṣṭaśabdenaiva vaktavyam । na tvātmaśabdenetyarthāśrayaṇānna virodhaḥ । anyathā uktavākyavirodhāpātāt । evaṃ cātra keṣāñcidanyathā candrikābhiprāyakathanam, tathā teṣāmeva samanvayasūtrāttadityatrāpyanuvartate iti candrikāvirodhoktirapi cintyā । sautradvivacanopapattyartham uddeśyasamarpaṇārthaṃ cāvaśyavaktavyātmānāviti padenaiva vidheyasyāpi bodhanasambhavenetaravyāvartakāvadhāraṇārthakatuśabdamātrasyaivar ikṣatisūtra ivātrānuvṛttyaucityāt । na ca tadityanuktau tuśabdasyānvayaḥ pratyetuṃ śakyate iti samanvayādhikaraṇīyasudhāvirodhaḥ । uddeśyavidheyapadāntarābhāva ityāśayāt ।

sū - oṃ।। viśeṣaṇācca । 
।।
ayaḥ seturījānānāmakṣaraṃ brahma yatparam'; iti ।।

evaṃ yadā niravakāśaguhānihitatvaliṅgasya sāvakāśāddvivacanaśrutito api prābalyādviṣṇoḥ prakṛtyarthabhoktṛtvasambhavācca sa eva pāteti siddhyati । kimu punarniravakāśaśrutyāpītyarthaṃ pratipādayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā tadabhipretaśrutimevodāharati - viśeṣaṇācceti ।। iti viśeṣaṇādityanvayaḥ । sūtre pibatoriti vipariṇāmenānuvartate । tathā ca ayaḥ setuḥ'; iti śrutau pibatorekavacanabodhyenaikatvena viśeṣaṇādeka eva pātā । sa ca yajamānasetutvabrahmatvākṣaratvādinā viśeṣaṇāt brahmaṇaśca paratvena viśeṣaṇādviṣṇureva, na jīva iti sūtrārthaḥ । na kevalaṃ liṅgāt, kintu - setvādiśrutito apīti cārthaḥ । ayaḥ'; ātmāntarātmākhyadvirūpo bhagavārn aijānānāṃ'; viṣṇumuddiśya yāgaṃ kurvāṇānāṃ asetuḥ'; āśrayaḥ yadakṣaraṃ paraṃ brahma, taṃ dhyātuṃ naciketasaṃ prati sādhanaṃ vaktuṃ aśakemahi'; śaktāssma iti kāṭhakaśrutyarthaḥ ।

pṛthagvaktuṃ guṇāstasya na śakyante amitatvataḥ ।
yato ato brahmaśabdena sarveṣāṃ grahaṇaṃ bhavet ।।

etasmādbrahmaśabdo ayaṃ viṣṇoreva viśeṣaṇam । amitā hi guṇā yasmānnānyeṣāṃ tamṛte prabhum । iti brāhme ।

brahmaśabdasya bhagavadekavācitvaṃ smārayati - pṛthagiti ।। atra yata ityāvartate । tathā ca yataḥ atasya'; viṣṇorguṇāḥ aamitatvataḥ'; asaṅkhyātatvato nimittāt apṛthak'; vivicya vaktuṃ na śakyante । jñātavyāśca sarvairadhikāribhiḥ sarve guṇā iti śeṣaḥ । yato brahmaśabdena sarveṣāṃ guṇānāṃ agrahaṇaṃ'; jñānaṃ bhavet ataḥ sarvaguṇajñānārthaṃ tasmin viṣṇau brahmaśabdaḥ prayujyate iti śeṣaḥ । yato brahmaśabdena sarveṣāṃ guṇānāṃ grahaṇaṃ bhavet । evaṃ ca sarvaguṇavācī brahmaśabdo bhavati, tatra vṛttimantareṇa tajjñānajanakatvāyogāditi bhāvaḥ । yasmādvibhuṃ taṃ viṣṇumṛte anyeṣāṃ jīvānāṃ nāmitā guṇāḥ, kintu - viṣṇoreva pramāṇasiddham, etasmātkāraṇādayaṃ brahmaśabdo viṣṇoreva aviśeṣaṇaṃ'; mukhyavācako nānyeṣāmityarthaḥ । brāhma ityanantaraṃ brahmaśabdasya bhagavadekavācitvamuktamiti śeṣaḥ ।

na ca jīve samanvayo abhidhīyate ।

atra paraiḥ pibantau buddhijīvāviti pūrvapakṣe prāpte jīveśvarāveveti vyākhyātaṃ, tannirākaroti - na ceti।। atreti śeṣaḥ । asminnadhyāye iti tadarthaḥ । hetau, svavyānena saha paravyākhyānanirākaraṇasya samuccaye vā caśabdaḥ tathā cāsaṅgatiriti bhāvaḥ ।

satya ātmā satyo jīvaḥ satyaṃ bhidā satyaṃ bhidā satyaṃ bhidā maivāruvaṇyo maivāruvaṇyo maivāruvaṇyaḥ ।। iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ ।

nanu nātra jīve samanvayakathanamasaṅgatam । jīveśvarabhedasyāsatyatvena tayoraikyāt । jīvasamanvayasyaiva brahmasamanvayarūpatvādityata āha - satya iti । asatyaṃ'; satyā abhidā'; bhedaḥ । yadyapyatrātmajīvayoḥ satyatvavacanenaiva tatsvarūpabhedasyāpi satyatvamuktaṃ bhavati । tathāpi punaḥ asatyaṃ bhidā'; ityuktirdarśanapratītābhedapratītinirāsatātparyārthā śapathāvṛttiḥ । kecidbhedamasatyamāhuḥ tatkathametadityatasteṣāṃ pakṣe śrutirabhīkṣṇaṃ dūṣaṇamabhidhatte - maiveti । aāruvaṇyaḥ'; arā doṣāstadvantaḥ, āsamantādaraśīlā vā āravaḥ tairasatyabhedajñānibhiḥ viṣṇuḥ sarvathā vanyo bhajanīyo netyarthaḥ । iti paiṅgiśrutirityanantaraṃ yata iti śeṣaḥ । asya nāsatyo bheda ityuttareṇānvayaḥ evaṃ bhāllaveyaśrutirityasyāpi । atra yadyapi bhāgavatatātparye - asatyatvaṃ ca bhedasyoktaṃ bhāllaveyaśrutau । sthāṇurheccakrāma sa prajāpatimuvāca ko asi ke smaḥ kaḥ saḥ iti । sahovāca yo asmi ye stha yaḥ sa iti । athainamupākrośat satyaṃ bhidā satyaṃ bhidā satyaṃ bhidā'; ityādinā asatyam'; iti vākyaṃ bhāllaveyaśrutyantargatatayā paṭhyate । bhāṣyapustake api kvacit asatyam'; iti vākyam aātmā hi'; iti vākyaṃ ca bhāllaveyaśrutitvenaiva paṭhyate । na tu śrutidvayasthatvena । tathāpi anayostātparyānusāreṇaikaśrutisthatvaṃ, bahutarapāṭhabalāt asatya ātmā'; iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ । aātmā hi'; iti bhāllaveyaśrutiḥ । tātparyodāhṛtā tu anyā tatsamākhyā rūpā cetyadoṣaḥ । asthāṇuḥ'; rudraḥ auccakrāma'; ūrdhvaṃ jagāma। asaḥ'; rudraḥ aprajāpatiṃ'; brahmāṇam upākrośaduvāca । kimiti? tvaṃ akaḥ'; kīdṛśaḥ । vayaṃ ake'; kīdṛśāḥ । saḥ viṣṇuḥ akaḥ'; kīdṛśaḥ । kiṃ bhinna utābhinna ityāśayaḥ । krameṇottaramāha - ahaṃ ayo'; yādṛśo agre sarvadā tādṛśo asmi । yūyaṃ aye'; yādṛśāḥ tādṛśāḥ stha । asaḥ'; viṣṇuryādṛśo mayā bhavadādibhiśca bhinnastādṛśa eveti śrutyarthaḥ ।

aātmā hi paramassvatantro adhiguṇo jīvo alpaśaktirasvatantro avaraḥ'; iti ca bhāllaveyaśrutiḥ । yatheśvarasya jīvasya bhedassatyo viniścayāt । evameva hi me vācaṃ satyāṃ kartumihārhasi ।।

yatheśvaraśca jīvaśca satyabhedau parasparam ।
tena satyena māṃ devāstrāyantu sahakeśavāḥ ।।
ityādernāsatyo bhedaḥ ।।
।। iti guhādhikaraṇam ।।

atroktabhedasādhakapramāṇatvena viruddhaguṇopanyāsāya aātmā'; iti dvitīyavākyaṃ pravṛttam । aātmā'; paramātmā aparamaḥ'; svatantraḥ । aadhiguṇaḥ'; pūrṇaśaktiḥ । ata evottaratra paramatvasvatantratvapūrṇaśaktitvaviruddhānāṃ dharmāṇām alpaśaktirityādipadairyutkrameṇābhidhānaṃ kṛtam ।

atraivārthe purāṇavākye paṭhati - yatheti ।। atra ṣaṣṭhyantaṃ vākyaṃ pādmasthaṃ, prathamāntaṃ skāndagatamiti tattvapradīpokteḥ । ame mām'; ityābhyāṃ tatprakṛto grāhyaḥ । aviniścayāt'; evārtho ayaṃ śabdaḥ । satyabhedāviti bahuvrīhiḥ । yathā satyabhedau tathaiva vidyamānānatikrameṇa jñātena asatyena'; satyabhedena bhedasatyatvajñānākhyakāraṇeneti yāvat । sahakeśavā ityekaṃ padaṃ, keśavasahitā devāḥ atrāyantu'; asmān rakṣantvityarthaḥ । ityādervākyānnāsatyo bhedaḥ, kintu - satya eveti jñāyata ityarthaḥ । atra pūrvavākye jīveśabhedasya dṛṣṭāntatvenopādānātprāmāṇikatvaṃ jñāyate, tādṛśasyaiva dṛṣṭāntatvāt । dvitīye tu viṣayānatikrameṇa bhedasatyatvajñānasya trāṇakāraṇatvoktyā bheda satyatvamapi jñāyata iti prakṛtasaṅgatiḥ । ādipadena grāhyavacanāni tattvapradīpe udāhṛtāni । tathāhi - dvau bhūtasargau loke asmin daiva āsura eva ca । daivo vistaraśaḥ proktaḥ āsuraṃ pārtha me śṛṇu ।।

asatyamapratiṣṭhaṃ te jagadāhuranīśvaram । ityārabhya - 
tānahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu narādhamān ।
kṣipāmyajasramaśubhānāsurīṣveva yoniṣu ।।

iti bhagavadvacanam asatyamapratiṣṭhaṃ te jagadāhuranīśvaram । ta āsurāḥ svayaṃ naṣṭāḥ jagataḥ kṣayakāriṇaḥ ।। 
indrāsomā tapataṃ rakṣa ujjataṃ nyarpayataṃ vṛṣaṇā tamovṛdhaḥ ।
parāśṛṇītamacito nyoṣataṃ hataṃ nudethāṃ niśiśītamatriṇaḥ ।। 
indrā somā vartayataṃ divasparyagnitaptebhiryuvamaśmahanmabhiḥ । tapurvadhebhirajarebhiratriṇaḥ; ityādikā śrutiḥ । yeṣāṃ bhijjagadīśvarajīvānāṃ nāsti te atriṇaḥ । svājñānakalpitajagatparameśvarasya jīvasya bhedakaluṣīkṛtabhūmabhāve । iti hi māyino vadanti । ācchādya vikṣipati saṃsphuradātmattvam । jīveśvarasya jagadākṛti tanmṛṣaiva । triryātudhānaḥ prasitiṃ tayetvṛtaṃ yo agne anṛtena hanti । vācā stenaṃ śarava ṛcchantu marman viśvasyaitu prasitiṃ yātudhānaḥ । atha jñānopasargāḥ ityārabhya yecānye mithyātarkairdṛṣṭāntaiḥ kuhakendrajālairvaidikeṣu paristhātumicchanti taiḥ saha na saṃvaset । prakāśyāhyete taskarā asvargyāḥ ityādiśrutiśatairandhaṃ tama eva māyināṃ gatiriti niścīyate । tathā ca skānde - 
sarvabrahmatvavettāro jīvabrahmatvavedinaḥ ।
anyasāmyavido viṣṇoḥ viṣṇudveṣṭāra eva ca ।
sarve yānti tamo ghoraṃ na teṣāṃ utthitiḥ kvacit ।।

।। iti guhādhikaraṇam ।।

।। antarādhikaraṇam ।।

āditye viṣṇurityuktam । aya eṣa āditye puruṣaḥ so ahamasmi sa evāhamasmi'; ityādāvagnīnāmevādityādisthatvamucyate ।

atrādhikaraṇe cakṣurantaḥsthatvaliṅgaṃ brahmaṇi samanvīyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyaṃ viṣayasaṃśayau sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ ca darśayati - āditya iti ।। ayaścāsāvāditye'; ityānandamayādhikaraṇodāhṛtāyāṃ tathā aantarāditye'; ityantarnayodāhṛtāyāṃ ca śrutāvānandamayo antasstho viṣṇurāditye astītyuktamityarthaḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha - ya iti । tadityādau saṃyojyam । aso ahaṃ sa evāham'; ityabhyāsopanyāsaḥ pūrvapakṣayuktipradarśanārthaḥ । prathamādipadena athainamanvāhāryapacano anuśaśāsa । ya eṣa candramasi puruṣo dṛśyate । so ahamasmi sa evāhamasmi । athainamāhavanīyo anuśaśāsa । ya eṣa vidyuti puruṣo dṛśyate so ahamasmi sa evāhamasmīti ca vākyadvaṃ gṛhyate । dvitīyādipadena candravidyutsthatvam । yadyapi ādityasthatvasyeva candravidyutsthatvayoragnerakṣisthatvasādhakatvābhāvāttadupādānaṃ na prakṛtopayuktam । tathā agnīnāmiti bahuvacanaṃ cānupayuktam, pūrvapakṣe gārhapatyasyaiva akṣisthatvasādhanena gārhapatyādīnāṃ trayāṇāṃ tasyāsādhanāt । candravidyutorakṣyekavidhatvābhāvena tatsthatvasyākṣisthatvāsādhakatvācca । tathāpi ādiśabdadvayaṃ bahuvacanaṃ ca pūrvapakṣe gārhapatyādibahvagniśrutirūpayuktisūcanārtham । yathā anvāhāryapacanākhyadakṣiṇāgnyāhavanīyayoḥ candravidyutsthatvamucyate, evaṃ gārhaptayasyāpi ādityasthatvamucyate iti dṛṣṭāntārthaṃ gārhapatyādīnāṃ trayāṇāṃ krameṇādityāditritayasthatve prasiddhagārhapatyasyaivādityasthatvamukhenākṣisthatvamāgacchatīti yuktipradarśanārthaṃ vā tadupādānamiti na vaiyarthyamiti dhyeyam।

ato akṣyādityayoraikyāt aya eṣo antarakṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate'; ityatrāpyagnirevocyate ।

tato api kimityata āha - ata iti ।। asya na sannihitena aaikyāt'; ityanenānvayaḥ । prakṛtasya ata ityanena parāmṛṣṭāsyādityāntaḥ sthatvasya aikye hetutvāyogāt । kintu vyavahitena aatrāpyagnirevocyate'; ityanenānvayaḥ । na kevalamādityavākya ityaperarthaḥ । tathā ca - yadānandamayākhyaviṣṇuniṣṭhatayoktamādityasthatvaṃ tacchāndogye aya eṣa āditye puruṣaḥ so ahamasmi'; ityādāvāgnīnāṃ gārhaptayākhyāgnereva aucyate'; pratīyate na viṣṇoḥ। kutaḥ? yato atra aagnīnāṃ'; gārhapatyadakṣiṇāgnyāhavanīyānāṃ trayāṇāṃ krameṇa ādityādisthatvamucyate, ataḥ । tataḥ kim? yato atra gārhapatyākhyāgnerevādityasthatvamucyate ato aya eṣo antarakṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate'; iti vākye apyakṣisthatvena gārhapatyāgnirevocyate, na sa viṣṇuḥ । śrutigatāhaṃśabdenāpi sa evocyate iti yojanā । tathā ca pūrvapakṣaśrutigatāhaṃśabdo agnāveva mukhya iti tasyaiva grahaṇamiti bhāvaḥ । nanvagnerādityasthatve api kuto akṣisthatvaprāptirityata āha - akṣyādityayoriti । aādityaścakṣurbhūtvākṣiṇī prāviśat'; ityaitareyaśruteracetanākṣyādityamaṇḍalayorādityacakṣuḥpadoditaikacetanādhiṣṭhitatvarūpaikadharmeṇaikavidhatvādityarthaḥ । yadvā - aaśanayodāhṛtādityastrivṛdiva vai cakṣuḥ śuklaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kanīnikā'; iti śrutyanusāreṇa tayostrivṛttvadharmeṇaikavidhatvādityarthaḥ । tathā ca - ādityasthatvoktyā arthādakṣisthatvamapi prāptameveti bhāvaḥ । yadyapi asayaścāyam'; iti pūrvodāhṛtataittirīyaśrutisthādityaśabdaḥ utkṛṣṭacetanamātropalakṣakatayā vyākhyātaḥ । tathāpi atrādhikaraṇe sūryābhimanyamānādityamaṇḍalaparatvamapyasyāṅgīkṛtya ākṣepaparihārau kṛtau । ata eva ṭīkāyāmakṣyādityayarekavidhatvādyuktam । tattvapradīpe tu - akṣīndriyaprerakādityayorekatvāditi yathāśrutameva vyākhyātam । candrikāyāmapi tattvapradīpānusāreṇa devatāparamevākṣipadam । ata eva bhāṣye sannyāyaratnāvalyāṃ ca akṣyādityayoraikyādityevoktam, na tvekavidhatvāditi । akṣyādityayorekavidhatvāditi ṭīkāpi bhāṣyānusāreṇa prakārabhedaniṣedhamukhena prakāryaikyaparā neyeti pakṣāntaramapyuktam । tathā ca - devatāparatve aāditye viṣṇurityuktam'; iti bhāṣyaśrutisthākṣyādityapadayośca yathāśruta evārthaḥ । maṇḍalaparatve tadbhāṣyasthādityapadaṃ pūrvodāhṛtataittirīyaśrutisthādityapadaṃ ca maṇḍalaparatayā vyākhyeyamiti vivekaḥ । anena chandogaśrutyuktākṣisthatvasyānyaniṣṭhatvākṣepamukhenānandamayanayodāhṛtāyāṃ taittirīyaśrutāvarthāduktasyāpi tasyānyaniṣṭhatvākṣepādānandamayādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । akṣisthatvaṃ viṣayaḥ । kimagnerviṣṇorveti sandehaḥ । agnīnāmeva akṣisthatvamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । atra ādityasthatvarūpayuktiścoktā bhavati । atra aya eṣa āditye puruṣaḥ'; aya eṣo antarakṣiṇi puruṣaḥ'; ityanayorvākyayoḥ aādityaścakṣurbhūtvā'; iti vākyadvārā ekārthatvamupapādya tanmukhena aya eṣa āditye'; iti vākyena ayaścāsāvāditye'; iti vākyasya saṅgatiṃ sampādya taddvārārthākṣiptatadarthārthakasya aya eṣo antarakṣiṇi'; iti vākyasyāpi tena saṅgatirityevaṃ vakrasaṅgatyaitadadhikaraṇārambhaḥ ādityasthatvaliṅgasyāpi samanvayasiddhyartham । anyathā anetaro anupapatteḥ'; ityādau viṣṇujñānānmokṣa ityuktam, sa mokṣaḥ atadyathā'; iti vākyena aya eṣo antarakṣiṇi'; ityuktākṣisthajñānātpratīyata iti vakṣyamāṇaṛjusaṅgatyaiva adhikaraṇamārambhaṇīyaṃ syāditi dhyeyam ।

ataḥ atadyathā puṣkarapalāśa āpo na śliṣyanta evamevaṃvidi pāpaṃ karma na śliṣyate'; ityagnijñānādeva sarvapāpāśleṣānmokṣopapattiriti ।

na kevalamakṣisthatvasiddhāvagnerānandamayatvaprāptiḥ । kintu yatpūrvaṃ anetaraḥ'; ityādau viṣṇujñānānmokṣa ityuktaṃ, tadapi bādhitaṃ syādityata āha - ata iti ।। aagnijñānādityetat'; asarvapāpāśleṣāt'; ityaneneva amokṣaḥ'; ityanenāpi sambadhyate । tathā ca yato agnirakṣistho atastajjñānādeva mokṣo api bhavet na viṣṇujñānāt । kuta etat? akṣisthāgnijñānātsarvapāpāśleṣāt । na ca tasyāsiddhiḥ । atadyathā'; iti tadarthavāde agnijñānādeva sarvapāpāśleṣokteḥ । na ca tajjñānātsarvapāpāśleṣamātreṇa kathaṃ mokṣa iti vācyam । yatastajjñānānmokṣaṃ vinā sarvapāpāśleṣāsambhavena tadanyathānupapattyaiva mokṣasyāpyupapattiriti yojanā । evaṃ ca pūrvapakṣe agnerakṣisthatvena atadyathā'; ityakṣisthasyoktaṃ muktihetujñānaviṣayatvamapi tasyaiva prāpnotīti anetaraḥ'; ityuktamayuktamiti bhāvaḥ । anena ṛjusaṅgatirapyasya darśitā bhavati । chāndogyehītthamākhyāyikā - kamalāyanasyāpatyaṃ kāmalāyanaḥ nāmataḥ upakosalaḥ satyakāmākhye gurau brahmacaryamuddiśyovāsa । sa ācāryasyāgnīn gārhapatyādīn dvādaśavarṣaparyantaṃ paryacārīt । satyakāmastvantevāsinaḥ svādhyāyaṃ grāhayan enamekameva nādhyāpayat । punaḥ punaḥ svajāyayokto api anuktvaiva vidyāṃ pravāsāya prātiṣṭhata । tadopakosalo vyādhipīḍito vidyāprāpticintayā svācāryabhāryayā aśānetyukto api nāśnāt । evaṃ brahmacāriṇyanaśnati tūṣṇīṃbhūte sati tadā gārhapatyādyagnayaḥ kāruṇyāviṣṭāḥ trayo api vayamasmai brahmacāriṇo vidyāṃ prabravāmeti pratijñāya militāssanto vidyāmūcuḥ । aprāṇo brahma kaṃ brahma khaṃ brahma'; ityādi । evaṃ sambhūyopadeśānantaramenaṃ pratyekam agnaya upadidiśuḥ ityucyate vedapuruṣeṇa aatha hainaṃ gārhapatyo anuśaśāsa ya eṣa āditye puruṣo dṛśyate so ahamasmi sa evāhamasmi'; ityādinā । evaṃ tribhiragnibhiḥ pratyekamupadiṣṭa upakosalaḥ athāsmābhiruktaṃ jñeyameva, nopāsyam, tattu tavadācārya āgatya vakṣyatīti tairukto abhūt । evaṃ sthite athācāryaḥ satyakāma ājagāma । āgatya copakosaloktaṃ śrutvā pratyuvāca । kimiti? yadagnibhistubhyamupadiṣṭaṃ tattvayā jñeyameva na tūpāsyaṃ, tattvamahamupadekṣye ityevaṃ pratijñāyādarajananāya vakṣyamāṇamastaut ayathā puṣkarapalāśa āpo na śliṣyanta evamevaṃvidi pāpaṃkarma na śliṣyata'; iti । evaṃ stutvopakosalāya vidyāmupādiśatsatyakāmaḥ । kimiti? aya eṣo antarakṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate eṣa ātmeti hovāca । etadamṛtametadabhayametadbrahmeti'; । atha sambhūyopadeśānantaraṃ enamupakosalaṃ gārhapatyo anuśaśāsa । kimiti? pṛthivyagnyannākhyaṃ brahmeti । evaṃ vyāptavidyāmuktvāntaryāmividyāmāha - ya iti । asya so ahamasmītyasya dvikartukatvādgārhapatyādyantaryāmī bhagavān svasyādityādyantaryāmiṇā gārhapatyādiḥ svāntaryāmiṇaḥ ādityādyantaryāmiṇā aikyamāhetyucyate । tathā ca - aheyatvāt pratyaktvāccāhaṃ madantaryāmī । āditye ca eṣa puruṣaḥ pūrṇaṣaḍguṇo bhagavān dṛśyate divyadṛṣṭyā so asmītyarthaḥ । ādityasthasya viṣṇormadantaryāmiṇaśca viduradharmādivadabhedamātraṃ na; kintu viśeṣābhāvaścetyāha - sa eveti । evamupāsakasya phalamāha - asa etadevaṃ vidvānupāste apahate pāpakṛtyāṃ lokī bhavati sarvamāyureti jyogjīvatīti'; । apāpakṛtyāṃ'; pāpakāryaṃ alokī'; bhagavallokī bhavati । asarvaṃ'; sampūrṇaṃ cāyuḥ prāpnoti । ajyok'; sarvajñassan jīvatīti । evaṃ aya eṣa candramasi'; aya eṣa vidyuti'; ityanayoḥ artho avagantavyaḥ । atat'; tatrārthe vakṣyamāṇadṛṣṭānto yathā apuṣkarapalāśe'; padmapatre āpo yathā ana śliṣyante'; na sajjante atathevaṃvidi'; vakṣyamāṇākṣisthatvena brahmāparokṣajñānini jñānottaraṃ pāpaṃ karma na śliṣyate ityarthaḥ । ya eṣo akṣiṇyantaḥpuruṣo dṛśyate divyadṛṣṭyā eṣa ātmā vāmanākhya iti hovāca upakosalaṃ prati satyakāmaḥ । aetadamṛtaṃ'; svato mṛtiśūnyaṃ nityamuktaṃ, aetadabhayaṃ'; svato bhūyaśūnyaṃ aetadbrahma'; guṇapūrṇamiti sidbhāntarītyā śrutyarthaḥ । pūrvapakṣī tvetatprakaraṇamagniparaṃ manyate ।

ato bravīti - sū - oṃ।।
antara upapatteḥ ।
।।

cakṣurantasstho viṣṇureva ।

siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe - ata iti ।। iti saṅgatisambhavāt śaṅkāsadbhāvācca । ataḥ tatparihārāya uttaramabravīt sūtrakāra ityarthaḥ । cakṣurantaḥstha ityanena antara ityaṃśo viṣṇurevetyanena anuvṛttastattvityaṃśaśca vyākhyātaḥ । yadyapi anuvyākhyāne śabdavaiyarthyaparihārāya antassthitvā ramaṇakṛditi vyākhyānāt atrāpi tadanusāreṇa ramaṇakṛcceti vaktavyam । tathāpyatra ramaṇakriyābodhakātmaśabdasya hetukaraṇānna tadarthasya pratijñāyāmanvayaḥ sambhavatīti antastha ityevoktam । tatratvātmaśabdārthasya hetutvāvivakṣāṇātsādhyānvayo na yujyata iti ramaṇakṛdityapyuktam । vastutastu - sūtre antarityanuktyā antara ityadhikokteḥ sārthakyāya atrāpi ramaṇakṛccetyapi upalakṣaṇayā vācyam । avayavārthavivakṣāvivakṣābhyām ātmaśabdasya sādhyasamarpakatāhetutvaṃ ca yujyate iti dhyeyam ।

atripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi'; ityādinā tasyaiva amṛtatvādyupapatteḥ ।

upapatterityetadanekaliṅgaparatayā liṅgānāṃ niravakāśatvoktiparatayā ca vyāṣṭe - tripāditi ।। ityādinā vākyena uktasyeti śeṣaḥ । tasyeti vipariṇataṃ padamāvartate । amṛtatvādityetadihāpi ṣaṣṭhyantatayā buddhyā viviktaṃ sambadhyate । prathamenādipadena aabhayaṃ? titīrṣatāṃ pāram'; aamṛtaivaiṣā devatā'; aātmājaro amṛto abhayo brahma'; ityādivākyaṃ dvitīyena abhayatvādikaṃ gṛhyate । tathā ca - tripādityādinā śrutyantaravākyena tasya viṣṇoreva uktasya aetadamṛtam'; iti vākye antaḥsthaniṣṭhatvenoktasyāmṛtatvādyupapatterliṅgasya tasmin viṣṇāveva upapatteryuktatvādanyatrāyuktatvāditi yojanā । anena liṅgasya niravakāśatvānekatvābhyāṃ prābālyamuktaṃ bhavati । aamṛtaṃ'; mṛtiharitaṃ ayadabhayaṃ'; bhayarahitaṃ yacca atitīrṣatāṃ'; saṃsārataraṇecchūnāṃ apāraṃ'; saṃsārasya pārasthaṃ taduttarāvadhibhūte śvetadvīpādau sthitaṃ muktaprāpyaṃ paraṃ brahma tat dhyātuṃ sādhanaṃ vaktuṃ vayaṃ aśakemahi'; śaktāḥ sma iti kaṭhaśrutyarthaḥ ।

brahmaśabdādyupapatteśca ।

yadaivaṃ niravakāśatvānekatvābhyāṃ balavalliṅgabalāccakṣurantaḥsthasya viṣṇutvaniścayaḥ, kimu tadobhayathā svabhāvaniravakāśatvābhyām anekatvācca balavacchrutito apīti bhāvena sautramupapatterityaṃśaṃ brahmādiśrutirūpahetvantaraparatayā tasya prābālyopayoginiravakāśatvopapādanaparatayā ca prakārāntareṇa vyācaṣṭe - brahmeti । ādipadenātmaśabdo gṛhyate । brahmātmādīti pāṭhe ādiśabdena puruṣaśabdo grāhyaḥ । atra śrutetyādau saṃyojyam । tasyaivetyanuṣajyate । tathā ca - atrāntasthaprakaraṇe śrutabrahmaśabdādestasya viṣṇorevopapatteranyasyānupapatterityarthaḥ । guṇapūrtivācibrahmaśabdasya viṣṇāveva mukhyatvādātmaśabdasyāpi ādeyamupādeyaṃ sukhaṃ mātyanubhavatīti vyutpattyā tatraiva mukhyatvāditi bhāvaḥ ।।

anena aya eṣo antarakṣiṇi'; iti śrutyukto antaraḥ tattu tattajjīvaprerakatvena tattaccakṣurantassthito viṣṇureva, na tvagniḥ । atra aetadamṛtamabhayametadbrahmaiṣa ātmā'; ityamṛtatvābhayatvādiliṅgaśravaṇādbrahmādiśabdaśruteśca teṣāṃ viṣṇāvevopapatteḥ, anyatrānupapatteriti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

aso ahamasmi'; ityādi tvantaryāmyapekṣayā ।

nanu niravakāśaśrutiliṅgabalādyadi viṣṇureva akṣisthastadādityastho api sa eva syāt । tarhi aso ahamasmi sa evāhamasmi'; ityahamādiśruteḥ kā gatirityata āha - so ahamasmītyādīti । ādipadena gārhapatyādiśabdānāṃ grahaṇam। tathā ca ityādivākyasthamahamādipadajātamityarthaḥ । apekṣayetyanantaraṃ pravṛttamiti śeṣaḥ।

antaryāmiṇamīśeśamapekṣyāhaṃ tvamityapi । sarve śabdāḥ prayujyante sati bhede api vastuṣu । iti mahākaurme ।।

antaryāmiṇi ahamādiśabdapravṛttiṃ smārayati - antaryāmiṇamiti ।। ādyo api samuccaye । dvitīyo yadyapi tathāpītyarther । iśānāṃ brahmādīnārṃ iśamityantaryāmitvopapādakam । tathā ca - avastuṣu'; agnyādijīveṣur iśādbhede satyapi tadabhedabodhako ahamitiśabdaḥ tvamitiśabdaḥ। kiṃ bahunābhedasādhakāḥ sarve tattacchabdāḥ prayujyante । katham? yato antaryāmiṇamapekṣyaivaite śabdāḥ prayujyante naitāvatā agnyādijīvānārṃ iśābhedaḥ śaṅkyaḥ । yataḥ so antaryāmīr iśeśo brahmādyuttama ityarthaḥ । mahākaurme ityasya uktatvādityadhyāhāreṇa so ahamiti pūrvavākyenānvayaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। sthānādivyapadeśācca ।।

atadyadasmin sarpirvodakaṃ vā siñcati vartmanī eva gacchati'; ityādisthānaśaktiḥ । vāmanirbhāmanirityādyātmaśaktiścocyate । tasya hyetalliṅgam ।

yuktyantareṇa viṣṇoścakṣurantaḥsthatvaṃ sādhayatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe - sthānādīti । sarpirityataḥ pūrvaṃ atadyadasmin'; iti śrutivākyapāṭhaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu - ayadidaṃ cakṣuṣi'; iti pāṭhabhedena pūrvavākyamudāhṛtam । ityādīti luptavibhaktikam । ityādāvityarthaḥ । ādipadena avartmanī eva gacchati'; ityādergrahaṇam। brahmasthānabhūtayorakṣṇorakṣisthaparamapuruṣasambandhādasaṅgatvākhyaśaktirityarthaḥ ucyata ityatrāpi sambadhyate । anena sautraṃ sthānapadaṃ paramātmasthānaśaktayupalakṣakatayā vyākhyātam । ucyate ityanena asiddhiparihārakavyapadeśaśabdārtho darśitaḥ । ādipadena aetaṃ saṃyadvāma ityācakṣate । etaṃ hi sarvāṇi vāmānyabhisaṃyanti eṣa u eva vāmanireṣa hi sarvāṇi vāmāni nayati । eṣa u eva bhāmanireṣa hi sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti'; iti samagravākyaṃ gṛhyate । ātmaśaktiriti । saṃyadvāmatvarūpātmasāmarthamityarthaḥ । anena sautrādiśabdo hyadhiṣṭhātṛparamātmaparassan tacchaktyupalakṣaka iti vyākhyāto bhavati । co hetusamuccaye śaktisamuccaye cādyo bhinnakramaḥ । ucyate yata iti śeṣaḥ । asyāto api cakṣurantaḥstho viṣṇureva iti pūrvapratijñāvākyenānvayaḥ । yasmādasaṅgo ayaṃ puruṣo akṣiṇi vidyate niyāmakatayā tattasmādyadi aasmin'; cakṣuṣi asarpiḥ'; ghṛtamudakaṃ vā asiñcati'; siñcetkaścidapi tarhi tadvartmanī ubhayamārgau pratyeva gacchati na cakṣuḥ spṛśatītyarthaḥ । evaṃ cākṣuṣaṃ vāmanākhyaṃ viṣṇuṃ saṃyadvāma ityācakṣate vidvāṃśaḥ । kutaḥ? hi yasmāt etaṃ asarvāṇi vāmāni'; strīrūpāṇi abhisaṃyanti prāpnuvanti । anena saṃyanti vāmāni enamiti vigraho darśitaḥ । aeṣa u'; cakṣurgata eva mukhyato vāmanirityucyate । kutaḥ hi yasmādeṣaḥ asarvāṇi vāmāni'; sundararamādistrīrūpāṇi anayati'; prerayati । eṣa u eva cākṣuṣaḥ puruṣo abhāmaniḥ'; mukhyataḥ tacchabdavācyaḥ । kutaḥ? hi yasmādeva asarveṣu lokeṣu'; puruṣeṣu bhāti tadīyatejaḥprakāśakatayā tatra dīpyate ityarthaḥ । yathoktaṃ tattvapradīpe - vāmaṃ saundaryaṃ bhāmaṃ tejaḥ tatpradhānatvāt strīpuruṣā vāmabhāmaśabditāstannetā vāmanirbhāmaniśceti । etalliṅgadvayasadbhāve api kuto akṣisthasya viṣṇutvaniścaya ityata āha - tasyeti । ahi'; yasmāt atasya'; viṣṇoḥ aetat'; svasambandhena akṣṇorasaṅgatvāpādakatvaṃ sarvasaundaryādhiṣṭhānastrīrūpanetṛtvaṃ ca aliṅgaṃ'; asādhāraṇo dharmaḥ tasmānnāprayojakatvamiti tena viṣṇutvaniścayopapattiriti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

asar iśaḥ so asapatnaḥ sa hariḥ saḥ paraḥ sa parovarīyān yadidaṃ cakṣuṣi sarpirvodakaṃ vā siñcati vartmanī eva gacchati sa vāmanaḥ sa bhāmanaḥ na ānandaḥ so acyutaḥ'; iti caturvedaśikhāyām ।।

kuta etasya talliṅgamiti jñāyate ityata āha - sa iti ।। liṅgasya viṣṇuniṣṭhatājñāpanāya asa hariḥ'; ityādeḥ aso acyutaḥ'; ityaṃśasya coktiḥ । idaṃcakṣuṣīti samastaṃ padam । anyathā sarpirādiviśeṣaṇatvaṃ pratīyate, tataśca pratyakṣasiddhagokaviśeṣaṇatvaṃ na jñāyeta । asmin cakṣuṣītyetatprakaraṇagataśrutivisaṃvādaśca syāt । cettarhyeradhyāhāraḥ । tathā ca - yadyasmātsannihitādhiṣṭhātuḥ yasya sāmarthyāditi yāvat । aidaṃcakṣuṣi'; asmiṃścakṣuṣi sarpirudakaṃ vā siñcati cetkaścit tarhi tadvartmanī pratyeva gacchati sar iśaḥ aso asapatnaḥ'; śatrurahitaḥ । asaparaḥ'; lokavilakṣaṇaḥ । parovarīyān । rudrādeḥ parato vāṇyāḥ parāccaturmukhātparataḥ śrītattvādva uttamaḥ । sa eva vāmanabhāmanānandācyutaśabdavācya ityarthaḥ । vidheyānekatvātsa ityasakṛdāvṛttiḥ । parovarīyānityatrāpi tacchabdo anuṣañjanīyaḥ । ekadeśavikṛtasyānanyatvādvāmanibhāmaniśabdārtha eva vāmanabhāmanaśabdayorarthaḥ । caturvedaśikhāyāmityanantaraṃ uktatvāditi śeṣaḥ । asya tasyaitalliṅgamiti jñāyate iti pūrveṇānvayaḥ ।

yatsthānatvādidaṃ cakṣurasaṅgaṃ sarvavastubhiḥ ।
sa vāmanaḥ paro asmākaṃ gatirityeva cintayet ।।

liṅgasvarūpasya tasya viṣṇurūpavyaktiviśeṣaniṣṭhatāyāśca śrutāvasphuṭatvāttadarthamatrārthe smṛtiṃ cāha - yaditi ।। yasya sthānatvādityarthaḥ । asya yacchabdasya sa iti tacchabdenānvayaḥ । asarvavastubhiḥ'; sarpirādibhiḥ। avāmanaḥ'; sundarastrīneteti vāmanākhyo viṣṇureva aasmākaṃ'; bhaktānāṃ aparaḥ'; parā agatiḥ'; prāpya iti cintayedityarthaḥ। yadvā - vāmana ityanena prāptālpatvaśaṅkāvāraṇāya aparaḥ'; pūrṇa ityuktam । vāmanākhyapurāṇa ityarthaḥ । asya caturvedaśikhāyāmitivadanvayaḥ । spaṣṭaḥ sūtrārthaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। sukhaviśiṣṭābhidhānādeva ca ।।

aprāṇo brahma kaṃ brahma khaṃ brahmeti'; 

prakaraṇabalāccakṣurantaḥsthatvaṃ viṣṇoḥ pratipādayatsūtramupanyasya tadupāttaśrutimevodāharati - sukheti ।। akhaṃ brahmeti'; ityantasya sūtreṇānvayaḥ upakrame prāṇasya śrutatve api naitatprakaraṇasya tatparatvam, pūrvasūtroktaviṣṇuśrutiliṅgādibādhakasadbhāvāditi pratipādayitum uttaratra śrautakarmaśabdena prāṇabrahmaṇostantreṇopādānātsūcanārthaṃ ca aprāṇo brahma'; ityaṃśodāharaṇam । sūtre caśabdaḥ pūrvoktahetoriha prakaraṇabalāccetyadhyāhṛtahetośca samuccaye । sūtrodāhṛtahetostvadhyāhṛtasādhyenānvayaḥ । viśiṣṭaṃ ca tatsukhaṃ ca sukhaviśiṣṭam । viśeṣaṇasya paranipātaḥ । sukhena viśiṣṭa iti vā, sukheṣu viśiṣṭa iti vā, vigrahaḥ । tatra dvitīye śraiṣṭhyarūpaṃ vaiśiṣṭyamarthātsukhe apyanveti । atra prakaraṇe hi mukhyaprāṇobrahmākhilajīvebhyaḥ pūrṇaḥ iti mukhyaprāṇasya pūrṇatvamuktvā akaṃ brahma khaṃ brahma'; ityanena akaṃ'; sukhaṃ abrahma'; pūrṇaṃ akhaṃ'; jñānaṃ pūrṇamiti sukhasaṃvidorapi pūrṇatvamucyate । tathā ca na kevalamuktahetubalāccakṣurantaḥstho viṣṇuḥ, kintu - prakaraṇabalācca । na ca prakaraṇasya vaiṣṇavatvāsiddhiḥ । asyopakrame asukhaviśiṣṭābhidhānāt'; pūrṇasukhokteriti sūtrārthaḥ । yadaivamupakrame kaṃ brahma iti pūrṇasukhābhidhānādevāsya prakaraṇasya vaiṣṇavatvaṃ siddhyati kimuta tadā akhaṃ brahma'; iti pūrṇajñānādapīti kaimutyanyāyasūcanāya sūtre evakāraḥ । yadyapi chāndogyabhāṣye aprāṇo brahma'; balarūpaṃ brahma । akaṃ'; pūrṇānandarūpaṃ brahma । akhaṃ'; pūrṇajñānarūpaṃ abrahma'; paraṃ brahmeti vyākhyātam । tathāpi tadbrahmaśabdasya parāparayo rūḍhyā vṛttyā vyākhyānāntaramityadoṣaḥ।

avijñānamānandaṃ brahma'; aānando brahmeti vyajānāt'; ityādestasyaiva hi tallakṣaṇam ।

nanu upakrame pūrṇasukhasaṃvidorabhidhāne api kuto asya prakaraṇasya vaiṣṇavatvamityāśaṅkya tayosatallakṣaṇatvāt tadrūpatvāt upakrame tadabhidhāne brahmaivopakrāntaṃ syāditi bhāvena pūrṇasukhajñānayorbrahmalakṣaṇatvaṃ śrutyā darśayati - vijñānamiti ।। vijñānādirūpaṃ brahmetyarthaḥ । atra vijñānādipadaṃ pūrṇajñānādivāci, saṅkoce kāraṇābhāvāditi prakṛtasaṅgatiḥ । idaṃ vājasaneye śrutam । aānando brahma'; iti । taittirīyavākyāditi śeṣaḥ । ādiśabdena aathaiṣa eva parama ānandaḥ'; asatyaṃ jñānam'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । tathā ca ityādervākyāt atasya'; brahmaṇaḥ atat'; pūrṇānandādikaṃ alakṣaṇaṃ'; svalakṣaṇaṃ jñāyata ityarthaḥ । tathā ca - śrutyantare brahmalakṣaṇatvenāvagatayoḥ pūrṇajñānasukhayoratra prakaraṇe abhidhānāt asya vaiṣṇavatvasiddhiriti bhāvaḥ ।

lakṣaṇaṃ paramānando viṣṇoreva na saṃśayaḥ । avyaktāditṛṇāntāstu vipruḍānandabhāginaḥ ।। iti brahmavaivarte ।

nanu sakalacetanānāmapi pūrṇānandatvātkathametadviṣṇulakṣaṇamityata āha - lakṣaṇamiti ।। svarūpadharmobhayārthako ayam । aparamānandaḥ'; niravadhikapūrṇānanda eva lakṣaṇam । iha lakṣaṇatvenābhipretaḥ na pūrṇānandamātram । sa ca viṣṇoreva nānyeṣām । anyeṣāṃ tvāpekṣikameva pūrṇaṃ sukhaṃ na viṣṇuvanniravadhikaṃ pūrṇamityarthaḥ । kuta ityata āha - yataḥ avyaktādīti । avyaktā śrīḥ saivādiryeṣāṃ te tathoktāḥ । tṛṇajīvā manuṣyottamā evānte viśeṣārthaḥ । avipruḍānandabhāginaḥ'; tāratamyena brahmānandapratibimbatvāpekṣikānandayuktā ityarthaḥ । ana saṃśayaḥ'; ityasyārthasya sāvadhāraṇatvamāha । brahmavaivarta ityasyoktatvādityadhyāhāreṇa atasyaiva tallakṣaṇam'; iti sāvadhāraṇapūrvavākyenānvayaḥ ।

na ca mukhye satyamukhyaṃ yujyate ।।

nanvagyādisukhasyāpekṣikatayāpi pūrṇatvasadbhāvātteṣāṃ pūrṇasukhamidaṃ kiṃ na syāt । tathā teṣāṃ tallakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ na syāt । tathā teṣāmevedaṃ prakaraṇaṃ kiṃ na syāt ityata āha - na ceti ।। amukhye'; niravadhikapūrṇatve akaṃ brahma'; iti śrutyarthatayā tallakṣaṇe sambhavati sati aamukhyam'; āpekṣikamanyādhīnaṃ pūrṇatvaṃ na yujyate ityarthaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। śrutopaniṣatkagatyabhidhānācca ।।

asa enān brahma gamayati'; iti ।

nanvetadupakrame sukhajñānayorabhidhāne api nākṣisthaprakaraṇasya vaiṣṇavatvaṃ yuktam । chāndogye aprāṇo brahma kam'; iti vidyāṃ aya eṣa āditye puruṣaḥ'; iti vidyāṃ coktvāgnibhirupakosalaṃ prati aupakosalaiṣā somya te asmadvidhā cātmavidyā coktā'; ityuktatvena akam'; ityādyavidyāyā viṣṇuviṣayatvasya aya eṣaḥ'; iti dvitīyāyāścāgniviṣayatvasyaiva yuktatvāt । na ca aasmadvidyā'; ityuktādityavidyāyā agniviṣayatve api nākṣisthavidyāyāstadyuktamiti vācyam । aya eṣontarakṣiṇi'; ityakṣisthavidyāyā ādityavidyayaikārthatvāt । na copakramavirodhaḥ । yathā ahvayāmyagniṃ prathamaṃ svastaye'; ityatrāgnerupakrame api asavitāramūtaye'; ahiraṇyayena savitā rathena'; ityādisavitṛśrutiliṅgādinā tatprakaraṇaṃ sāvitramiti prakaraṇavicchedaḥ, tathātrāpi brahmaṇa upakrame api aasmadvidyā'; ityagnerasmacchabdenoktatvādagnīnāmevedaṃ prakaraṇaṃ na viṣṇoḥ । na ca aasmadvidyā'; ityetadantaryāmiparatayā yojyam । tathāsati aātmavidyā'; iti pṛthaguktyayogāt । tasmādagniviṣayatvameva cakṣurantaḥsthavidyāyā ityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā tadupāttaśrutimevodāharati - śruteti ।। itītasya sūtreṇānvayaḥ । atra sūtre śrutetyulakṣaṇaṃ, matadhyātetyapi draṣṭavyam । keti vāyurucyate । ako vāyuriti śabditaḥ'; iti abhidhānāt । kaśabdasyāvṛttyā gatirityanenāpi sambandhe kagatiriti parabrahmagatirucyate । akaṃ brahma'; iti vākyabodhitaparabrahmaprakaraṇādetadarthaniścayāt । tathā ca - śrutopaniṣadāṃ śrutamatadhyātaitadvidyānāṃ puṃsāṃ kena vāyunā kagateḥ akaṃ brahma'; iti vākyabodhitabrahmaprāpteḥ asa enān brahma gamayati'; ityupasaṃhāre abhidhānāt viṣṇuviṣayaivākṣisthavidyā, na tvagniviṣayeti sūtrārthaḥ । yadvā - śrutopaniṣadamupakosalaṃ pratyagnibhiretadvidyāphalatvena brahmagatyabhidhānādvaiṣṇavamevedaṃ prakaraṇaṃ, natvagniviṣayamityarthaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu - asa enān brahma gamayati'; iti śrutopaniṣatkānāṃ śrutopaniṣadgatopāsanānāṃ brahmagatyabhidhānācca āntaro viṣṇureva । asyāmupaniṣīdati brahmetyupaniṣat upāsanā । anayā brahma upaniṣīdatīti vetyuktam । śrutaviṣayiṇī yā upaniṣat matidhyānarūpopāsanā tatkānāṃ tadgataṃ tadviṣayakaṃ dhyānarūpopāsanaṃ tadvatāmityarthaḥ । anena upaniṣacchabdo matidhyānarūpopāsanāparaḥ । brahmetyanena bahuvrīhisamāsāvayavabhūtaḥ kaśabda āvṛtto brahmavācaka ityuktaṃ bhavati । ata evāha ṭīkākṛt - śrutapadaṃ manananididhyāsanayorupalakṣakamityādinā । tattvapradīpapakṣe - upaniṣacchabda upāsanāparaḥ । ṭīkākṛtpakṣe vidyāparaḥ । ṭīkāyāṃ vāśabdaścārthaḥ । yadyapyasya sūtrasya prakaraṇavicchedaśaṅkāparihārāyopasaṃhārasthaliṅgoktiparatvaṃna paramasādhye yuktyantarapratipādakatvābhāvādatra caśabdo na prayojyaḥ । tathāpi asa enān brahma'; ityupasaṃhārasthasyaitadvidyāvettṛṇāṃ brahmaprāptirūpaliṅgasya cakṣurantaro viṣṇureveti paramasādhye api sākṣādanvayādasya ca liṅgasya ādyasūtroktāmṛtatvaliṅgāpekṣayottaravākyasthadvitīyasūtroktaliṅgāpekṣayā tṛtīyasūtroktaprakaraṇāpekṣayā yuktyantaratvāttadvivakṣayā sūtre caśabdaprayogopapattiriti kecidāhuḥ । vastutastu - atra prakaraṇavicchedaśaṅkāparihāre api pūrvasūtre atra caitatprakaraṇasya vaiṣṇavatvarūpadhyāhṛtāvāntarasādhyasyaikatvenatatrānena yuktyantarābhidhānāccaśabdopapattiḥ । aatha yadu caivāsmiñchavyaṃ kurvanti yadi canārciṣamevābhisambhavanti । arciṣoharanha āpūryamāṇapakṣaṃ āpūryamāṇapakṣādyān ṣaḍudaṅṅeti māsānstānmāsebhyaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ saṃvatsarādādityamāditiyāccandramasaṃ candramaso vidyutaṃ tatpuruṣo mānavaḥ sa enān brahma gamayati'; iti chandogaśruterayamarthaḥ - athetyarthāntare । aatha'; avasitakarmaṇi aasmin'; jñāniviṣaye putrādayo yadi aśavyaṃ'; śavayogyaṃ dahanādikarma kurvanti । ayadi ca na'; yadi vā na kurvanti atadārciṣam'; arcirnāmakadevalokaṃ sambhavanti prāpnuvantyeveme jñānina iti vipariṇāmenānvayaḥ । saṃviśatītyekavacanāntaviśidhātupāṭhaḥ ate'; iti pāṭhaśca prameyadīpachandogapāṭhaviruddhaḥ । tato aharlokaṃ, tata aāpūryamāṇapakṣaṃ'; śuklapakṣalokaṃ, tataḥ sūryo ayān'; ṣaṇmāsān udaṅṅeti tanmāsadevalokam uttarāyaṇalokaṃ ca, tataḥ saṃvatsarādādityacandravidyudabhimānilokānkrameṇa prāpnuvanti । tataḥ atasyāḥ'; vidyunnāmnyā bhāratyāḥ apuruṣo'; bhartā amānavo'; manusaṃjñasya viṣṇoḥ priyo mukhyavāyustaṃ gacchanti । asaḥ'; vāyuḥ aenān'; svamāptān pratīkālambanān caturmukhākhyaṃ kāryaṃ brahmāpratīkālambanāṃstu paraṃ brahma gamayatīti ।

na hyanyavidyayānyagatiryuktā ।।

astvetadvidyāyāḥ phalatvena brahmaprāptyabhidhānaṃ, tathāpi kuto nāgniviṣayatvamasyā ityata āha - na hīti ।। ahi'; yasmādanyasyāgnervidyayānyagatiranyasya brahmaṇaḥ prāptirna yuktā । yasmāccātra parabrahmaprāptiḥ phalatvenocyate ityarthaḥ । tasmānnānyavidyeyaṃ brahmavidyaiveti vākyaśeṣaḥ । hiśabdena vipakṣe - adevān devayajo yānti madbhaktā yānti māmapi'; iti smṛtivirodhaṃ sūcayati । aasmadvidyātmavidyā'; iti vacanavirodhastu tayorantaryāmisarvagatarūpadvayaviṣayakatvena pariharaṇīyaḥ । sāvakāśaśruterapi niravakāśaśruteḥ prābalyāditi bhāvaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। anavasthiterasambhavācca netaraḥ ।।

jīvasya jīvāntaraniyāmakatve anavasthiteḥ, sāmyādasambhavācca na jīvaḥ ।

evamupapattyādibhirviṣṇorakṣisthatvaṃ pratipādya vipakṣe bādhakenāpi tatsamarthayatsūtraṃ paṭhati - anavasthiteriti । atrāntarastattajjīvaprerakatayā tattaccakṣussthitaḥ aitaraḥ'; pūrvaprakṛtāt kaśabdoditāt brahmaṇo anyo agnijīvo na । kutaḥ? yataḥ sa itaro jīva iti hetusādhyayojanāmabhipretya atra vipakṣe aniṣṭaprasaṅgābhidhāyakatayānavasthiterityaṃśaṃ yojayati - jīvasyeti । asāmyāt'; iti sūtre adhyāhṛtaṃ padam, idaṃ ca tattvapradīparītyā dehalīdīpanyāyenobhayatra sambadhyate । jīvasya jīvāntaraniyāmakatve ityetadvipariṇatamasambhavādityanenāpi sambadhyate । itara ityasyāgnirityarthe vācye jīva iti sāmānyenoktiḥ sādhyahetvostantreṇābhidhānārtham । na jīva ityasya āntara ityuddeśyasamarpakānuvṛttapadenānvayaḥ । anena tattajjīvaprerakatayā tattaccakṣurantaro netaraḥ nāgniḥ । kutaḥ? yataḥ sa itaro jīvaḥ jīvatvāditi yāvat । na ca vipakṣe bādhakābhāvaḥ, jīvasya jīvāntaraniyāmakatve prerakatve āntarajīvasyāpi jīvatvasāmyatāttasyāpi niyāmakaṃ jīvāntaraṃ vācyamityanavasthiterasiddhaparamparākalpanarūpānavasthākhyāniṣṭāpatteḥ । abhyupagamya cedamuditam । vastutastu - jīvasya jīvāntaraniyāmakatvāsambhavācca netaro agnirantaraḥ । kuto asambhavaḥ? agnerjīvasya preryajīvāntareṇa saha paratantrarūpajīvatvasāmyāditi sūtravṛttirdarśitā bhavati ।

niyamapramāṇābhāvāt । anīśvarāpekṣatvācca ।।
।। iti antarādhikaraṇam ।।

nanu jīvaprerakāgneḥ svātantryābhyupagamānnānavasthā । na caivaṃ jīvāntarasyāpi svātantryaṃ syāt jīvatvasāmyādityuktamiti vācyam । jīvatvasāmye apyagnereva svātantryaṃ nānyeṣāmiti niyamābhyupagamādityata āha - niyameti ।। jīvatvasāmyepyagnereva svātantryaṃ nānyeṣāmiti niyame pramāṇābhāvādityarthaḥ । ato agneḥ svātantryāyogātsusthaivānavasthitiriti bhāvaḥ । nanvastvagnerasvātantryaṃ, tathāpi tatprerakasyeśvarasya svātantryasambhavānnānavasthetyata āha - anīśvaretir । iśvaraṃ jagatprerakatvena yo apekṣate abhyupaiti sar iśvarāpekṣaḥ, sa na bhavatītyanīśvarāpekṣaḥ, tasya bhāvastattvaṃ tasmādityarthaḥ । pūrvavādina iti śeṣaḥ । hetusamuccaye caśabdaḥ । evaṃ vā - nanu paratantratvasāmye api jīvānāṃ jīvāntaraniyāmakatvātkathaṃ tadasambhava ityata āha - anīśvareti । vyākhyānaṃ pūrvavat । tathā ca - yathāsmatpakṣe sati rājñi maṇḍaleśe prajānāṃ rājaśaktyā niyamyaniyāmakabhāvavart iśvaraśaktyā jīvānāṃ jīvāntaraniyāmakatvasambhavaḥ, na tathā parapakṣe sambhavati, pareṇar iśvarānabhyupagamāditi bhāvaḥ । idaṃ ca vākyadvayasya yojanādvayam । ṭīkāyāṃ tattvapradīpoktamevoktam । uktaṃ hi tattvapradīpe - niyamapramāṇābhāvo anīśvarāpekṣatvaṃ cetyubhau ubhayatra heturiti । aubhayatra'; anavasthityasambhavayorityarthaḥ ।। iti antarādhikaraṇam ।।

।। antaryāmyādhikaraṇam ।।

ayaḥ pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhan pṛthivyā antaro yaṃ pṛthivī na veda yasya pṛthivī śarīraṃ yaḥ pṛthivīmantaro yamayatyeṣa ta ātmāntaryāmyamṛtaḥ'; ityādi antaryāmyucyate ।

atrādhikaraṇe antaḥsthatvarūpabhāvasahitaṃ niyamanakriyātmakaṃ liṅgaṃ brahmaṇi samanvīyate । viṣayavākyodāharaṇapūrvakaṃ viṣayaṃ darśayati - ya iti ।। ityādīti prathamā saptamyarthe । tṛtīyārthe vā । asaptasu prathamā'; iti sūtrāt । akriyāviśeṣaṇaṃ vā'; iti tattvapradīpokteḥ aityādinā'; iti pāṭhastadviruddhaḥ । vākye, vākyeneti vā śeṣaḥ। ayo apsu tiṣṭhan'; ayo bhūteṣu tiṣṭhan'; ityādikamādiśabdena gṛhyate । antaryāmītyanena viṣayo darśitaḥ । bṛhadāraṇyake uddālakaṃ prati yājñyavalkyenoktaṃ idaṃ vākyam । ayaḥ pṛthivyāṃ'; pṛthuṃ viṣṇumūḍhvā vāti gacchatīti pṛthivī garuḍaḥ tasmin tiṣṭhan apṛthivyāḥ'; tadabhimānicetanāt aantaro'; viviktaḥ । ayaṃ ca pṛthivī'; tadabhimānī cetano na veda sākalyena । ayasya ca pṛthivī'; tadvaśatvanimittāt śarīrabhūtā । na kevalaṃ tatra sthitimātraṃ, kintu ayo antaraḥ'; antaḥsthitvā bāhyaviṣayāpekṣāṃ vinā ramamāṇaḥ । svato nityatṛptaḥ - bāhyāpekṣāṃ vinā yastu ramate so antarassmṛtaḥ'; ।।

iti bṛhadbhāṣyokteḥ । yadvā - atipriyatvācca harerantaratvamudāhṛtam ।।

iti tatraivokteḥ । apreyaḥ putrāt'; ityādiśrutyā paramapreyorūpatvāt aantaraḥ'; atipriyaḥ san apṛthivīṃ'; garuḍaṃ ayamayati'; niyamayati । eṣaḥ ate'; tava aantaryāmyātmā'; niyāmakaḥ puruṣaḥ aamṛtaḥ'; nitya iti śrutyarthaḥ । etena antaro vivikta iti ṭīkāyā bṛhadbhāṣyavirodho nirastaḥ । bṛhadbhāṣyasya aya ātmānam'; ityatrasthāntaraśabdaviṣayatvāt । ata eva na śrutau paunaruktyam । dvayorbhinnārthatvāt । pūrvapakṣī tvidaṃ vākyamanyaparaṃ manyate ।

tatra ca aetadamṛtam'; ityuktamamṛtatvamucyate । sa ca ayasya pṛthivī śarīram'; ityādinā sarvātmakatvāt prakṛtistattajjīvo vā yuktaḥ ।

pūrvādhikaraṇatadviṣayavākyasaṅgatiṃ darśayati - tatreti ।। iyamatra tattvapradīpoktā yojanā - ayaḥ pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhan'; ityādivākyeṣvantaryāmyucyate । tatra tadvākyeṣveva tasminnevāntaryāmiṇi aetadamṛtametadabhayam'; iti pūrvanayodāhṛtachāndogyavākye akṣipuruṣasyoktamamṛtatvaṃ aeṣa ta ātmāntaryāmyamṛtaḥ'; ityanena ucyate iti । anena bṛhadāraṇyakoktāntaryāmiṇi viṣṇvanyatvākṣepamukhena taduktāmṛtatvasyāpyanyaniṣṭhatvaṃ sampādya tasya pūrvādhikaraṇoktākṣisthatvasya viṣṇutvasādhakatvākṣepātpūrveṇākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tataḥ kimityataḥ sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣayati - sa ceti । caśabdo hetusamuccaye । ādipadena ayasyāpaḥ śarīram'; ityādeḥ saṅgrahaḥ । tacchabdasya vipariṇāmena hetuvākyena sambandhaḥ । ātmaśabdaḥ svarūpaśarīrobhayārthaḥ । tathā ca so antaryāmī jaḍacetanobhayarūpā prakṛtiḥ pṛthivyāditattajjīvo vā yuktaḥ । kutaḥ? śrautaśarīraśabdasya idaṃ pūrvapakṣaśarīramityādāviva svarūpārthatvāt । jaḍaprakṛteśca sarvopādānatvena sarvātmakatvāt । citprakṛteśca sarvābhimānitvena sarvātmakatvāt pṛthivyādijīvasya pṛthivyādisarvaśarīratvāditi yojanā ।

na hi viṣṇoḥ pṛthivyādiśarīratvamaṅgīkriyate iti ।

nanu yathā prakṛtyādiliṅgena teṣāmantaryāmitvaṃ tathā amṛtatvaliṅgena viṣṇostatkiṃ na syādityata āha - na hīti ।। pṛthivyādi śarīraṃ yasya sa tathoktaḥ, tasya bhāvastattvaṃ tvapratyayāpāṭhe tvanvayaḥ ṛjuḥ । siddhāntineti śeṣaḥ । tasya pṛthivyādijaḍabhinnaciccharīratvāditi hiśabdābhiprāyaḥ । tathā ca - saiddhāntikaliṅgāpekṣayā pūrvapakṣaliṅgasya niravakāśatayā balavattvādanena tasya bādhānnāntaryāmī viṣṇuriti bhāvaḥ ।

ata āha - sū - oṃ।।
antaryāmyadhidaivādiṣu taddharmavyapadeśāt ।
।।

ayaṃ pṛthivī na veda, yaḥ pṛthivyā antaraḥ'; ityādinā adhidaivādiṣu taddharmavyapadeśāt viṣṇurevāntaryāmī ।

siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe - ata iti ।। ityādinā vākyena iti śeṣaḥ । tatra yadyapi sautravyapadeśapadena abhipretaṃ ayaṃ pṛthivī na veda yaḥ pṛthivīmantaro yamayati'; iti vākyamevodāhartavyam । atroktāntaratvasyaiva sautradharmaśabdārthatvāt, na tu apṛthivyāmantaraḥ'; iti vākyam । atrātyantaraśabdasya viviktārthatvena taduktārthasyāhetutvāt । tathā ca tadudāharaṇaṃ na prakṛtopayuktam । tathāpi tatpratīkatvenodāhṛtamityadoṣaḥ । ādiśabdena prakaraṇatrayavākyaṃ gṛhyate । prakaraṇeṣviti śeṣaḥ । prakaraṇaṃ nāma ekaprameyapratipādakānekavākyāni । tatra ayaḥ pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhan'; ityadhidaivataprakaraṇam । ayassarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhan'; ityādibhūtaprakaraṇam । ayaḥ prāṇe tiṣṭhan'; ityadhyātmaprakaraṇam । sūtre bhāṣye cādhidaivetyuktyā pṛthivyādīnāṃ jaḍatvena tadaviditatvaṃ sarvasyāpi sambhavatīti śaṅkā vāritā । atroktānāṃ pṛthivyādīnāṃ adhidaivatvena cetanatvāt aprāṇe'; iti śrutau prāṇaśabdaḥ prāṇavāyudevatāparaḥ, saiva prameyadīparītyā prāṇendriyadevatā । adhidaivādiṣvityanekaprakaraṇagrahaṇena na kevalamekatra taddharmoktiḥ, kintu - bahuṣu sthaleṣviti sūcitam । anuvṛttasya tattvityasyārthamāha - viṣṇureveti । tadityasya napuṃsakatve api antaryāmītyuddeśyasamarpakasautrapadānusāreṇa viṣṇureveti vyākhyātam । anena aeṣa ta ātmā'; ityuktāntaryāmī sa viṣṇureva । kutaḥ? adhidaivādiṣu prakaraṇeṣu ataddharmavyapadeśāt'; tasya viṣṇoḥ dharmasya aviditatvāntaratvādeḥ ayaṃ pṛthivī na veda'; ityādinoktatvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sa hi ana te viṣṇo jāyamāno na jātaḥ'; asa yo ato aśruto agato amato anato adṛṣṭo avijñāto anādiṣṭaḥ sarveṣāṃ bhūtānāmantarapuruṣaḥ'; ityādināvidito antaraśca ।।

aviditatvādeḥ kuto viṣṇudharmatvamityata āha - sa hīti ।। asaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ । aityādinā'; vākyeneti śeṣaḥ । ādipadena adivyo deva eko nārāyaṇaḥ'; ityupakramya ayasya pṛthivī śarīraṃ yaḥ pṛthivīmantaraḥ sañcaran yaṃ pṛthivī na veda eṣa sarvabhūtāntarātmā apahatapāpmā divyo deva eko nārāyaṇaḥ'; ityupasaṃhṛtyādhītaṃ śrutyantaraṃ gṛhyate । aaviditaḥ'; sākalyenājñātaḥ aantaraḥ'; antassthitvā ramaṇakṛtprasiddha iti śeṣaḥ । ca samuccaye । ana te'; iti vākyaṃ ca te devamahimnaḥ paramantaṃ mahimānaṃ śrotrādinā nāpa iti prakṛtānuguṇyena sarvatrādhikaraṇe vyākhyātam । asaḥ'; iti vākyamapi tatraiva vyākṛtam ।

sū - oṃ।। na ca smārtamataddharmābhilāpāt । 
।।
triguṇatvādipradhānadharmānukterna smṛtyuktaṃ pradhānamantaryāmī ।।

evaṃ niravakāśaliṅgena viṣṇorantaryāmitvaṃ samarthya yaduktaṃ pūrvapakṣiṇā prakṛtyāderantaryāmitvaṃ tatprakṛtijīvasādhāraṇaṃ yuktyā nirākurvatsūtramupanyasyati - na ceti ।। atra aataddharmābhilāpāt'; ityetat aatacchabdāt'; itivadavyayībhāvasamāsarūpam । ata eva avyayamityāśayenāniyamābhiprāyeṇādau hetuvākyaṃ vyākhyāti - triguṇatvādīti । sattvādirūpāstrayo guṇā yasya kāryabhūtāstattriguṇaṃ, tasya bhāvastriguṇatvaṃ tadādiryeṣāṃ te tathoktāḥ, pradhānasya prakṛterdharmāḥ, triguṇatvādayaścate pradhānadharmāśca te jaḍatvasaṃsāritvādīnāṃ grahaṇam । pradhānapadaṃ jīvasyāpyupalakṣakam । ādiśabdo vātra saṃyojyaḥ । sādhyadharmapratiyoginirdeśāya pūrvapakṣe yuktisūcanāya ca prayuktaṃ smārtamityedvyācaṣṭe - smṛtyuktamiti । pṛthivyādyātmakatayā kāpilasmṛtipratipāditamityarthaḥ । smṛtyuktamevaitanna śrutyuktamiti jñāpanāyedam । paryavasitārthamāha - pradhānamiti । jīvasyāpyupalakṣakamidam । śārīraśceti vakṣyamāṇasyātrāpyanvayo darśitaḥ । antaryāmiṇo anyarūpatvaniṣedhāya pravṛtte sūtre apekṣitaṃ sādhyadharmiṇaṃ darśayati - antaryāmīti । antaryāmī na pradhānamiti yojanā । na pradhānamantaryāmītyanena sautracaśabdaḥ antaryāmī viṣṇureva na tu pradhānamiti tuśabdārthaḥ । sa ca na śārīra ityādāviva parapakṣaniṣedhamātraṃ na kriyate, kintu, svapakṣavidhirapīti parapakṣaniṣedhasya svapakṣavidhipūrvakatvarūpaviśeṣārtha iti sūcitaṃ bhavati । anenāntaryāmī viṣṇureva, na tu smārtaṃ pṛthivyādyātmakatayā smṛtau pratipāditaṃ pradhānam । śārīro jīvaḥ । kutaḥ? atra aataddharmābhilāpāt'; triguṇatvasaṃsāritvādirūpapradhānajīvadharmoktyabhāvāditi sūtravṛttirdarśitābhavati । tattvapradīpe tu - nañastadviruddhārthatvamāśrityātmatvāmṛtatvādṛṣṭatvadraṣṭṛtvādyataddharmābhilāpācca iti hetuvākyasya vṛttyantaramapi darśitam।

sū - oṃ।। śārīraścobhaye api hi bhedenainamadhīyate ।।

aya ātmani tiṣṭhannātmano antaro yamātmāna veda yasyātmā śarīraṃ ya ātmānamantaro yamayatyeṣa ta ātmāntaryāmyamṛtaḥ'; ayo vijñāne tiṣṭhan vijñānādantaro yaṃ vijñānaṃ na veda yasya vijñānaṃ śarīram'; ityubhaye api hi śākhino bhedenainaṃ jīvamadhīyate ।

yajjīvo antaryāmītyuktam । tatsādhakābhāvena nirastamapi punarbādhakākhyaviśeṣayuktyā nirākurvatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe - śārīra iti ।। ityabhidhīyate ityanvayaḥ । ubhaye ityasya viśeṣyapadaṃ darśayati - śākhina iti । kāṇvā mādhyandināścetyarthaḥ । ātmano antara iti mādhyandināḥ vijñānādantara iti kāṇvāḥ । apiśabdaḥ śākhāsamuccaye । antaryāmiṇaḥ iti vipariṇatamatrānuvartate । enamityanūdyajīvamiti vyākhyātam । ato na śārīraścāntaryāmīti śeṣaḥ । tena sautracaśabdo nañaḥ samākarṣakaḥ । na kevalaṃ na smārtaṃ, kintu śārīraśceti samuccaye apītyuktaṃ bhavati । tattvapradīpe tu - citprakṛterapyatra pūrvapakṣaviṣayatāmāśritya śrībhūdurgārūpāyāḥ tasyāḥ ayastejasi tiṣṭhan'; ayastamasi tiṣṭhan'; ityādyantaryāmiṇaḥ sakāśādbhedenādhyayanānna sāpyantaryāmīti samuccayārthaścaśabda ityuktam । anena ahi'; yasmāt aubhaye api'; śākhinaḥ aenaṃ'; jīvamantaryāmiṇaḥ sakāśādbhedena aadhīyate'; āmananti । tasmādbādhakānnāntaryāmī aśārīraḥ'; śarīrābhimānī jīva iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । śrutau ayaḥ pṛthivyāḥ'; iti vākyasyāditve api tadvihāyātmavijñānavākyayoścetanaparatvenobhayaparatvādaikārthyācca te evātrobhayakartṛkabhedādhyayanatayodāhṛte । aātmano'; jīvāt aantaro'; viviktaḥ । evaṃ vijñānaśabdo api aya ātmani'; iti śrutisamākhyānājjīvasāmānyaparaḥ । yadyapi bṛhadbhāṣye ātmādiśabdasya caturmukhākhyajīvaparatayā vyākhyātatvādidaṃ sūtraṃ jīvaviśeṣasya yogino antaryāmitvanirāsakamiti । ata eva tattvapradīpe yogino antaryāmitvaṃ nirākarotītyuktam । tathāpi yadā sarvajīvābhimānicaturmukhādapi tanniyāmakatvādinā bhinno antaryāmī tadā kimu tadabhimanyamānasarvajīvāditi kaimutyadyotanāya tatra tathoktiriti candrikāyāmuktatvājjīvasāmānyāntaryāmitvaniṣedhaparatayā pravṛttāyā etatsūtraṭīkāyāḥ bṛhadbhāṣyatattvapradīpavirodhaḥ ।

śāryate nityamevāsmādviṣṇostu jagadīdṛśam ।
ramate ca parohyasmin śarīraṃ tasya tajjagat ।
iti vacanānna śarīratvavirodhaḥ ।।

।। iti antaryāmyadhikaraṇam ।।

nanu na viṣṇorantaryāmitvaṃ yuktam । pṛthivyādiśarīratvasya pradhānadharmasyātrokteḥ tasya viṣṇāvasambhavāt । kathaṃ pradhānadharmānuktiḥ pṛthivyādiśarīratvasyaiva taddharmatvādityata āha - śīryata iti ।। tuśabdo avadhāraṇe । tathā ca ahi'; yasmārt aidṛśaṃ'; vartamānajagatsadṛśaṃ kālatrayābādhyaṃ vā ajagat'; pṛthivyādi asmāt viṣṇoreva anityaṃ'; niyataṃ pratikalpaṃ aśīryate'; naśyati । ātmādicetanānāmapi dehadvārā śīryatā satyaiva । yasmācca aparaḥ'; paramātmā aasmin'; jagati sthitassan ramate atat'; tasmādeva atasya'; viṣṇoḥ ajagat'; pṛthivyādikaṃ śarīramucyate, na rūḍhyetyarthaḥ । ana śarīratvāvirodhaḥ'; iti । na pṛthivyādiśarīratvavirodha ityarthaḥ । viṣṇvantaryāmitāyā ataddharmābhilāpokterveti śeṣaḥ । viṣṇoḥ pṛthivyādyātmakatvataccharīratvābhyāṃ pṛthivyādiśarīratvānupapattāvapi śarīraśabdasya pṛthivyādiṣu yogavṛttimāśritya tasmin pṛthivyādiśarīratvavyapadeśopapatteritaratra tadanupapatteriti bhāvaḥ । yattu bṛhadāraṇyabhāṣye - 
pṛthivyādyā devatāstu dehavadyadvaśatvataḥ ।
śarīramiti cocyante yasya viṣṇoḥ mahātmanaḥ ।।

iti pramāṇānusāreṇa pṛthivyāderbrahmaśarīratvaṃ gauṇamityuktam । tatpurāṇādiṣu prapañce brahmakāyatvādyuktisamarthanāyeti na tadvirodhaḥ ।।

।। iti antaryāmyadhikaraṇam ।।

।। adṛśyatvādhikaraṇam ।।

adṛśyatvādiguṇā viṣṇoruktāḥ ।

atrādhikaraṇe dṛśyatvādyābhāvākhyaliṅgaṃ brahmaṇi samanvīyate । pūrvādhikaraṇatadviṣayasaṅgativiṣayavākyodāharaṇapūrvakaṃ viṣayasaṃśayau sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ ca sūcayati - adṛśyatvādīti। aguṇāḥ'; śubhadharmāḥ । ādipadenānātmyādigrahaṇam । uktā iti । ānandamayasya aadṛśye'; iti vākyeneti śeṣaḥ । upalakṣaṇametat । antaḥsthasya ana vijānanti'; ityanena sarvagatasya asa yo ato aśrutaḥ'; ityanena antaryāmiṇo ayaṃ pṛthivī na veda'; ityavyavahitapūrvādhikaraṇodāhṛtavākyena cetyapi draṣṭavyam ।

tatra ayattadadreśyamagrāhyamagotramavarṇamacakṣuḥśrotraṃ tadapāṇipādam । nityaṃ vibhuṃ sarvagataṃ tadavyayaṃ tadbhūtayoniṃ paripaśyanti dhīrāḥ'; ।। ityuktvā -

uktā ityāvartate । auktvā'; ityanantaram āmnāta iti śeṣaḥ । tena ktvāpratyayopapattiḥ । candrikāyāṃ tu - ityuktvā pratīyata iti bhāṣye kriyayoḥ samānakartṛkatvābhāve api ktvāpratyayo ayadorvaṃśaṃ naraḥ śrutvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate'; itivaddraṣṭavyamityukterapyayamevābhiprāyaḥ । para itītyanantaraṃ vākya iti śeṣaḥ । atasmācca'; iti padadvayaṃ bhāṣyakārīyam । tathocetthaṃ yojanā - pūrvaṃ ye adṛśyatvādiguṇā viṣṇoruktāste yatra kasyacidakṣarasyoktāstatrātharvaṇe adṛśyatvādiguṇakākṣaraviṣaye ayattadadreśyamagrāhyam'; ityādyuktvā tathā tatraiva ayathorṇanābhiḥ'; ityādi aviśvam'; ityantaṃ vākyaṃ coktvā paṭhitvā anantaramāmnāte - 
divyo hyamūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ sa bāhyābhyantaro hyajaḥ ।
aprāṇo hyamanāḥ śubhrohyakṣarātparataḥ paraḥ ।।

iti uttaravākye atasmādakṣarāt'; prakṛtādakṣarādapi aparaḥ'; uttamaḥ apratīyate'; pratipādyatayā jñāyata iti । anena pūrvoktādṛśyatvasya viṣṇvanyaniṣṭatvākṣepātpūrveṇānandamayādyadhikaraṇena asyākṣepikī saṅgatiḥ । adṛśyatvādirūpo viṣayaḥ । kiṃ viṣṇoranyasya veti sandehaḥ । na viṣṇoradṛśyatvādīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । adṛśyatvādiviśiṣṭe aakṣarātsambhavati'; ityakṣaraśabdaśravaṇāttasya ca tatparatvoktyā viṣṇoḥ niravakāśatvāditi pūrvapakṣayuktiśca sūcitā bhavatīti । śrutyarthastu - ayat'; paravidyāgamyamakṣaraṃ atadadreśyaṃ'; dṛśyaśabditacakṣurādijñeyabhinnam । aagrāhyaṃ'; manogrāhyabhinnam । aagotraṃ'; na vidyate gotrādikaṃ yasya taddhi tathocyate iti sudhoktervaśiṣṭhādigotrahīnam । aavarṇaṃ'; prākṛtaśuklādivarṇahīnam । adṛśyatvādiśabdairdṛśyādyanyonyābhāvābhidhīyate iti sudhokteḥ gotravarṇabhinnatvaṃ cārthaḥ । yat aacakṣuḥśrotraṃ'; prākṛtajñānendriyādiśūnyam । tat aapāṇipādaṃ'; prākṛtakarmendriyaśūnyaṃ anityaṃ'; svarūpanāśarahitaṃ avibhuṃ'; samarthaṃ asarvagataṃ'; vyāptaṃ asusukṣmam'; atyantāvyaktaṃ ayadbhūtayoniṃ'; adhīrāḥ'; jñāninaḥ paripaśyanti atadakṣaram'; avyayaṃ dehato nāśaśūnyamiti । atra tacchabdasya sarvatrānvayāya trirgrahaṇam । bhūtayonipadaṃ ca sattarkadīpāvalyāṃ bhūtānām ākāśādīnāṃ brahmādicetanānāṃ vā keṣāṃcit strīvyavadhānena vinā svasvadehādevotpādakamiti vyākhyātam । dhīrā ityanenādṛśyatvadṛśyatvayorvirodhaḥ parihṛtaḥ ।

yathorṇanābhissṛjate gṛhṇate ca yathā pṛthivyāmoṣadhayaḥ sambhavanti । yathā sataḥ puruṣātkeśalomāni tathākṣarātsambhavatīha viśvam । ityuktvā tasmācca aakṣarātparataḥ paraḥ'; iti paraḥ pratīyate -

etadeva dṛṣṭāntoktyā spaṣṭayati - yatheti ।। ayathorṇanābhiḥ'; tantuvāyaḥ asṛjate'; svopabhuktavastūni tantvātmanā pariṇatāni svadehānniṣkāsayati । agṛhṇate'; cakrādyākāratayā bahirniṣkāsitaṃ vastu punarantaḥ svodare gṛhṇāti । tathā viśvaṃ pralaye nigīrṇaṃ sṛṣṭau akṣarātsambhavati । dṛṣṭāntāntaramāha - yatheti । aoṣadhayaḥ'; aṅkurādayaḥ । dṛṣṭāntāntaramāha - yatheti । asato'; jīvavataḥ puruṣāccharīrāt śirasthāḥ keśāḥ, anyāni lomāni tāni । aiha'; loke aviśvaṃ'; nānāvidhakāryaṃ asambhavati'; jāyate ityarthaḥ । atra brahmaṇo bhūtakāraṇatvaṃ tatkartṛtvarūpaṃ na tūpādānatvamiti vaktumādyo dṛṣṭāntaḥ । aṅkurādijanane pṛthivī bījamiva viśvasṛṣṭau brahma tatkarmāpekṣata iti vaktuṃ dvitīyaḥ । anāyāsena sṛṣṭiriti vaktuṃ tṛtīyaḥ । divya ityādivākyaṃ tu adivyaḥ'; adbhutaḥ aamūrto'; niyataparicchinnaparimāṇarahitaḥ । kintu bāhya ābhyantaraśca । aprāṇo hyamanā iti padābhyāṃ ṣoḍaśakalārāhityamucyate । aśubhraḥ'; śuddhaḥ jaḍāt aparataḥ akṣarāt'; citprakṛteḥ para iti karmanirṇayaṭīkāyāṃ vyākhyātam।

ato bravīti - sū - oṃ।।
adṛśyatvādiguṇako dharmokteḥ ।।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati - ata iti ।। itisaṅgatisambhavāt iti śaṅkāsadbhāvācca taduttararūpaṃ sūtramabravīdbādarāyaṇaḥ ityarthaḥ । tatsūtraṃ paṭhati - adṛśyatvādīti ।।

pṛthivyādidṛṣṭāntamuktvā aakṣarātsambhavatīha viśvam'; ityataḥ paraṃ tatparataḥ parābhidhānāt akūṭastho akṣara ucyate'; iti smṛteśca prakṛteḥ prāptiḥ ।

nanvadṛśyatvādikaṃ viṣṇorna cet - tarhi vākyasya nirviṣayatayā aprāmāṇyaṃ syāt ityataḥ pūrvapakṣaṃ viśadayati - pṛthivyādīti ।। śrutāvūrṇanābhidṛṣṭāntasya prāthamye api tatra sṛjata ityanena kartṛtvamātrapratīteḥ pūrvapakṣānukūlasyopādānatayā jagatkāraṇatvasyāpratīteḥ taṃ parityajya pṛthivyādītyuktam । tathācetthaṃ yojanā - pṛthivyādidṛṣṭāntamuktvā anantaramuktāt aakṣarātsaṃbhavatīha viśvam'; ityato vākyāt aparam'; anantaramadhītena aakṣarātparataḥ paraḥ'; iti vākyena atatparataḥ'; tasmātkāraṇībhūtādakṣarātparataḥ parasyottamasyoktatvāt, tathā akūṭastho akṣara ucyate'; iti smṛteśca jaḍaprakṛteścitprakṛteścādṛśyatvādiprāptiriti । atrāyaṃ vivekaḥ - yadā jaḍaprakṛteḥ pūrvapakṣaviṣayatā tadākṣaraśabdastatparo hetuḥ tatparataḥ parābhidhānaṃ ca । tasya niravakāśatve akṣarātparata iti ca vyadhikaraṇe pañcamyau । yadā ca citprakṛtestadākṣaraśabdastatparohetuḥ । samānādhikaraṇe pañcamyau । smṛteścetyapi heturiti । smṛtiścātrādhikaraṇe vyākhyātā ।

brahmaśabdāttatparataḥ parābhidhānādeva ca hiraṇyagarbhasya ।

pūrvapakṣāntaraṃ vakti - brahmaśabdāditi ।। asa brahmavidyām'; ityādau śrutabrahmaśabdādityarthaḥ । brahmaśabdo viṣṇāveva mukhya iti tasyaiva sādhako netarasyetyato hetvantaramāha - parata iti ।। vyadhikaraṇe pañcamyau । tathā ca - hiraṇyagarbhākhyādakṣarāt aparataḥ'; śrītattvātparasya viṣṇorabhidhānādityarthaḥ । evaśabdena hetorniravakāśatvaṃ nātra hetvantaraṃ gaveṣaṇīyamiti sūcayati । hiraṇyagarbhasya prāptirityanvayaḥ । akartāramīśam'; itīśaśabdaśravaṇāt rudrasya vā adṛśyatvādiprāptiriti vakṣyamāṇamatrāpi draṣṭavyam । asmin pakṣer iśaśabdasya viṣṇau sāvakāśatvaśaṅkāyāmanantaraṃ tatparataḥ parābhidhānādityapi yojyam । atrāpi vyadhikaraṇe pañcamyau ।

atamevaṃ vidvānamṛta iha bhavati'; tatkarma haritoṣaṃ yatsā vidyā tanmatiryayā । atha dve vāva vidye veditavye parācaivāparā ca । tatra ye vedā yānyaṅgāni yānyupāṅgāni yāni pratyaṅgāni sāparā । atha parā yayā sa harirveditavyo yo asāvadṛśyo nirguṇaḥ paraḥ paramātmā ityādinā taddharmatvenāvagataparavidyāviṣayatvokterviṣṇurevādṛśyatvādiguṇakaḥ ।।

evaṃ prāptaṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ pratikṣeptuṃ sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe - tamevamiti ।। atamevam'; ityekaṃ śrutivākyam । atat'; ityaparaṃ smṛtivākyam । aatha'; ityanyacchrutivākyam । ādipadena atadetadbrahma'; atripādasyāmṛtam'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । tasya viṣṇordharmastaddharmaḥ tasya bhāvasatattvaṃ teneti vigrahaḥ । avagatatvaṃ prasiddhatvaṃ viṣayatvaviśeṣaṇam । amṛtatvāderupalakṣakametat । sūtre anuvṛttasya tattvityasyārtho viṣṇureveti atrādṛśyatvaṃ dṛśyabhinnatvam । tacca svarūpam, na tu gotrādyatyantābhāvavadbrahmabhinnam । tatra tadvattvaṃ brahmasvarūpamiti viśeṣaṃ vaktum adṛśyatvādayo guṇā yasyeti bahuvrīhitvaṃ ca sūcayituṃ śubhadharmārthakaguṇaśabdaprayogaḥ kapratyayaśca । tathācetthaṃ sūtrabhāṣyayojanā - adṛśyatvādiguṇakastattu viṣṇureva । kutaḥ? atra prakaraṇe aatha parā yayā tadakṣaramadhigamyate'; atadetadakṣaraṃ brahma'; apuruṣa evedaṃ viśvaṃ karma tapobrahma parāmṛtam'; iti vākyeṣu tasyādṛśyatvādiguṇakasya paravidyāviṣayatvarūpadharmokteḥ । na ca tasya paravidyāviṣayatvoktāvapi kuto viṣṇutvamiti vācyam । yatastat atamevam'; ityādinā taddharmatvenāvagatamiti । atra atamevam'; iti śrutau mokṣasādhanajñānaviṣayatvoktyā viṣṇoḥ paravidyāviṣayatvamuktaṃ bhavati । mokṣasādhanavidyāyā eva paravidyātvāt । tatkarmeti smṛtāvapi yaddharituṣṭikaraṃ tadeva karma । yayā atanmatiḥ'; hareḥ jñānaṃ bhavati, saiva vidyetyuktatvena tasya paravidyāviṣayatvamucyate । adve vidye veditavye'; ityatrāpi viṣṇoḥ paravidyāviṣayatvamucyate iti na hetuviśeṣaṇāsiddhiḥ । atheti prakaraṇārambhe । cau parasparasamuccaye । tathā ca parā cāparā ca dve vidye jñātavye । atatra'; parāparayormadhye aye vedāḥ'; ṛgādyāḥ yāni śikṣādiṣaḍaṅgāni ayānyupāṅgāni'; āyurvedagāndharvādīni । ayāni pratyaṅgāni'; śiṣṭāḥ kalā vidyāḥ sāparā । yo asau aadṛśyo'; dṛśyādanyo anirguṇaḥ'; sattvādihīnaḥ aparo'; vilakṣaṇaḥ aparamātmā'; svottamo vyāptaḥ sa hariryayā veditavyaḥ sā ṛgādirūpaiva pareti śrutyarthaḥ । yathaikasya karmaṇaḥ sakāmatvaniṣkāmatvarūpopādhibhedāt pravṛttinivṛttapadoditatvaṃ tathā viṣṇuviṣayakatvakarmādiviṣayakatvarūpopādhibhedādṛgādīnām eva parāparavidyātvopapattiriti bhāvaḥ । na cānuvyākhyāne brahmasūtrasya paravidyātvoktivirodhaḥ । anugrāhyatayā ṛgādīnāmanugrāhakatayā brahmasūtrasya ca paravidyātvopapatteḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। viśeṣaṇabhedavyapadeśābhyāṃ ca netarau ।।

taduktaṃ prakṛtiviriñcayoradṛśyatvādiguṇakatvamiti tatsiddhāntahetoḥ parapakṣanirāse api vyāpārāt taddharmokterityanenoktasya paravidyāviṣayatvasya viṣṇoranyatra niravakāśatvānyathānupapattyā nirākṛtamapi viśeṣayuktyā nirākurvatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe - viśeṣaṇeti ।। vyapadeśaśabda ubhayānvayītyāśayenobhayaśrutimāha - ya iti । abhedaḥ'; anyatvam । caśabdasya na kevalaṃ dharmokteḥ, arthāt kintu viśeṣaṇabhedavyapadeśābhyām iti samuccayārthatvasya spaṣṭatvānna tasyārtha uktaḥ । prakṛtiḥ viriñca ityanena itarā itaraśceti vigrahāśrayeṇetaraśabdārtho abhihitaḥ । ubhayatrādṛśyatvādiguṇaka ityanuṣajyate । prakṛtipakṣe liṅgavipariṇāmaḥ । tathā ca ayassarvajñaḥ'; iti vākye tasyādṛśyatvādiguṇakasya aviśeṣaṇāt'; sārvajñyādiviśeṣaṇokterna dṛśyatvādiguṇā jaḍaprakṛtiḥ । evaṃ atasmāt'; iti vākye viriñcasya tasmādakṣarājjanyatvarūpabhedakadharmoktyā bhedavyapadeśānnādṛśyatvādiguṇo viriñca iti yojanā ।

ayassarvajñassarvavidyasya jñānamayaṃ tapaḥ'; iti viśeṣaṇānna prakṛtiḥ । atasmādetadbrahma nāma rūpamannaṃ ca jāyate'; iti bhedavyapadeśānna viriñcaḥ ।

ātharvaṇe ayaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvavit'; ityataḥ pūrvavākye atapasā cīyate brahma'; ityatra parabrahmatapasā sambadhyata ityuktam । tat tapaśśabdasyālocanārthatayājñānapratītau tannirāsāya ayasya jñānamayaṃ tapaḥ'; iti vākyāntaraṃ pravṛttam । tasya yasya atapaḥ'; ālocanakriyā ajñānamayaṃ'; tadātmakameva na saṃśayādyātmakamityarthaḥ । kutastapasaḥ santāpānyapūrṇayathārthajñānātmakatvamityākāṅkṣāyāṃ tasya sarvajñatvādāptakāmatvāditi hetupradarśanāya ayassarvajñaḥ'; iti pūrvavākyopanyāsaḥ । tadarthastu - ayassarvajñaḥ'; sarvaviṣayakasāmānyajñānavān asarvavit'; sarvaviṣayakaviśeṣajñānavāṃśca । sarvasya labdhā sarvakāmaḥ sarvotpādakoveti । tattvapradīpe tu - vidasattāyāmiti dhātuvyākhyānāt sarvatra vidyate iti sarvavidityuktam । ayasya yaḥ'; iti yacchabdadvayasya atasmāt'; akṣarāt aetadbrahma'; caturmukhākhyaṃ anāma rūpamannaṃ'; tadabhimānidaivataṃ cotpadyata iti uttaravākyagatatacchabdenānvayaḥ ।

aparaṃ tvakṣaraṃ yā sā prakṛtirjaḍarūpikā ।
śrīḥ parā prakṛtiḥ proktā cetanā viṣṇusaṃśrayā ।।

tāmakṣaraṃ paraṃ prāhuḥ parataḥ paramakṣaram ।
harimevākhilaguṇamakṣaratrayamīritam ।।

iti skānde tryakṣarābhidhānādakṣarātparataḥ para ityapi viśeṣaṇameva ।

nanu na viṣṇoradṛśyatvādiguṇakatvaṃ, parataḥ parābhidhānenākṣaraśruteḥ tatra niravakāśatvādityato viśeṣaṇabhedavyapadeśāditi sūtrakhaṇḍasyārthāntaramāha - aparamiti ।। tuśabdo avadhāraṇe । aakṣaratrayam'; akṣarasya trayarm airitam'; akṣaraṃ trividhaṃ proktam iti yāvat । tisro vidhāḥ vyaktinirdeśapūrvakaṃ darśayati - aparamiti । yā yadaparamakṣaraṃ sā jaḍarūpikā prakṛtireva । yā yatparamakṣaraṃ aproktā'; proktaṃ vṛddhaistāṃ tat yā viṣṇusaṃśrayā parā uttamā cetanā prakṛtiḥ śrīḥ lakṣmīḥ tāṃ prāhuḥ । yatparataḥ paramakṣaramīritaṃ tajjaḍaprakṛteḥ parāchrītattvādakhilaguṇaṃ harimeva prāhuriti smṛtyarthaḥ । iti skānde ityasya atryakṣarābhidhānāt'; akṣaratraividhyasyoktatvādityanenānvayaḥ । akṣarātparataḥ para ityapīti । itivākyoktamakṣarātparataḥ paratvaṃ viruddhamiti vācyam । aaparam'; iti skānde tryakṣarābhidhānāt akṣarāntarātparādasyākṣarasya paratvopapatteriti yojanā । akṣaratrayābhidhānena akṣarātparataḥ para ityatra sāmānādhikaraṇyena vaiyadhikaraṇyena vā anvayo darśitaḥ । prameyadīpe tu - akṣarācchrītatvātparataḥ paro atyuttama iti tadbhāṣyadiśā śrutyartha uktaḥ । anenākṣarātparataḥ para ityapi tasyaiva viśeṣaṇaṃ, na tu anyasya । na cākṣarātparataḥ paratvaṃ viruddhamiti vācyam । bhedavyapadeśāt । aakṣaratrayamīritam'; ityakṣarāṇāmavāntarabhedokteḥ pāṇḍavasyārjunasya svādhamakārtavīryārjunādiva akṣarātparādakṣarāntarādasyākṣarasya paratvopapattiriti sūtrakhaṇḍasyārthāntaramuktaṃ bhavati ।

ajuṣṭaṃ yadā paśyatyanyamīśasya mahimānamiti vītaśokaḥ'; iti bhedavyapadeśādīśapadaprāpto api na rudraḥ ।।

nanu aanyam'; itiśabdaśravaṇādadṛśyatvādiguṇako rudraḥ kiṃ na syāditi śaṅkottaratayāpi bhedavyapadeśānnetara iti sūtrāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - juṣṭamiti ।। yadyapi tathāpītyarthe apiśabdaḥ । rudro apīti samuccaye vā । na kevalaṃ pūrvahetoḥ, kintu bhedavyapadeśādapīti samuccaye vā । rudra itītaraśabdasyārthāntaroktiḥ । na cetaraśabdasya jaḍaprakṛtiviriñcarudraparatve dvivacanānupapattiriti vācyam । viriñcirudrayoścetanatvenaikīkṛtatvāt । tathā ca yadyapīśaśabdādrudro apyadṛśyatvādiguṇakatvena aprāptaḥ'; pratītaḥ tathāpi ajuṣṭam'; iti vākye pravṛttaviṣṇvākhyākṣarasyeśaśabditarudrādanyatvavyapadeśādapi nādṛśyatvādiguṇako rudra iti yojanā । śrutistu - ānandamayādhikaraṇe vyākhyātā ।

sū - oṃ।। oṃ।।

ayadā paśyaḥ paśyate rukmavarṇaṃ kartāramīśaṃ puruṣaṃ brahmayonim'; iti ।

yuktyantareṇa viṣṇorevādṛśyatvādiguṇakatvaṃ sādhayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā tadupāttaśrutimevodāharati - rūpopanyāseti ।। iti rūpopanyāsādityanvayaḥ । sūtre caśabdo yuktisamuccaye । tathā ca - na kevalaṃ dharmokteḥ, kintvadṛśyatvādiguṇakasya ayadā'; iti śrutau śuddharukmarūpokteścādṛśyatvādiguṇako viṣṇureveti yojanā । atra yadeti vākyasya atadā vidvān puṇyapāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramaṃ sāmyamupaiti'; iti vākyaśeṣeṇānvayaḥ । paśyatīti paśyo draṣṭā jīvaḥ । yadā arukmavarṇaṃ'; śuddhahemavarṇaṃ abrahmayoniṃ'; hiraṇyagarabhakāraṇaṃ, ata eva jagataḥ kartāraṃ apuruṣaṃ'; pūrṇaṣaḍguṇam । asvasyeśaṃ'; viṣṇuṃ apaśyate'; paśyati tadāsau avidvān'; jīvanmuktaḥ apuṇyapāpe'; aprārabdhe aniṣṭapuṇyaṃ pāpaṃ ca vidhūya anirañjanaḥ'; jñānottaravikarmakṛtāśucitvādidoṣarahitaḥ añjanākhyāvidyārahita iti sudhokterajñānarahito vā aparamaṃ sāmyaṃ'; pūrṇānandatvādisāmyaṃ nirduḥkhatvādisāmyaṃ vā aupaiti'; prāpnotīti śrutyarthaḥ । tattvodyotaṭīkāyāṃ tu iyaṃ śrutiḥ muktaparatayā vyākhyātā । paramamityetadabhivyaktamiti ca vyākhyātam ।

aeko nārāyaṇa āsīnna brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ । sa munirbhūtvā samacintayat । tata ete vyajāyanta viśvo hiraṇyagarbho agniryamo varuṇarudrendrā iti । tasya haitasya paramasya nārāyaṇasya catvāri rūpāṇi śuklaṃ raktaṃ raukmaṃ kṛṣṇamiti । sa etānyetebhyo abhyacīkḷpat । vimiśrāṇi vyamiśrayat'; ।

nanu brahmādīnāmapi rūpasadbhāvātkuto rūpopanyāsenāsya viṣṇutvaniścaya ityata āha - eka iti ।। aidamagre'; ityupaskriyate । ata eva nyāyadīpikāyāṃ jagadādāvityuktam । hetyāsvādane । etebhya iti tādarthye caturthī । tathā ca idamasya jagato agre pralaye nārāyaṇaḥ aekaḥ'; svatantra āsīt । na tadā caturmukhaśaṅkarau, na svasvavyāpārāvāstām । asaḥ'; viṣṇustadā amuniḥ'; mananaśīlo maunī vā bhūtvā asamacintayat'; ete jāyantāmiti dhyānarūpāṃ cintāmakarot । atataḥ'; tasya cintanādete vyajāyanta । ke te? yo aviśvo'; vāyuḥ, yaśca hiraṇyagarbhaḥ, ye agnyādaya eta ityarthaḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha - atasya'; śrutyādiprasiddhasya aetasya'; sarvajīvaśarīragasya aparamasya'; sarvottamasya nārāyaṇasya arūpāṇi'; varṇāścatvāri bhavanti । kāni tāni? śuklādīni । kiñjātaḥ? asaḥ'; nārāyaṇaḥ pūrvameva avimiśrāṇi'; svena miśrīkṛtāni rūpāṇi aetebhyo'; vāyuprabhṛtyuktadevānāmarthe aabhyacākḷpat'; kḷptānyakarot । tāni vimiśrāṇi punarapi avyamiśrayat'; mānuṣādau viśeṣeṇa miśrīcakāra yadvā - sa etāni rūpāṇi vyamiśrayat, vimiśrāṇi caitebhyo abhyacīkḷpadityarthaḥ । śuddhāni rūpāṇi tu svasyaivākaroditi bhāvaḥ । atrādyayojanā tattvapradīpaṭīkayoruktā । dvitīyā tu ṭīkāyāmiti dhyeyam ।

ata etādṛgetadrūpamiti tasyaiva hi rūpāṇyabhidhīyante ।।
।। iti adṛśyatvādhikaraṇam ।।

tataḥ kimityata āha - ata iti ।। ato miśrīkaraṇāt tadrūpaṃ tasya viṣṇo rūpam aetādṛgeva'; śuddhaṃ śuklādisvarūpameva । na tu vāyvādirūpamiva miśramityarthaḥ । yadyapyatra atasya haitasya'; ityādikamevodāharaṇīyam, prakṛtopayuktatvāt, na tu aeko nārāyaṇaḥ'; ityādikam । tathāpi aetebhyaḥ'; ityasyārthasya pratyayārthaṃ tadaṃśodāharaṇaṃ kṛtam । itīti । ahi'; yasmāt iti udāhṛtavākyena arūpāṇi'; śuddharaukmādirūpāṇi tasya viṣṇoreva abhidhīyante, netareṣāṃ, tasmānnāprayojakatā śaṅkayetyarthaḥ । anena sūtre sāmānyenoktatve api rūpaśabdaḥ śuddharūpaparaḥ । adhyeyaḥ sadā'; iti sūrye pratītamapi miśrameveti liṅgasyānyatra niravakāśatvamuktaṃ bhavati ।। iti adṛśyatvādhikaraṇam ।।

।। vaiśvānarādhikaraṇam ।।

adṛśyatvādiguṇeṣu sarvagatatvaṃ ayastvetamevaṃ prādeśamātramabhivimānamātmānaṃ vaiśvānaramupāste'; iti vaiśvānarasyoktamiti ।।

atrādhikaraṇe pācakatvādyanekaliṅgasamanvayasiddhyarthaṃ brahmaṇi vaiśvānaranāmasamanvayaḥ kriyate । pūrvādhikaraṇasaṅagtiṃ viṣayavākyodāharaṇapūrvakaṃ viṣayādikaṃ sūcayati - adṛśyatvādīti ।। uktamityasyāvṛttiḥ śrutāviti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca - gatādhikaraṇodāhṛtamuṇḍakaśrutyuktādṛśyatvādiguṇeṣu madhye anityaṃ vibhuṃ sarvagatam'; ityanena yatsarvagatatvamuktaṃ tacchabdogaśrutau ayastvetam'; ityanena vaiśvānarasyoktamiti yojanā । anena chandogaśrutisthavaiśvānaraśabdasyānyaniṣṭhatvākṣepamukhena pūrvoktasarvagatatvāderanyaniṣṭhatvākṣepātpūrveṇāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । vaiśvānaro viṣayaḥ, viṣṇuranyo veti sandehaśca sūcitaḥ । śrutyarthastu - ayastu'; adhikārī aprādeśamātraṃ'; dehahṛdaye tāvatparimāṇakam । tattvapradīparītyādhikāryapekṣayā prādeśamātramiti vā । aabhivimānam'; abhito vigataṃ mānaṃ maryādā yasya taṃ, sarvagatam iti yāvat । aātmānam'; ātataguṇam aetaṃ'; śarīrasthaṃ avaiśvānaraṃ'; tadākhyaviṣṇum aevaṃ'; vakṣyamāṇarītyā upāste aso annamatti'; svayogyabhogyamanubhavatīti ।

ata āha - sū - oṃ।।
vaiśvānaraḥ sādhāraṇaśabdaviśeṣāt ।
।।
agnāviṣṇvoḥ sādhāraṇasya vaiśvānaraśabdasya viṣṇāveva prasiddhātmaśabdena viśeṣaṇādvaiśvānaro viṣṇureva ।।
