siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati - ata iti ।। sādhāraṇasyetyanantaramapīti śeṣaḥ । sādhāraṇyaṃ sāmyam । tatra śruternobhayatra prasiddhatvarūpaṃ, vaiśvānaraśabdasyānyatraiva prasiddhatvāt । kintu śruteḥ prasiddhato liṅgena sāmyarūpaṃ, tadapi niravakāśatvena prakāreṇa, vaiśvānaraśruteḥ viṣṇau prasiddhyabhāvena tatra niravakāśatvātpūrvoktasarvagatatvasyāpi viṣṇoranyatra niravakāśatvāt । tathā ca - yadyapi agnāviṣṇvoḥ pratijñāviṣayayoḥ satoḥ pūrvapakṣasādhakavaiśvānaraśabdo niravakāśatvena prakāreṇottarapakṣasādhakaliṅgasādhāraṇaḥ । śrutiliṅgayorniravakāśatvena sāmye api liṅgācchrutiḥ prabalā tasmādagnireveti prāptam । tathāpi sādhāraṇasyāpi vaiśvānaraśabdasya viṣṇvekaniṣṭhatayā śrutyādisiddhena aātmānaṃ vaiśvānaram'; ityātmaśabdena aviśeṣaṇāt'; viśeṣitatvādviṣṇuparatvasambhavāt । prasiddhyāderanyathopapannatvena nirṇayakāraṇābhāvācchabdaviśeṣādātmaśabdādvaiśvānaro viṣṇureva, ana devatābhūtaṃ ca'; ityāvṛttyā sūtrabhāṣyayoryojanā । anena nirṇayenaiva pūrvapakṣaḥ sūcitaḥ । atra pakṣe liṅgaprābalyanirāsāya sādhāraṇyoktiḥ । siddhāntaśruteḥ sāvakāśatvajñāpanāya sādhāraṇyoktiriti kecit । yadvā - bhāṣyaṭīkāsvārasyādanirṇayenaiva pūrvapakṣaḥ । atra pakṣe sādhāraṇyaṃ prati dharmitvaṃ śabdasyaiva, na liṅgasyāpi । naraśabdaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ sambhavadvṛttikaḥ । tathāpi prasiddhamukhena niravakāśatvena liṅgasya sādhāraṇaśca । tataḥ pūrvottarapakṣasādhakayoḥ samabalatvādanirṇayaḥ । tathāpyubhayatra sādhāraṇasyāpi vaiśvānaraśabdasyetyādikā yojanā draṣṭavyā ।

sū - oṃ।। smaryamāṇamanumānaṃ syāditi ।।

ahaṃ vaiśvānaro bhūtvā prāṇināṃ dehamāśritaḥ । iti smaryamāṇamatrāpi sa evocyate ityasyānumāpakam ।

nanvātmaśabdasyāgnyādiṣvamukhyatvābhyupagamena sāmānādhikaraṇyāvirodhātteṣāmeva vaiśvānaratvaṃ kiṃ na syādityāśaṅkāṃ parihartuṃ samākhyarūpahetvantareṇa vaiśvānarasya viṣṇutvaṃ niścāyayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe - smaryamāṇamiti ।। sūtrabhāṣyayoḥ asmaryamāṇam'; aahaṃ vaiśvānaro bhūtvā'; iti gītāsmṛtyuktaṃ viṣṇorvaiśvānaratvam aatra'; vaiśvānaravidyāyāmapi asaḥ'; gītokto bhagavāneva vaiśvānarapadena ucyate aityasya'; evaṃrūpasyārthasya aanumānam'; anumāpakaṃ asyāt'; bhavediti yojanā ।

samākhyānāt । itiśabdaḥ samākhyāpradarśakaḥ ।।

nanvahamiti viṣṇunā kṛṣṇenokteḥ smṛtyuktavaiśvānarasya viṣṇutve api atroktavaiśvānarasya kuto viṣṇutvamityata āha - samākhyānāditi ।। asyāḥ smṛteriti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca gītāsmṛteḥ vaiśvānaravidyāsamānoktirūpatvādasyāstatsamākhyānānniścayo bhavatītyarthaḥ । samākhyāyuktirna sūtroktetyata āha - iti śabda iti । apradarśakaḥ'; sūcakaḥ । tathā ca - itismaryamāṇamityasya itisamākhyāyamānamityarthābhyupagamāditiśabdaḥ samānoktirūpasamākhyālakṣaṇaliṅgajñāpaka iti bhāvaḥ । atra sūtresamākhyārūpahetvantaroktāvapi tasyātmaśabdākhyapūrvahetoraniścāyakatvaśaṅkāmukhena tannirāsāya pravṛttatvāccaśabdābhāvaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। śabdādibhyo antaḥpratiṣṭhānānneti cenna tathā dṛṣṭyupadeśādasambhavātpuruṣavidhamapi cainamadhīyate ।।

aayamagnirvaiśvānaraḥ'; avaiśvānaramṛta ājātamagnim'; ityādiśabdaḥ । avaiśvānare taddhutaṃ bhavati'; ahṛdayaṃ gārhapatyo mano anvāhāryapacana āsyamāhavanīyaḥ'; ityādyagniliṅgamādiśabdoktam । ayenedamannaṃ pacyate'; atadyadbhaktaṃ prathamamāgacchettaddhomīyam'; ityādinā pācakatvenāntaḥpratiṣṭhānaṃ ca pratīyate । tasmānna viṣṇuriti cet - 

vaiśvānarasya viṣṇutvamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasya ākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - śabdādibhya iti ।। aayamagnirvaiśvānaro yo ayamantaḥpuruṣe'; iti bṛhadāraṇyakavākyam amūrdhānaṃ divo aratiṃ pṛthivyāṃ vaiśvānarama-ta ājātamagnim । kaviṃ saṃrājamatithiṃ janānāmāsannā pātraṃ janayanta devāḥ ।।'; iti ṛgvedavākyam । ityādīti karmadhārayaḥ । tathā ca ityādirūpaḥ śabdaḥ sautraśabdapadenokta ityarthaḥ । yadvā - aityādi'; evamādivākyajātaṃ aśabdaḥ'; sautraśabdapadena gṛhīta ityarthaḥ । ādiśabdenaitajjātīyakaṃ śrutyantaravākyaṃ gṛhyate । avaiśvānare'; iti śrutyantaravākyam । hṛdayamityādichandogaśrutiḥ । ityādyagniliṅgamiti । evamādivākyoktāgniliṅgamityarthaḥ । ādiśabdena anābhiṃ yajñānāṃ sadanaṃ rayīṇām'; ityādivākyoktāni gṛhyante । aādiśabdoktaṃ'; sautrādiśabdoktamityarthaḥ । ayenedamannaṃ pacyate yadidamadyate'; ityetadapi aayamagnirvaiśvānaro yo ayamantaḥ puruṣe'; ityataḥ paraṃ bṛhadāraṇyakaśrutam । atadyadbhaktam'; iti chandogyavākyam । ityādineti । kurupāṇḍavanyāyena asarvakarmā sarvaliṅgaḥ'; iti śrutyanusārādādipadoktaliṅgātpārthakyena karma bodhayituṃ sūtre antaḥpratiṣṭhānādityuktam । yadvā - apācakatvenāntaḥpratiṣṭhānaṃ pradhānaliṅgatvenābhimatatvātpṛthaguktam'; iti tattvapradīpokteḥ pradhānaliṅgatvādidaṃ pṛthaguktamityabhipretya talliṅgaṃ tatkarmoktyā darśayati pācakatveneti । itthaṃbhūtalakṣaṇe tṛtīyā । anena sūtre antaḥpratiṣṭhānapadena na kevalaṃ tattaddhṛdayāntaravasthānamātraṃ vivakṣitaṃ, kintu savyāpāramityuktaṃ bhavati । ata eva ayenedamannaṃ pacyate'; atadyadbhaktam'; ityubhayabodhakaśrutyudāharaṇam । tataḥ kimityata āha - tasmāditi ।। yasmādevamagnipakṣe api śrutiliṅgādyasti, viṣṇupakṣe tu tvayaivātmaśabdaḥ samākhyānaṃ coktam, tasmādubhayatra śrutyādisāmyādvaiśvānaro viṣṇureveti niścayo na yujyate ityarthaḥ । nanu ayastvetam'; iti vicāryavākye vaiśvānaraśabdasamānādhikṛtāgniśabdābhāvādvākyāntaragatāgniśabdasya kathaṃ śaṅkāhetutvamiti cet - na, atra sarvavaiśvānaravidyānāṃ vicāryatvāt, ata evānekavākyoddhāraḥ । yadvā - pūrvapakṣe api siddhānta iva samākhyāṃ pradarśayituṃ samākhyārūpeṇa tattadvākyoddhāro yuktaḥ । ayamiti vākye ayamityuktaḥ ka ityata āha - yo ayamiti ।। tathā ca - ayo ayamantaḥ puruṣe'; puruṣasyāntaḥsthito bhagavān ayamagniḥ aṅgaśabditaśarīranetṛtvāttacchabdavācyaḥ । viśvaguṇasambandhī narīyate ceti vaiśvānaraśceti yojanā । tadvyāpāramāha - yeneti idaṃ kimityata āha - yadidamiti । adyate bhakṣyate prāṇibhiḥ । amūrdhānam'; iti mantre ṣaṣṭhyarthaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvasambandhaḥ । amūrdhatvaṃ viṣṇoraṅgāṅgyabhedāt'; iti tattvapradīpokteḥ mūrdhānamaratimityabhedoktiḥ । ṛtāyeti vedāntare pāṭhādṛci ṛta iti saptamī tādarthye । tathā ca divaḥ kāraṇabhūtamūrdhānaṃ loke gamanenāratidarśanāt rativiruddhagatisādhanatvādgauṇyā vṛttyā aaramalamatati gacchati yena puruṣaḥ so aratiḥ pādaḥ'; iti tattvapradīpokteḥ mukhyayā vṛttyā aratiḥ pādaḥ । ṛgatāvityasmātkaraṇe atipratyaye niṣpanno aratiśabdaḥ pāde mukhya evetyapi kecit । tattu tattvapradīpacandrikānuktam । tattvapradīpe araśabdopapadādatateḥ, candrikāyāṃ nañupapadādramerasya niṣpatteruktatvāt । tathā ca - pṛthivyāḥ aratiṃ kāraṇībhūtapādaṃ janānām āṛte samyagjñānāya ajātam'; abhivyaktaṃ akaviṃ'; sarvajñaṃ asamrājam'; akhaṇḍeśam aannaṃ tham'; iti śruteḥthaśabdo annavācī । tathā ca aatithim'; atyannam । pātramityanenāpi janānāmityetatsambadhyate । tathā ca janānāṃ apātāraṃ'; rakṣakaṃ avaiśvānaraṃ'; viśvajīvāntaratvayogena tacchabdavācyam aagnim'; aṅganetāraṃ viṣṇuṃ prasiddhaṃ ca devā āsan । avibhaktiko ayaṃ nirdeśaḥ । āsyaśabdasyāsannādeśaḥ । tathā ca āsan svāsyatayā ājanayanta । aḍabhāvaśchāndasaḥ । āsamantātsarvakarmasvakurvanniti siddhāntarītyā śrutyarthaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu - viśvanarastham ṛte vede aā samantājjātaṃ'; vyaktam aagnim'; aṅganetāraṃ asaṃrājaṃ'; samyagrājantam aatithiṃ'; sarvānatiśayya sthitaṃ pātāram agniṃ janānām aāsan'; āśrayam ājanayanta āsamantājjanayāṃcakruḥ । agnyādidevā iti viśeṣārtha uktaḥ । kecittu - janibādhakāṅyogādājanayanta akurvannityuktamityāhuḥ । tattūdāhṛtatattvapradīpaviruddham । ato anekārthatvāddhātūnāṃ viṣṇujanye agnau devajanyatvāyogāt janerutpattyarthāyogācca akurvannityuktamiti āṅviśleṣeṇaiva ṭīkā vyākhyeyā । pūrvapakṣī tu śrutigatāgnyādiśabdānprasiddhāgniparāneva manyate । avaiśvānare taddhutam'; iti vākyārthastu - atasmāduhaivaṃ vidyadyapi caṇḍālayocchiṣṭaṃ prayacchedātmani haivāsya vaiśvānare hutaṃ syāt'; iti chandogasamākhyāvākyādavagantavyaḥ । tadarthastu - yadi aevaṃvit'; uktarītyā vaiśvānarajñānī ucchiṣṭādyanarhāyāpi caṇḍālāyocchiṣṭaṃ aprayacchet'; dadyāt । tadā taddattamucchiṣṭaṃ caṇḍālāntaryāmiṇi vaiśvānare hutaṃ syānna pāpakaraṃ bhavati । pratyuta mahāphalameveti । anenāhutisthānatvaliṅagamucyate । ahṛdayaṃ'; hṛdayastho viṣṇurgārhapatyapadavācya ityarthaḥ । aanvāhāryapacano'; dakṣiṇāgniranvāhārya odano atra pacyata iti vyutpatti sambhavāt । pūrvapakṣe tu garhapatyaṃ vaiśvānarasya prasiddhāgnerhṛdayasthānīyamityādirarthaḥ । atadyadbhaktam'; iti vākyārthastu - atat'; tadā bhojanavelāyāṃ ayadyadbhaktam'; annaṃ aprathamamāgacchet'; āsyaṃ prati prāṇāhutirūpeṇa । ataddhomīyaṃ'; pācakatvenāntaḥsthitasyāgnerhemadravyamiti । anenāgnau hūyamānadravyasyāgniḥ pācaka iti siddhamiti pācakatvākhyaliṅgamuktaṃ bhavati । yadyapi ayenedam'; iti pūrvavākye aayamagniḥ'; iti tatpūrvavākyasāhityāt pācakatvenāntaḥpratiṣṭhānoktāvapi na atadyadbhaktam'; iti vākye tatpratīyate । tathāpi ataddhomīyam'; ityanenāntassthitasya homyamityuktatvāttatpratyāyakatvopapattiḥ ।

na, aatha hemamātmānamaṇoraṇīyāṃsaṃ parataḥ paraṃ viśvaṃ harimupāsīteti । sarvanāmā sarvakarmā sarvaliṅgaḥ sarvaguṇaḥ sarvakāmaḥ sarvadharmaḥ sarvarūpa iti'; ।

parihārasūtrāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - neti ।। tasmānna viṣṇuriti pūrvavākyenāsya nañarthasyānvayaḥ । kuto netyatastatra bhāṣye atasmādityuktam'; ityāvṛttyā hetutvena saṃyojyam । sūtretu ata ityākarṣaṇīyam । ātmaśabdādipūrvahetoreveti tadarthaḥ । na cetaratrāpyasti śrutyādikamityanirṇayaḥ । teṣāmanyatra mukhyato yogena viṣṇāveva sāvakāśatvopapatterityadhyāhāraḥ । kuto agnyādināmakarmaṇāṃ viṣṇāveva sāvakāśatvaṃ jñāyata ityatastatra hetusamarpakaṃ atathādṛṣṭyupadeśāt'; ityaṃśam upadeśapadoktaśrutyudāharaṇapūrvakaṃ vyācaṣṭe - atheti । prakaraṇāntarārambhārtho ayamathaśabdaḥ। prathametiśabdo vidhisamāptau । dvitīyasya ityupāsītetyanvayaḥ । tathā ca aetamātmānam'; ādānādikartāram aaṇoraṇīyāṃsaṃ'; sūkṣmādapi sūkṣmaṃ aparato'; mahataḥ paraṃ aviśvaṃ'; pūrṇaṃ harimupāsītetyarthaḥ । kimitītyataḥ upāsanāprakāramāha - sarveti । itiśabdaḥ pratyekaṃ sambadhyate । tathā ca mukhyataḥ indrādisarvanāmavānityupāsīta । asarvakarmā'; anar te tvatkriyate'; ityādeḥ svātantryeṇa sarvakriyākartetyupāsīta। liṅgaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ, vajradharatvādisarvaliṅga ityupāsīta। jñānānandādisarvaguṇapūrṇa ityupāsīta । etadicchayaiva sarvaṃ bhavatīti sarvakāmaḥ pūrṇakāma ityupāsīta । bhedasaṃyogavibhāgādisarvadharmāstadadhīnā iti vā, sarvajñatvādisarvadharmavatvādvā sarvadharma ityupāsīta । sarvatra rūpamasya iti vā sarvaṃ jagadasya rūpaṃ pratimeti vā sarvarūpa ityupāsīta ।

asa ya etamevamātmānaṃ viśvaṃ harimārādaramupāste tasya sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu deveṣu sarveṣu vedeṣu kāmacāro bhavati'; iti tattannāmaliṅgādinā tasyaiva dṛṣṭyupadeśānmahopaniṣadi ।।

evamupāsakasya phalamāha - sa iti ।। asaḥ'; prasiddhaḥ yo adhikārī etamātmānam aṇoraṇīyāṃsaṃ parataḥparameva viśvaṃ harimeva, nānyam, aārāt'; samīpe svahṛdaye aaram'; alaṃ samyagupāste tasyaivamavyāpte vyāptarūpopāsakasya sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu abhūteṣu'; prāṇiṣu sarveṣu lokeṣu sthiteṣu bhūteṣviti vā । vedeṣu sarveṣu, vedeṣu yatheṣṭasañcāraḥ kāmasañcaraṇasarvapūjyatvasarvajñatvādiḥ syāt ityarthaḥ tattvapradīpe abhihitaḥ । aiti'; mahopaniṣadītyanvayaḥ । sautratathāśabdārthamāha - tattaditi । agnyādināmaliṅgādimattvenetyarthaḥ । ādipadena tattatkarmādergrahaṇam । pradhānasūtre abhihitaṃ tattvityetadatrāpi vipariṇāmena saṃyojyamityāśayenāha - tasyaiveti । na tvagnyāderityevārthaḥ । adṛṣṭyupadeśāt'; upāsanopadeśāt । śrutau harimeva upāsta ityavadhāraṇenānyavyāvṛttyavagamāditi bhāvaḥ ।

anāttatvādanātmāna ūnatvādguṇarāśitaḥ । abrahmāṇaḥ pare sarve brahmātmā viṣṇureva hi । ityādinā, ako na ātmā kiṃ brahma'; ityārambhācca anyeṣāmasambhavāt viṣṇureva vaiśvānaraḥ ।

evamanyaśrutiliṅgadīnāṃ viṣṇau sāvakāśatvopapādakatayā tathetyaṃśaṃ vyākhyāya ātmaśabdāderanyatra niravakāśoktiparatayāsambhavādityaṃśaṃ pramāṇodāharaṇapūrvakaṃ vyākhyāti - anāttatvāditi ।। yojanātu - ityādinā pramāṇena viṣṇoranyeṣām ātmatvabrahmatvāsambhavokteḥ ata eva ātmaśabdāderanyatrāsambhavāditi । yadvā - na kevalamātmaśabdaśrutisamākhyābhyāṃ, kintu prakaraṇabalācca vaiśvānarasya viṣṇutvaniścayo bhavatītyāha - anāttatvāditi । ādiśabdena abrahmaśabdaḥ pare viṣṇau'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । tathācetthaṃ yojanā - ako na ātmā kiṃ brahma'; aityārambhācca'; ityārabhyādhītātprakaraṇācca viṣṇureva vaiśvānaraḥ । brahmātmaśabdayoretadupakrame śravaṇe api kuto asyāḥ vaiśvānaravidyāyāḥ viṣṇuprakaraṇatvam? aanāttatvāt'; ityādinā pramāṇena viṣṇoranyeṣāmātmaśabdārthavyāptatvaguṇapūrṇatvayorasambhavāvagamāditi । anena sūtre ārambhāditi padamadhyāhṛtya tenāpiśabdaḥ saṃyojyaḥ । asambhavāditi hetustu ātmaśabdāderanyatrānavakāśatvasādhakatayobhayatra saṃyojyaḥ ityuktaṃ bhavati । ata eva bhāṣye agniśrutyādīnāṃ viṣṇau sāvakāśatvasādhakatayetyādivyākhyānantaraṃ viṣṇupakṣasādhakātmaśabdāderanyatrānavakāśatvasādhakāsambhavāditi hetau vyākhyātavye api tadvihāyārambhādityadhyāhṛtahetūpanyātrāstyavakāśa iti pratijñāya prakaraṇabalāccetyadhyāhāryahetuṃ ca pradarśya, anantaramātmaśabdaprakaraṇayorniravakāśatvasādhakāsambhavādityaṃśo vyākhyātaḥ । tathādṛṣṭyupadeśādasambhavāditivat nādhyāhṛtahetoravāntarasādhyenānvayaḥ, kintu pradhānenaiveti jñāpanāya viṣṇureva vaiśvānara iti punaruktiḥ । uddeśyavidheyanirdeśasyaicchikatvādvyatyāsaḥ । ahi'; yasmādviṣṇoḥ apare'; anye guṇaiḥ aanāttatvāt'; avyāptatvāt sarvotkṛṣṭatvena vaidikairasvīkṛtatvādvā aanātmānaḥ'; anātmaśabdamukhyārthāḥ । yasmācca guṇarāśita ūnatvādabrahmāṇaśca । tasmāt abrahmātmā'; tacchabdamukhyavācyo viṣṇureva siddha ityarthaḥ । chāndogye hi ako na ātmā kiṃ brahma'; iti militvā mīmāṃsamānaiḥ pratyabdayajñakṛttvanimittānmahāśālasaṃjñaiḥ pañcabhirmahāmunibhiḥ uddālakoddiṣṭaistadyuktaiḥ paripṛṣṭo rājāśvapatirvaiśvānaramupadideśa । anaḥ'; asmākam upāsya ātmā akaḥ'; kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ । brahma ca akiṃ'; kiṃlakṣaṇamityarthaḥ ।

acandramā manaso jātaḥ । cakṣossūryo ajāyata'; ityādinā yaḥ puruṣākhyo viṣṇubhihitastadvidhamevātra amūrdhaiva sutejāścakṣurviśvarūpaḥ prāṇaḥ pṛthagvartmā'; ityādinā enaṃ vaiśvānaramadhīyate ।।

śrutisamākhyayā ca vaiśvānarasya viṣṇutvamupapādayituṃ pravṛttaṃ apuruṣavidhamapyenamadhīyate'; ityaṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - candramā iti ।। atra acandramāḥ'; iti vākyaṃ pratīkatvena gṛhītam । udāharaṇavākyaṃ tu acakṣossūryo ajāyata'; itīti dhyeyam । prathamādipadena aśīrṣṇodyaussamavartata, prāṇādvāyurajāyata, padbhyāṃ bhūmiḥ', ityādikaṃ dvitīyādipadena asandoho bahulo vastireva rayiḥ pṛthivyeva pādau'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । etamityasya vyākhyānaṃ - vaiśvānaramiti । tathā ca - yasmātpuruṣasūkte aśīrṣṇodyaussamavartata, cakṣossūryo ajāyata'; ityādinā śabdena yaḥ puruṣākhyo viṣṇuḥ yadvidho dyubhvādijanakaśīrṣādimānabhihitaḥ, tadvidhameva dyubhvādijanakaśīrṣādimattvaprakāropetamevātra chāndogye amūrdhaiva sutejāḥ'; ityādinā vākyenainaṃ vaiśvānaramadhīyate chandogāḥ tasmātpuruṣasūktasamākhyayāpi vaiśvānaro viṣṇureveti yojanā ।

caśabdena sakalavedatantrapurāṇādiṣu viṣṇuparatvaṃ puruṣasūktasya darśayati ।

nanu puruṣasūktasya viṣṇuparatve bhavettatsamākhyayā etadvidyāyā viṣṇuparatvaṃ, tadeva kuta ityata āha - caśabdeneti ।। śruterādhikyātprathamaṃ pratijñā । apuruṣasūktasya'; ityanantaraṃ aprasiddhamiti'; śeṣaḥ । adarśayati'; sūcayati sūtrakāra ityarthaḥ । ātmaśabdasmṛtisamākhyāprakaraṇasamuccayasyeva prakaraṇaśrutisamuccayasyāpi apipadenaiva siddhatvānna tatropakṣīṇaścaśabda iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tathā ca brāhme - yathaiva pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ nityaṃ viṣṇuparāyaṇam । tathaiva me mano nityaṃ bhūyādviṣṇuparāyaṇam ।।

kiṃ tadvedādītyataśśruteḥ sākṣātpratijñātārthāsādhakatvātpratijñākramamatikramya sākṣātpratijñātārthasādhakatvādādau purāṇavākyaṃ paṭhati - tathā ceti ।। sūtre puruṣasūktasya viṣṇuparatvaṃ siddhamiti yathoktaṃ tathā brāhme coktamityarthaḥ । evam uttaratrāpi auktam'; iti padādhyāhāreṇa saptamyantapadānāmanvayo draṣṭavyaḥ । anityaṃ'; niyamena aviṣṇuparāyaṇaṃ'; viṣṇau mahātātparyavat । dvitīyasya nityamityasya sadetyarthaḥ । aiti brāhma iti'; iti śabdānvayaḥ siddhārthasyaiva dṛṣṭāntatvādanena brāhmavacanena vivakṣitārtho jñāyate ।।

caturvedaśikhāyāṃ ca - sahasraśīrṣā puruṣassahasrākṣassahasrapāt । iti eṣa hyaivācintyaḥ paraḥ paramo harirādiranādirananto anantaśīrṣo anantākṣo anantabāhuranantaguṇo anantarūpa iti ।

pratijñātāṃ śrutiṃ darśayituṃ prathamameva tatsthānamāha - caturvedaśikhāyāṃ ceti ।। atra caturvedaśikhāśrutiḥ asahasra'; ityārabhya asahasrapāt'; ityantena puruṣasūktamupanyasya aeṣahyeva'; ityanena asahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ'; ityukto harireva nānya ityetatsūktaṃ viṣṇuparatayā vyākhyātīti prakṛtasaṅgatiḥ । supa ākāro vaidikaḥ । eṣaḥ ka ityato yaḥ aparo'; vilakṣaṇaḥ ata eva aacintyo'; manasā aparamaḥ'; uttamaḥ aādiḥ'; kāraṇabhūtaḥ aanādiḥ'; utpattiśūnyaḥ aanantaḥ'; nāśaśūnyaḥ, svarūpato aparicchinno vā hariḥ sa ityāha । kutaḥ ayaṃ puruṣaḥ sahasraśīrṣā? ahi'; yasmādanantaśīrṣā । kutaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ? yasmādayamanantākṣaḥ । kutaḥ ayaṃ sahasrapāt? yasmādanantabāhuḥ । anantapādityasyāpyupalakṣakametat । evaṃ pūrvavākye api asa bhūmim'; ityuttaravākyepyupapādakamāha - anantaguṇo anantarūpo anantākāra iti । caturvedaśikhāyāmityanvayaḥ ।

bṛhatsaṃhitāyāṃ ca - yathā hi pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ viṣṇorevābhidhāyakam । na tathā sarvavedāśca vedāṅgāni ca nārada ।।

brāhmavākyasya puruṣasūktasya lakṣaṇayā viṣṇuparatve anyaparatve api vā sāvakāśatvānnatatpratijñātārthaniścāyakamityato vyākhyānavyākheyabhāvākhyadvāramantareṇa puruṣasūktaṃ mukhyato viṣṇorevābhidhāyakamiti sākṣātpratijñātārthasādhakaṃ smṛtivākyaṃ tatsthānanirdeśapūrvakaṃ paṭhati - bṛhatsaṃhitāyāṃ ceti । cakāraḥ pūrvasamuccayārthaḥ । avedāṅgāni'; śikṣādīni brahmavākyametat । bṛhatsaṃhitāyāmuktamityanvayaḥ । ādipadena asarvataḥ pauruṣe sūkte guṇā viṣṇorudīritāḥ'; iti brahmatarkādigrahaṇam । asarvataḥ'; sarve guṇāḥ । sarvasmin, sarvasmāt vedatadaṅgebhyo atiśayeneti vā ।

yasmādyajjāyate cāṅgāllokavedādikaṃ hareḥ ।
tannāmavācyamaṅgaṃ tadyathā brahmādikaṃ mukham ।।

iti nāradīyavacanānnābhedoktivirodhaḥ ।।

nanu puruṣasūkte dyubhvādijanakaśīrṣādimatvaṃ puruṣasyocyate । vaiśvānaravidyāyāṃ tu vaiśvānarasya tadabheda ucyate । tadubhayorviruddhārthatvānneyaṃ samākhyetyata āha - yasmāditi ।। alokaḥ'; svargādiḥ avedaḥ'; ṛgādiḥ । yadyapi nātra chāndogye vedābheda ucyate iti na tadgatirvaktavyā । tathāpi śrutyantaragatābhedavākyārthanirṇayāyāyamaṃśaḥ pravṛttaḥ। yadvā - vedaśabdena aura eva vediḥ'; ityuktā vedirgṛhyate । atṛtīyo atiśaye'; ityuktatvāt । avedyādikam'; iti pāṭhaḥ svarasaḥ । tathā ca yasmādyasmāt hareraṅgāt yadyat lokavedādikaṃ jāyate, yadāśritya tiṣṭhati, yatra līyate ca tajjanakamaṅgaṃ tasmāt atannāmavācyaṃ'; tasya lokāderyannāma vācakaśabdaḥ tena mukhyavācyaṃ bhavati । ata eva tadabhinnatvena pratīyate ca । na tāvatā tayorabhedo mantavya ityarthaḥ । atra dṛṣṭāntamāha - yatheti । mukhamityupalakṣaṇam । tathā ca - bhagavanmukhādirbrāhmaṇādijātijanakatvāt brāhmaṇādināmnocyate abrāhmaṇo asya mukhamāsīt'; ityādau । ata eva tadabhinnatvena pratīyate ca sāmānādhikaraṇyāt । tadvadrāpītyarthaḥ । na hyatra puruṣottamamukhādibhirabhedo brāhmaṇādīnāmucyate, apadbhyāṃ śūdro ajāyata'; ityuttaravākyavirodhāt । iti vacanādityuktatvādvaiśvānarāṅgānāṃ amūrdhaiva'; iti lokādyabhedoktinimitto virodho netyarthaḥ । abhedapratyāyakoktestajjanyajanakabhāvavivakṣāpūrvakatvāditi bhāvaḥ । anena bhagavato mūrdhā sutejastvādiguṇayogātsutejaḥśabditasvargajanakatvāt sutejā ityucyate । evaṃ acakṣurviśvarūpaḥ'; sarvaprakāśakatvaguṇayogāt viśvarūpaśabditasūryajanakatvāttacchabdenocyate । aprāṇaḥ pṛthagvartmātmā'; vāyujanakatvāttacchabdita iti śrutyarthassūcitaḥ । ātmaśabdaḥ svarūpārtho madhyadehārtho vā । chāndogyabhāṣye tu - amūrdhā viṣṇośśiraḥ svargādhāraṃ dyunāmakam'; atitejasā suptejonāmakaṃ ca । viśvāni rūpāṇi viṣayatvena yasyeti vigrahāśrayeṇa sarvarūpātidarśanāt cakṣurviśvarūpākhyam । evaṃ viṣṇoḥ prāṇo nṛsiṃhākhyo vāyvādiprāṇaśakyaṃ yanna bhavati tasya pṛthagvartmātmā pṛthagvilakṣaṇo mārgo yasya sa cāsāvātmā ceti, iti nimittāntareṇa śrutirvyākhyātā । evaṃ bahularayipṛthivīśabditākāśavārivasundharādevatājanakatvāt sandohavastipādapadoktāni madhyadehakaṭiprapadarūpāṇi bhagavato vaiśvānarasyāṅgāni tattacchabdavācyānītyapi jñātavyam । anena aśabdādibhyaḥ'; agnyādiśruteḥ gārhapatyādyaṅgavatvādiliṅgācca pācakatvenāntaḥpratiṣṭhānācca vaiśvānaro viṣṇureveti niścayo na yujyata iti cet - na, anyaśrutiliṅgādīnāṃ viṣṇau sāvakāśatvena ātmaśabdādereva niścayopapatteḥ । kutaḥ sāvakāśatvam? atathādṛṣṭyupadeśāt a; agnyādināmaliṅgakarmavatvena viṣṇorupāsanopadeśāt । na cātmaśabdāderanyatrāstyavakāśaḥ, anyatrātmatvāderasambhavāt । na kevalamātmaśabdasmṛtisamākhyānādvaiśvānaro viṣṇureveti niścayaḥ, api tu ārambhācca prakaraṇabalācca। na ca vaiśvānaravidyāyā viṣṇuprakaraṇatvasiddhiḥ, ako na ātmā kiṃ brahma'; iti vicārapūrvakamasyārabhyādhītatvāt। na cātmatvabrahmatvopakrame api kuto asya viṣṇuparatā, ātmatvabrahmatvādīnāmagnyādāvasambhavāt । na kevalaṃ smṛtisamākhyāprakaraṇabalādvaiśvānaro viṣṇureveti niścīyate, kintu yataḥ puruṣasūkte puruṣo yadvidho abhihitaḥ tadvidhamevainaṃ viṣṇuṃ amūrdhaiva'; ityādinādhīyate chandogāḥ । ataḥ śrutisamākhyānādapi caśabdaḥ puruṣasūktasya viṣṇuparatvaṃ bahupramāṇasiddhamiti dyotayatīti sūtravṛttirdarśitā bhavati ।

sū - oṃ।। ata eva na devatā bhūtaṃ ca । 
।।
agnivaiśvānarādiśabdastejasi bhūte agnidevatāyāṃ ca prasiddho apyataḥ pūrvoktahetuta evātra na sā taccābhidhīyate ।।

nanu vaiśvānaraśabdasya devatābhūtayoḥ prasiddhatvādatrāpyasau tatparaḥ kiṃ na syādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasyati - ata eveti ।। atra caśabdasya samuccayārthatvaṃ yadyapi tathāpītyarthatvaṃ cāśritya sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe - agnīti । samudāyaikavacanametat । ādiśabdena jātaveda ādiśabdo gṛhyate । vidyāntaropalakṣaṇayāgniśabdādiśabdayorgrahaṇam । na cāgnyādītyanenaivopalakṣaṇasambhavātkiṃ śabdadvayagrahaṇeneti vācyam । vaiśvānaraśabdasyeha vicāryatvena atiprasiddhatvādagniśabdasya ca grahaṇopapatteḥ । yadvā - ādiśabdasyobhayatrānvayena agnyādīti ādhibhautikavidyāntarasya vaiśvānarādītyādhyātmikavidyāntarasyopalakṣaṇārthamagnyādivaiśvānarādigrahaṇam । atejasi bhūte'; iti sāmānādhikaraṇyam । caḥ samuccaye aprasiddhaḥ'; ityanena pūrvapakṣe prasiddhatvāditi yuktiḥ sūcitā । sautramataḥśabdamanūdya vyākhyāti - ata iti । pūrvokteti । ātmaśabdāditihetuta ityarthaḥ । na tatra hetvantaraṃ gaveṣaṇīyamityevārthaḥ । aatra'; vaiśvānaravidyāyāṃ vidyāntare ca asā'; agnidevatā atat'; tejobhūtaṃ prasiddhiprādhānyābhyāṃ nirdeśavyatyāsaḥ । caśabdaḥ samuccaye । abhidhīyate atena'; iti śeṣaḥ । vaiśvānarādiśabdeneti tadarthaḥ । aatra'; iti pāṭhābhāve tadapyadhyāhāryam ।

sū - oṃ।। sākṣādapyavirodhaṃ jaiminiḥ ।।

nāgnyādayaḥ śabdā agnyādivācakāstathāpi sākṣādevānanyayogena brahmavācakaiśśabdaiḥ vyavahārārthamanabhijñānācca anyatra vyavaharantītyabhyupagame avirodhaṃ jaiminirvakti ।

nanu loke vede ca agnyādipadānārm iśādanyatra vyavahāraprasiddhidarśanāt tasya ca kāraṇāntarābhāvāttadanyathānupapattyānyeṣāṃ vāṭcvamaṅgīkāryam । anyathā tadvirodhaḥ syādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe - sākṣāditi ।। atra tathāpītyapiśabdavyākhyānādyadyapīti labhyate । agniśabdaḥ svaparaḥ । agniśabda eva ādiryeṣāṃ te agnyādaya iti vigrahaḥ । apiravadhāraṇe apītyāśayena sākṣādevetyuktam । arthāntarāvyavadhānenetyarthaḥ । phalitārthamāha - ananyeti ।। śakyarūpānyasambandhamantareṇa mukhyavṛttyetyarthaḥ । yadvā - tattvapradīparītyānyatra yogavṛttyabhāvena brahmaṇi samyagyogenetyarthaḥ । brahmavācakairapītyapiśabdānvayaḥ । atairagnyādiśabdaiḥ'; iti śeṣaḥ । avyavahārārthaṃ'; hānādivyavahārasiddhyarthaṃ aanabhijñānāt'; mukhyavācyajñānābhāvāt । caśabdo na kevalaṃ vyavahārārthaṃ kintvanabhijñānācceti samuccaye । aanyatra'; agnyādiṣu tān tatra vyavaharanti jñānino ajñāninaśceti krameṇa śeṣaḥ । aityabhyupagame'; iti nimittasaptamī । evamaṅgīkārāt aavaridhaṃ'; jñānyajñānivyavahāravirodhābhāvaṃ jaiminirācāryo vaktītyarthaḥ । ayatnānavasaraḥ'; ityuktervaktītyuktam । anenāgnyādiśabdāḥ nāgnyādivācakāḥ, kintu brahmavācakā eva। tathāpi nānyatra prasiddhivirodhaḥ । na vānyathānupapatyānyeṣāṃ vācyatvaṃ kalpyam । kutaḥ? yato vācyārthadhīvyavahitaṃ lakṣaṇādikaṃ vinā sākṣānmukhyavṛttyāpi brahmavācakānagnyādiśabdān mukhyārthajñāninaḥ ajāmilacaramatanaye nārāyaṇaśabdamiva hānādisiddhyarthaṃ tadajñāninastvanabhijñānādeva tān jvalanādiṣu vyavaharantītyabhyupagamenānyatrāvirodhaṃ vyavahāravirodhābhāvaṃ prasiddhivilopābhāvaṃ vaktyasya iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।।

vyāsacittasthitākāśādavacchinnāni kānicit ।
anye vyavaharantyetānyūrīkṛtya gṛhādivat ।।

iti skāndavacanānna matānāṃ parasparavirodhaḥ ।।

nanu jaiminyādimatānāṃ bhagavanmatāvirodhitve jaiminyādigrahaṇavaiyarthyāt tadvirodhitve vā kathaṃ viruddharāddhāntena parihāra ityata āha - vyāseti ।। vyāsacittasthitaṃ matāparaparyāyaṃ jñānākhyamahākāśamapekṣya gṛhādyavacchinnākāśavat aavacchinnāni'; viviktāni parimitaviṣayāṇi kānicidetāni matānyūrīkṛtya aanye'; kecana jaiminyādyāḥ vyavaharantītyarthaḥ । yathoktaṃ sattarkadīpāvalyām - ākāśavadvyāptatvātprakāśamānatvācca vyāsacittasthitamatākhyākāśāt aavacchinnāni'; svasvamatyā viviktāni tāni matāni idaṃ madīyaṃ idaṃ madīyaṃ ityūrīkṛtyānye vyavaharanti । yathā gṛhanagarādibhirākāśapradeśānavacchidyāyaṃ madīyaḥ pradeśo ayaṃ madīyaḥ pradeśa iti janāḥ vyavaharantīti । matānāmiti bahuvacanaṃ vakṣyamāṇamatavivakṣayā । tathā ca jaiminyādimatānāṃ vyāsamatena parasparaṃ cāvirodha ityarthaḥ ।

sū - oṃ।। abhivyakterityāśmarathyaḥ । 
।।
tatra tatra prasiddhāvapyagnyādiṣu brahmaṇo abhivyakteragnyādisūktaniyama ityāśmarathyaḥ ।।

nanu laukikaprasiddherajñānādimūlatvenānyathopapattāvapi vaidikāgnyādisūktamantrādiprasiddhyanyathānupapattyāgnyādīnāṃ sūktādigatāgnyādiśabdavācyatvaṃ syāt, tatrājñānādimūlakatvakalpanāyogenānyathopapattyabhāvāt । nāpi vyavahārārthatvena anyathopapattiḥ, anāditvādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtraṃ paṭhati - abhivyakteriti ।। atra pūrvasmādapiranuvartanīyaḥ । tacchabdaścānuvṛtto anekadhā vipariṇetavya ityāśayena tadvyācaṣṭe - tatreti । atatra tatra'; sūktādau tasya brahmaṇa eva aprasiddhāvapi'; pratipādyatve api agnyādīnāmapratipādyatve apītyarthaḥ । agnyādiṣviti sāvadhāraṇam । sūtre avirodhamiti anuṣaktapadatātparyamāha - agnyādīti । ādiśabdaḥ ubhayatra yojyaḥ । yujyata iti vaktīti śeṣaḥ । anenāpi - tattatsūktādau brahmaṇa eva pratipādyatve api agnivāyvādīnāmapratipādyatve api avirodhaḥ । agnyādisūktaniyamaḥ idamagnisūktam idaṃ vāyusūktam iti sūktaniyamaḥ, iyamagnividyā iyaṃ vāyuvidyeti vidyāniyamaśca yujyate । kathaṃ? tairagnyādisūktādibhistasya brahmaṇastasyāmupāstau kṛtāyāṃ tatrāgnyādiṣveva tasya brahmaṇaḥ aabhi'; svecchayābhivyaktiniyamāttadabhiprāyeṇa tatprasiddherupapatterityevaṃ vaidikāgnyādisūktādiprasiddhyavirodhamāśmarathyācāryo vaktīti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।।

sū - oṃ।। anusmṛterbādariḥ । 
।।
tatra tatroktasya viṣṇoragnyādiṣvanusmaryamāṇatvāttanniyama iti bādariḥ ।।

prakārāntareṇa sūktādiniyamasyānyathopapattiṃ kathayatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe - anusmṛteriti ।। atra pūrvavadadhyāhārādiḥ । atatra tatra'; agnyādividyāsu । sūtre avirodhamityanuṣaktapadatātparyamāha - tanniyama iti ।। anenāpi - viṣṇoreva agnyādividyāpratipādyatve api yatastasyāgnyādividyāsu uktasya viṣṇostaistattatsūktādyupāsakaistatrāgnyādiṣveva aanusmṛteḥ'; anusmartavyatvāt pratipattavyatvāt avirodhastanniyamaḥ agnyādisūktādivyavasthā yujyate । ato naitadanyathānupapattyānyeṣāṃ vācyatvaṃ kalpyamiti sūktādiprasiddhyavirodhaṃ abādariḥ'; bādarātmajaḥ śukācāryo vaktīti sūtravṛttirdarśitā bhavati ।

sū - oṃ।। sampatteriti jaiministathā hi darśayati । 
।।
sākṣādapyavirodhaṃ vadan jaiminiḥ sūktādiniyamamagnyādisamprāptyā manyate ।।

rītyantareṇa sūktādiniyamasyānyathopapattiṃ kathayatsūtramupanyasyati - sampatteriti ।। jaiminimatasya pūrvamupanyastatvātkimarthaṃ punarvacanamiti mandāśaṅkānirāsāya ubhayānvayīti śabdaparāmṛṣṭapūrvoktānuvādena viṣayabhedaṃ darśayan sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe - sākṣāditi ।। agnyādiśabdānāṃ mukhyato brahmavācakatve api aavirodhaṃ'; laukikavyavahāravirodhābhāvaṃ vadannityarthaḥ । atrāpyanuvṛttasya avirodhamityasyārthamāha - sūktādīti ।। saṃprāptyā nimittabhūtayeti śeṣaḥ ।

ataṃ tathā yathopāsate tadeva bhavati'; iti darśayati ।।

nanvagnyādiṣu bhagavadupāstau agnyādiprāptirbhavatītyetatkuta ityataḥ sūtrasūcitāṃ śrutimudāharati - tamiti ।। ataṃ'; paramātmānaṃ yena yena prakāreṇa upāsate adhikāriṇaḥ tena prakāreṇa tadeva rūpaṃ abhavati'; prāpnuvantītyarthaḥ । tattvapradīpe api ayādṛśo bhāvitastvīśastādṛśo jīva ābhavet'; iti tṛtīyatātparyokteḥ atadeva bhavati'; tathaiva bhavati । yatprakāreṇopāste tatprakāreṇa bhavatītyayamevārtha uktaḥ । tattvapradīpakārapakṣe upāsate ityekavacanaṃ dhātvantarametat । anena yato agnyādisūktādiṣu mukhyataḥ parabrahmaṇa eva pratipādyatve apyavirodhaḥ, sūktādiniyamo yujyate । ataḥ na tadanyathānupapattyānyeṣāṃ vācyatvaṃ mantavyam । kathamidaṃ yujyate? tairagnyādiṣu bhagavadupāsakānām agnyādisampatteḥ prāpteḥ । ahi'; yasmāttamiti prasiddhā śrutiḥ । atathā'; agnyādyadhikaraṇakopāstyā agnyādiprāptirbhavatīti adarśayati'; pratipādayati । sākṣāditi laukikavyavahāre avirodhaṃ vadan jaiminiḥ sūtreṣu aavirodham'; aniyamākhyavirodhābhāvaṃ niyamaṃ amanyate'; varṇayatīti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । yadyapyuttarasūtradvaye sādhakavyāpārokteralpākṣaratvācca dṛṣṭeriti vācyam, na tvabhivyakteriti, tasyār iśvaravyāpāratvāt । tathāpyabhivyaktiṃ vinā dṛṣṭerayogāttadgrahaṇenobhayalābhātprādhānyādīśvaravyāpāra evoktaḥ । yadyapyanusmṛtiśabditopāstyanantaramabhivyakteḥ tadanantaraṃ tatsampatteḥ prathamamanusmṛteriti vaktavyam । tathāpyabhivyaktisampatyubhayānantaramapyupāstiḥ kāryeti darśayitumanusmṛtermadhye niveśa iti draṣṭavyam । yadyapi ṛgbhāṣye - pṛthagrūpāṇi viṣṇostu devātāntaragāṇi tu । agnyādiśabdavācyāni nāmnā sūktabhidā bhavet ।।

ityagnyādyantargataviṣṇuvācakāgnyādiśabdayogaḥ sūktasya vyavasthāpaka uktaḥ । tathā cāgnyādiśabdāstattatsūktāni ca agnyādigatabrahmarūpeṣveva mukhyāni । evaṃ bahirgatarūpeṣu ca atītānāgatavartamānāgnyādisūktopāsakairagnyādigatatvena anusmartavyatvaṃ vā saṃprāptirvā tattatsūktavyavasthāpakamityanuṣṭhānaviśeṣopayogitayā saurasāvitravāmanaviṣṇvādisūktādivyavasthārthaṃ ca vyavasthāpakāntaramuktamityavirodhaḥ । laukikavaidikavyavahārayoragnyādāvupacaritatvabījaṃ tu tayostatra mukhyatvāṅgīkāre atathā dṛṣṭyupadeśāt'; ityanena sūcita asarvanāma'; ityādiśrutivirodhādirūpaprāguktānupapattiriti ṭīkāyāmevoktam ।

na hyanyopāsako anyaṃ prāpnuta iti yujyata ityata āha - sū - oṃ।।
āmananti cainamasmin ।
।।

enaṃ viṣṇumasminnagnyādāvāmananti ।

yaduktamagnyādisūktādibhiḥ brahmopāsakasyāgnyādiprāptirbhavatīti tacchrutyuktamapi na yuktam । amadbhaktā yānti māmapi'; ityāderanyopāsakasyānyaprāpterayogāt । aśrutopaniṣatkagatyabhidhānāt'; ityādau tadanabhyupagamācceti bhāvenāśaṅkya tatparihāratayā sūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe - na hīti ।। ṭīkāyāmāśaṅkyāvatāryetyanvayaḥ । śaṅkārūpasūtrāvatārikāṃ pradarśyetyarthaḥ । ahi'; yasmādanyopāsako anyaṃ prāpnuta ityetatpramāṇavirodhānna yujyate । tasmāduktamayuktamityarthaḥ । enamityanuvādena viṣṇumiti vyākṛtam । asminnityasya vyākhyānamagnyādāviti । aāmananti'; pratipādayanti śrutaya iti śeṣaḥ । caśabdaḥ viṣṇūpāsakasyāgnyādiprāptirayukteti pūrvapakṣiśaṅkāvyāvartakaḥ । tena siddhāntipratijñā, agnyādiprāptipadena tadantargatabhagavatprāptereva vivakṣitatvāditi sākṣāddhetuśca sūcitaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu - na kevalamekatraivāmananti paṭhanti vājasaneyāḥ, kintvanyatra asa yaścāyamasmin'; ityādau, evamanye āmananti aya eṣa etasmin'; ityādau, anye cāmananti aetasyām'; ityādau, anye ca atatsṛṣṭvā'; । tadevānuprāviśat ityādau । smaranti ca smṛtikartāraḥ ayaccandramasi yaccāgnau'; ityādīni । samuccayārthaścaśabda ityuktam ।

ayo agnau tiṣṭhan'; aya eṣa etasminnagnau tejomayo amṛtamayaḥ puruṣaḥ'; ityādinā ।।

।। iti vaiśvānarādhikaraṇam ।।

iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite brahmasūtrabhāṣye prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

tāḥ śrutīḥ darśayati - ya iti ।। ayo agnau tiṣṭhan'; ityekaṃ vājasaneyaṃ vākyam । aya eṣaḥ'; ityaparaṃ chāndogyavākyam । ubhayatra yacchabdasya tatratyatacchabdenānvayaḥ । atejomayaḥ'; tejorūpaḥ aamṛtamayaḥ'; nityātmā । ādiśabdena aetamagnāvadhvaryavaḥ'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । ityādinā āmanantītyanvayaḥ । anena - na viṣṇūpāsakasyāgnyādiprāptyukitirayuktā । kutaḥ? agnyādiprāptipadena tadantargatabhagavatprāptervivakṣitatvāt । na ca viṣṇoragnyādyantargatatvāsiddhiḥ । yata aenaṃ'; viṣṇuṃ aasmin'; agnyādau āmananti śrutayo ata iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । ।। iti vaiśvānarādhikaraṇam ।।

iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryāṇāṃ sarvatantrasvatantrāṇāṃ 
śrīmadraghunāthatīrthapūjyapādānāṃ śiṣyeṇa śrīmajjagannāthayatinā kṛtāyāṃ
śrīmadbrahmasūtrabhāṣyadīpikāyāṃ
prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

।। atha tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

।। dyubhvādhikaraṇam ।।

tatra cānyatra ca prasiddhānāṃ śabdānāṃ viṣṇau samanvayaṃ prāyeṇāsmin pāde darśayati । viṣṇoḥ paravidyāviṣayatvamuktam ।

etatpādapratipādyaṃ darśayati - tatreti ।। anyonyasamuccaye caśabdau । devatādhikaraṇāpaśūdrādhikaraṇayoḥ samanvayākaraṇāttadvyāvṛttyarthaṃ - aprāyeṇa'; prācuryeṇeti । tathā ca prāyeṇāsmin tṛtīye pāde atatra'; harau tasmāt aanyatra'; rudraprakṛtyādau ca śrutiliṅgādibhiḥ prasiddhānāṃ nāmaliṅgātmakaśabdānāṃ viṣṇau asamanvayaṃ'; paramamukhyayā vṛttyā tātparyaprabalahetubhiḥ adarśayati'; pratipādayati sūtrakṛdityarthaḥ । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyamudāhṛtya viṣayasaṃśayasayuktikapūrvapakṣān darśayati - viṣṇoriti ।

tatra ayasmin dyauḥ pṛthivī cāntarikṣamotaṃ manaḥ saha prāṇaiśca sarvaiḥ tamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānam'; ityatra । aprāṇānāṃ granthirasi rudro mā'viśāntakaḥ'; aprāṇeśvaraḥ kṛttivāsāḥ pinākī'; ityādinā rudrasya prāṇādhāratvapratīteḥ । asa eṣo antaraścarate bahudhā jāyamānaḥ'; iti jīvaliṅgācca tayoḥ prāptiriti ।।

uktamityāvartate । tatretyavyayaṃ tadityarthe api । atretyapyāvartate । ādiśabda ubhayānvayī । rudrasyeti śeṣe ṣaṣṭī । tayorityetat pradhānavāyvorapyupalakṣakam । tathā ca adṛśyatvādiguṇakākṣarasya viṣṇoḥ paravidyāviṣayatvaṃ yatroktaṃ tatraivātharvaṇe tatparavidyāviṣayatvaṃ 
yasmin dyauḥ pṛthivī cāntarikṣamotaṃ manaḥ saha prāṇaiśca sarvaiḥ ।
tamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānamanyā vāco vimuñcatha ।। 
aamṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ'; ityatra iti vākye tatra dyubhvādyāśraye uktamityekā yojanā । tatra dyubhvādyāyatanatve atayoḥ'; rudrajīvayoḥ prāptiḥ । kutaḥ? atravākye dyubhvādyāyatane prāṇādhāratvapratīteḥ śravaṇāt । tathā sa eṣa iti jīvaliṅgaśravaṇācca । na ca prāṇādhāratvaśravaṇe api kuto atra rudrasya prāptiriti vācyam । aprāṇānāṃ granthirasi rudromāviśāntakastenānnenāpyāyasva'; iti taittirīyavākyena, tathā - yo brahmā brahmaṇa ujjabhāra prāṇeśvaraḥ kṛttivāsāḥ pinākīr । iśāno devassa na āyurdadhātu ityādikhilasaṃhitāvākyena ca rudrasya prāṇādhāratvapratīteḥ ityaparā yojanā । yadvā - asminneva pakṣe tayorityetatsaptamyantamāśritya liṅgaliṅgirūpadharmadvayaparatayā vyākhyeyam । tathātve ādiśabdo arudro vāva lokādhāraḥ'; iti vākyagrāhī । evaṃ tatra tayoḥ prāptiriti dūrānvayena atatra'; paravidyāviṣayatve tayo rudrajīvayoḥ prāptirityanyā yojanā । tatra ādyayojanāyāṃ dyubhvādyāyatanatvasya viṣṇvanyatvākṣepamukhena atamevam'; ityādinā aamṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ'; iti vākyaśeṣabalātpratītasya mokṣajanakajñānajanakavidyāviṣayatvarūpasya tattvapradīparītyānanyayogena prādhānyena jñeyatvarūpasya vā paravidyāviṣayatvasya pūrvoktasya viṣṇoritaratvākṣepāt adṛśyatvādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tathā dyubhvādyāyatanatvarūpo viṣayaḥ darśitaḥ । dvividhadvitīyayojanāyāṃ sayuktikapūrvapakṣo darśitaḥ । tṛtīyāyāṃ tu pūrvapakṣaphalaṃ darśitamiti draṣṭavyam । ayasmin'; paramātmani dvyādilokāḥ amanaḥ'; tadabhimānī asarvaiḥ prāṇaiḥ'; indriyaistadabhimānibhiśca saha ataṃ'; praviṣṭaṃ paramātmānam aekaṃ'; pradhānaṃ ajānatha'; jānīdhvam iti śrutyarthaḥ । rudra u mā āviśa iti padacchedaḥ । u ityavyayaṃ sambuddhidyotako nipātaḥ । mā ityavyayaṃ, nāsmadādeśaḥ māśabdaḥ । yadvā metyanenāsmadādeśo māśabdaścetyubhau tantreṇopāttau । sa ca niṣedhārthaḥ । tathā ca - he rudra tvaṃ aprāṇānām'; indriyāṇāṃ grathyate asminniti agranthiḥ'; āśrayaḥ aantakaḥ'; saṃhartā cāsi । sa tvaṃ amā'; mām aāviśa'; praviśa mayi sannidhiṃ kurvityarthaḥ । yadvā - he rudra antakastvaṃ māṃ mā praviśetyarthaḥ । atena'; āhutirūpeṇa dattena aannena'; mām aāpyāyasva'; sukhaya । yo abrahmaṇe'; caturmukhāya abrahma'; vedān aujjabhāra'; ujjahāra, sa aprāṇeśvaraḥ'; indriyeśaḥ akṛttivāsāḥ'; kṛttiścarma vasanaṃ yasyāsau, apinākīr'; iśāno na āyuḥ adadhātu'; puṣṇātviti śrutyantarārthaḥ । siddhānte tu rudrādiśabdāḥ viṣṇuparāḥ । ya eṣa jīvo abahudhā'; bahuśarīreṇotpadyamānaḥ śarīrāntaḥsañcārītyātharvaṇaśrutyarthaḥ ।

ata ucyate - sū - oṃ
dyubhvādyāyatanaṃ svaśabdāt ।।
atamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānam'; ityātmaśabdāt
dyubhvādyāśrayo viṣṇureva ।
ātmabrahmādayaḥ śabdāstamṛte viṣṇumavyayam ।
na sambhavanti yasmātternaivāptā guṇapūrṇatā ।।

iti brahmavaivarte ।।

siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe - ata iti ।। sautrasvaśabdasya svaśabdaparyāyātmaśabdāditi viṣṇutattvanirṇayokteḥ, svetiśabdaḥ svaśabda iti vyutpattyā svaśabdaparyāyātmaśabdagrāhitvaṃ viṣṇoḥ svarūpasyaiva sākṣādvācako hyayamātmaśabda iti tattvapradīpokteḥ, svasya viṣṇoreva vācakaḥ śabdaḥ svaśabda iti vigrahāśrayeṇa ca ātmaśabdaparāmarśitvamāśritya svaśabdādityetadātmaśabdāditi vyākhyātam । tathā ca aityātmaśabdāt'; ityatrātmaśabdaśravaṇādityarthaḥ । dyubhvādyāśraya ityanenāyatanaśabdo vyākhyātaḥ । kvacidāyatanaśabdasyaiva pāṭhaḥ । viṣṇurevetyanena samanvayasūtrānuvṛttaṃ tattvityetat śrutyanusārālliṅgavipariṇāmena vyākhyātam । anena - asvaśabdāt'; viṣṇuvācisvaśabdaparyāyātmaśabdāt svaśabdāt adyubhvādyāyatanaṃ'; svargabhūmyādisarvāśrayaḥ atattu'; viṣṇureveti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । ātmāśabdādapi kuto ayaṃ viṣṇurityata āha - ātmeti ।। yasmāt ataiḥ'; viṣṇoritaraiścaturmukhādijīvaiḥ guṇapūrṇatā anaivāptā'; na sarvathā prāptā । tasmādātmabrahmādayaḥ śabdāḥ aavyayaṃ'; nityaniratiśayapravṛttinimittavantaṃ viṣṇum aṛte'; vinā tadanyaṃ ana sambhavanti'; na mukhyato vācakatvena prāpnuvantītyarthaḥ । anenātmaśabdasyāpi guṇapūrtirartha ityuktaṃ bhavati । brahmavaivarta ityanantaramanyatra niravakāśatayoktāditi śeṣaḥ । tasyātmaśabdādityanenānvayaḥ।

sū - oṃ ।। muktopasṛpyavyapadeśāt ।।

aamṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ'; iti ।

nanu viṣṇau mukhyo apyātmaśabdo jāyamānatvarūpajīvaliṅgabalādamukhyārthaḥ kiṃ na syāt । tathā ca na tato viṣṇordyubhvādyāyatanatvanirṇaya ityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya tadupāttaśrutimevādāharati - mukteti ।। iti muktāprāpyatvavyapadeśādityanvayaḥ । sūtre dyubhvādyāyatanasyeti vipariṇāmena anuvartanīyam । muktopasṛpyeti bhāvanirdeśaḥ। upasṛpyatvaṃ ceha śrautasetuśabdabalātprāpyāntararahitatve sati prāpyatvaṃ vivakṣitam । nanvarcirādivatprāpyatvamātram । tathā ca - dyubhvādyāyatanasya aamṛtasya'; iti muktopasṛpyatvokterviṣṇutvaniścayānnātmaśabdasyāmukhyārthatvamāśritya viṣṇoranyat dyubhvādyāyatanaṃ kalpyamiti । amuktānām'; iti smaraṇādamṛtasyeti jātāvekavacanam । tathā ca aamṛtasya'; muktajātasya aeṣaḥ'; paramātmā asetuḥ'; seturiva seturmukhyāśraya ityarthaḥ ।

brahmavidāpnoti param । anārāyaṇaṃ mahājñeyaṃ viśvātmānaṃ parāyaṇam'; amuktānāṃ paramā gatiḥ'; 
aetamānandamayamātmānamupasaṅkrāmati'; ityādinā
tasyaiva muktāprāpyatvavyapadeśāt ।
bahunātra kimuktena yāvacchvetaṃ na gacchati ।
yogī tāvanna muktassyādeṣa śāstravinirṇayaḥ ।।

ityādityapurāṇe ।।

nanu dyubhvādyāyatanasya muktaprāpyatvaṃ kutaḥ viṣṇutvaniścāyakamityāśaṅkāparihārakatayāpi sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe - brahmaviditi ।। aityādinā'; vākyena atasya'; viṣṇoḥ evetyanena prāpyatvaṃ prāpyāntararahitatve sati prāptatvam । anena dyubhvādyāyatanasya muktopasṛpyatvavyapadeśāttasya viṣṇoreva muktopasṛtapyatvavyapadeśādityāvṛttyā sūtraṃ vyākhyātam। pradhānasūtre anuvṛttaṃ tattvityetadiha vipariṇāmena anuvartanīyamiti sūcitam । upasṛpyapadaṃ bhāvapradhānaṃ kṛtvā vyākhyātam। evakāro liṅgasyānyaniṣṭhatvavyavacchedakaḥ । abrahmavit'; viṣṇujñānī muktassan aparaṃ'; viṣṇumāpnotīti taittirīyaśrutyarthaḥ । anārāyaṇam'; iti taittirīyopaniṣadi mahopaniṣadi ca śrutam । atra atadviśvamupajīvati'; ityanuvartate । tathā ca atadviśvaṃ'; jagat mahanīyaṃ jñeyaṃ, pūjyajñeyaṃ vā । viśvasvāminaṃ aparāyaṇaṃ'; muktānāmāśrayamupajīvatīti śrutyarthaḥ। amuktānāṃ paramā gatiḥ'; iti sahasranāmagatamekaṃ nāma । paramā mukhyā gamyata iti gatirāśrayaḥ । aetam'; iti taittirīyavākyamānandamayanaye vyākṛtam । ādipadena aetamānandamayamātmānamupasaṅkramya'; aparamaṃ yaḥ parāyaṇam'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । nanūdāhṛtavākyairastu viṣṇoḥ muktaprāpyatvaṃ, tathāpyatrānyavyavacchedābhāvādviṣṇuvadanyasya muktaprāpyatvaṃ kiṃ na syāditi liṅgasya sāvakāśatvamāśaṅkya anyatra prāpyatvamātrasambhave api niruktopasṛpyatvaṃ sautramuktaśabditavivakṣitamuktyupetajīvaprāpyatvaṃ vānyatra niravakāśamiti pramāṇenāha - bahuneti ।। aatra'; prāpyamokṣatatsādhanaviṣaye abahunoktena'; idamidaṃ ceti pratyekaṃ bahunā vacanena akiṃ prayojanaṃ'; na kimapi, pratyutoktigauravameveti bhāvaḥ । tarhi kathaṃ nirṇaya ityata āha - yāvacchvetamiti । aśvetaṃ'; śvetadvīpākhyaṃ viṣṇusthānaṃ ayāvanna gacchati'; na prāpnoti, tatratyaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca na paśyati atāvadyogī'; aparokṣajñānākhyopāyavān mukto na syāt । bhagavadicchārūpāvaraṇānmuktaḥ samyagāvirbhūtajñānānandādimān na bhavediti aeṣaḥ'; upadeśaḥ aśāstravinirṇayaḥ'; śāstratattvaviṣayakanirṇayasādhanamityarthaḥ । eṣor'thaḥ aśāstravinirṇayaḥ'; tajjanyanirṇayaviṣaya iti vā । bhāvabodhe tu - sūtre purāṇe ca muktapadena liṅgabhaṅgavān vivakṣita ityuktam । atra śvetadvīpāganturamuktatvoktyā śvetadvīpaṃ prāptasyaiva muktatvaṃ jñāyate । tathā ca tatsthitasya viṣṇorevetaravyavacchedena muktaprāpyatvaṃ siddhamiti bhāvaḥ । ityādityapurāṇe ityasya tasyaiva muktaprāpyatvavyapadeśādityanenānvayaḥ । anena tasyaivetyevakārasyopayogo jñāpito bhavati । asya hetorna liṅgasya sāvakāśatvaṃ śaṅkyamityadhyāhṛtasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। nānumānamatacchabdāt ।।
nānumānam atacchabdāt ।।
nānumānātmakāgamaparikalpitarudro atra vācyaḥ ।

nanu prāguktarītyā rudraprakṛtyordyubhvāyatanatvaṃ kiṃ na syādityatastatsādhakābhāvānna tayostadityāha sūtrakṛt - nānumānamiti ।। atra nānumānamiti sādhyāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - nānumānātmaketi । aanumānaprāptaprāmāṇyāsadāgamo anumātmakaḥ'; iti tattvapradīpokteḥ anumānātmake anumānasiddhaprāmāṇyake pāśupatādyāgame sarvāśrayatvena kalpito bodhita ityarthaḥ । kecittu - pramāṇatvena anumīyata ityanumānamiti vyācikhyuḥ । etatpakṣe ātmakaśabdavaiyarthyaṃ, tattvapradīpaṭīke viruddhe । rudrapadaṃ pradhānāderupalakṣakam । pradhānasūtrādanuvṛttena dyubhvādyāyatanapadenopasthāpitaṃ nañarthapratiyoginaṃ darśayati - atreti । dyubhvādyāyatanaprakaraṇa ityarthaḥ । avācyaḥ'; pratipādyaḥ । sarvāśrayatveneti śeṣaḥ ।

bhasmadharogratvāditacchabdābhāvāt ।

evaṃ sūtre pratijñāṃśaṃ vyākhyāya hetvaṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - bhasmadhareti ।। tasya rudrasya śabdastacchabdaḥ । tacchrutiliṅgātmakaḥ । tathā ca bhasmadharogratvādidharmaviśiṣṭadharmibodhakabhasmadharogrādiśabdābhāvādityarthaḥ । atha vā - akimucyate bhasmadharogratvādīnāṃ tacchabdatvam'; ityuttaraṭīkābalādbhāvabhavitrorabhedavivakṣayā svārthe tvapratyayaḥ । tatprayogastu liṅgātmakaśabdasyāpi saṅgrahāya । bhāvabodhe tu - bhasmadharetyanena rudravācakanāmātmakaśabdo gṛhyate । ugratvapadena ugratvarūpaliṅgātmakaśabdo gṛhyate । ādipadena nāmaliṅgātmakaśabdāntarāṇi gṛhyante । samākhyāderupalakṣakametat । tathā ca - bhasmadharādirudraśrutīnām ugratvādirūpatalliṅgānāṃ rudraprāpakasamākhyādīnāṃ cābhāvādityartha ityuktam । atra rudraśivāditacchabdābhāvādityanuktvā bhasmadharogratvādīti vacanaṃ arudro bhasmadharo nagnaḥ'; iti vacanādviśeṣanāmābhiprāyeṇa । ata evaitadvacanoktāḥ nagnādiśabdā evādipadena grāhyā iti dhyeyam । bhasmadharetyetatpradhānatriguṇatvādirūpaprakṛtiprāpakaśrutiliṅgādyabhāvādityarthāntaropalakṣakatayāpi vyākhyeyam । yadyapi atacchabdādityasya tacchabdābhāvāditi vyākhyāne nañaḥ kriyāsāpekṣatvenāsamarthatvātsamāsānupapattiḥ । tathāpi nirmakṣikamityādāviva aarthābhāve yadavyayam'; ityavyayībhāvasamāsāśrayaṇānnānupapattiḥ । pañcamītvāt nātrām bhavati । anena sūtre jagatkartṛtvenānumīyate ityanumānaśabdena vā aānumānamanumānasambandhi'; iti sattarkadīpāvalyukterānumānamiti padacchedenānumānaśabdena vā anumānasiddhaprāmāṇyakapāśupatādyāgamasiddhaṃ rudrapradhānādhikaṃ gṛhyate । yadvā - pramāṇatvenānumīyata ityanumānaṃ pāśupatādyāgamaḥ । tato matvarthe arśa ādibhyo ac, tena tatpratipādyamucyate । evamānumānamiti padacchede apyaṇantātpunaraṇ kāryaḥ । tatra prathamāṇantarapadenāgama ucyate । dvitīyena pratipādyatvam । tathā ca anumānātmakapāśupatādyāgamapratipādyaṃ rudrādikaṃ na dyubhvādyāyatanaṃ na ayasmin'; ityādiprakaraṇe sarvāśrayatvena pratipādyaṃ, kutaḥ? aatacchabdāt'; rudrapradhānādisādhakaśrutiliṅgādyabhāvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

aso antakaḥ sa rudraḥ sa prāṇabhṛtsa prāṇanāyakaḥ sar iśo yo hariryo ananto yo viṣṇuryaḥ parovarīyān'; ityādinā prāṇagranthirudratvāderviṣṇorevoktatvāt ।

nanvātharvaṇe rudrādijñāpakābhāve api atroktaprāṇādhāratvapratipādikāyāṃ aprāṇānāṃ granthirasi rudra'; ityādisamākhyāśrutau rudrādiśabdānām antakatvādiliṅgānāṃ coktatvāttadbalāttatroktaṃ dyubhvādyātanatvaṃ rudrādeḥ kiṃ na syādityata āha - sa iti ।। yo antakassaṃhartā sa eva tacchabdavācyaḥ śrutaḥ sa viṣṇureva । yo rudraḥ śrutaḥ so api viṣṇureva । yaḥ aprāṇabhṛt'; prāṇādhāratvabodhakaprāṇagranthiśabdavācyaḥ, so api viṣṇureva । yaḥ aprāṇanāyakaḥ'; tatsvāmī tata eva prāṇeśa śabditaḥ so api viṣṇureva । yar iśaḥ śrutaḥ so api viṣṇureva । yo anantastacchabdavācyaḥ so api trividhaparicchedaśūnyatvādviṣṇureva, na śeṣaḥ । yaḥ parovarīyān so api rudrādeḥ parato vāṇyādeḥ parādviriñcāt parataḥ prakṛteḥ paratvāddharireva nānya iti śrutyarthaḥ । atrāntarādhikaraṇodāhṛtacaturvedaśikhāvākye ca aparasmāduttamaṃ proktam'; iti vacanānusāreṇa paraparataravaravaratamānāṃ caturṇāṃ pratyāyanāya vṛttivākye subādeśasya sorutvotvaguṇasamānaśabdalopā jñātavyāḥ । pratyuddeśyaṃ vidheyānvayajñāpanāya bahūnāṃ yattadāṃ prayogaḥ । aityādinā'; śrutyantaravākyena aprāṇagranthirudratvādeḥ'; prāṇagranthitvaliṅgasya rudraśabdavācyatvasya ca tasyaiva viṣṇorevoktatvādityarthaḥ । prāṇeśvarādiśabdavācyatvamantakatvādiliṅgaṃ cādiśabdārthaḥ । prakṛtiśrutiliṅgāderapyupalakṣakametat । na tu rudrāderityevakārārthaḥ । evakāreṇānyatrāmukhyatassattvamanumanyate । uktatvādityasya ana rudrādiśrutiliṅgavirodhaḥ'; ityadhyāhṛtasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

brahmāṇḍe ca -
rujaṃ drāvayate yasmādrudrastasmājjanārdanarḥ ।
iśānādeva ceśāno mahādevo mahattvataḥ ।।

pibanti ye narā nākaṃ muktāssaṃsārasāgarāt ।
tadādhāro yato viṣṇuḥ pinākīti tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

śivaḥ sukhātmakatvena śarvaḥ śaṃrodhanāddhariḥ ।
kṛtyātmakamimaṃ dehaṃ yato vaste pravartayan ।।

kṛttivāsāstato devo viriñcaśca virecanāt । bṛṃhaṇādbrahmanāmāsāvaiśvaryādindra ucyate ।।

nanu tathāpi na prāṇādhāratvadyubhvādyāyatanatvabodhakasamākhyāśrutau viṣṇoḥ pratipādyatvaniścayaḥ । tatratyānāṃ rudrādiśabdānāṃ paśupatyādāveva rūḍhatvena viṣṇau tadabhāvāt, bhāve vā punaraniścayāt । viṣṇau yogavṛttisambhave api tasyā rūḍhito durbalatvenāniścāyakatvāt । na hi śrutyantare viṣṇuliṅgādyastītyata āha - brahmāṇḍe ceti । co apyarthaḥ samuccaye । uktatvādityanuvartate । tenāsyānvayaḥ । kimuktamityato rudrādiśabdānāṃ mahāyogavidvadrūḍhipratipādakaṃ vākyaṃ paṭhati - rujamiti । arujaṃ'; rogam utpattyādikaṃ adrāvayate'; nirvāpayati nivartayati yasmāttasmādrudra ityucyate । ka ityata stadrūpaviśeṣamāha - janārdana iti । jananamardayatīti vyutpattirḥ । aiśanārt iśānāṃ'; brahmādīnāṃ ceṣṭakatvādīśāno api sa evetyarthaḥ । mahattvata ityupalakṣaṇam । dyotanādeścetyapi draṣṭavyam । ye anarāḥ'; janāḥ saṃsārasāgarānmuktāḥ santo anākaṃ'; paramasukhaṃ apibanti'; bhuñjate te pinākāḥ । viṣṇuryataḥ atadādhāraḥ'; teṣāmādhārastataḥ pinākīti asmṛtaḥ'; abhihitaḥ śrutāviti śeṣaḥ । śruta iti pāṭhaḥ svarasaḥ । aśaṃrodhanāt'; muktiparyantaṃ svarūpabhūtamapi sukhaṃ rudhvā vartanāt āsurasakhaṃ nirudhya vartanādvā śarva ityarthaḥ । yataḥ akṛtyātmakaṃ'; carmamayamimaṃ dehaṃ apravartayan'; sṛjan niyamayan vā tena svātmānaṃ jīvaṃ vā avaste'; ācchādayati tadantarvartate । yadvā - dehaṃ vaste adhivasatītyataḥ kṛttivāsā ityucyata ityarthaḥ । avirecanāt'; jagatsarjanādasau viṣṇuḥ bṛṃhaṇādvardhanādvā brahmanāmā । asau paramaiśvaryādindra ityucyate ।

evaṃ nānāvidhaiśśabdaiḥ eka eva trivikramaḥ । vedeṣu sapurāṇeṣu gīyate puruṣottamaḥ ।।

evaṃ viṣṇau rudrādiśabdānāṃ mahāyogamuktvā vidvadrūḍhiṃ cāha - evamiti ।।

nimittairityadhyāhāryam । tathā ca aevam'; uktarītyā nānāvidhairnimitaiḥ sapurāṇeṣu vedeṣu gataiḥ etairnānāvidhaiḥ śabdairviṣṇureka eva agīyate'; mukhyato abhidhīyata ityarthaḥ । kathamanyatrādṛṣṭaṃ sarvaśabdamukhyavācyatvamasyetyataḥ apuruṣottamastrivikramaḥ'; ityābhyāṃ tatropapādakamuktam । tribhuvanārthaśabdavyāpī hi trivikramaḥ । sarvapuruṣaśabdanimittakasvāmī hi puruṣottamaḥ । tathā cānena viṣṇau rudrādiśabdānāṃ mahāyogavidvadrūḍhikathanāt tayośta rūḍhimātrātprābalyādyuktaḥ samākhyāśrutyantare api viṣṇoḥ pratipādyatvaniścaya iti bhāvaḥ । apuruṣottama iti'; ityantasya abrahmāṇḍe'; iti pūrveṇānvayaḥ ।

vāmane ca - na tu nārāyaṇādīnāṃ nāmnāmanyatra sambhavaḥ। anyanāmnāṃ gatirviṣṇuḥ eka eva prakīrtitaḥ ।।

nanu yadi rudrādiśabdānāṃ viṣṇuparatvamuktvā arudro mā'viśāntakaḥ'; ityādiśrutīnāmanirṇāyakatvamucyate, tarhi nārāyaṇādināmnāṃ rudrādiparatvena anārāyaṇaṃ mahājñeyam'; ityādiśrutīnāmanirṇāyakatvaṃ ca syādityata āha - vāmane ceti ।। co apyarthe । asyāpyuktatvādavirodhaiti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । kimuktamityatastadvākyaṃ paṭhati - na tviti । anārāyaṇādīnāṃ'; nārāyaṇa ityādīnamanyatra rudrādau sambhavo mukhyavṛttiḥ astīti śeṣaḥ । aanyanāmnāṃ'; rudrādiśabdānāṃ aviṣṇureka eva gatiḥ'; mukhyavācyaḥ prakīrtita ityarthaḥ । itiśabdasya vāmana ityanenānvayaḥ । tasya nārāyaṇādināmnāṃ anyatra niravakāśatvokteḥ na tacchrutīnāmanirṇāyakatvamiti vivakṣitasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

skānde ca - ṛte nārāyaṇādīni nāmāni puruṣottamaḥ । prādādanyatra bhagavān rājevarte svakaṃ puram ।।

bhagavannāmatvāviśeṣādrudrādināmavannārāyaṇādināmnāmapi rudrādau vṛttiḥ kiṃ na syādityata āha - skānde ceti ।। co apyarthaḥ samuccaye । asyāpyuktatvāditi pūrveṇānvayaḥ । kimuktamityatastadvākyaṃ paṭhati - ṛta iti ।।

vinetyarthaḥ । aanyatra'; anyebhyo rudrādibhyaḥ anyāni rudrādināmānītiśeṣaḥ । ādiśabdena viṣṇurityādikaṃ gṛhyate। atra dṛṣṭāntamāha - rājeti ।। yathā rājā svakaṃ puramṛte anyadamātyādibhyo dadāti tadvadityarthaḥ । itītyantasya skānde ityanenānvayaḥ । tasya ca nārāyaṇādināmnāmanyatra vṛttyabhāvasyoktatvānna sāmyamityupaskṛtenānvayaḥ । anena skānde nārāyaṇādināmnāṃ viṣṇorevoktatvānna sāmyamityanvayena pūrvaprayuktaivakārasya kṛtyāntaraṃ sūcitaṃ bhavati ।

caturmukhaśśatānando brahmaṇaḥ padmabhūriti ।
ugro bhasmadharo nagnaḥ kapālīti śivasya ca ।
viśeṣanāmāni dadau svakīyānyapi keśavaḥ ।।

iti ca brāhme ।।

yadyevaṃ rudrādiśabdāḥ viṣṇvaikaparāḥ tarhi kimucyate bhasmadharogratvādīnāṃ tacchabdatvam । viṣṇudattatvābhiprāyeṇa cet - tarhi rudrādiśabdā api tādṛśā iti kathaṃ tairnirṇayābhāva ityata āha - caturmukha iti ।। yadyapi svakīyāni, tathāpi akeśavaḥ'; brahmarudrapravartako viṣṇuḥ asvakīyāni'; mukhyataḥ svavācakānyeva caturmukhaḥ śatānandaḥ padmabhūriti aviśeṣanāmāni'; nāmaviśeṣāneva abrahmaṇo'; brahmaṇe dadāvityarthaḥ । anagnaḥ'; digambaraḥ । brāhma ityasyāpyuktatvāditi pūrveṇānvayaḥ । rudrādau bhasmadharogratvādereva viṣṇossakāśātprāptatveneti tadarthaḥ । tasya ca pūrvoktaṃ yuktamiti sādhyenānvayaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। prāṇabhṛc ca ।।

etaireva hetubhirna jīvo vāyuśca ।

nanu asa eṣo antaścarate bahudhā jāyamānaḥ'; iti jīvaliṅgaśravaṇātprāṇitvaprasiddheśca jīvasāmānyasya vā, viṣayabhūtalokādhāratvasya avāyunā vai gautama sūtreṇāyaṃ lokaḥ paraśca lokaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni saṃdṛbdhāni bhavanti'; iti śrutyantare vāyuniṣṭhatvena prasiddhatvādvāyorvātra prakaraṇe dyubhvādyāśrayatvena pratipādyatā kiṃ na syādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe - prāṇabhṛcceti ।। etairiti । ātmaśabdaḥ muktopasṛpyatvamatacchabdo rudrādiprāpakaśrutīnāṃ viṣṇuparatvamityevaṃrūpaiḥ pūrvoktahetubhirityarthaḥ । nātra hetvantaraṃ vācyamityevaśabdārthaḥ । jīvo vāyurityanena prāṇabhṛcchabdo vyākhyātaḥ । atra vācya ityanuṣajyate । anena sūtre caśabdaḥ prāguktahetūnāṃ nānumānamityato nañaśca samākarṣakaḥ । na kevalaṃ rudro atra na vācyaḥ, kintu jīvo vāyuśceti samuccayārthaścetyuktaṃ bhavati ।

aajāyamāno bahudhā vijāyate'; iti tasyaiva bahudhā janmokteḥ ।।

nanu avāyunā vai gautama'; ityādiśruterviṣṇuparatvena vāyusādhakatvābhāve api bahudhā janmākhyaliṅgena jīvo atra vācyaḥ kiṃ na syādityata āha - ajāyamāna iti ।। dehataḥ aajāyamānaḥ'; avikurvāṇo abahudhā'; rāmakṛṣṇādirūpeṇa avijāyate'; tatra tatra prādurbhavatītyarthaḥ । iti puruṣasūktagatavākyenetyarthaḥ । yasya janmāsambhavo abhihitaḥ pūrvavādinā tasyaiva viṣmorna jīvasyetyevaśabdārthaḥ । tathā ca liṅgaṃ sāvakāśamiti na tadvirodha iti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। bhedavyapadeśāt । 
।।
na caikyaṃ vācyam । ajuṣṭaṃ yadā paśyatyanyamīśamasya mahimānam'; iti bhedavyapadeśāt ।।

nanu kiṃ jīvaliṅgasya viṣṇugatatvapratipādanāyāsena, liṅgabalājjīvasyaiva dyubhvādyāyatanatvaṃ syāt । na coktātmaśabdādihetuvirodhaḥ । jīveśābhedābhiprāyeṇa jīve apyātmaśabdādyuktisambhavādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe - bhedeti । jīveśvarayoratrābhipretamiti ca śeṣaḥ । anena sūtre nānumānamityato nañanuvartanīyaḥ । sa ca hetugatabhedapratiyoginā saṃyojya ityuktaṃ bhavati । caśabdo jīveśaikyaprayuktātmaśabdavācyataitatprakaraṇabodhyatāpi netisamuccayārthaḥ । kau'sau vyapadeśa ityata āha - juṣṭamiti । iti bhedavyapadeśāditi । iti bhedaśruterityarthaḥ । anena - ajuṣṭam'; iti vākye apaśyati'; iti darśanakartṛtvena prakṛtajīvasyar iśapadokteścar iśvarādbhedokteḥ na tayoraikyamatrābhipretamiti vācyamiti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । śrutistavānandamayanaye vyākṛtā ।

sū - oṃ ।।

adve vidye veditavye'; iti tasya hyetatprakaraṇam ।।

nanvatra jīvasya kasmāccidīśādanyatvamucyate, na paramātmanaḥ, ato na tayorbheda ityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe - prakaraṇāditi ।। itītyanantaram aityupakramyādhītam'; iti śeṣaḥ । ahi'; yataḥ aetat'; juṣṭamityādivākyajātaṃ yataḥ atasyaiva'; paravidyāviṣayasya paramātmana eva aprakaraṇaṃ'; nānyasyetyevaśabdārthaḥ । anena svaprakaraṇāt adve vidye veditavye'; iti paravidyāviṣayavastuno atrādhītatvena viṣṇuprakaraṇatvātparamātmana eva bhedavyapadeśāvagateḥ na jīvaparamātnorabhedo atrābhipreta iti vācyamiti sūtrayojanā darśitā bhavati ।

sū - oṃ ।। sthityadanābhyāṃ ca ।।

dvāsuparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samānaṃ bṛkṣaṃ pariṣasvajāte ।
tayoranyaḥ pippalaṃ svādvattyanaśnannanyo abhicākaśīti ।। 
itir iśajīvayoḥ sthityadanokteḥ ।।
।। iti dyubhvādhiprakaṇam ।।

na kevalaṃ ajuṣṭam'; iti bhedaśruterna jīveśabhedo atra prakaraṇe vivakṣita iti jñāyate, kintu liṅgādapītyāha sūtrakṛt - sthitīti ।। tadasiddhivāraṇāya śrutyudāharaṇena vyācaṣṭe - dvā suparṇeti । anena - advā suparṇā'; ityatra śrutābhyāḥ karmaphalānupajīvanāvasthititadupajīvanābhyāṃ hetubhyāṃ ca naivātra jīveśayoraikyaṃ vācyamiti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । caśabdastu hetusamuccāyaka iti spaṣṭatvānna vyākhyātaḥ । śrutāvadanasya prāthamye api sthiterīśasambandhitvenābhyarhitatvādalpākṣaratvācca sūtre tadanusāreṇa bhāṣye ca śrautakramamullaṅghya sthiteḥ prathamamuktiḥ । asayujā'; sayujau saṃyuktau upakāryopakārakabhāvavattayā parasparāparihāreṇa vartamānau asakhāyā'; sakhāyau prītyā ekadeśasthau advā'; dvau asuparṇā'; suparṇau । asuparṇā sakhāyā'; iti viśeṣaṇasvārasyādasya samajīvamātraviṣayatve suṣṭhuparamānandarūpau jīveśvarau asamānam'; ekaṃ avṛkṣaṃ'; dehākhyam aśvatthaṃ apariṣasvajāteḥ'; āliliṅgatuḥ । atayoḥ'; suparṇayormadhyer iśvarāt aanyo'; jīvaḥ apippalam'; aśvatthaphalarūpaṃ dehajanitakarmaphalam aatti'; asvādveva svādutvenaiva aśnāti । jīvāt aanyarḥ'; iśvarastu aanaśnan'; jīvādyamevābhuñjānaḥ aabhi'; abhitaḥ acākaśīti'; prakāśate । na tu svasthityai jīvavatkarmaphalamapekṣata iti muṇḍakaśrutyarthaḥ ।।

।। iti dyubhvādhikaraṇam ।।

।।

aprāṇo vā āśayā bhūyān'; ityuktvā ayo vai bhūmā tatsukham'; ityuktestasyaiva bhūmatvaprāptiḥ ।

atrādhikaraṇe bhūmanāmno viṣṇau samanvayaḥ pratipādyate । bhūmaśabdaśca abhūmnaḥ kratuvat'; ityādau kvaciddharmavācako apyatra pūrṇarūpadharmivacanaḥ । pūrṇatvaṃ ca guṇata uttamatvamiti dhyeyam । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayan sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ darśayati - prāṇa iti ।। achāndogye'; ityādau upaskāryam । aityuktvā'; ityupakrametyupalakṣaṇam । taduttamamanuktvetyapi draṣṭavyam । ata eva tasyaiva prāṇasyaivetyevakāro anyavyavacchedakaḥ prāyoji । śrutau pūrvapakṣe prāṇaśabdo vāyumātraparaḥ । siddhānte tu bhāṣyarītyā vāyuviṣṇūbhayaparaḥ । nyāyavivaraṇachāndogyabhāṣyarītyā tu vāyumātraparaḥ । na ca vāyuviṣṇūbhayavācitvaṃ vāyumātravācitvamityarthadvayaṃ viruddham । antaryāmivivakṣayā bhāṣyasya tadavivakṣayā vivaraṇādeḥ pravṛttatvāt । yathā aātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ'; ityatra sambhūtaśabdasyānekārthatve antaryāmiviṣṇurapyākāśapadenocyate । tasya janimātrārthatve tu na tena sa ucyate । tathā tattvapradīpe tu aabhyupagamavādatvāt'; ityādinā ayaṃ prāṇo viṣṇurityabhyupetya vādena bhāṣyaṃ pravṛttam, ityuktam । tathā cādyapakṣe prāṇaḥ aāśāyāḥ'; bhāratyāḥ abhūyān'; guṇato jyeṣṭhaḥ । evaṃ aprāṇaḥ'; tadantaryāmī viṣṇurantaryāmitvādeva tata āśāyāśca bhūyānityarthaḥ । anena pūrvamānandamayaśabdoktasajātīyotkṛṣṭatvarūpapūrṇatvasyeha vāyāvākṣepādānandamayādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiḥ sūcitā । chāndogaśrutyukto bhūmākhyo viṣayaḥ, kiṃ vāyuruta viṣṇuriti sandehaśca sūcitaḥ । tathā tasyaiva bhūmatvaprāptiriti pūrvapakṣaḥ । tatra prāṇopakramataduttamānuktirūpayuktiśca darśitā bhavati । ayo vai bhūmā tatsukhaṃ nālpe sukhamasti bhūmaiva sukham'; iti vākye sukhaśabdaḥ pūrṇasukhārthaḥ । ayatsukhaṃ sa bhūmā'; iti vyāsatīrthīyokteḥ, sarvanāmāni paryāyeṇa tattalliṅgabhāñjītyukteśca nirupapadasukhaśabdamātrasyāpi pūrṇasukhārthatvāt । yadananyādhīnapūrṇānandasukhaṃ sa bhūmā guṇataḥ pūrṇo nārāyaṇa ityuddeśyavidheyayorvyatyayaḥ । ata eva svātantryeṇa sukhasya viśeṣaṇāt na muktajīveṣvanaikāntyamityāśayena tadupapādayati - nālpa iti । aalpe'; apūrṇe muktajīve tatprasādaṃ vinā yataḥ sukhaṃ nāstītyarthaḥ । nigamayati - bhūmaiva sukhamiti ।

autkrāntaprāṇān'; ityāditalliṅgatprāṇaśabdaśca vāyuvācīti ।

nanu aprāṇo vā āśāyā bhūyān'; ityuktaprāṇaśabdasya aata eva prāṇaḥ'; ityuktarītyā viṣṇuparatvādviṣṇoreva bhūmatvaprāpteḥ kathaṃ prāṇaśabdabalādvāyorbhūmatvaprāptirityata āha - utkrānteti ।। ityādīti । luptavibhaktiko nirdeśaḥ । ādiśabdena autkrāntaprāṇān śūlena samāsaṃ vyatiṣaṃ dahet nainaṃ brūyuḥ pitṛhāsīti'; samagravākyaṃ gṛhyate । tacca tat liṅgaṃ ca, tasya liṅgamiti ca vigrahaḥ । ayamiti śeṣaḥ । caśabdo avadhāraṇe । vāyuvācī ceti bhinnakramaḥ । tathā ca aayaṃ'; prāṇaśabdo avāyuvācyeva'; na viṣṇuvācī । kutaḥ? autkrāntaprāṇān'; ityādau atalliṅgāt'; tasya prāṇasyotkramaṇādirūpaliṅgaśravaṇāditi yojanā । utkrāntaḥ prāṇo yebhyaste tathoktāḥ । tānmātṛpitrācāryādīn asamāsaṃ'; sākalyena avyatiṣam'; ekadeśena ca śūlena viluṇṭhya yadi dahetputraḥ śiṣyo vā tathā nainaṃ brūyuḥ janāḥ । kimiti? - pitṛhāsīti mātṛhāsīti । mukhyaprāṇasannidhānābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ ।

ato vakti - sū - oṃ ।।
bhūmā saṃprasādādadhyupadeśāt ।
।।

asamprasādāt'; pūrṇasukharūpatvāt aadhyupadeśāt'; sarveṣāmuparyupadeśācca viṣṇureva bhūmā ।

siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati - ata iti ।। sūtre prasīdatyanena jana iti prasādaḥ sukham, samyakprasādaḥ samprasādaḥ, tasmāditi vigraharḥ । iśvare sukhamiva duḥkhamapi syāditi nāśaṅkyaṃ, pūrṇasukhakāryeṇa samyakprasādena duḥkhābhāvaniścayādityāśayena prayuktaṃ samprasādāditi hetumanūdya vyācaṣṭe - samprasādāditi । uttarasūtrasthacaśabdo atrākarṣaṇīya ityāśayena aadhyupadeśāt'; ityetaddhetvantaraparatayānūdya vyākhyāti - adhyupadeśāditi ।। nāmādīnāṃ sarveṣām aupari'; taduttamatvena aupadeśāt'; ukterityarthaḥ । atrādhītyeva hetuḥ, na tu samagra eko hetuḥ । sa ceśvaravacano bhāvapradhānaḥ, viśeṣānukteḥ akhileśvaratvāditi hetvarthaḥ akhileśatvādityanuvyākhyānasudhokto jñātavyaḥ । asiddhiparihārāyopadeśaparyantaṃ dhāvanam । prāyapāṭhādbhūmno akhilādhipaprāṇādhipatye akhilādhipatyaṃ siddhyatīti bhāvaḥ । samanvayasūtrādanuvṛttasya tattvitividheyasamarpakasyārthamāha - viṣṇureveti bhūmā viṣṇurevetyanvayaḥ।

asahasraśīrṣaṃ devaṃ viśvākṣaṃ viśvaśambhuvam ।
viśvaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ devamakṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam ।।

viśvataḥ paramāṃ nityam'; iti hi śrutiḥ ।

pūrṇasukhatvādikaṃ kuto viṣṇutvaniścāyakamityata āha - sahasreti ।। iti hīti । ahi'; yasmāt aiti'; nārāyaṇānuvākagatā śrutirasti, tasmātsamprasādāt viṣṇutvaniścayo bhavatyevetyarthaḥ । asahasraśīrṣaṃ'; sahasrapadopalakṣitāmitamūrdhānaṃ adevaṃ'; prakāśarūpaṃ viśvato darśanādakṣyasyeti viśvākṣaṃ aviśvaśambhuvaṃ'; pūrṇasukhāśrayaṃ aviśvaṃ'; jagatpraviṣṭatvena vartamānaṃ anārāyaṇaṃ'; muktasaṅghe vyaktam aakṣaraṃ'; svarūpato nāśarahitam akṣeṣu ramamāṇaṃ vā । parebhyo brahmādibhyo adhikatvena mīyata iti parā mā yasyeti vā paramastaṃ paramaṃ apadaṃ'; prāpyaṃ viśvataḥ paramaścāsāvaśceti vigrahaḥ, savarṇadīrghaḥ । somapāśabdavadayaṃ śabdaḥ । sudhārītyā ābantatvāśrayeṇa liṅgavyatyayo vā । tathā ca aviśvataḥparamāṃ'; sarvasmāduttamam akāravācyaṃ sarvottamaṃ vā anityaṃ'; dehato nāśarahitaṃ aviśvaṃ'; guṇaiḥ pūrṇaṃ yajñeṣu haviḥsvīkaraṇāt harivarṇatvācca ahariṃ'; adevaṃ'; krīḍādiguṇakaṃ anārāyaṇaṃ'; tadākhyaṃ devaṃ tadviśvamupajīvatīti śrutyarthaḥ । yadyapi viśvataḥ paramam iti drāviḍapāṭhaḥ । tathāpyāndhrapāṭhamanusṛtya paramāmityuktam ।

atamutkrāmantaṃ prāṇo anūtkrāmati'; ityādinā notkramaṇādiliṅgavirodho api ।।

atra prāṇaśabdena viṣṇorvācyatvāṅgīkāre prāguktatkramaṇādiliṅgavirodha ityato netyāha - tamiti ।। prathamādiśabdena taduttaravākyāni dvitīyena talliṅgāntarāṇi ca gṛhyante । apiśabdaḥ samuccaye, yadyapi tathāpītyarthe ca । tathā ca - na kevalaṃ prāṇaśabdopakramavirodhaḥ, tasya viṣṇuparatvāt, kintu aapi'; atra prāṇaśabdena viṣṇorvācyatvāṅgīkāre utkramaṇādiliṅgavirodho nāsti । kutaḥ? aapi'; tathāpi sarvagate api viṣṇāvutkramaṇādiliṅgasya atamutkrāmantam'; ityādinā vājasaneyavākyena siddhatvāditi yojanā । śrutisiddher'the lokadṛṣṭivirodho akiñcitkara iti bhāvaḥ । atasya haitasya hṛdayasyāgraṃ pradyotate । tena pradyotenaiṣa ātmā niṣkrāmati'; iti pūrvavākye prakṛtaḥ paramātmā tacchabdena parāmṛśyate । tathā ca pradyotitahṛdayāgreṇāparokṣajñānidehāt autkrāmantaṃ'; nirgacchantaṃ paramātmānamanusṛtya aprāṇo'; mukhyavāyuḥ autkrāmati'; dehānnirgacchatīti śrutyarthaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। dharmopapatteś ca ।।
sarvagatatvādidharmopapatteśca ।।
।। iti bhūmādhikaraṇam ।।

yuktyantareṇa viṣṇorbhūmatvapratipādakaṃ sūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe - dharmeti ।। ādipadena svātantryasvapratiṣṭhitvādikaṃ gṛhyate । asya hetorviṣṇureva bhūmeti pradhānasādhyenānvayaḥ । yadyapi chāndogye ayatra nānyat'; iti svātantryabodhakavākyānantaraṃ asa evādhastāt'; iti sarvagatatvābhidhāyakavākyaśravaṇāt prathamaśrutasvātantryadharmaṃ svaśabdena gṛhītvā sarvagatatvāmādiśabdena grāhyam । tathāpi tadvākye bhūmatvaniyatasarvagatatvasya spaṣṭaṃ pratītestadeva vācakaśabdena gṛhītamiti draṣṭavyam । anena - sūtre co yuktisamuccaye dharmaśabdātparamanveti । liṅgasya niravakāśatvajñāpanāyopapattiparyantaṃ dhāvanam । tathā ca na kevalaṃ samprasādādeḥ, kintu asa evādhastātsa upariṣṭātsa paścātsa purastātsa dakṣiṇataḥ sa uttarataḥ sa evedaṃ sarvam'; iti vākye, tathā - ayatra nānyatpaśyati nānyacchṛṇoti nānyadvijānāti sa bhūmā'; iti vākye, tathā - asa bhagavaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti sve mahimni'; ityādi vākye ca sarvagatatvādidharmaśravaṇācca bhūmā viṣṇureva, teṣāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ viṣṇāvevopapatteriti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । asaḥ'; bhūmaśabdito nārāyaṇaḥ adhaḥ upari paścātpurastāddakṣiṇata uttarataḥ sarvatrāsti । tatprayojanamāha - sa evedaṃ sarvamiti । tenaivedaṃ jagadvyāptaṃ sa eva sarvasattāpradastadarthameva sarvatra tiṣṭhatītyarthaḥ । ayatra'; yadvinā yadadhīnaṃ vinā anyannapaśyatyadhikārī sarvameva tadadhīnaṃ paśyati, tathaiva śṛṇoti, vijānāti ca sa bhūmetyarthaḥ । ayatra'; yasmin dṛṣṭe anyatsvatantraṃ na paśyatīti vā । he abhagavo'; bhagavān sa bhūmā kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti nāradapraśne mahimaguṇātmake asve'; svasmin svakīye mahimni vā svayaṃ apratiṣṭhitaḥ'; āśrita iti sanatkumāraḥ pratyāheti śrutyarthaḥ ।।

।। iti bhūmādhikaraṇam ।।

।। akṣarādhikaraṇam ।।

adṛśyatvādiguṇā viṣṇoruktāḥ । aadṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭraśrutaṃ śrotṛ'; ityādinā । aahaṃ somamāhanasaṃ bibharmi'; ityādestasyāpi sambhavānmadhyamākṣarasyoktā iti ।

atrādhikaraṇe akṣaranāmasamanvayaḥ kriyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyamudāhṛtya viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayan sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ ca darśayati -adṛśyatvādīti ।। ādyādiśabdenāgrāhyatvādi gṛhyate । guṇā ityanena candrādityādyādhāratvaguṇo api gṛhyate । dvitīyādiśabdena aaśrutaṃ śrotramataṃ mantravijñātaṃ vijñātṛnānyadato asti draṣṭṛ nānyadato asti śrotṛ nānyadato asti mantṛ nānyadato asti vijñātṛ etasmin khalvakṣare gārgyākāśa otaśca protaśca'; iti śiṣṭavākyam, tathā - aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ'; iti vākyaṃ ca gṛhyate । tṛtīyādiśabdena aahaṃ tvaṣṭāramuta pūṣaṇaṃ bhagam'; iti vākyam, tathā - ye tvakṣaramanirdeśyamavyaktaṃ paryupāsate । sarvatragamacintyaṃ ca kūṭasthamacalaṃ dhruvam ।। 
iti gītāvākyam ।
āsīdidaṃ tamobhūtamaprajñātamalakṣaṇam ।
apratarkyamavijñeyaṃ prasuptamiva sarvataḥ ।।

iti tadbhāṣyodāhṛtavākyaṃ ca gṛhyate । caśabdenākṣaraśabdasya śrītattve prasiddheśceti akṣarapadasūcito hetuḥ samuccīyate । tasyetipadamāvartate, vipariṇamyate ca । na kevalaṃ viṣṇoreva, kintu atasya'; akṣarasyāpītyaperarthaḥ । viṣṇujaḍavyāvṛttyarthaṃ - madhyameti । abhūmatvaprāptiḥ'; iti pūrvapākyādbuddhyā vivekena prāptiritipadamatrānuvartate । tathā ca - pūrvamadṛśyatvādhikaraṇe ye adṛśyatvādiguṇā akṣarasya viṣṇoruktāḥ । te vājasaneyake atadvā etadakṣaraṃ gārgi adṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭṛ'; ityādinā vākyena amadhyamākṣarasya'; śrītattvasya auktāḥ'; ucyante ityekā yojanā । aparā tu - atasya'; teṣāmadṛśyatvādiguṇānāṃ atasya'; tasmin madhyamākṣare api sambhavādyuktatvāt atasya'; candrādyādhāratvaliṅgasyāpi aahaṃ somamāhanasam'; ityādivākyāttasminnakṣare upapatteḥ atasya'; akṣaraśabdasya tasmin madhyamākṣare prasiddheśca atasya'; madhyamākṣarasyāpi atasya'; akṣaranāmavācyatvasya prāptiriti । tatrādyayojanāyām adṛśyatvādhikaraṇoktādṛśyatvādiguṇakākṣarasya viṣṇvanyatvākṣepāttenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tathākṣarākhyo viṣayaḥ, draṣṭṛtvābhidhāyakottaravākyaparyālocanayā jaḍavyāvṛtteḥ । kiṃ cetanaprakṛtirutaviṣṇuriti saṃśayaśca sūcitaḥ । dvitīyayojanāyāṃ sayuktikaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ pradarśita iti jñātavyam । atadvā'; ityādeḥ siddhāntarītyāyamarthaḥ - atat'; ākāśāśrayatvena vakṣyamāṇam aakṣaraṃ'; na kṣaratītyakṣaraśabdavācyaṃ brahma aetat'; etallakṣaṇakaṃ ca prasiddham । tadevāha - adṛṣṭamityādinā । anyaiḥ sākalyena adṛṣṭatvātsvayaṃ draṣṭṛtvādadṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭrityucyate । evamuttaravākyamapi vyākhyeyam । draṣṭṛtvādau viśeṣamāha - neti । aataḥ'; akṣarādanyat svātantryeṇa draṣṭṛ śrotṛ mantṛ jñātṛ ca nāstītyarthaḥ । aetasmin'; evaṃbhūte akṣaraśabdite brahmaṇi dīptinimittākāśapadoktaṃ śrītattvam aotaśca protaśca'; atrotaṃ ca protaṃ ca । tathā ca sarvakāreṇa tadāśritaṃ khalvityarthaḥ । gārgīti yājñavalkyakartṛkapatnīsambodhanam । aetasya vā akṣarasya'; viṣṇoḥ apraśāsane'; ājñāyāmiti nimittasaptamī । tathā ca ājñāmātrāt asūryācandramasau'; akeśau sūryavidhū matau'; iti bṛhadbhāṣyokterbrahmarudrau bhāṣyaṭīkārītyā prasiddharavicandrau ca avidhṛtau'; viśeṣeṇa dhṛtau bhavata iti । pūrvapakṣī tu akṣaraśabdaṃ śrītattvaparaṃ manyate । tatpakṣe ākāśaśabdaḥ prakṛtyanyatatpoṣyaparaḥ । aham aāhanasaṃ'; svābhimanyamānalatādvārā yajñeṣvabhiṣūyamāṇaṃ asomaṃ'; somalatābhimāninaṃ candraṃ tvaṣṭāraṃ ca auta pūṣaṇaṃ'; pūṣaṇaṃ ca bhagaṃ ca abibharmi'; dadhāmītyaṃbhraṇīvākyasyārthaḥ । tvaṣṭrādayastu sūryaprabhedāḥ । tattvapradīpasattarkadīpāvalyostu bṛhadbhāṣyānusāreṇa asomam'; umayā sahitam aāhanasam'; āsamantāt hantāraṃ saṃhartāraṃ rudraṃ bibharmīti vyākhyātam । aakṣaraṃ'; dehato apyavināśi, aanirdeśyaṃ'; śabdāgocaraṃ, asarvatragaṃ'; deśato vyāptam, aacintyaṃ'; manasāgrāhyaṃ, guṇabāhulyāt, kūṭe ākāśe abhimānitvena tiṣṭhatīti akūṭastham', aacalaṃ'; kadāpi svapadādabhraṣṭaṃ adhruvam'; utpattivināśaśūnyam, aavyaktaṃ'; śrītattvaṃ ye paryupāsate iti gītārthaḥ । pralaye aabhūtam'; ajātam aaprajñātaṃ'; pratyakṣāvedyam avedyalakṣaṇatvādalakṣaṇam ata eva aatarkyam'; anumānāvedyam aavijñeyam'; āgamāvedyam anādyavidyābhimānitvāt, tamaḥśabdavācyamidaṃ lakṣmyākhyaṃ tattvaṃ aprasuptamiva'; nirvyāpāraṃ asarvataḥ'; sarvatrāsīditi smṛtyarthaḥ ।

ato brūte - sū - oṃ ।।
akṣaramambarāntadhṛteḥ ।
।।

aetasmin khalvakṣare gārgyākāśa otaśca protaśca'; ityambarāntasya sarvasya dhṛterbrahmaivākṣaram ।

siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati - ata iti ।। sūtre gahanārthatvātprathamaṃ hetubhāgaṃ vyākariṣyamāṇo asiddhiparihārāya śrutimudāharati - etasminniti । itītyanantaraṃ avākye'; iti śeṣaḥ । anyapadārthaṃ darśayanvigrahaṃ darśayati - ambareti । ambaramākāśaḥ anto yasya sarvasya pṛthivyāderdhārakatvokterityarthaḥ । yadyapi aetasmin'; iti vākye ambaradhṛtirevocyate । na tu tadantarasarvadhṛtiḥ । tathāpi ayadūrdhvaṃ gārgi divo yadarvākpṛthivyā yadantarā dyāvāpṛthivī ākāśa eva tadotaṃ ca protaṃ ca'; ityanenākāśasya citprakṛteḥ sarvādhāratvamuktvānantaram aetasmin'; iti vākye akṣarasya tādṛśaprakṛtyādhāratvokteḥ prakṛtidvārākṣarasyāmbarāntasarvādhāratvamatroktameveti na doṣaḥ । etacca sūtre ambarāntetyantapadaprayogātsūcitam । sūtre tattvityanuvṛttapadadvayopetapratijñābhāgaṃ vyākhyāti - brahmaiveti । akṣaraṃ brahmaivetyanvayaḥ । anena akṣarasya aetasmin'; iti prakṛtidvārā'kāśāntasarvādhāratvaśruterakṣaraṃ brahmaiveti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

ya u tridhātu pṛthivīmuta dyā meko dādhāra bhavanāni viśvā । 

sarvādhāratvaṃ kuto viṣṇutvaniścāyakamityataḥ tasya viṣṇuliṅgatvena śrutisiddhatvādityāha - ya iti ।। vyākhyāteyaṃ śrutirjanmanaye ।

bhartā sanbhriyamāṇo bibharti । eko devo bahudhā niviṣṭaḥ । yadā bhāraṃ tandrayate sa bhartum । parāsya bhāraṃ punarastameti । 

abhartā san'; iti taittirīyāṇāṃ śrutiḥ । adevaḥ'; prāṇākhyo bhagavān svayaṃ jagatā jīvena vā hṛdi bhriyamāṇaḥ tat abibharti'; dhatte puṣṇāti ca । tarhi jagadīśayoḥ sāmyāpattirityata āha - bhartā sanniti । jagato mūlabhartā sanneva bhriyamāṇaḥ, na svakīyasthityetyarthaḥ । nanvekasyaiva bhagavataḥ bhartā bhriyamāṇo bibhartītyanekavidhavyavahāraviṣayatvaṃ kathamityata āha - eko bahudheti । eko api bhartṛtvādinā abahudhā'; bahurūpeṇa ca aniviṣṭo'; vyāpta ityarthaḥ । tatra praviṣṭa iti vā । ayadā bhāraṃ tandrayate sa bhartuṃ parāsya bhāraṃ punarastameti'; iti vākyaśeṣaḥ । asa'; viṣṇuryadā taṃ jagadbhāraṃ aparāsya'; adho nidhāya punarbhartuṃ atandrayate'; necchati tadā asau bhāraḥ aastameti'; naśyatītyarthaḥ ।

yasminnidaṃ saṃcavicaidhi sarvaṃ yasmin devā adhi viśve niṣeduḥ ।

ayasmin'; ityapi taittirīye anyadvākyam । atra yacchabdasya atadeva brahma paramam'; ityuttaravākyasthatacchabdenānvayaḥ । cau prakārasamuccaye । tathā ca - ayasminnidaṃ'; sarvaṃ jagat asaṃ'; samyak avi'; vividhaṃ acaidhi'; avardhata । edhaterliṅi chāndasaṃ rūpametat । yadvā - edhivardhate । astīti vārthaḥ । asmin pakṣe asterlaṭi madhyamapuruṣaikavacane chāndasaṃ rūpam । vastuto loṭi madhyamapuruṣaikavacane rūpametat । yasmiṃśca aviśve'; sarve devāḥ aadhiniṣeduḥ'; yamadhyagustadeva brahmetyarthaḥ । ityādiśruterityasya ambarāntadhṛterityanenānvayaḥ । brahmaṇyavagatāyā iti śeṣaḥ । tṛtīyārthe pañcamī । ādiśabdena ayenāvṛtaṃ khaṃ ca divaṃ mahīṃ ca yenādityastapati tejasā bhrājasā ca'; ityādikam, atameva mṛtyumamṛtaṃ tamāhustaṃ bhartāraṃ tamu goptāramāhuḥ'; ityādi ca gṛhyate । tathā ca viṣṇuliṅgatvena śrutisiddhāt sarvādhāraṇāt viṣṇutvaniścayo bhavatyeveti bhāvaḥ ।

pṛthivyādi prakṛtyantaṃ bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhavacca yat ।
viṣṇureko bibhartīdaṃ nānyastasmātkṣamo dhṛtau ।।

iti ca skānde ।

viṣṇuvadanyasyāpi sarvādhāratvaṃ kiṃ na syādityata āha - pṛthivyādīti ।। prakṛtyantapadena sautrāntapadaṃ vyākhyātam । abhūtam'; atītaṃ abhavyaṃ'; bhaviṣyat abhavat'; vartamānaṃ ayat'; idaṃ viśvaṃ tadviṣṇuḥ aeka eva'; asahāyo bibharti । tasya dhṛtau tasmādviṣṇoranyaḥ akṣamaḥ'; samartho netyarthaḥ । iti skānda ityasya auktatvāt'; ityadhyāhāreṇa na sāvakāśatvaṃ liṅgasyeti vākyaśeṣeṇānvayaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। sā ca praśāsanāt ।।

sā ca dhṛtiḥ prasāsanāducyate । aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ'; ityādinā ।

yuktyantareṇa viṣṇorevākṣaratvaṃ pratipādayatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe - sā ceti ।। asā ca'; sarvadhṛtirapi ityādinā praśāsanāducyate yato ato api brahmākṣaramityanvayaḥ । ādiśabdenaivaṃrūpāṇyekaprakaraṇagatānekavākyāni gṛhyante । anena - yadā asā'; pūrvoktā sarvadhṛtireva akṣarasya viṣṇutvasādhikā, tadā sutarāṃ, yā tu aetasya'; iti śrutivākye akṣarasya praśāsanādeva asaṅkucitaviṣayānanyāyattaprakṛṣṭājñāmātrādeva sarvadhṛtirucyate seti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

tacca praśāsanaṃ viṣṇoreva ।

nanu sarvadhṛtihetupraśāsanena kuto akṣarasya viṣṇutvaniścaya ityatastasya viṣṇukartṛkatvādityāha - tacceti। sarvadhṛtikāraṇaṃ praśāsanaṃ tvityarthaḥ । na kevalaṃ sarvadhṛtiḥ, kintu taddhetupraśāsanaṃ ceti samuccaye vā caśabdaḥ । aviṣṇoreva'; viṣṇukartṛkameva । na tvanyakartṛkamiti evārthaḥ । evakārasyottaratropayogaḥ ।

saptārdhagarbhā bhuvanasya reto viṣṇostiṣṭhanti pradiśā vidharmaṇi । 

kuta etajjñāyata ityatastaccetyanena pratijñātārthe śrutiṃ pramāṇayati - sapteti ।। ā ṛddhagarbhāḥ ārdhagarbhāḥ । brahmāṇḍākhyātisamṛddhagarbhāḥ । nigaraṇena bhriyanta iti garbhāstadāvaraṇabhūtā iti yāvat । reta iti liṅgavyatyayenaikavacanaṃ prathamābahuvacanārthe । tathā ca - abhuvanasya'; lokasya aretaso'; ratipradāḥ sārabhūtā vā । yadvā - bhūmatvātpūrṇatvādvananīyatvādbhajanīyatvādbhuvanasya viṣṇo retorūpāḥ asapta'; mahadahaṅkārapañcamahābhūtākhyāḥ brahmādayo devāḥ । bhavanasya areto'; retaso jagadratipradasya viṣṇoḥ apradiśā'; ādeśenājñayā avidharmaṇi'; vividhaviśvadhāraṇe tiṣṭhantīti ṛṅmantrārthaḥ । viśveśvaratīrthīye tu aardhasya'; viṣṇoḥ agarbhāḥ'; sapta devāḥ bhuvanasya aretaḥ'; kāraṇam । ete ca viṣṇoḥ pradiśā vidharmaṇi tiṣṭhantītyartha uktaḥ ।

caturbhissākaṃ navatiṃ ca nāmabhiścakraṃ na vṛttaṃ vyatīravīvipat ।

acaturbhiḥ'; iti vākyaṃ tu janmanaye vyākhyātam । evaṃjātīyakaśrutirādiśabdārthaḥ । śruterityasya jñāyata ityadhyāhāreṇa tacceti pūrvavākyenānvayaḥ ।

ekaśśāstā na dvitīyo asti śāstā । yo hṛcchayastamahamiha bravīmi ।

sarvadhṛtihetupraśāsanaṃ viṣṇorivānyasyāpi kiṃ na syādityata āha - eka iti ।। idaṃ ca bhāratavākyaṃ sabhāparvagam । aśāstā'; sarvadhṛtihetvājñākartā । aekaḥ'; na tu dvitīyo asti, sa ca viṣṇurevetyarthaḥ । agarbhe śayānaṃ puruṣaṃ ko asti śāstā'; iti śiṣṭavākyam । ayo hṛcchayaḥ'; ityanyadvākyamuttaravākyaparyālocanayā prakṛtasaṅgatam । ayaḥ'; sarvadhṛtihetupraśāsanāya ahṛcchayaḥ'; sarvahṛdayanivāsī tamahamiha sthāne bravīmītyarthaḥ ।

na kevalaṃ me bhavataśca rājan । sa vai balaṃ balināṃ cāpareṣām । ityādeśca ।।

ana kevalam'; ityādi hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prati prahlādavākyam । he rājan na kevalaṃ me bhavataśca asaḥ'; bhagavān abalaṃ'; balaprado dhṛtihetuḥ, kintvanyeṣāṃ balināṃ ca balamityarthaḥ । ityādeścetyasya atacca praśāsanaṃ viṣṇoreveti jñāyate'; ityanenānvayaḥ । anena viṣṇorevetyevakārasya kṛtyaṃ sūcitam ।

sū - oṃ ।। anyabhāvavyāvṛtteśca ।।

aasthūlamanaṇu'; ityādinā sthūlāṇvādīnāmanyavastusvabhāvānāṃ vyāvṛtteśca ।

hetvantareṇa viṣṇorevākṣaratvaṃ pratipādayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe - anyeti ।। ādiśabdena aetadvai tadakṣaraṃ gārgi brāhmaṇā abhivadanti asthūlamanaṇvahrasvamadīrghamalohitamasnehamacchāyamatamo avāyvanākāśamasaṅgamarasamagandhamacakṣuṣkamaśrotramavāgamano atejaskamapramāṇamamukhamamātramanantaramabrāhmaṃ na tadaśnāti kiñcana na tadaśnāti kaścana'; iti samagravākyaṃ gṛhyate । asthūlāṇvādīnām'; iti bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ । vyāvṛtterityanantaraṃ akathanāt'; iti śeṣaḥ । asyāpi brahmaivākṣaramiti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । anena - na kevalaṃ pūrvoktahetubhyāṃ, kintvanyeṣāṃ sakalavastūnāṃ bhāvānāṃ svarūpāṇāṃ sthaulyādidharmāṇāṃ vyāvṛtteḥ ananyāpekṣārāhityasya aasthūlam'; ityādinākṣare kathanādapyakṣaraṃ brahmaiveti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । śrutyarthastu - atat'; ākāśāśrayatvena vakṣyamāṇam aakṣaraṃ'; na kṣaratītyakṣaraśabdavācyaṃ brahma etallakṣaṇakaṃ abrāhmaṇāḥ'; jñānino abhivadanti vai prasiddham । tatkiṃ lakṣaṇamityata āha - asthūlamiti । svaprabuddhārthāntaraṃ tu - aetat'; akṣaraṃ brāhmaṇāḥ atat'; citprakṛtyākhyamiti vadanti pūrvapakṣayanti tadbrahmetyabhivadanti siddhāntayanti । siddhāntasādhakaṃ hetumevāha - asthūlamityādineti । anena aprasiddhasthūlasūkṣmādivailakṣaṇyājjanārdanaḥ'; iti bṛhadbhāṣyoktarītyā prasiddhasthūlādivailakṣaṇyamucyate । sthūlāṇvādipadasya bhāvapradhānatve tu lokikasthaulyādirāhityamanenoktaṃ bhavati । aalohitaṃ'; lohitaśabditaraktādyupalakṣitaprākṛtarūpasāmānyarahitam । aasnehaṃ'; prākṛtasneharahitam । aacchāyaṃ'; achāyātvavidyā samproktā'; iti vacanādajñānarahitam । jīvadehasyeva chāyārahitaṃ ca । aatamaḥ'; āvaraṇarahitam । aavāyu'; pīḍārūpaśvāsocchvāsarahitam । yadvā - vyāsatīrthīyoktarītyā avāyvanākāśamatejaskamityetaistadārabdhaśarīrarahitamityucyate । ata eva aacchāyamatamo avāyvanākāśam'; ityatra sarvātmanā niṣedha ityuktaṃ sudhāṭīkayoḥ। aasaṅgaṃ'; sarvagatamapi tatkṛtaleparahitam । arasamagandhamityābhyāmupalakṣaṇayā prākṛtarasagandhādirāhityamucyate । acakṣuṣkamityādinā prākṛtasvabhinnacakṣurādirāhityam । aatejaskaṃ'; prākṛtavarcorahitam । aaprāṇam'; uktacakṣurādivyatiriktaprākṛtajñānendriyakarmendriyarahitam । vyāsatīrthīyoktarītyā prāṇavāyurahitamiti vā । aamukhaṃ'; prākṛtavigraharahitaṃ vā । aamātraṃ'; parimitiśūnyam । mīyante ebhiriti mātrā indriyāṇīti ṭīkokteḥ amātraṃ cakṣurādīndriyarahitamiti vyāsatīrthīyoktiḥ । sarvātmanā śarīrārambhakapañcamātraśūnyaṃ vā । na vidyate antaraṃ bāhyaṃ ca yasmāttadanantaramabāhyam, idameva sarvasmādantaraṃ bāhyaṃ cetyarthaḥ । atat'; brahma akiṃ ca na'; annādikaṃ śubhamaśubhaṃ vā sāśanānaśanatvena naradevau yathoditau । attiṃ vināpyadaurbalyāttathānattirharerbhujiḥ ।।

iti smṛterupajīvanārthaṃ anāśnāti'; nātti । akaścana'; ko api samarthaḥ atat'; brahma anāśnāti'; na saṃharatīti ।

aasthūlo anaṇuramadhyamo madhyamo avyāpako vyāpako yo asau harirādiranādiraviśvo viśvaḥ saguṇo nirguṇaḥ'; ityāderviṣṇoreva te dharmāḥ ।

laukikasthaulyādirāhityaṃ kathaṃ viṣṇutvaniścāyakaṃ, taddharmatvenāniścitatvādityata āha - asthūla iti। aasthūlaḥ'; laukikamahattvarahitaḥ, aanaṇuḥ'; laukikāṇutvarahitaḥ, aamadhyamaḥ'; laukikamadhyamaparimāṇarahitaḥ । na ca parimāṇādirāhitye viṣṇorasvabhāvatvāpattiriti vācyam । laukikasthaulyādirāhitye apyalaukikaparimāṇādisadbhāvādityāha - madhyama ityādinā ।। na cānena sthūlatvāderanukternacoktaparihāra iti vācyam । amadhyamo vyāpakaḥ'; ityādyukteḥ sthūlo aṇuścetyupalakṣakatvāt । na camadhyamaparimāṇavattve viṣṇoranityatvāpattiriti vācyam । anityatvānāpādakamadhyamaparimāṇābhyupagamāt । tattvapradīpe tu aamadhyamo'; madhyamaparimāṇaniyativarjitaḥ avyāpto aṇurmadhyamastathā'; ityukteḥ madhye mīyamānatvānmadhyama iti vyākhyātam । asmin pakṣe niyatamadhyamaparimāṇa- śūnyatvānnānityatvamiti parihāro abhipretaḥ । na vidyate anyo vyāpako yasyāsāvavyāpakaḥ । lokavilakṣaṇavyāpaka iti vā । avyāpakaḥ'; sarvadeśakālavyāpī । ādiḥ kāraṇamanādistacchūnya utpattiśūnya iti vā । na vidyate viśvaḥ pūrṇo yasmādaviśvaḥ । pūrṇatvādviśvaḥ । yadvā - aaviśvo'; laukikeṣvapraviṣṭaḥ । aviśvaḥ'; jagaddhṛdayaṃ vā praviṣṭaḥ । asaguṇo'; jñānānandādiguṇavān । anirguṇaḥ'; sattvādiguṇahīna ityarthaḥ । aityādeḥ'; itivākyāt । ādiśabdena aaṇoraṇīyānmahatomahīyān'; iti kaṭhaśrutirgṛhyate । ate'; asthūlatvādayaḥ । yata iti niścitā iti śeṣaḥ । asya ataste akṣarasya viṣṇutvaniścāyakā bhavantītyupaskṛtavākyenānvayaḥ । nanu tathāpi te viṣṇoreveti kathaṃ, yasmātte aprākṛtavigrahe madhyamākṣare api santi । naiṣa doṣaḥ - yataste yatra bhagavadapekṣayaiva santi । anyānapekṣā eva dharmāhyatra hetutvena vivakṣitāḥ ।

asthūlo anaṇurūpo asāvaviśvo viśva eva ca ।
viruddhadharmarūpo asāvaiśvaryātpuruṣottamaḥ ।।
iti ca brāhme ।।
।। iti akṣarādhikaraṇam ।।

nanu laukikaparimāṇādirāhityaṃ kathaṃ viṣṇoryuktaṃ, loke sarvapadārthānāṃ prākṛtaparimāṇasyaiva darśanādityata āha - asthūleti ।। aasau puruṣottamaḥ'; bhagavān aasthūlo anaṇurūpo bhavati'; prākṛtalaukikasthūlāṇutvarūpadharmarahitavapurbhavati । evaṃ aaviśvo viśvaśca'; lokabahirbhūto lokāntargataśca bhavati । tathā viruddhadharmarūpaśca bhavati । loke parasparaṃ viruddhāḥ sthūlatvāṇutvādayo dharmāḥ svarūpabhūtā yasya saḥ tathoktaḥ । kathamityato ghaṭakamāha - aiśvaryāditi ।। acintyaiśvaryasāmarthyādityarthaḥ । aiśvaryādevetyanena nātropapādakāntaramanveṣaṇīyamutyuktaṃ bhavati । iti brahmāṇḍe ityasya uktatvāt yuktā ityadhyāhāreṇa te dharmāḥ viṣṇoryuktā eveti pūrvavākyenānvayaḥ ।। iti akṣarādhikaraṇam ।।

।।

asadeva somyedamagra āsīt'; ityādinā sataḥ sraṣṭṛtvamucyate ।

atrādhikaraṇe anekaprakaraṇātmakaṃ asadeva'; ityādisthānaṃ samanvīyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyamudāhṛsya viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayati - saditi ।। aityādinā'; chāndogyavākyena । ādiśabdena aekamevādvitīyaṃ, tattejo asṛjata, sanmūlāḥ somyemāḥ, satā somya tadā sampanno bhavati'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । taccetyataḥ tadityākṛṣyate । tathā ca ityādinā sataḥ atat'; janmanayoktaṃ asraṣṭṛtvam'; ananyādhīnakāraṇatvam । sarvottamatvasarvādhāratvasuptigamyatvādikaṃ ca aucyate'; pratipādyate iti yojanā । anena janmādhikaraṇoktakāraṇatvasya viṣṇvanyasmin pradhāne ākṣepāttenāsya ākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tathā viṣayavākyam, sadākhyo viṣayaścoktaḥ । asadeva'; ityuddālakavākyam । he asomya'; bhaktijñānalakṣaṇasomārha śvetaketho aidam'; asya jagataḥ aagre'; tatsṛṣṭeḥ pūrvaṃ pralaye sacchabdoktaṃ brahmaivāsīt svātantryeṇeti śeṣaḥ। tatsat aekamevādvitīyaṃ'; svagatasvāvayavabhedābhedaśūnyaṃ sarvottamam । prajāḥ asanmūlāḥ'; sadbrahmaiva mūlaṃ yāsāṃ tāstathoktāḥ । atadā'; suptau satā sampanno bhavati supta iti siddhānte śrutyarthaḥ । brahmalakṣaṇābhidhāyakānekavākyasaṅgrahakādiśabdaprayogena siddhānte apyatra pradhānasya pratipādyatvābhyupagamenāniṣṭābhāvādadhikaraṇavaiyarthyamiti śaṅkā nirastā bhavati । atra prakaraṇe śrutānāṃ brahmalakṣaṇānāṃ pradhāne asambhavena brahmaṇo api pratipādyatvena pradhānamātrasya pratipādyatvānabhyupagamāt ।

tacca sat abahu syāṃ prajāyeya'; iti pariṇāmapratīterna viṣṇuḥ ।
