sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣayati - tacceti ।। ca śabdaḥ pradhānamiti padākarṣako avadhāraṇe ca । tadityāvṛttaṃ vipariṇamyate । tathā ca atat'; chāndogye śrutaṃ satpradhānameva bhavet, na tu viṣṇuḥ । kutaḥ ? atasya'; sato abahu syām'; ityuttaravākyena bahubhāvākhyapariṇāmasya vikārasya pratīteriti yojanā । aprajāyeya'; prajanayeyaṃ jagatsṛjāni। tadarthaṃ abahu syām'; niyāmakabahurūpī bhaveyamiti । abahu syām'; tadarthaṃ prajāyeyeti vā śrutyarthaḥ ।

sa hi aavikārassadā śuddho nitya ātmā sadā hariḥ'; ityādināvikāra prasiddha iti ।

vikāritvapratītāvapi kuto ayaṃ na viṣṇurityata āha - sa hīti ।। ahi'; yasmāt asaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ aavikāraḥ sadā'; ityādipramāṇairavikāraḥ aprasiddhaḥ'; tattvena niścitastasmāt tadasambhavāt pradhāne ca tatsambhavāt atra ca vikārapratīteḥ tatsat na viṣṇuḥ, kintu pradhānameveti yojanā । śrutau dvitīyasya sadāśabdasya sadāvikāra ityanvayaḥ । ādyasya tu sadā aśuddho'; nirmala iti ।

ato bravīti - sū - oṃ ।।
īkṣatikarmavyapadeśāt saḥ ।
।।

atadaikṣata'; itīkṣatikarmavyapadeśātsa eva viṣṇuratrocyate ।

siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe - ata iti ।। sūtroktaṃ vyapadeśaṃ darśayati - taditir । ikṣatīti dhātunirdeśena tadarthekṣaṇakriyā lakṣyater । ikṣatikarmeti sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ tatkartṛtvaparam । tathā ca atadaikṣata'; iti śrutāvīkṣaṇākhyavyāpāre kartṛtvokterityarthaḥ। yadvā karmaśabdena sṛṣṭyādikriyocyate । tathātve vaiyadhikaraṇyarm । ikṣatipūrvakasṛṣṭyādivyapadeśādityarthaḥ । samanvayasūtrāttadityasya anuṣaṅgasambhave api aeko nārāyaṇa āsītsamunirbhūtvā'; ityādisamākhyāmapi pramāṇīkartuṃ sa ityuktam । tadanūdya viṣṇuriti vyākhyātam । viṣṇurevetyanvayaḥ । eveti tu śabdārthaḥ । anena samanvayasūtrāttuśabdamātramanuvartanīyamiti sūcitam । sūtre samanvetavyānukterāha - atreti । asadeva'; ityādisthāna ityarthaḥ । sacchabdeneti pradhānamiti sādhyavākyārthaḥ । anena atra sadevetyādisthāne sacchabdenocyamānaḥ sa viṣṇureva, na pradhānam । kutarḥ ? aikṣatikarmavyapadeśāt saḥ'; tataḥ atadaikṣata'; itīkṣaṇākhyakriyākartṛtvaśravaṇādīkṣitṛtvasṛṣṭyādikriyayorvā śravaṇājjaḍaprakṛtau ca tadasambhavāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । sūtre sacchabdeneti śeṣaṃ vinā sa ityasyāvṛttiḥ, tatraikasya pratīkagrahaṇārthatvamiti pakṣer ikṣatikarmavyapadeśāt asaḥ'; aso akāmayata'; ityādiprakaraṇapratipādyaḥ sa viṣṇureva bhavet, na pradhānamitayartho avaseyaḥ ।

anānyo ato asti draṣṭā'; anānyadato asti draṣṭṛ'; ityādinā tasyaiva hi tallakṣaṇam ।

nanvīkṣaṇakartṛtvaṃ viṣṇuvatpradhānasya kiṃ na syādityataścetanasyāpi iha hetutvenābhimataṃ mukhyekṣaṇaṃ na sambhavati, kimu jaḍasyetyāśayena tatra pramāṇamāha - neti ।। aato'; brahmaṇaḥ sakāśāt aanyaḥ'; svātantryeṇa draṣṭā draṣṭṛ ca nāstīti vājasaneyaprakaraṇadvayagatavākyadvayasyārthaḥ । ādiśabdenaivaṃjātīyakaṃ vākyaṃ gṛhyate । atasya'; viṣṇoreva । hi śabdaḥ prasiddhau । svātantryeṇekṣaṇakartṛtvalakṣaṇaṃ liṅgaṃ uktamiti śeṣaḥ । asya tasmānna liṅgasya anyagāmitvaṃ mantavyamityupaskṛtavākyenānvayaḥ ।

bahutvaṃ cāvikāreṇaivoktam aajāyamāno bahudhā vijāyate'; iti ।।
।। iti sadadhikaraṇam ।।

nanu viṣṇoravikāritayā siddhatvena tatra bahubhāvākhyavikārānvayāyogānniravakāśavikāritvaliṅgenātrekṣatirgauṇo vyākhyeyaḥ । asattvātsañjāyate jñānam'; iti smaraṇāt jñānopādānatayā siddhe pradhāne tatkartṛtvāsambhavena tatra tasyāmukhyatvādityata āha - bahutvaṃ ceti ।। aavikāreṇa'; vikāritvaṃ vinaiva svarūpabahutvenaivetyarthaḥ। ityādinoktamityanvayaḥ। tathā ca bahutvasya sāvakāśatvāt na tadbalenar ikṣatergauṇatvaṃ kalpanīyamiti bhāvaḥ। yadvā - abahutvaṃ'; abahu syām'; iti bahubhāvavacanaṃ ca auktaṃ'; vyākhyātam । tathā ca ityevamādipramāṇavākyena abahu syām'; iti bahubhāvavacanam aavikāreṇa'; vikāraṃ vinaiva niyāmakasvarūpabahutvenaiva mukhyapratipādyenaiva yuktamityuktam iti yojanā । tathā ca - siddhānte abahu syām'; ityasya tattanniyāmakasvarūpabahubhāvasaṅkalpor'tha ityuktaṃ bhavati । na caivaṃ niyāmakasvarūpabahubhāvasaṅkalpānantaraṃ niyamyasṛṣṭirayukteti vācyam । gurutvarājatvādeḥ śiṣyabhṛtyasāpekṣatvena tatsaṅkalpānantaraṃ śiṣyādisampādanavat niyāmakatāyā niyamyasāpekṣatvena niyāmakabahubhāvasaṅkalpānantaraṃ tatsāpekṣaniyamyasṛṣṭeryuktatvāt aajāyamānaḥ'; avikurvāṇaḥ iti śrutyarthastu dyubhvādinaye abhihitaḥ ।।

।। iti sadadhikaraṇam ।।

।। daharādhikaraṇam ।।

candrādityādyādhāratvaṃ viṣṇoruktam । tacca aatha yadidamasmin brahmapure daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ veśma daharo asminnantara ākāśaḥ kiṃ tadatra vidyate a; aubhe asmin dyāvāpṛthivī antareva samāhite ubhāvagniśca vāyuśca sūryācandramasāvubhau vidyunnakṣatrāṇi'; ityādinā'kāśasya pratīyate ।

atrādhikaraṇe sarvādhāratayānveṣṭavyatayā ca sākṣādvā vyavadhānena vā sāmānyato hṛtpadmasthatvaliṅgasya brahmaṇi samanvayaḥ kriyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyamudāhṛtya viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayan sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣayati - candreti ।। aetasya vā akṣarasya'; ityādineti vartate । ādipadena dyāvāpṛthivyādikaṃ gṛhyate । tataḥ kimityata āha - tacceti ।। caḥ samuccaye avadhāraṇe ca । tathā ca atatra'; chandogaśrutau yadakṣaranayodāhṛtavākyoktaṃ candrādityādhāratvaṃ tadeva tathā tatsamānādhikaraṇaṃ hṛtpadmasthatvaṃ ca ākāśasya aatha'; ityādinā vākyena pratīyata iti yojanā । yadyapi bṛhadbhāṣye akṣaranayodāhṛtabṛhadāraṇyakaśrutigatasūryacandrapadayorbrahmarudraparatayā vyākṛtatvādevamanuvādo anupapannaḥ । tathāpi tayoḥ prasiddhacandrasūryaparatvasyāpyanumatatvādevamuktiḥ । yadvā - atra bhāṣye api candrādityapade rudrabrahmapare । ata eva tattvapradīpe akṣaranaye aahaṃ somam'; iti vacane somaśabdo rudraparatayā vyākṛtaḥ । tathā ca na ko api virodhaḥ । anenākṣaranayoktacandrādityādyādhāratvasya sākṣāt hṛtpadmasthākāśaniṣṭhatākṣepāttena asyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । evaṃ sarvādhāratvānveṣṭavyatvasamānādhikaraṇaḥ sākṣādvyavadhānena vā sāmānyato hṛtpadmasthatvarūpo viṣayaśca darśitaḥ । na caivaṃ acandrāditya'; iti bhāṣyeṇa sa candrādityādyādhāraḥ kiṃ daharākāśaḥ syāt? āhosvittatsthaḥ kaścit? iti tattvapradīpena ca virodha iti vācyam । tayorakṣarādhikaraṇākṣepeṇa atra pūrvapakṣa iti darśayituṃ pravṛttatvena viṣayapradarśanāyāpravṛttatvāt । aākāśasya'; ityanena prasiddhabhūtākāśasyaiva sarvādhāratayā sākṣāt hṛtpadmasthatvamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ pradarśitaḥ । tathā praśnaprativacanapūrvakaṃ sākṣādākāśasyaivātra sarvādhāratayā hṛtpadmasthatvakathanāditi pūrvapakṣayuktiśca pradarśitā bhavati । atra yadyapi aatha yadidamasmin brahmapure daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ veśma daharo asminnantarākāśaḥ tasmin yadantastadanveṣṭavyaṃ tadvāva vijijñāsitavyamiti । taṃ cadbrūyuḥ kiṃ tadatra vidyate yadanveṣṭavyaṃ yadvā va vijijñāsitavyamiti । sa brūyādyāvānvāyamākāśastāvāneṣo antarhṛdaya ākāśaḥ । ubhe asmin dyāvāpṛthivī antareva samāhite । ubhāvagniśca vāyuśca sūryācandramasāvubhau । vidyunnakṣatrāṇi'; ityādisamagravākyamudāhartavyam, na tu vicchidya । tathāpi samānajātīyaśrutyantaropasaṅgrahāyaivamudāhṛtamiti dhyeyam । śrutāvathaśabdaḥ prameyāntarārambhārthaḥ । abrahmapuram'; ityetat brahmaṇaḥ puraṃ nivāsasthānamiti brahmaiva pūrṇatvātpuramiti ca dvedhā vyākhyeyam । aantarhṛdaye'; iti saptamyantam । aākāśaḥ'; iti prathamāntam । tathā ca etasmin brahmapure śarīre yatpuraṃ brahmāsti aasmin'; tasminbrahmaṇi adaharaṃ'; dabhramalpaṃ apuṇḍarīkam'; abjaṃ aveśma'; tasya sadmarūpamasti asmin aantardaharaḥ'; alpo bhūtākāśo asti । kiṃ cātaḥ? atasmin'; ākāśe antaryadvartate atadanveṣṭavyaṃ'; jñātavyaṃ mārgitavyaṃ vā । nanu na ghaṭādivadanveṣaṇaṃ yuktam, apratyakṣatvādityatastadeva vivṛṇoti - tadvāveti ।। tathā ca tadeva avijijñāsitavyaṃ'; vicāritavyam । iti guruṇokte ataṃ'; guruṃ prati acet'; yadi śiṣyāḥ abrūyuḥ'; pṛccheyuḥ । kimiti? aatra'; bhūtākāśe yadanveṣṭavyaṃ yadvāva vijījñāsitavyamityuktaṃ atat'; ādheyasvarūpaṃ akiṃ'; kiṃmahimaṃ ceti । na ca brahmapure brahmaṇo veśmetyuktyaivākāśasya brahmatvaniścayātpraśnāyoga iti vācyam । anyapure apyanyasya veśmasambhavādanyaveśmanyapyanyasyāvasthānasambhavāttadukteraniścāyakatvāt । evaṃ śiṣyaiḥ pṛṣṭe asaḥ'; gururbrūyāt । kimiti? hṛdo antaḥ antarhṛt tasminnayate astīti vyutpattyā aantarhṛdaye'; tacchabdabodhye hṛtpadmagatabhūtākāśe dyāvāpṛthivyādyāśrayaḥ aākāśaḥ'; tadākhyaḥ paramātmāstīti । nanvaṇau tasmin kathaṃ dyāvāpṛthivyādyavasthitirityatastasya vyāptatvamāha - yāvāniti ।। aayaṃ'; bahiḥsthitaḥ aākāśaḥ'; tadākhyo bhagavān guṇataḥ parimāṇataśca yāvān eṣa āntaro api tāvāneva । tathā cāṇāvapi rūper iśaśaktyā mahattvasyāpi sattvādvyāptasya tasyānekādhāratvaṃ yujyata eveti bhāvaḥ । anyaparityāgenāsyaiva jijñāsyatve ko heturityato asya sarvādhāratvākhyaṃ mahimānamāha - ubha ityādinā ।। asminnantare ye ubhe muktāmukte dyāvāpṛthivyau devyau asamāhite'; samavasthite । evamubhayavidhau agniśca vāyuścetyetau devau samāśritau । tathā ubhau muktāmuktau sūryācandramasau vidyut nakṣatrāṇi ca samāśritānīti chāndogyabhāṣyarītyā śrutyarthaḥ । nyāyavivaraṇe tadvivaraṇarūpaṭīkāyāṃ - atasmin yadantaḥ'; ityatra hṛtpadmasthākāśagataṃ brahmānveṣṭavyamityuktam । na ca padmasthasya brahmatvāsiddhiḥ । śarīrapuṇḍarīkayorbrahma prati puratvaveśmatvoktyaiva anveṣṭavyasya brahmatvasiddheḥ । tathā ca padme brahmāstītyukte api tadbrahma kiṃ prakāramiti bhāvena punaḥ akiṃ tadatra vidyate'; iti pṛṣṭe tatprakārajñāpanāya ayāvān'; ityādyāha guruḥ । anena ca yadbrahmānveṣṭavyatayoktaṃ tadbrahmāntarhṛdaye yāvāneṣa prasiddhākāśastāvān sarvo apyākāśo vartate । tasmiṃścākāśe pṛthivyādikaṃ sarvaṃ samāśritam । apahatapāpmatvādiguṇakaṃ ca tadityevamākāśādisarvāśriyatvādapahatapāpmatvādiprakāra ukto bhavatīti prakārāntareṇa vyākhyātam । pūrvapakṣī tu - ahṛdaya ākāśe'; iti padaṃ saptamyantaṃ kṛtvā daharākāśastho vyāptākāśo anveṣṭavya iti vā ākāśaḥ iti prathamāntaṃ kṛtvā prāguktadaharabhūtākāśamanūdya yāvānityanena bāhyākāśatulyatayā taṃ viśiṣya jijñāsyatvena tatra dyāvāpṛthivyādikamucyata ityāha ।

sa cākāśo na viṣṇuḥ । atasyānte suṣiraṃ sūkṣmaṃ tasmin sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam'; iti śruteriti ।

nanvastvākāśasya sarvādhāratayā hṛtpadmasthatvaṃ tasya cākāśasya aākāśastalliṅgāt'; iti nyāyena viṣṇutvena viṣṇoreva hṛtpadmasthvaṃ sidhyatītyata āha - sa ceti ।। castvarthaḥ, pratijñāsamuccaye vā । tathā ca yassarvādāratayā hṛtpadmasthatvena ca śrutyuktaḥ asa cākāśo na viṣṇuḥ'; bhūtameva na tu viṣṇurityarthaḥ । kuto vā na viṣṇurityata āha - tasyānta iti । sa cetyanuṣaktaścaśabdo atra buddhyā viviktasuṣirapadenānvīyate avadhāraṇe ca ayam । śrutisamānoktyupalakṣakaṃ caitat । tathā ca atasyānte'; iti vākye asuṣirapadaśruteḥ'; suṣiraśabdaśravaṇāt suṣirasya chidrātmakaprasiddhākāśasyaiva śruteḥ sarvādhāratayā hṛtpadmasthatvokteḥ tatsamākhyānādityarthaḥ । atasya'; apadmakośapratīkāśaṃ hṛdayaṃ cāpyadhomukham'; iti pūrvavākye prakṛtasya hṛtpadmakośasya aante'; antare tanmadhye sūkṣmaṃ asuṣiraṃ'; chidramasti, tasmin asarvaṃ'; jagatpratiṣṭhitamiti taittirīyaśrutyarthaḥ ।

ata āha - sū - oṃ ।।
dahara uttarebhyaḥ ।
।।

aya ātmāpahatapāpmā vijaro vimṛtyurviśoko avijighatso apipāsaḥ satyakāmassatyasaṅkalpaḥ so anveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ'; ityādibhya uttarebhyo guṇebhyo dahare viṣṇureva ।

siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe - ata iti ।। aityādibhyaḥ'; ityādirūpebhyaḥ auttarebhyaḥ'; viṣayavākyānantarabhāvibhyaḥ aśabdebhyaḥ uktebhyaḥ'; iti śeṣaḥ । ityādyuttaravākyebhya iti paryavasitārthaḥ । yadvā aguṇebhyo'; guṇavacanebhya ityarthaḥ । hetvasiddhiparihārāya śrutyudāharaṇam । ādipadena aviśoko avijighatso apipāsaḥ satyakāmaḥ satyasaṅkalpaḥ so anveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । guṇebhyaḥ ityanenottarapadamuttaratraśrutānekaśabdavācyaguṇopalakṣakamityuktaṃ bhavati । adahare'; hṛtpadmagatālpākāśe ityanena sūtre adahare'; iti saptapyantaṃ padaṃ, na paramata iva prathamāntamityuktaṃ bhavati । sthito anveṣṭavyatayokta iti śeṣaḥ । samanvayasūtrādanuvṛttasya vidheyaparasya tattvityasyārtho viṣṇoreveti । anena - ayaḥ'; iti daharavākyāduttaravākye śrutebhyo guṇebhyo adahare'; vijijñāsyatayoktaḥ atattu'; viṣṇureva na bhūtākāśādiriti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । yo hṛtpadmākāśagataḥ paramātmā ana vadhenāsya hanyate'; iti prāk śarīrasya nāśenāvadhyatvenoktaḥ saḥ aapahatapāpmā'; nityameva svato apahatapāpmā pāpātyantābhāvavāniti yāvat । ata eva na tatkāryaṃ jarādikamasyetyucyate - vijara ityādinā । aavijighatsaḥ'; bubhukṣārahitaḥ । aapipāsaḥ'; pānecchārahita iti । abubhukṣādinā pīḍābhāva ucyate'; iti jñānapādīyaṭīkokternādanapānecchābhāvobhi'dhīyate, pramāṇabādhitatvāt । kintu tatpīḍābhāvaḥ । atra hetuḥ - satyakāma iti । tasya yadiṣṭaṃ tatsvataḥ eva bhavediti satyakāmaḥ । tatrāpi hetuḥ - asatyasaṅkalpaḥ'; apratihatasaṅkalpa iti। ya evaṃ bhūtaḥ so anveṣṭavya iti śrutyarthaḥ ।

ayo aśanāyāpipāse śokaṃ mohaṃ jarāṃ mṛtyumatyeti'; asa eṣa sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhya uditaḥ'; ityādinā viṣṇoreva hi te guṇāḥ ।

apahatapāpmatvādikaṃ kathaṃ viṣṇutvaniścāyakaṃ, tadgatatvenāsiddhatvādityata āha - ya iti ।। bṛhadāraṇyakaśrutiriyam । aaśanāyā'; aśanecchā । apipāsā'; pānecchā । te aatyeti'; atikramya vartate । yaśca aśokaṃ'; duḥkhaṃ amohaṃ'; mūrchāṃ ajarāṃ'; maraṇaṃ cāpyetītyarthaḥ । atratyasya yacchabdasya atamātmānaṃ viditvā'; iti tacchrutisthatacchabdenānvayaḥ । asa eṣaḥ'; iti chandogaśrutiḥ । asa eṣaḥ'; paramātmā apāpmabhyaḥ'; pāpebhyaḥ auditaḥ'; nityaṃ svata evodgataḥ pāparahita ityarthaḥ । aityādinā'; vākyena ādiśabdena satyakāmatvādiguṇāntarabodhakavākyāni gṛhyante । hi śabdo yata ityarthe । te apahatapāpmatvādirūpottaravākyoktāḥ siddhā iti śeṣaḥ । tasmānna teṣāṃ viṣṇuliṅgatvaniścayaḥ iti vākyaśeṣeṇāsyānvayaḥ । anyatra pāpādyabhāvasya kathañcidyoge api sarvathā satyakāmatvādikaṃ na yujyata iti jñāpanāyādiśabdabahuvacanayoḥ prayogaḥ ।

nityatīrṇāśanāyādireka eva harissvataḥ ।
aśanāyādikānanye tatprasādāttaranti hi ।।

tathāpi naite guṇā viṣṇoreva, ramādiṣvapi sambhavādityata āha - nityeti ।। asvataḥ'; anyānapekṣayā nityaṃ tīrṇā aśanāyādayo yena sa harireka eva, nānyo asti । hareranye ramābrahmādayastu aaśanāyādikān'; aśanapānecchāśokādidoṣān atatprasādāt'; tasya hareranugrahādeva ataranti'; atiyanti, na svata ityarthaḥ । hi śabdaḥ prasiddhau । apādme'; uktamiti śeṣaḥ । ato nirapekṣaguṇānāmanyatrābhāvāt viṣṇorevetyuktamiti bhāvaḥ ।

sāpekṣanirapekṣayośca nirapekṣaṃ svīkartavyam ।

nanu ramādiṣvapahatapāpmatvādīnāmanyānadhīnānāmabhāve api yathā kathañcitsattvādanyagataistaiḥ kathaṃ viṣṇutvaniścaya ityata āha - sāpekṣeti ।। asāpekṣam'; anyādhīnaṃ anirapekṣam'; anyānadhīnaṃ tayormadhye ityarthaḥ । co avadhāraṇe, nirapekṣameveti sambadhyate । apahatapāpmatvādikamiti viśeṣyaṃ prakṛtatvāllabhyate । asvīkartavyaṃ'; liṅgatveneti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca vivakṣitaliṅgasyānyatrābhāvāttena viṣṇutvaniścayo bhavatyeveti bhāvaḥ ।

satyakāmaḥ paro nāsti tamṛte viṣṇumavyayam ।
satyakāmatvamanyeṣāṃ bhavettatkāmyakāmitā ।।

kiṃ ca sāpekṣatvanirapekṣatvādiviśeṣitānāmapahatapāpmatvādīnāmabhāvarūpāṇāmanyatrākāśādau sākṣādvābhimānidvārā vā yathākathañcidvṛttāvapi na kathañcidanyatra satyakāmatvādyastīti yuktastena viṣṇutvaniścaya ityāha - satyakāma iti ।। aavyayam'; akṣīṇakāmamamoghakāmaṃ satyakāmaṃ viṣṇum aṛte'; vinā aparo anyaḥ'; viṣṇoranyaḥ satyakāmaḥ satyasaṅkalpaśca nāsti । viṣṇau tadbhāvasya tadanyasmin tadabhāvasya ca pratipādanāya vakroktiḥ । viṣṇoranyeṣāṃ ramādīnāṃ kvacidāgame pratīyamānamapi satyakāmatvaṃ atatkāmyakāmitā'; viṣṇukāmanāviṣayaviṣayakakāmanāvattvarūpameva bhavenna mukhyamityarthaḥ । tathā cāpahatapāpmatvaṃ svataḥ parādhīnaṃ ceti yathā dvividhaṃ, na tathā satyakāmatvaṃ kiṃ tvekavidhaṃ, tacca mukhyaṃ viṣṇāveva, anyatra tu pāribhāṣikamiti bhāvaḥ । askānde'; uktamiti śeṣaḥ। ataḥ satyakāmatvādivivakṣayā viṣṇoreva hi te guṇā ityuktaṃ yuktamiti bhāvaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। gatiśabdābhyāṃ tathā hi dṛṣṭaṃ liṅgaṃ ca ।।

aaharahargacchantya etaṃ brahmalokaṃ na vindanti'; iti suptasya tadgatirbrahmaśabdaścocyate ।

yuktyantareṇa viṣṇorhṛtpadmasthatvaṃ pratipādayatsūtramupanyasyāsiddhiparihārāya śrutyudāharaṇapūrvakaṃ vyācaṣṭe - gatīti ।। aimāḥ'; suptāḥ prajāḥ aaharahaḥ'; pratidinametaṃ agacchantyaḥ'; prāpyamāṇāḥ aetaṃ'; brahmalokaṃ brahmaṇo viṣṇorāvāsasthānabhūtaṃ hṛtpadmaṃ taddvārā tatratyaṃ brahma sākṣāllokapadoktaṃ brahmākhyamāśrayaṃ vā ana vindanti'; na vijānanti, sa eṣa ātmā hṛdīti śrutyarathaḥ । iti chandogavākye asuptasya'; cetanasya atadgatiḥ'; aharaho hṛdgataṃ brahmalokaṃ prati gatiḥ prāptiḥ aucyate'; vyapadiśyata ityarthaḥ । abrahmaśabdaḥ'; ityatrāpi taditi padaṃ buddhyā vivicya vipariṇāmena sambadhyate । tathā ca tasmin prāpyamāṇe hṛdgate brahmaloke abrahmaśabdaḥ'; aucyate'; śrūyate ityarthaḥ । ucyate ca ityapi sambandhaḥ । asyāto api dahare viṣṇureveti pradhānasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

asatā somya tadā sampanno bhavati'; iti śrutestaṃ hi supto gacchati ।

suptaprāpyatvaṃ kuto viṣṇutvaniścāyakamityata āha - sateti ।। he asomya'; bhaktijñānārha śvetaketo atadā'; suptikāle asatā'; brahmaṇā asampannaḥ'; saṅgato bhavatītyarthaḥ । uddālakavākyametat । śruteriti pañcamī । hi śabdaḥ prasiddhau । agacchati'; prāpnoti । iti jñāyate iti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca suptaprāpyatvasya viṣṇuliṅgatvena śrutiprasiddhatvāt tena viṣṇutvaniścayo bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।

aaraśca ha vai ṇyaścārṇavau brahmaloke'; iti liṅgaṃ ca tathā dṛṣṭam ।

aliṅgaṃ ca tathā hi dṛṣṭam'; iti sūtraśeṣaṃ hetvantaraparatayā vyācaṣṭe - araśceti ।। ca śabdo hetusamuccaye । yathā suptagamyatvam aaharahaḥ'; iti śrutau hṛtpadmasthe dṛṣṭam, tathā araṇyanāmāmṛtasamudradvayāśrayalokavattvarūpaṃ liṅgamapi aaraśca'; iti śrutau hṛtpadmasthe dṛṣṭaṃ śrutamiti । upamāyāṃ tathāśabdaḥ । anenāsiddhiḥ parihṛtā । na ca gatiśabdayorivāsya sannidhau hṛtpadmasthasyānukterasiddhyanivṛttiriti vācyam । hṛtpadmasthasya brahmaṇa āvāsatvena nimittena tallokabhūte hṛtpadme aetaṃ brahmalokam'; iti prayuktasya brahmalokaśabdasyāṇyāśrayaloke api prayogāttanmukhena tādṛśalokavattvarūpaliṅgasya hṛtpadmasthabrahmaniṣṭhatāyā prāptatvāt । dṛṣṭamityanantaraṃ yata iti śeṣaḥ। asyāto api dahare viṣṇureveti pratijñāvākyenānvayaḥ । śrutau havā iti nipātau prasiddhidyotakau । samudrayoranyonyasamuccaye ca śabdau । tathā ca brahmaṇo viṣṇorloke śvetadvīpe araṇyākhyārṇavau sudhāsamudrau arṇavopame sudhāsarasī vā sta iti śrutyarthaḥ ।

araśca vaiṇyaśca sudhāsamudrau tatraiva sarvābhimatapradau dvau ।
ityādinā tasyaiva hi tallakṣaṇatvenocyate ।।

nanu hṛtpadmasthasyāraṇyāśrayalokavattvaliṅgaśravaṇe api kuto ayaṃ viṣṇurityato araṇyāśrayatvasya viṣṇulokaikaliṅgatvena smṛtisiddhatvādityāśayena sautrahiśabdābhipretāṃ smṛtiṃ darśayati - araśceti ।। vaiśabdaḥ prasiddhau । caśabdau parasparasamuccaye । atatraiva'; kṣīrābdhimadhyasthitaviṣṇuloka eva asarvābhimatapradau'; sarveṣṭakarau sta ityarthaḥ । evakāro anyatra sattvavyāvartakaḥ । tenāraṇyāśrayalokavattvaliṅgasya viṣṇutvenāvyabhicāraḥ siddhyati । ata eva bhāṣye tasyaivetyevakāraḥ । aityādinā'; puruṣottamadhyānacakravākyena atasyaiva'; viṣṇoreva atat'; sudhārṇavadvayāśrayalokavattvaṃ alakṣaṇatvena'; liṅgatvena aucyate'; pratipādyate ityarthaḥ । ahi'; yasmādityarthe । tasmādetalliṅgabalāt viṣṇutvaniśrayo yukta iti vākyaśeṣaḥ । yadvā - brahmalokamiti hṛtpadmasya viṣṇulokatvokteḥ tadantargato viṣṇurityuktaṃ, brahmalokapadaṃ kuto viṣṇulokavācītyata āha - araśceti । brahmalokapadasya viṣṇuloke aaraśca'; iti vākye prayogādatra hṛtpadme prayuktam aetaṃ brahmalokam'; iti padamapi viṣṇulokaparameva । na ca aaraśca'; iti śrutāvapi brahmalokapadaṃ kuto viṣṇulokaparamiti vācyam । yatastatrāraṇyāśrayatvaliṅgaṃ śrutamityarthaḥ । athāpyaraṇyāśrayatvasya bhagavallokaliṅgatvaṃ kuta ityata āha - araśceti ।। asmin pakṣe sautraṃ liṅgapadaṃ hṛtpadmasthasya brahmatvarūpapradānasādhye hetutvābhāvātsūtre liṅgaśabdena pṛthaguktiḥ । pūrvavyākhyāne api gatiśabdayorivāsya liṅgasya viṣṇuniṣṭhatāyā upapādanasāpekṣatvena spaṣṭatvābhāvādgatiśabdaliṅgairityanuktvā liṅgaṃ ceti pṛthaguktiryuktā । anena - na kevalamuttarebhyo guṇebhyaḥ, kintu gatiśabdābhyāṃ ca aaharahaḥ'; iti vākye hṛtpadmasthaniṣṭhatayā śrutābhyāṃ suptaprāpyabrahmaśabdābhyāṃ ca dahare viṣṇureveti jñāyate । na kevalametābhyāmeva, kintu yataḥ aaraśca'; iti śrutau atathā'; gatiśabdayoriva ahi'; viṣṇuliṅgatvena smṛtisiddhamaraṇyāśrayalokavattvarūpaṃ liṅgaṃ hṛtpadmasthe viṣṇuloke prayuktabrahmalokapadasya hṛtpadme prayogāt adṛṣṭaṃ'; śrutamato api dahare viṣṇureva । yadvā - kuto atra prayuktasya brahmalokapadasya viṣṇulokaparatvam? aaraśca'; iti vākye viṣṇuloke brahmalokapadaprayogāt । atrāpi aetaṃ brahmalokam'; iti tasyaiva prayogāt । na ca tatrāpi viṣṇulokaparatvaṃ kutaḥ? yato araṇyāśrayatvaṃ liṅgaṃ adṛṣṭaṃ'; śrutamata iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sū - oṃ ।। dhṛteśca mahimno asyāsminnupalabdheḥ ।।

aeṣa seturvidhṛtiḥ'; iti dhṛteḥ, 

hetvantareṇa viṣṇorhṛtpadmasthatvaṃ pratipādayatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe - dhṛteriti ।। aiti dhṛteḥ'; ityasya aasminnasya'; iti padānuvartanenetyasminvākye asya hṛtpadmasthasya dhṛtipadoktasarvādhāratvaśruterityarthaḥ । asya dahare viṣṇureveti pratijñāvākyenānvayaḥ । śrutau vidhṛtiḥ seturityanvayaḥ । tatra vidhṛtirityetatsetutve hetuḥ । tathā ca ya ātmā hṛtpadmasthatvenoktaḥ sa eṣa aeṣāṃ'; bhūrādilokānām aasambhedāya'; asāṅkaryāya avidāraṇāyeti, vyāsatīrthīyoktarītyā varṇāśramasāṅkaryābhāvāyeti vā avidhṛtiḥ'; dhāraṇapoṣaṇasamartho ata eva seturiva asetuḥ'; āśraya ityarthaḥ । dhārakatvaṃ ca na dhāryādbahiṣṭhatayā, kintvantaḥkṛtajagattvena, aśritamasmin jagatsarvamiti seturitīritaḥ'; ityukteḥ mukhyārtha eva vā setuśabdaḥ । yadyapi asa seturvidhṛtiḥ'; iti chandogaśrutipāṭhaḥ । tathāpi śākhāntarāṇāmapyatropasaṅgrahāyaivamuktiḥ । evamanyatrāpīti sampradāyavidaḥ ।

aeṣa bhūtādhipatireṣa bhūtapālaḥ'; ityādyasya mahimno asminnupalabdheḥ ।

evaṃ setusamuccāyakasautracaśabdasya yathāśrutānvayena liṅgoktiparatayā dhṛteścetyaṃśaṃ vyākhyāyedānīṃ samagraṃ sūtraṃ samānoktirūpasamākhyāparatayā vyācaṣṭe - eṣa iti ।। dhṛteritipadamatrānuṣajyate । asmin pakṣe sautracaśbada upalabdheścetyanveti । tathā ca na kevalaṃ dhṛterliṅgāt, kintu adhṛteḥ'; dhṛtiyuktāyāstadbodhikāyā upalabdheḥ vāsaneyake aya eṣo antarhṛdaya ākāśastasmin śete sarvasya vaśī'; ityādyuktvā āmnātāyāḥ aeṣa sarveśvara eṣa bhūtādhipatireṣa bhūtapāla eṣa seturvidharaṇa eṣāṃ lokānāmasambhedāya'; ityukteḥ samānokteśca dahare viṣṇureveti yojanā । samākhyāyāḥ kuto viṣṇuparatvamityata āha - eṣa iti । ityādīti luptatṛtīyāvibhaktiko nirdeśaḥ । ādiśabdena aeṣa sarvasya vaśī eṣa sarvasyādhipatireṣa sarveśvaraḥ'; iti pūrvavākyam aeṣa seturvidharaṇa eṣāṃ lokānāmasambhedāya'; ityuttaravākyaṃ ca gṛhyate । ata eva madhyasthavākyagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam । asya mahimna iti vyadhikaraṇaṣaṣṭhyau । upalabdherityāvṛttamatrānveti । tathā ca aasmin'; vājasaneyake aeṣa bhūtādhipatiḥ'; ityādinā vākyena aasya'; viṣṇorbhūtādhipatitvādimahimnaḥ aasmin'; daharākāśagate vastuni aupalabdheḥ'; uktatvāditi yojanā । ya eṣa sarvasyādhipatiḥ, yaścaiṣa sarveśvaro, yaścaiṣa prasiddho abhūtādhipatiḥ'; bhūta evādhipatirnāsyādhipatyamādimat, yaścaiṣa bhūta eva pālako, yaśca aeṣāṃ'; bhūrādilokānām aasambhedāya'; amelanāya eṣāṃ avidharaṇaḥ'; vidhāraṇasamarthaḥ, na kevalaṃ sāmarthyamātraṃ, kintu ya eṣāṃ lokānāṃ asetuḥ'; āśrayaśca, tametaṃ bhagavantaṃ brāhmaṇā vividiṣantīti śrutyarthaḥ । anena - na kevalaṃ pūrvoktahetubhyaḥ, kintu vidhṛteścāsmin prakaraṇe asa seturvidhṛtiḥ'; iti sarvādhāratvaliṅgaśravaṇādapi daharapadmastho viṣṇureva । na cāsya hṛtpadmasthatvaṃ kuta iti vācyam । aasya'; hṛtpadmasthasya amahimnaḥ'; apahatapāpmatvāderlakṣaṇasya aasmin'; sarvādhāre asarve pāpmāno ato nivartante'; ityanena aupalabdheḥ'; uktatvāt । na kevalaṃ dhṛterliṅgāt, kintu dhṛterdhṛtiyuktāyā upalabdherukteḥ । aya eṣo antarhṛdaya ākāśastasmin śete eṣa seturvidharaṇaḥ'; iti vājasaneyasamākhyāyāśca dahare viṣṇureva । samākhyāyā api kuto viṣṇuviṣayatvam? aasmin'; vājasaneyake aasya'; viṣṇoḥ amahimno'; bhūtādhipatitvāderuktatvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । yadyapi aasya mahimnaḥ'; ityādyaṃśo bhāṣye dhṛteścetyasya liṅgaparatayā yojanāyāṃ nānvitaḥ । tathāpi ṭīkāyāṃ asarve pāpmāno ataḥ'; iti tallakṣaṇokteścetyuktatvāt liṅgasya hṛtpadmasthatvarūpapakṣadharmopapādakatayāpi yojanīyaḥ ।

aetasmin khalvakṣare gārgyākāśa otaśca'; aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi'; 

yaduktaṃ sarvādhāratvaliṅgaśravaṇāt hṛtpadmastho viṣṇuriti, tatra sarvādhāratvaṃ kuto viṣṇutvaniścāyakaṃ, tatsamānādhikaraṇatvenāsiddhatvādityata āha - etasminniti ।। aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane'; iti pratīkagrahaṇena aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ, etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi dyāvāpṛthivyau'; ityādibahuvākyāni sūcayati । imānyakṣaranaye vyākṛtāni ।

asa hi sarvādhipatiḥ sa hi sarvapālaḥ sar iśaḥ sa viṣṇuḥ'; apatiṃ viśvasyātmeśvaram'; ityādiśrutibhyastasya hyeṣa mahimā ।

nanu samākhyāśrutyuktaḥ sarveśvaratvādimahimā kuto viṣṇoravagata ityata āha - sa hīti ।। asa hi'; ityārabhya asa viṣṇuḥ'; ityantamekaṃ vākyaṃ śrutyantaragatam । apatiṃ viśvasya'; iti nārāyaṇānuvākasthaṃ vākyam । aviśvasya'; acetanaprapañcasya patiṃ aātmeśvaraṃ'; cetaneśvaraṃ nārāyaṇaṃ tadviśvamupajīvatītyarthaḥ। evamādiśrutivākyebhya ityarthaḥ । ādiśabdenaitajjātīyaṃ gṛhyate । tṛtīyārthe pañcamī। atasya'; viṣṇoḥ ahiḥ'; prasiddhau hetau vā । aeṣa sarveśvaraḥ'; ityādimahimā । tasmānnaiteṣāṃ viṣṇutvarūpasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyāsiddhiriti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

sarveśo viṣṇurevaiko nānyo asti jagataḥ patiḥ ।
iti ca skānde ।।

nanu sarveśvaratvādikaṃ viṣṇuvadanyasyāpi kiṃ na syādityata āha - sarveśa iti ।। atra sarvajagacchabdau cetanācetanaprapañcaparau । yadvā - jagataḥ patiriti pratiyogitvenaivoktasyānuvādaḥ । athavā - apatiḥ'; pālakaḥ । tathā ca sarveśvaraḥ sarvapālakaśca viṣṇureka eva nānyo astītyarthaḥ । iti skānda ityasya evakāroktapadādhyāhāreṇa tasyahyeṣa mahimeti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । tasmānnaitalliṅgānāmanyatra sāvakāśatvaṃ śaṅkyamiti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। oṃ ।।
atatrāpi daharaṃ gaganaṃ viśokastasmin yadantastadupāsitavyam'; iti prasiddheśca ।।
samākhyāntararūpayuktyantareṇa viṣṇorhṛtpadmagatākāśasthatvaṃ sādhayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe - prasiddheśceti ।। itītyanantaraṃ śrutāviti śeṣaḥ । atasya'; viṣṇoḥ atasya'; hṛtpadmasthasyeti tadarthaḥ । anena - sūtre asyāsminnitipadadvayaṃ pūrvasūtrādanuvartanīyam । tathā ca na kevalaṃ vājasaneyasamākhyānāt, kintu aasmin'; tatrāpīti taittirīyaśrutivākye aasya'; hṛtpadmasthasya viṣṇutvaprasiddheśca tatsamākhyānādapi daharapadmastho viṣṇureveti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । adivye brahmapure hyeṣa vyomnyātmā sampratiṣṭhitaḥ'; ityātharvaṇe prasiddheśca । aya eṣo antarhṛdaya ākāśastasminnayaṃ puruṣaḥ'; iti taittirīyavākyāntare prasiddheśceti sūtrasya yadvṛttyantaraṃ ṭīkāyāṃ sūcitaṃ, tadbhāṣyasthetiśabdasyādyarthatvamāśrityeti draṣṭavyam । śrutau adaharaṃ vipāpmaṃ paraveśmabhūtaṃ yatpuṇḍarīkaṃ puramadhyasaṃstham'; iti vākye yat adaharam'; alpaṃ parasya brahmaṇaḥ sadmabhūtam, ata eva vigatapāpaṃ dehākhyabrahmapuramadhye saṃsthaṃ hṛdayakamalaṃ prakṛtaṃ tattatreti parāmṛśyate । tathā ca atatrāpi'; puṇḍarīke api yat adaharam'; alpaṃ gaganamasti tasmin aantaḥ'; antare aviśoko'; viśokaṃ viśokapadopalakṣitaṃ jarādiśūnyaṃ yadbrahma tadupāsitavyamityarthaḥ । viśokaḥ iti liṅgavyatyayaḥ chāndasaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu - liṅgavyatyāsastasya puruṣatvajñāpanārthaḥ । aya ātmāpahatapāpmā vijaro vimṛtyurviśokaḥ'; ityādāvuditaguṇānāmadhikaraṇaikyabalena sannidhīyamānānāmanukarṣaṇārthaśceti prayojanamuktam ।

tadantassthatvāpekṣatvānna suṣiraśrutivirodhaḥ ।।

nanu sākṣāt padmagatasya viṣṇutvābhyupagame suṣiraśrutivirodhaḥ । evaṃ padmagatākāśasyaiva viṣṇutvābhyupagame api suṣiraśrutivirodhaḥ, suṣiraśabdasyākāśavācitvāt । etadvihāya daharapadmasyākāśatvaṃ, viṣṇostvākāśagatatvaṃ, tasyaiva sarvādhāratvamityupagame api suṣiraśrutivirodhaḥ । tatra sākṣātsuṣirasya sarvādhāratvokterityata āha - tadantasstheti ।। buddhyā viviktasuṣiraśrutipadaṃ ṣaṣṭhyantamatrānvīyate । tathā ca asuṣiraśruteḥ'; iti suṣirapadaghaṭitaśruteḥ atadantassthāpekṣatvāt'; padmagatasuṣirāntassthaparamātmānamapekṣya pravṛttatvāttasya ca sarvādhāratvānna suṣiraśrutivirodho asmadabhyupagamasyetyarthaḥ । yathā mandirasthamañjūṣāntargatamapi vastu mandirasthamiti saṅgīyate, evamihāpīti bhāvaḥ । tadantassthatveti pāṭhe paramātmanaḥ suṣirāntassthatvamapekṣya śruteḥ pravṛttatvādityarthaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। itaraparāmarśātsa iti cennāsaṃbhavāt ।।

aparaṃ jyotirupasampadya svena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate,'; aeṣa ātmeti hovāca'; iti jīvaparāmarśātsa iti cet - 

bhagavato hṛtpadmasthatvamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasyākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - itareti ।। aniṣpadyate'; ityanantaramityuktasyeti śeṣaḥ । asya ca samāsapraviṣṭajīvapadenānvayaḥ । anena sūtre asminnasyetyasyānuvṛttiḥ । itarapadaṃ siddhāntyabhimatabrahmapratiyogijīvaparam । ata eva śrutāveṣa iti jīvaparāmarśaḥ । siddhānte śrutyarthastu vakṣyate ।

na, tasya svato apahatapāpmatvādyasambhavāt ।।

dhṛtisūtrāt aasyāsmin upalabdheḥ'; ityasyānuvṛttimabhipretyaparihārāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - neti ।। hṛtpadmastho na jīva ityarthaḥ । kuto netyatastatrānuvṛttavākyena aasmin'; prakaraṇe aasya'; apahatapāpmatvāderupalabdherityasya hetorlābhāttamanupanyasyoktahetorjīve niravakāśatvoktiparatayāsambhavādityaṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - tasyeti ।। muktabhāvamādāya jīve sambhavāt asiddhivārāṇāya - svata iti ।। svātantryeṇetyarthaḥ । satyakāmatvādikamādiśabdārthaḥ । anena - aasmin'; aparaṃ jyotiḥ'; itivākye abhivyaktikartṛtvenoktasya prakṛtasyopasampattikarmībhūtādbrahmaṇa itarasyāsya jīvasyātmeti aya ātmā'; ityuktahṛtpadmasthātmatvavidhānāya aeṣaḥ'; ityetacchabdena aparāmarśāt'; upasthāpanāt । jīvaparāmarśakaitacchabdaśravaṇāditi yāvat । dahare sa jīva eva, na viṣṇuriti cet - na hṛtpadmastho jīvaḥ। kutaḥ? asminprakaraṇe asyāpahatapāpmatvāderupalabdheḥ śravaṇāt । asya cāsmin jīve svato asambhavāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sū - oṃ ।। uttarāccedāvirbhūtasvarūpastu ।।

asa tatra paryeti jakṣan krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ'; ityādyuttaravacanājjīva eveti cet - 

jīvasyāpahatapāpmatvādyasambhavamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasyākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - uttarāditi ।। aityādyuttaravacanāt'; evaṃrūpāddaharavākyāpekṣayā parāmarśavākyāpekṣayā vānantarādvacanādityarthaḥ । vacanādityanantaram asyāsminnupalabdherityanuṣajyate । sambhavāditi śeṣaḥ । aasya'; satyakāmatvasya aasmin'; jīve pratītestata eva viśokatvādeḥ aupalabdheḥ'; siddheruktaguṇānāṃ sambhavāditi tadarthaḥ । jīva ityanena pūrvasūtrātsa ityasyānuvṛttiḥ sūcitā। neśvarā iti evaśabdārthaḥ । hṛtpadmastha iti vartate ।

na, tatra hi parameśvaraprasādādāvirbhūtasvarūpo mukta ucyate ।

nañanuvṛttyā parihārāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe - neti ।। naitadvākyabalena jīvasya satyakāmatvādiguṇān sambhāvya hṛtpadmasthatvaṃ vācyamityarthaḥ । kuto netyato abhihitam aāvirbhūtasvarūpastu'; ityaṃśaṃ tatreti padādhyāhāreṇa vyācaṣṭe - tatreti ।। asa tatra'; ityuttaravākya ityarthaḥ । tatra aāvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ'; ucyate iti sambandhaḥ । āvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ ityasya vyākhyānaṃ mukta iti । hiśabdo yata ityarthe । uttaravacanādityatrāpi sambadhyate । tathā ca auttaravacanāt'; asvena rūpeṇa'; iti jaḍadehatyāgottarakālīnasvarūpābhivyaktiśruteḥ । atra muktasyokteḥ hṛtpadmasya ca dehāntaravṛttitayā muktatvāyogāt nāyaṃ jīva iti bhāvaḥ । nanvasya muktaviṣayatve api muktasyāpi jīvatve nāstyeva jīve apahatapāpmatvādisambhavaḥ । na ca tasya hṛtpadmasthatvāyogaḥ, yato jīvo bhāvibhāvenāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇaḥ idānīṃ hṛtpadmagatatayocyata ityata āha - parameśvaraprasādāditi । evetyanuvartate । anena tu śabdo vyākhyātaḥ । parameśvaraprasādādityanena uttarādityetaduttamādityapi vyākhyātam । atra mukta iti na sautrapadavyākhyānamātram । kintūddeśyasamarpakaṃ ca । anena āvṛttistuśabdasya yathāśrutānvayaśca sūcitaḥ । tathā ca yo atra mukta ucyate sa tu parameśvaraprasādādeva aāvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ'; āvirbhūto vyaktaḥ svarūpaḥ apahatapāpmatvādiḥ svadharmo yasya sa tathoktaḥ । ato na svato apahatapāpmatvādiguṇakaḥ, ato na daharasthaḥ jīva iti yojanā ।

yatprasādātsa mukto bhavati sa bhagavān pūrvoktaḥ।।

nanu aparaṃjyotirupasampadya svena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate'; ityatra muktasyābhivyaktāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇakatvamevocyate, na tu tadguṇānāṃ parameśvarādhīnatvam । atastatsvata evetyata āha - yaditi ।। asya yacchabdasya dvitīyatacchabdenānvayaḥ । prasādo nāma icchāviśeṣaḥ । punaḥ sa ityuktyā sūtre anuvṛttasya sa ityasyāvṛttiḥ sūcitā । pūrvokta ityanena sūtre uttaratretyasya pratiyogitayā pūrvatretyupaskāryamityuktaṃ bhavati । tathā ca ayatprasādāt'; yasyānugrahāt asaḥ'; jīvo amuktaḥ'; apahatapāpmatvādiguṇo bhavati । asaḥ'; guṇapradātā bhagavān, apūrvoktaḥ'; aparaṃjyotirupasampadya'; iti pūrvavākye atathā'; guṇapradātṛtayā ukta iti yojanā। anyathā lyabantapadaṃ vyarthaṃ syāditi bhāvaḥ । ukta ityanantaraṃ yata iti śeṣaḥ । asyātonātra muktaguṇaprāpteḥ parameśvarādhīnatvoktyabhāva ityupaskṛtavākyenānvayaḥ । athavā - nanu jīve anyādhīnasya tadguṇajātasya sattvātsa evāpahatapāpmatvādinokto hṛtpadmasthaścāstvityata āha - yaditi । yojanā tu - yatprasādātsa jīvo jaḍadehānmukto bhavati, mukto bhūtvā ca sopahatapāpmatvādiguṇo bhavati, sa bhagavāneva apūrvoktaḥ'; aeṣa ātmāpahatapāpmā'; ityādipūrvavākye tathāpahatapāpmatvādinokto na jīvaḥ । dātṛpratigṛhītrormadhye dātureva mukhyatvānmukhyāmukhyayośca mukhyasyaiva grāhyatvāditi ।।

anena - asya aeṣa samprasādo asmāccharīrātsamutthāya'; ityaktasya jīvasya auttarāt'; daharavākyāpekṣayā parāmarśavākyāpekṣayā vānantarāt asa tatra paryeti'; ityādivacanāt aasmin'; pūrvaprakṛte jīve aasya'; satyakāmatvasya aupalabdheḥ'; pratīteḥ, tata evāsya viśokatvādeḥ siddheśca । ata evāsyoktaguṇāsambhavābhāvātsa hṛtpadmastho jīva eva neśvara iti cet - na, yatastatra asvena'; ityuttaravākyabalādāvirbhūtasvarūpo mukta ucyate । sa ca dehānantargatatayā na hṛtpadmastho bhavatīti bhāvaḥ । na ca muktasyāpi jīvatvena tatrāpahatapāpmatvahṛtpadmasthatvayorbhinnakālīnatve api sāmānādhikaraṇyopapatterasti punastasya prāptiriti vācyam । yato atra vākye yo mukta ucyate sa uttarāduttamātparameśvaraprasādādevāvirbhūtasvarūpo na svataḥ । na cātra muktasya tadguṇatvamevocyate, na parameśvarādhīnatvaṃ tadguṇajātasyeti vācyam । yataḥ pūrvatra aparaṃ jyotiḥ'; iti pūrvavākye yatprasādātsa mukto bhavati sa paramātmā tathā guṇapradātṛtayocyate । na ca yathākathaṃ cit jīvasyāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇakatvātpunastatprāptiriti vācyam । yato yasmāduttarāduttamādbhagavatastatprasādātsa muktaḥ aāvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ'; abhivyaktāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇakaḥ sa tu bhagavāneva pūrvatra aeṣa ātmāpahatapāpmā'; iti pūrvavākye ukto, na muktajīva iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । śrutyarthastu aeṣaḥ'; jīvo yataḥ asamprasādaḥ'; samyagviṣṇuprasādavān ato aasmāt caramaśarīrāt'; asamutthāya'; muktaḥ ayatparaṃ'; ajyotiḥ'; brahma aupasampadya'; prāpya svena rūpeṇa aabhiniṣpadyate'; abhivyajyate asa uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ'; paraṃ jyotirakhyaḥ । muktasya viṣayaiścaraṇaprakāramāha - sa iti । asaḥ'; prāptinijānandāvirbhāvo muktaḥ atatra'; muktisthāne paramātmānugraheṇaiva ajakṣan'; svāpekṣitaṃ bhakṣayan hasanvā jñātibhissaha muktaiḥ ajñātibhiḥ pūrvakalpamuktaiḥ akrīḍan'; strībhiḥ aramamāṇaḥ'; ratiṃ prāpnuvan prākṛtastryādiviṣayasaukhyamanubhavan aparyeti'; paritaḥ sañcaratīti ।

sū - oṃ ।। anyārthaśca parāmarśaḥ ।।

yaṃ prāpya svena rūpeṇa jīvo abhiniṣpadyate sa eṣa ātmeti paramātmārthaśca parāmarśaḥ ।।

nanu aeṣaḥ'; iti jīvaṃ parāmṛśya aātmā'; iti tasya hṛtpadmasthātmatvābhidhānādamukhyāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇo api jīvaḥ etacchabdaparāmarśabalena hṛtpadmasthātmā kiṃ na syādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya aitaraparāmarśātsa iti cenna'; ityanuvṛttapūrvavākyenāpekṣitasya siddhāntapratijñāyāśca lābhānnetyuktasādhye hetutayā sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe - anyeti ।। śrutau aparaṃjyotiḥ'; iti napuṃsakapadanirdiṣṭasya yamiti pulliṅgena nirdeśo liṅgasyāvivakṣitatvādvā viśeṣyaśabdavivakṣayā vā yuktaḥ । anena śrutau paraṃjyotiriti ekaṃ padam । yadvakṣyati aparaṃjyotiḥśabdena paramātmaivocyate'; iti, tacca aparaṃjyotiḥ paraṃbrahma'; iti paurāṇikarūḍhyā viṣṇuvācītyuktaṃ bhavati । jyotiḥ prakāśarūpaṃ paraṃ brahmeti bhinne pade ityapi kecit । asmin pakṣe uktabhāṣyavirodhaḥ । kiṃ ca yaṃ aparaṃjyotirākhyaṃ bhagavantam'; iti yacchabdavyākhyānaparaṭīkāvirodhaḥ । aparaṃjyotiḥ paramātmānam'; iti viṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkāvirodhaśca । śrutāvupasampadyetyasyārthaḥ prāpyeti । sautrānyapadaṃ pūrvapakṣyabhimatajīvapratiyogitayā vyākhyāti - paramātmeti ।। paramātmaivārtho abhidheyo yasya sa tathoktaḥ । aparāmarśaḥ'; etacchabdaḥ । yadvā - paramātmana evātmatvavidhānamarthaḥ prayojanaṃ yasya sa, tathoktaḥ । tathātve aparāmarśaḥ'; etacchabdena parigrahaṇamityarthaḥ । sūtrabhāṣyayoścaśabdastu na kevalaṃ jīvapakṣe apahatapāpmatvāsambhavākhyabādhakasadbhāvaḥ, kintu parāmarśākhyasādhakābhāvaśceti samuccayārthastuśabdārtho vā । candrikāyāṃ tu - na kevalaṃ parāmarśasyar iśvarapakṣe bādhakatvābhāvaḥ, kintu jīvapakṣasādhakatvābhāvaścetyuktatvātparāmarśo jīvānyeśvarārtha eva ityavadhāraṇārthatayā vyākhyātaḥ । anena - aitaraparāmarśāt'; itaraṃ jīvaṃ aeṣaḥ'; iti parāmṛśya tasya hṛtpadmasthatvavidhānātsa hṛtpadmastha ātmā jīva eva neśvara iti cet - na, kutaḥ? yataḥ aeṣaḥ'; iti parāmarśaḥ aanyārthaḥ'; jīvānyeśvarārtha eva, na jīvārthaḥ, ataḥ । athavā - na kevalamasambhavāt, kintu yataḥ parāmarśo anyārtho api । yadvā - asambhavānna hṛtpadmastho jīvaḥ, kintvīśvara eva । na caivaṃ parāmarśāyogaḥ । yataḥ aparāmarśaḥ'; etacchabdastu anyārtha iti tredhāsūtrārtha ukto bhavati । ayaṃ prāpya'; yatsamīpaṃ prāpyeti । anena jīvaḥ paraṃ jyotirākhyaṃ paramātmānamupasampadyāparokṣato jñātvā atha samīpaṃ prāpyavidyāvidhūnanenānandādinā svena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate āvirbhūtasvaguṇo bhavatīti yāvat । yaṃ prāpya svarūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate jīvaḥ, sa eṣa ātmā ya ātmeti prāguktaḥ paramātmeti hovāca brahmādīn prati rameti siddhānte śrutyarthaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। alpaśruteriti cettaduktam ।।

adaharaḥ'; ityalpaśruterneti cet - 

uktamākṣipya samādadhātsūtramupanyasya śrutyudāharaṇenākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - alpeti ।। adaharaḥ'; iti pratīkagrahaṇena adaharo asminnantara ākāśastasminyadantaḥ'; iti vākyaṃ gṛhyate । alpapadaṃ cālpasthānasthitiparam । śruterityanantaramasambhavādityanuvartate । tathā ca adaharaḥ'; iti vākye aasmin'; daharagate vastunyalpasthānasthitirūpaliṅgaśrutestasyāścāsminparamātmani aasambhavāt'; anupapatterityanvayaḥ । asmāddhetorna dahare viṣṇuḥ, kintu sa jīva evetītarasūtrānuvṛttapratijñayānvayaḥ ।।

na, anicāyyatvādevaṃ vyomavacca'; ityuktatvāt ।

sūtre anuvṛttanaña āvṛttimabhipretya parihārāṃśaṃ vyākhyāti - neti ।। nālpasthānasthitiśravaṇaṃ viṣṇāvanupapannamityarthaḥ । kuto netyataḥ pravṛttaṃ taduktamityaṃśaṃ yata ityadhyāhārābhiprāyeṇa hetutayā vyākhyāti - nicāyyatvāditi । atrāpīti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca anicāyyatvāt'; ityatra sarvagatasyāpi viṣṇorvyomavadalpasthānasthiteruktatvādityarthaḥ ।

aeṣa ma ātmāntarhṛdaye jyāyān'; iti śrutyuktatvācca ।।
।। iti daharādhikaraṇam ।।

nanu yuktaṃ vyomnoṃ'śato alpaukastvam, aṃśasyāpūrṇatvāt । brahmaṇi tu aṃśo api pūrṇa iti kathaṃ tasyāṃśato alpaukastvamityataḥ sūtraśeṣaṃ prakarāntareṇa vyācaṣṭe - eṣa ma iti ।। ca śabdo yuktisamuccaye । sūtrakṛcchrutyuktisamuccaye vā । aguṇāḥ śrutāḥ'; iti śrutisamuccaye vā । ayasmin'; iti smṛtisamuccaye vā । anena aalpaśruteḥ'; adaharaḥ'; iti vākye sarvagate vastunyalpasthānasthitiśravaṇāt, tasyāśca viṣṇāvasambhavādanupapatterna dahare viṣṇuḥ, kintu sa jīva eveti cet - na, yataḥ ataduktaṃ'; tatra nicāyyatvāditi pūrvatra tasya sarvagatasyāpi viṣṇorvyomavattadalpasthānasthitatvam, tasmādupāsanārthaṃ yuktamityuktam । na cāṃśatopi sarvagatatayā tatra tadanupapattiḥ । yatastasyāṃ aeṣa ma ātmā'; iti chandogaśrutau tena sarvajyāyastvena vṛddhatamatvena vyāptatvenaiva prakāreṇa tasya viṣṇostaddhṛdayasthatvamuktaṃ smṛtyuktaṃ cāta iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । na ca śrutismṛtyuktamapi kathametadaṅgīkārārhaṃ, yuktivirodhāditi vācyam । brahmaṇo acintyaśaktitvādupapatteḥ । aguṇāḥ śrutāḥ'; ayasminviruddhagatayaḥ'; ityādivacanācca । mama hṛdaye ya aātmā'; paramātmāsti । upalakṣaṇametat । sarvahṛdaye ca ya āste eṣaḥ hṛdayasthāṃśarūpo bhagavān ajyāyān'; vṛddhatamaḥ deśakālaguṇaiḥ pūrṇa iti śrutyarthaḥ । upaniṣaddraṣṭṛṛṣivākyametat ।।

।। iti daharādhikaraṇam ।।

।। anukṛtyadhikaraṇam ।।

adṛśyatvādayaḥ parameśvaraguṇā uktāḥ । ateṣāṃ sukhaṃ śāśvataṃ netareṣām । tadetaditi manyante anirdeśyaṃ paramaṃ sukham'; ityādinā jñānisukhasyāpyanirdeśyatvamajñeyatvaṃ cocyata iti ।।

atrādhikaraṇe akathaṃ nu tadvijānīyām'; iti vākyoktaṃ jñānārthaṃ jñeyaprārthanāviṣayatvaṃ vā akathaṃ nu tadvijānīyāṃ kimu bhāti'; iti brahmajñānānukūlābhivyaktyākhyabhānaprārthanāviṣayatvarūpaṃ vā ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvaṃ liṅgaṃ brahmaṇi samanvīyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayan sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ darśayati - adṛśyatvāditi। auktāḥ'; ānandamayādhikaraṇe udāhṛtādṛśya iti vākye iti bhāvaḥ । uktā ityanantaraṃ tatra praviṣṭamiti śeṣaḥ । prathamādipadenāniruktatvādeḥ, dvitīyena akathaṃ nu tadvijānīyāṃ kimu bhāti na bhāti vā'; iti samanvetavyaliṅgabodhakottarārdhasya ca grahaṇam । na kevalaṃ viṣṇoḥ, kintu jñānisukhasyāpītyaperarthaḥ । evārtho vāpiśabdaḥ ānumānikasūtragatāpipadavat । aajñeyatvaṃ'; sākalyenājñeyatvaṃ durjñeyatvamiti yāvat । caśabdaḥ parasparasamuccaye, ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvarūpasamanvetavyaliṅgasamuccaye vā । pūrvaśratyanusārādadṛśyatvādaya iti, etacchrutyanusārādanirdeśyatvamiti vyutkramaḥ। yadyapi atadetaditi'; etadevodāhartavyam । tathāpi pūrvapakṣe tacchabdārthapradarśanāya ateṣām'; iti pūrvavākyaikadeśopanyāsaḥ । ata eva tattvapradīpe teṣāmiti prastutiḥ pūrvapakṣotthāpiketyuktam । tathācetthaṃ yojanā - pūrvamānandamayādhikaraṇe ye adṛśyatvādayo guṇāḥ parameśvarasyoktāḥ । tatra teṣu praviṣṭamanirdeśyatvamajñeyatvaṃ ca ateṣāṃ sukham'; iti prakṛtyāmnātena atadetat'; ityādinā kāṭhakavākyena pūrvapakṣirītyā samīpasthāttacchabdāt parāmṛṣṭasya ajñānisukhasyāpi'; jñānisukhasyaivocyata iti । pūrvārdhenānirdeśyatvasyottarārdhe ca akimu bhāti na bhāti'; ityanena durjñeyatvaparyavasitājñeyatvasya cārthāduktatvāditi bhāvaḥ । ṭīkāyāmadṛśyatvapadasyānirdeśyatvaparatvādanirdeśyatvamiti pāṭhābhyupagamādvā na tadvirodhaḥ । atrānirdeśyatvamajñeyatvaṃ cocyata iti phaloktiḥ, ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvasyaivātra vicāryatvāt । tattu dvitīyādiśabdopāttavākyena caśabdena vā sūcitamiti draṣṭavyam । yata evamataḥ pūrvoktamayuktamiti bhāvaḥ । anenānandamayādhikaraṇoktādṛśyatvājñeyatvarūpasyānirdeśyatvāniruktatvarūpasya ca tatrānyatra ca sattve jñānisukhe ativyāptyākṣepāt itaramātraniṣṭhatvetvasambhavākṣepātphalatastenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tathā caśabdasūcitamānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvaṃ viṣayaḥ । viṣṇoranyasya veti sandehaḥ । jñānisukhasyaiveti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । anirdeśyatvājñeyatve ca tasyaiveti phalaṃ, sukhaśrutiḥ, prakṛtatvādirupayuktiśca sūcitā bhavati ।

ato vakti - sū - oṃ ।।
anukṛtestasya ca ।
।।

atameva bhāntamanubhāti sarvam'; ityanukṛteḥ, atasya bhāsā sarvamidaṃ vibhāti'; iti vacanācca paramātmaiva anirdeśyasukharūpaḥ ।

siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe - ata iti ।। aityanukṛteḥ'; ityanubhānaśruterityarthaḥ । anubhānaṃ nāma tadicchānurodhena bhānaṃ kriyāviśeṣaḥ । sūtre tasyetyasyānukṛterityanenāpi sambandhe tenaivānukaraṇapratisambandhina ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya tatkartuḥ sūryāditejasaśca lābho bhavatīti spaṣṭatvāttadubhayānuktiḥ । yadvā - pūrvasūtrāttadityasya vipariṇatasyehānuvartanādubhayalābho bhavatītyāśayena tadubhayānuktiḥ । na kevalaṃ tasyetyetat samanvetavyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvākhyaliṅgadharmiṇaḥ, sūryāditejasaśca parāmarśakaṃ, kintu śrutipratīkarūpamapi sarvajagatprakāśakatvaparaṃ cetyāśayena taddhetvantaraparatayā vyācaṣṭe - tasyeti । aiti vacanāt'; ityanena sūtre ityukteriti śeṣo darśitaḥ । yadyapi sūtrabhāṣyayoḥ aanubhāti'; itiśrutyanusārādanubhānāditi vācyam । tathāpi tāpinī pācinī caiva śoṣiṇī ca prakāśinī । naiva rājan raveśśaktiḥ śaktirnārāyaṇasya sā ।।

iti aitareyabhāṣyodāhṛtapādmavacanātsūryādikartṛkapratapanādikamapi paramātmādhīnamiti darśayitumanukṛterityuktam । sūtre tadanusāribhāṣye ca caśabdo dvitīyasūtrasya vakṣyamāṇavyākhyānabhedena sarvajagatprakāśakatvarūpoktahetusamuccaye vā, sūryādyaprakāśyatvarūpānuktahetusamuccaye vā draṣṭavyaḥ । sūtre samanvayasūtrādanuvṛttasya vidheyaparasya tattvityasyārthamāha - paramātmaiveti । na tu jñānisukhamityevaśabdārthaḥ । liṅgasamanvayena bhavatphalaṃ darśayati - anirdeśyeti । anirdeśyaścāsau sukharūpaśca iti vā, anirdeśyaṃ yatsukhaṃ tadrūpa iti vā vigrahaḥ । atra rūpaśabdo bhinnakramaḥ । tathā cānirdeśyaṃ paramaṃ sukhaṃ paramātmarūpamityanvayaḥ । eka ityādau pulliṅgena prakṛtasyaitaditi napuṃsakaliṅgena grahaṇāya rūpaśabdaprayogaḥ । anugrāhyascetyapi draṣṭavyam । vastutastu - vacanāccetiśabdasya sukharūpaścetyapi sambandhe tenaivānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇākhyaḥ sādhyadharmī sūcita iti dhyeyam । yadyapyanirdeśyatvamajñeyatvaṃ cetyupakramādubhayaṃ grāhyaṃ, na tvekaṃ, sukharūpamiti cādhikam । tathāpi pūrvapakṣyuktasukhaśruteḥ sukharūpe brahmaṇi sāvakāśatvajñāpanāya atadetat'; itivākyoktamanirdeśyasukharūpatvameva gṛhītam । ajñeyatvamapi draṣṭavyam । yadyapyatra bhāṣye liṅgadvayasyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya vā anirdeśyasukharūpasya vā viṣṇutve sādhye sākṣāddhetutvaṃ bhāti । ṭīkāyāṃ tu - atadetat'; iti śrutisthatacchabdena samīpoktajñānisukhaparityāgena acetanaścetanānām'; iti vyavadhānena prakṛtaparamātmagrahaṇe liṅgadvayaṃ hetutvena yojitam । tathāpi hetudvayena tacchabdena jñānisukhaparityāgena paramātmana eva grahaṇasiddhau tata eva tacchabdagṛhītasya paramātmana evānirdeśyasukharūpatvaṃ paryavasyatītyāśayena bhāṣye liṅgadvayasya prakṛtasādhyahetutvenoktirityavirodhaḥ । kecittu - aparamātmaivānirdeśyasukharūpaḥ'; iti bhāṣyamevānukṛtisūtre aānandamayobhyāsāt'; ityādāviva samanvetavyaśabdāderviṣṇuparatva eva heturnocye, kintvanirdeśyaṃ sukhamityatra samīpoktajñānisukhaparityāge heturucyate ityatra jñāpakaṃ, ṭīkāpi tadanusāriṇītyāhuḥ । tathā cāyaṃ siddhānte śrutyarthaḥ - 
eko vaśī sarvabhūtāntarātmā ekaṃ rūpaṃ bahudhā yaḥ karoti ।
tamātmasthaṃ ye anupaśyanti dhīrāḥ ।।

iti pūrvavākye aya eko'; jñānānandādyabhinnaḥ samābhyadhikaśūnyo vā yaḥ sarvamasya vaśe astīti asarvavaśī'; yaḥ asarvabhūtāntarātmā'; sarvaprāṇināmantarniyāmakaḥ aya ekaṃ'; svasvarūpaṃ bahudhā karoti niyamyānantyāt । ataṃ'; prakṛtam aātmasthaṃ'; jīvahṛdayasthitaṃ ye adhīrāḥ'; jñāninaḥ anupaśyantīti prakṛtā ye jñāninasteṣāmeva aśāśvataṃ sukhaṃ'; nityābhivyaktasaukhyaṃ netareṣām । anena brahmasāmarthyamuktaṃ bhavati । evaṃ anityo nityānām'; iti vākyamapi brahmamāhātmyaparatayā vyākhyeyam । atadetat'; ityādināpi prakṛtabhagavatsvarūpameva viśeṣataḥ pratipādyate iti । manyante ityasyottaratrānvayaḥ । tathā ca ayato vāco nivartante'; aeṣo asya parama ānandaḥ'; ityādau prasiddham anirdeśyaṃ paramaṃ sukhaṃ kathaṃ nu tadvijānīyāmiti manyante ityānukūlyena gṛhṇanti । jñānārthaṃ tadbhānaṃ vā prārthayante । akimu bhāti na bhāti vā'; iti tasya durjñeyatvaṃ ca vadanti jñāninaḥ । tat brahmaṇo rūpaṃ svarūpabhūtaṃ sukhametadekaṃ rūpaṃ bahudhā yaḥ karotītiprakṛteśvararūpābhinnamiti manyante jñānina iti । etacchabdasyeśvaraparatve api rūpaśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyāt napuṃsakaliṅgatopapattiḥ । taduktaṃ nyāyavivaraṇe - ayadbrahmānirdeśyaṃ sukhamiti vadanti tadetatsvarūpamiti manyanta iti'; । kāṭhakabhāṣye tu - tad aguhyaṃ brahma sanātanam'; ityupakrāntam । arūpaṃ rūpaṃ pratirūpo babhūva'; iti jīvasya pratibimbatvamuktam । rūpaśabdena prakṛtametat aekaṃ rūpam'; ityatra prakṛtaṃ ca bhagavadrūpam aanirdeśyam'; itthamiti sākalyena nirvaktumaśakyaṃ paramaṃ sukhamiti manyante jñānina iti sukharūpatvavidhiparatayā vyākhyātam । bhāṣye apyanirdeśyasukharūpa ityetāvanmātragrahaṇena śrutau sukharūpatvaṃ vidheyamiti sūcitam । tadanirdeśyaparamasukhātmakaṃ bhagavadrūpaṃ tatparasādamṛte kimu bhāti na bhāti veti samyagbhāti na bhātīti kathaṃ nvahaṃ jānīyāmiti śiṣṭavākyārthastatraivoktaḥ । vivṛtaṃ caidvyāsatīrthīye - atat'; anirdeśyaparamasukhātmakaṃ bhagavadrūpaṃ tatprasādamṛte kimu samyagbhāti? na bhāti vāti? iti praśnottarabhūtam ekaṃ niścitārthaṃ akathamahaṃ vijānīyāṃ'; na kenāpi prakāreṇeti । atretiśabda ubhayānvayī । tathā ca kimu bhātīti praśnasyottarabhūtaṃ na bhātītivākyoktamekamajñeyatvarūpamarthamiti yojanā । kecittu - yadevaṃ brahma tatprasādamṛte anu'; idānīṃ akathamahaṃ vijānīyām'; prārthanīyāṃ liṅ । na kathamapītyarthaḥ । jñānivākyānukaraṇametat । bhagavatprasādādapi kiṃ sākalyena tajjñānaṃ bhavatīti naciketā yamaṃ pṛcchati - kimu bhātīti । uśabdaḥ samyagityarthe । tathātve samyagiti śeṣaḥ । uttaramāha yamaḥ - na bhātīti । vāśabdoṣa'vadhāraṇe । na bhātyeveti vyākhyāti ।

na hi jñānisukhamanubhāti sarvaṃ, na ca tadbhāsā ।

nanu atameva bhāntam'; iti vākye sūryāditejasāṃ paramātmādhīnaprakāśakartṛtvasya atasya bhāsā'; itivākye ca sarvasya jagatastatprabhāprakāśyatvasya ca śravaṇena asiddhiparihāre kutastayorviṣṇutvasādhyenāvyabhicaritatvam, yena talliṅgadvayabalātsamīpoktajñānisukhapāmarśaparityāgaḥ syādityata āha - na hīti ।। sarvamityubhayānvayī । tathā ca ahi'; yasmāt asarvaṃ'; sūryāditejaḥ jñānisukhamanusṛtya ana bhāti'; na prakāśate । tathā atadbhāsā'; tasya jñānisukhasya prakāśena asarvaṃ'; jagat ana bhāti'; na prakāśate cetyarthaḥ । vakṣyamāṇapramāṇavirodhāditi bhāvaḥ । caśabdaḥ samuccaye । ato na liṅgadvayamanyatrāvakāśavaditi vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

aahaṃ tattejo raśmīt'; iti nārāyaṇabhāsā hi sarvaṃ bhāti ।।

astvetadubhayaṃ jñānisukhe anupapannam । tathāpyanena kutaḥ paramātmano grahaṇaṃ, asya paramātmatvasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyāniścayādityatastatra dvitīyasūtrasthāpipadena sūcitāṃ śrutimāha - ahamiti ।। ahamitītyanantaraṃ śruteriti śeṣaḥ । itiśabda ādyārthe । tena atameva bhāntamanubhāti sarvaṃ tasya bhāsā sarvamidaṃ vibhāti'; ityātharvaṇaśrutirapi gṛhyate । nārāyaṇeti । nārāyaṇādhīnabhāsetyarthaḥ । hiśabdo yata ityarthe, prasiddhau ca । asarvaṃ'; sūryāditejaḥ abhāti'; prakāśate । yadvā - anārāyaṇabhāsā'; nārāyaṇīyabhāsā asarvaṃ'; jagat abhāti'; prakāśasya ityarthaḥ । aiti jñāyate'; iti śeṣaḥ । śrutau araśmīt'; ityanena sūryāditejasāṃ nārāyaṇādhīnaprakāśakartṛtvasya, atejaḥ'; ityanena sarvasya jagato nārāyaṇīyaprakāśaprakāśyatvasya coktatvāditi bhāvaḥ । aaham'; iti, śrutistvantarnaye vyākhyātā । anena - taduktamityataḥ sūtre tadityanuvartate । tasyetyāvartate vipariṇamyate ca । asambhavāditi cānuvartate । tathā ca - 
tadetaditi manyante anirdeśyaṃ paramaṃ sukham ।
kathaṃ nu tadvijānīyām ।।

ityānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇaṃ tadetacchabdaparāmṛśyaṃ sukham anirdeśyaṃ sukhaṃ tattu viṣṇurūpameva, na samīpoktajñānisukham । kutaḥ? atasya'; sūryāditejasaḥ atasya'; ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya sukhasya tasmin atameva bhāntam'; iti aanukṛteḥ'; anubhānaśravaṇāttasyaitadadhīnaprakāśakartṛtvaśravaṇādasyānyatejoniyantṛtvaśravaṇāditi yāvat । tathā tasya sarvasya jagatastasya tatprakāśaprakāśyatvasya atasya bhāsā'; iti śrutāvuktatvāttasya sarvajagatprakāśatvokteriti yāvat । tasya ca liṅgadvayasya aahaṃ tattejaḥ'; ityādiśrutyā smṛtyā ca tasminviṣṇāveva niścayenopapatterjñānisukhe ca aasambhavāt'; anupapatteḥ । tathā tasminnupasaṃhāre tasyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya ana tatra sūryo bhāti'; iti vākye tasya sūryādyaprakāśyatvasyacokteśceti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sū - oṃ ।। oṃ ।।

yadādityagataṃ tejo jagadbhāsayate akhilam । yaccandramasi yaccāgnau tattejo viddhi māmakam ।।

yadetalliṅgadvayasya viṣṇuniṣṭhatvam aaham'; iti śrutyopapāditam । tatsmṛtyāpyupapādayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā tāṃ smṛtimudāharati - apīti ।। iti smaryata ityanvayaḥ । ayat'; ādityādiṣu sthitaṃ tejastat amāmakaṃ'; madadhīnaṃ madīyaṃ ca, matteja evādityādiṣu prerakatvenāsti । tadevākhilaṃ jagat abhāsayate'; prakāśayatīti gītāsmṛtyarthaḥ ।

na tadbhāsayate sūryo na śaśāṅko na pāvakaḥ । yadgatvā na nivartante taddhāma paramaṃ mama ।।

।। iti anukṛtyadhikaraṇam ।।

kiṃ ca pāṭhake ana tatra sūryo bhāti na candratārakaṃ nemā vidyuto bhānti kuto ayamagniḥ'; ityādyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya sukhasya sūryādyaprakāśyatvamucyate । tacca viṣṇoreva smaryate, ato viṣṇureva atadetat'; ityatra pratipādyaḥ, na jñānisukhamiti sūtrasyārthāntaramapipadasya yuktisamuccayārthatvaṃ cābhipretya tāṃ smṛtimudāharati - na taditi ।। atrāpītiśabdasya smaryata ityanvayaḥ । jñānino ayadgatvā'; yatprāpya punastasmānnanivartante, tanmama paramaṃ adhāma'; svarūpaṃ, tadetaddhāma sūryo ana bhāsayate'; na prakāśayate, evaṃ aśaśāṅkaḥ'; candraḥ । yadā caivaṃ tadā kuto ayamavamo agniriti gītāsmṛtyarthaḥ । anena - pūrvavyākhyāne na kevalamanukṛtyādiḥ aahaṃ tattejaḥ'; iti śrutyantare atamevabhāntamanubhāti'; ityātharvaṇādau viṣṇudharmatvena śrūyate, kintu yadādityeti smaryatepīti śrutisamuccayārthe apiśabdaḥ । dvitīyavyākhyāne tu atameva bhāntamanubhāti'; ityuttaravākyoktānukṛtyādihetoḥ ana tatra sūryo bhāti'; iti pūrvavākyoktasūryādyaprakāśyatvahetośca samuccaye apiśabdaḥ । tathā ca na kevalaṃ atadetat'; ityatroktānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya viṣṇutvarūpapradhānasādhye hetūkṛtamanukṛtyādikam aahaṃ tattejo raśmīt'; ityādau śrūyate, kintu yadādityeti smaryate apīti vā apiḥ । kiñca - yato na kevalaṃ prathamasūtroktaliṅgadvayaṃ, kintu tato anyadapi ana tatra'; iti kāṭhakavākye tasyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasyoktaṃ sūryādyaprakāśyatvarūpaṃ liṅgaṃ tasya viṣṇoḥ sambandhitvenaiva ana tat'; iti smaryate । atastadetat akathaṃ nu tadvijānīyām'; ityatra viṣṇureva pratipādya iti vā sūtrasyārthadvayamuktaṃ bhavati । ana tatra'; ityāderayamarthaḥ । pūrvaṃ brahma na samyagbhātīti tasya durjñeyatvamuktaṃ, tatkuta ityataḥ idamucyate - yasyaivaṃvidhaṃ sukhaṃ rūpaṃ atatra'; brahmaṇi sūryo ana bhāti'; tanna prakāśayatīti yāvat । candratārakamiti dvandvaikavadbhāvaḥ। evaṃ tat vidyuto api ana bhānti'; na bhāsayantīti । atameva bhāntam'; ityuttaravākyaṃ tu yadyapi vyāsatīrthakṛtātharvaṇaṭīkāyām - aetatsamākhyārūpamātharvaṇavākyaṃ'; abhāntaṃ'; bhāsayantaṃ paramātmānamanusṛtyaiva sūryādayo abhānti'; prakāśate iti vyākhyātam । tathāpi ṭīkānusārāt asarvaṃ'; sūryāditejaḥ abhāntaṃ'; prakāśamānaṃ bhagavantamanusṛtyaiva abhāti'; prakāśate । atasya'; bhagavato abhāsā'; prakāśena aidaṃ sarvaṃ'; jagati abhāti'; prakāśyata iti vyākhyeyam । vyāsatīrthīyaṃ tu vyākhyānāntaraṃ ṭīkākṛdabhipretaṃ bhaviṣyatīti tadvirodhaḥ ।।

।। iti anukṛtyadhikaraṇam ।।

।। vāmanādhikaraṇam ।।

viṣṇureva jijñāsya ityuktam । tatra ūrdhvaṃ prāṇāmunnayatyapānaṃ pratyagasyati । madhye vāmanamāsīnaṃ viśve devā upāsate ।। iti sarvadevopāsyaḥ kaścitpratīyate ।

atrādhikaraṇer iśānanāmasamanvayaḥ kriyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayasaṃśayau ca sūcayati - viṣṇureveti । jijñāsāsūtre viṣṇurevasarvairmumukṣubhirmokṣārthaṃ jijñāsya ityuktamityarthaḥ । na ca tatra jijñāsyatvāyogavyavaccheda eva kṛtaḥ, na tvanyayogavyavaccheda iti vācyam । anyasyāpi jijñāsyatve tasyāpi mokṣadātṛtvāpattyā ayato nārāyaṇaprasādamṛte'; ityādivivaraṇānupapatteranyayogavyavacchedasyāpi tatrābhipretatvāt । ato atraivakāra ubhayānvayitayā vyākhyeyaḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha - tatreti । tatretyavyayaṃ tadityarthe api । tathā ca aathāto brahmajijñāsā'; iti yatpūrvaṃ viṣṇorjijñāsyatvamuktaṃ atatra'; jijñāsyatve atatrar'; aiśāno bhūtabhavyasya'; ityuktvā āmnāte aūrdhvam'; iti kāṭhakavākye akaścirt'; iśāno dharmitvena pratīyate । katham? yato ayaṃ asarvadevopāsyaḥ'; tairjijñāsyaḥ pratīyate ata iti vākyayojanā । na ca vāyoḥ sarvadevopāsyatve api na viṣṇossarvadevopāsyatvahāniriti vācyam । tāvatāpi sarvairmumukṣubhirviṣṇureva jijñāsya iti niyamasyāsiddheḥ । na ca śrutigataviśvedevaśabdasya gaṇaviśeṣavācitvāt sarvadevopāsya ityuktiranupapanneti vācyam । gaṇaviśeṣaparatve tasya guṇādhikyāsiddhyā sarvadevaparatvāvaśyaṃbhāvāt । anenar - iśānaśabdasyānyaniṣṭhatvākṣepamukhena phalato mumukṣukartṛkajijñāsyatvasyānyaniṣṭhatvākṣepāt jijñāsādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tatheśānākhyo viṣayaśca sūcitaḥ ।

sa ca aevamevaiṣa prāṇa itarān prāṇān pṛthakpṛthageva sannidhatte'; ayo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ'; akuvidaṅga'; ityādinā prāṇavyavasthāpakatvānmadhyamatvātsarvadevopāsyatvācca vāyureveti pratīyate । ato abravīt - sū - oṃ ।।
śabdādeva pramitaḥ ।
।।

vāmanaśabdādeva viṣṇuriti pramitaḥ ।

sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣayati - sa ceti ।। atretthaṃ yojanā - asa ca'; sarvadevopāsyaśceśāno vāyureva bhavet, na viṣṇuḥ । kutaḥ? atra prāṇavyavasthāpakatvaśravaṇāt । tathā madhyamatvokteḥ sarvadevatopāsyatvokteśca । na caiṣāṃ vāyvekaniṣṭhatvāsiddhiḥ । yato ayaṃ vāyuḥ aevamevaiṣa prāṇaḥ'; ayo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ'; akuvidaṅga'; ityādinā vākyena prāṇavyavasthāpakatvadimān pratīyate, ata iti । kāṭhake hi - 
aṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣo madhya ātmani tiṣṭhatir ।
iśāno bhūtabhavyasya ।।

ityanena bhagavato aṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ pūrṇaṣaḍguṇatvaṃ dehamadhyasthatvaṃ bhūtabhaviṣyadvartamāneśānatvamityādimāhātmyamabhidhāyeśānapadoktasya tasyaiva aūrdhvam'; ityādinā mahimāntaramucyate । tatra madhyaśabdaḥ siddhānte ūrdhvaṃpratyakchabdasamabhivyāhārāt deśaviśeṣavacanaḥ, natvavāntareśvaratvādirūpamadhyamatvārthakaḥ । tathā ca yaḥ prāṇākhyarūpeṇa aprāṇaṃ'; prāṇākhyavāyumūrdhvam aunnayati'; udgamayati ūrdhvagatimattayā prerayati । apānarūpī cāpānākhyaṃ vāyuṃ apratyak'; adhastādviṇmūtrādiniṣkāsanahetutayā aasyati'; nirasyati prerayatīti yāvat । taṃ adehamadhye'; hṛdaye aāsīnam'; upaviṣṭaṃ avāmanaṃ'; saundaryapradhānāḥ striyo vāmāḥ tāḥ netāraṃ viṣṇuṃ aviśve devāḥ'; sarve devāḥ aupāsate'; jijñāsanta iti siddhāntarītyā śrutyarthaḥ । pūrvapakṣī tvidaṃ vāyuparaṃ matvā madhyaśabdo ayo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ'; iti śrutyantarasamākhyānānmadhyameśvaratvavacano na deśaviśeṣavacana ityāha । aevam'; iti ṣaṭpraśnavākyaṃ ca ayathā samrāḍevādhikṛtānviniyuṅkte etāngrāmānadhitiṣṭhasveti'; iti dṛṣṭāntavākyena saha vyākhyeyam । tatprakārastu - yathā asamrāṭ'; sārvabhaumaḥ aadhikṛtān niyogino adhikṛtya viniyuṅkte'; । katham? tvam aetān'; pāṭalīputrādīn grāmān aadhitiṣṭhasva'; tadādhipatyena tiṣṭhasveti । aevamevaiṣaḥ'; aātmata eṣa prāṇo jāyate'; ityātmajātatvenokto mukhyaprāṇaḥ aitarān'; bhinnān svajanyatvenopacāreṇātmapravibhāgān prāṇān vāyūn pṛthaksthāneṣu hṛdayādiṣu sthāpayatīti । ayo ayam'; ityādibṛhadāraṇyakavākyam । tatra hi pūrvaṃ vāgādīnāṃ mṛtyugrastatvamuktvā aathainameva nāpnot'; ityanena mukhyaprāṇasya tadanāttatvena tebhyaḥ śraiṣṭhyamabhidhāya ayo ayam'; ityanena prāṇaśabdavācyeṣu viṣṇuvāyutaditareṣu cetaneṣu triṣu viṣṇoruttamatvādanyeṣāmadhamatvādvāyormadhyamatvādasmānnimittādvā avāntareśvaratvādvā mukhyaprāṇasya sarvottamatvarūpakāṣṭhātvāvirodhimadhyasthatvamevocyate, na tu madhyadeśasthatvam । tathā tatraiva caturthādhyāye aayaṃ vāva śiśuḥ yo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ'; iti candrikodāhṛte vākye sthūladehākhyavistṛtapradeśagataliṅgaśarīrarūpagṛhe viṣṇurūpāyāṃ sthūṇāyām annākhyena śrīrūpeṇa dāmnā baddho govatsarūpovāyurmadhyamatvenocyate । 
kuvidaṅga namasā ye vṛdhāsaḥ purā devā anavadyāsa āsan ।
te vāyave manave bādhitāyāvāsayannuṣasaṃ sūryeṇa ।।

iti ṛṅmantre aaṅga'; iti priyasambodhanam । tathā ca ye devāḥ vāyoḥ anamasā'; namaskāropalakṣitasevādinā avṛdhāsaḥ'; vṛddhā jñānādiguṇapūrṇāḥ aanavadyāsaḥ'; anavadyāḥ ajñānarāgādyavadyavidhurāśca purā sasūryā āsan । te akuvit'; kvacidrahasyasthāne sūryeṇa sākaṃ amanave'; jñānine abādhitāyā'; saṃsārakleśavadbhiḥ śaraṇaṃ prāptāya avāyave'; vāyumuddiśya auṣasam'; uṣa prakāśe, asun, buddhim aavāsayan'; tadviṣayāmakurvanniti śrutyarthaḥ । siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe - ata iti ।। avāmanaśabdāt'; vāmanaśruteḥ । evakāro vāyuliṅgasadbhāvāt vāyureveśānaḥ kiṃ na syāditi codyaparihārāya liṅgebhyaḥ śruteḥ prābalyamāha । yathoktaṃ sudhāyām - evaśabdavyākhyānaṃ balavaditi aśabdādeva pramitaḥ'; iti yatheti । samanvayasūtrādanuvṛttasya tadityasyārtho viṣṇuriti । vidheyabhūtaviṣṇutvasyānvayayogyoddeśyadyotanāyetiśabdaprayogaḥ । āvartate cāyam । itiśabdātparamapi evaśabdo yojyaḥ । tenānuvṛttastu śabdo vyākhyātaḥ । tathā car aiśāno bhūtabhavyasya'; iti śrutar iśāno viṣṇureva bhavet । kutaḥ? yastatra pramito viṣṇāveva mahāyogavidvadrūḍhibhyāṃ prasiddho amadhye vāmanam'; itiśruto vāmanaśabdastasmādeveti yojanā । pramitapadaṃ śruterniravakāśatvasūcakam । anena sūtre itiśabdo adhyāhārya iti sūcitam । tathā car aiśāno bhūtabhavyasya'; itiśrutariśānaḥ atattu'; viṣṇureva bhavet । kutaḥ? yastatra viṣṇāveva pramito mahāyogavidvadrūḍhibhyāṃ prasiddho anyatra niravakāśo amadhye vāmanamāsīnam'; itiśruto liṅgātprabalo vāmanaśabdastacchrutistasmāditi sūtrārthaḥ ।

na hi śruterliṅgaṃ balavat ।

sūtre evakāraprayogena sūcitaṃ śruteḥ prābalyaṃ liṅgasya prābalyaniṣedhamukhena darśayati - na hīti ।। śruteriti pañcamī । hiśabdo vakṣyamāṇapramāṇavirodhāditi hetusūcakaḥ । tathā ca ahi'; yasmāt na śruterliṅgaṃ balavat, kintu durbalameva । tasmālliṅagāt prabalāt vāmanaśabdādeveśāno viṣṇurevetyarthaḥ ।

śrutirliṅgaṃ samākhyā ca vākyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ tathā । pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ balīyaḥ syādevamāgamanirṇayaḥ । iti skānde ।

kuto na śruterliṅgaṃ balavadityatastathāsati śruterliṅgātprābalyavacanavirodhāpatterityāśayena tadvākyaṃ paṭhati - śrutiriti ।। iti skānda ityanantaraṃ vacanāditi śeṣaḥ । asya na hītyanenānvayaḥ । vācakaśabdaḥśrutiḥ । asādhāraṇadharmo vā, tadbodhakaśabdo vā liṅgam । nirṇītasyānyatra samānoktiḥ samākhyā । sā dvividhā - arthataśśabdato apīti । samabhivyāhṛtapadairevākāṅkṣāpūrtau tacchāntyarthaṃ padāntaranirapekṣāṇi padāni vākyam । ekaprameyapratipādakānekavākyāni prakaraṇam । anuktasthānasamuccaye tathetiśabdaḥ । anekaprameyapratipādakamekārthatātparyayuktaṃ vacanaṃ sthānam । atra avākyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ sthānaṃ samākhyā ca tathāvidhā'; ityanuvyākhyānusāreṇa samākhyāyāḥ sthānānantaryameva grāhyaṃ, na tvatroktakramānusāreṇa vākyādyapekṣayā prāthamyam । atroktakramasyāvivakṣitatvāt । uktaṃ hi pramāṇalakṣaṇaṭīkāyāṃ - samākhyāditvena grahaṇaṃ aśrutirliṅgaṃ samākhyā ca'; ityavivakṣitakramaṃ vākyamanusṛtyeti । ata eva jaiminiḥ - aśrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyānāṃ samavāye pāradaurbalyamarthaviprakarṣāt'; iti smṛtyuktādanyathākramamāha - pūrvaṃpūrvamiti । pūrvoddiṣṭamityarthaḥ । ekatra samavetaṃ viruddhamiti ca śeṣaḥ । abalīyaḥ'; atiśayena svabhāvato balavat yathātraivādhikaraṇe anantaroddiṣṭaliṅgāpekṣayā pūrvoddiṣṭā vāmanaśrutiḥ svataḥ prabalā। vākyāpekṣayā prabalaṃ liṅgam। yathā - daharādhikaraṇe daharākāśasya sākṣātsarvādhāratvaprāpakāt akiṃ tadatra vidyate ubhe asmin dyāvāpṛthivī'; iti vākyātprabalaṃ viṣṇostatprāpakāpahatapāpmatvādikaṃ liṅgam । prakaraṇāpekṣayā prabalaṃ vākyam। yathā - jyotirdarśanāt ityadhikaraṇe jīvasya ahṛdyantarjyotiḥ'; itivākyabodhyajyotiṣṭvasādhakājjīvaprakaraṇātprabalaṃ viṣṇorjyotiṣṭvaprāpakaṃ akatama ātmā'; iti praśnavākyam । sthānāpekṣayā prabalaṃ prakaraṇam । yathā - samagropaniṣadar iśvaraparatvasādhakāt ṣaṭpraśnarūpasthānāt prabalam aātmata eṣa prāṇo jāyate'; ityetatkhaṇḍarūpaṃ mukhyaprāṇaprakaraṇam । ata evātrādhikaraṇe ṣaṭpraśnoktaprāṇavyavasthāpakatvādīnāṃ mukhyaprāṇaliṅgatvamupetya śrutyā bādha uktaḥ । samākhyāpekṣayā prabalaṃ sthānam । yathā - annamayādiśabdānāṃ kośaparatvasādhakāt aannamayaprāṇamayamanomayavijñānamayānandamayā me śudhyantām'; iti nārāyaṇānuvākasamākhyāyāḥ prabalaṃ teṣāṃ viṣṇutvasādhakaṃ brahmaparānekaprakaraṇasandarbharūpaṃ sthānam । etānyeva śrutyādinār'thanirṇayasthalāni । ādyayā samākhyayā nirṇetavyaṃ yathā - puruṣasūktasamākhyayā vaiśvānarasya viṣṇutvam । dvitīyayā yathā - ambhraṇīsūktasamākhyayā viśvakarmasūktoktasyājasya viṣṇutvam । astvevaṃ tataḥ kimityata āha - evamiti । viruddhaiteṣāṃ samavāye sati prabalena pūrveṇottarabādhe ca sati aāgamanirṇayaḥ'; āgamārthasya vipratipannasyaitaiḥ nirṇayo bhavatītyarthaḥ ।

tacca liṅgaṃ viṣṇoreva । tasyaiva prāṇatvokteḥ atadvai tvaṃ prāṇo abhavaḥ'; iti ।।

nanvastu śruteḥ svabhāvataḥ prābalyam । tathāpi bāhulyena pūrvapakṣyuktaliṅgānāmapi prābalyātsāmyenānirṇaya evetyata āha - tacceti ।। liṅgamiti samudāyaikavacanam । tathā ca atat'; pūrvavādyuktaṃ liṅgajātaṃ tu viṣṇoreva yuktam, na vāyorityarthaḥ । tathā ca bāhulye api liṅgānāṃ sāvakāśatvāttebhyaḥ śruterekasyā api niravakāśāyāḥ prābalyānnānirṇaya iti bhāvaḥ । nanu na liṅgaṃ viṣṇau sāvakāśaṃ, pūrvapakṣyudāhṛtasamākhyārūpaśrutyantareṇa tasya prāṇaniṣṭhatayaivoktatvādityata āha - tasyaiveti । atadvai tvam'; iti śrutau atasya'; viṣṇoḥ prāṇatvasya prāṇaśabdavācyatvasyokteruktatvādityarthaḥ । evaṃ aata eva'; ityatrādhyātmikāśeṣaśabdasya samanvayaṃ bruvatā tathā - aśāstradṛṣṭyā'; ityatrāntaryāmiparatvaṃ bruvatā sūtrakāreṇetaravyāvṛttyā tasyaiva prāṇatvokteḥ sādhitatvādityapi vyākhyeyametat । tathā ca śrutyantare prāṇaniṣṭhatayā liṅgasyoktāvapi na tadvirodhaḥ । tasya prāṇasya viṣṇutvābhyupagamāditi bhāvaḥ । nanu tathāpi akuvidaṅga'; iti ṛci vāyuniṣṭhatayā liṅgoktestadvirodha ityasyāpīdamevottaram । asmin pakṣe prāṇatvamiti vāyutvamupalakṣyate । tathā cāntarnaye ādhidaivikāśeṣaśabdasamanvayaṃ bruvatā sūtrakāreṇa atasyaiva'; viṣṇoreva aprāṇatvokteḥ'; vāyuśabdavācyatvarūpavāyutsyoktatvādityarthaḥ । tathā ca na tadvirodhopīti bhāvaḥ । na ca siddhānte api sthānāpekṣayā prabalātprakaraṇāt aevamevaiṣaḥ'; itiśrutyantaragataprāṇaśabdasya, tathā ayo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ'; ityasya, tathā akuvidaṅga'; iti mantrasthavāyuśabdasya mukhyavāyuparatvaṃ, tatroktaliṅgānāmapi tatparatvamupetya teṣāṃ śrutyā bādhasyoktatvāt kathaṃ śrutyantarasthaprāṇavāyuśabdayoḥ viṣṇuparatvāṅgīkāreṇa samādhānam । ata eva candrikāyām - madhyamaśabdo api aūrdhvaṃ prāṇam'; iti prāṇasya sthānāntaranirdeśāttatyāgena madhyamasthānasthabrahmaparaḥ, na tu śrutyantare madhyamaśabdoktaprāṇapara ityuktam । ataḥ aevamevaiṣaḥ'; iti vākyaṃ sthānātprakaraṇasya prābalye udāhṛtamiti vācyam । uktarītyā mukhyataḥ śrutyantaragataprāṇaśabdāderbrahmaparatvena liṅgānāṃ tattadantaryāminiṣṭhatve api samākarṣanyāyenānyaparatvasyāpyaṅgīkārāt । śrutyantaroktaliṅgānāmanyaniṣṭhatve api vā nānupapattiḥ । na caivaṃ kāṭhakoktaliṅgānāmapyanyaniṣṭhatvāpattyā anyeṣāmīśānatvādyāpattiḥ । niravakāśaśrutyā kāṭhakoktaliṅgānāṃ viṣṇuniṣṭhatānirṇayopapatteḥ । nanu tathāpi kathamīśāno viṣṇurbhavecchrutāvīśānasyāṅguṣṭhaparimitatvokteḥ । sarvagate ca harau tadayogāt । na ca vyomavatsarvagatasyāpyaṇutvaṃ yujyata iti pratipāditamiti vācyam । tathāpi aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ'; iti tanmātraparimāṇatvokterayogāt । na ca aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ'; ityatra śrutaḥ parimāṇārthako mātracpratyaya eva, na tvavadhāraṇārthako mātraśabdaḥ । adehāṅguṣṭhamito dehe jīvāṅguṣṭhamito hṛdi'; iti smṛtau mita ityanena parimāṇasyaivokteḥ । tathā ca nānupapattiriti vācyam । tathātve aṅguṣṭhamātratvābhidhātryām aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ'; iti śrutau amadhya ātmani'; ityasya smṛtau hṛdītyasya ca vaiyarthyāpātāt । tanmātraparimitatvoktyarthaṃ hi tatra hṛdayarūpasūkṣmasthānoktiḥ । tasmādavadhāraṇārthakamātraśabda evāyamaṅgīkāryaḥ uktaṃ hi candrikāyām - mātraśabdasyāvadhāraṇārthakatvāditi ।

sū - oṃ ।। hṛdyapekṣayā tu manuṣyādhikāratvāt ।।

sarvagatasyāpi tasyāṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ hṛdyavakāśāpekṣayā yujyate ।

tathā ca sarvagate harāvaṅguṣṭhamātratvoktiranupapanneti nātreśāno viṣṇurityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya tadakṣarāṇi vyācaṣṭe - hṛdīti ।। sarvagatasyāpītyanena tuśabdo yadyapitathāpītyarthatayā vyākhyātaḥ । hṛdyapekṣayetyanena sūcitahetoranvayayogyaṃ sādhyaṃ darśayati - tasyeti । yojanā tu - yadyapi viṣṇuḥ sarvagatastathāpi atasyāṅguṣṭhamātratvam'; aṅguṣṭhamātratvoktiryujyate । katham? yato ahṛdyavakāśopekṣayā'; hṛdi vidyamāno yo ayamavakāśo aṅguṣṭhaparimitadeśastadapekṣayā tatrābhivyaktatāvatparibhitabhagavanmūrtiviśeṣamapekṣya tasya viṣṇoraṅguṣṭhamātratvam astyata iti। yadvā - ahṛdyavakāśāpekṣayā'; hṛdi vidyamānāvakāśamapekṣya tatsambandhāttasyāṅguṣṭhamātratvavacanaṃ yujyata ityāvṛttiṃ vinā yojanā । prathamapakṣe śaktyāparimite api bhagavati mūrtiviśeṣe vyaktyātmanāṅguṣṭhamātratvasya sthānini brahmaṇi tatsambandhādupacāreṇoktiriti bhedaḥ । atra ṭīkāyāṃ hṛdyavakāśāpekṣayeti bhāṣyaṃ sāvadhāraṇaṃ kṛtvā sautratuśabdo avadhāraṇatayā vyākhyātaḥ । tena viṣṇoṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ hṛdyapekṣayaiva, na tu lokavatparicchinnatvādityuktaṃ bhavati । tattatsthāneṣu vyaktamūrtiviśeṣāpekṣayā vā upacāreṇa vā tattatparimāṇatvoktyā ayastvetameva prādeśamātram'; iti chāndogye aprādeśamātraṃ puruṣam'; ityanyatra aprādeśaḥ puruṣottamaḥ'; ityaparatra ca hṛdgatasya viṣṇoḥ prādeśaparimitatvokteḥ । aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣo aṅguṣṭhaṃ ca samāśritaḥ'; iti śrutyantare aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣaḥ'; iti kaṭhavalyāṃ ca aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣaḥ'; ityaparatra cāṅguṣṭhaparimitatvokteḥ aaṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇakaḥ'; iti kvacidaṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇakatvoktervirodha iti codyaṃ parihṛtaṃ bhavati । dehe hṛdayākāśe prādeśaparimitarūpaviśeṣasya hṛdayagatakamalakarṇikāmūlagatākāśe aṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇakarūpāntarasya karṇikāgragatākāśecāṅguṣṭhaparimitarūpāntarasya ca vyaktisambhavāt, tattatsthānadharmasya sthāninyupacaritatvasambhavācca । yathoktaṃ bṛhadāraṇyakabhāṣye - 
hṛdaye sarvaśo vyāpī prādeśaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।
jīvānāṃ sthānamuddiṣṭaḥ sarvadaivasanātanaḥ ।।

hṛtkarṇikāmūlagataḥ so aṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇakaḥ ।
mūleśa iti nāmāsmin sarve jīvāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।।

aṅguṣṭhamātre puruṣe karṇikāgrasthite harau ।
prāviśanti suṣuptau tu prabudhyante tatastathā ।।

asmin mūleśavyāpinormadhye aṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ ca dehe dehāṅguṣṭhamitatvaṃ jīvahṛdi jīvāṅguṣṭhamitatvamiti vivektavyam । atra aaṅguṣṭhaṃ ca samāśritaḥ'; ityanena karmendriyādhiṣṭhitatvamucyata iti prameyadīpoktamapi jñātavyam । nanu adakṣiṇākṣimukhe viśvo manasyantastu taijasaḥ'; ityādivacanājjāgradādyavasthāprerakaviśvataijasaprājñānāṃ dakṣiṇākṣyādiṣu sattvaṃ tāvatsiddham । yadi caivaṃ tadā jīvo api jāgradavasthāyāṃ dakṣiṇākṣisthaḥ svapne kaṇṭhadeśasthaḥ suptau hṛdayastho bhavati, ahṛdayasthātparājjīvo dūrastho jāgradeṣyati'; ityukteḥ । dūrastho akṣistho jāgrajjāgratvamiti tasyārthaḥ । tathā ca kathaṃ hṛdayavyāptaprādeśaparimitabhagavadrūpasya sarvadā jīvasthānatvam? kathaṃ ca hṛtkarṇikāmūlagatabhagavadrūpe sadā pratiṣṭhito jīvaḥ? suptau hṛtkarṇikāgragate harau praviśatītyuktiriti cet - na, yatassarvadā hṛdi sthitameva jīvasvarūpaṃ jāgaritādāvakṣyādiṣvapi viśeṣasannihitaṃ dīpaprakāśavadityaṅgīkṛtam । yathoktamaitareyabhāṣye - hṛde sthitameva tasya rūpaṃ jāgarite apyakṣyādiṣu viśeṣasannihitaṃ bhavatīti । ekasyaiva jīvasya sthāpanadhṛtyākhyapratiṣṭhāpanasuptiprāpaṇākhyaprayojanabhedādekadehe anekadhā sthitānāṃ bhagavanmūrtīnāṃ śaktyā sarvagānāmapi tatra tatra vyaktyātmanā anekālpaparimāṇavattvaṃ ca yujyata iti na kācidanupapattiḥ ।

itaraprāṇināmaṅguṣṭhābhāve api manuṣyādhikāratvānna virodhaḥ ।।
।। iti vāmanādhikaraṇam ।।

nanu tathāpi nāṅguṣṭhaparimāṇavattvaṃ viṣṇoryuktam । tathā hi kiṃ tattadaṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ vā yatkiñcidaṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ vā । nādyaḥ, paśvādīnāmaṅguṣṭhābhāvena tadantargatasya viṣṇoraṅguṣṭhaparimitatvāyogāt । na dvitīyaḥ, aṅguṣṭhamātratvoktestaistaistathopāsanārthatvena tasya cāṅguṣṭhavyaktiviśeṣanirdhāraṇa vināyogena yatkiñcidaṅguṣṭhamātratvoktervyarthatvāt । pipīlikādihṛdayasthe aṅguṣṭhamātratvasābhānyasyāpyasambhavāccetyāśaṅkāṃ pariharan manuṣyādhikāratvāt itisūtraśeṣaṃ tuśabdasya kākākṣinyāyena atrāpyanvayaṃ tasyāpyarthatvaṃ ca abhipretya tatsambandhipradarśanapūrvakaṃ vyācaṣṭe - itareti ।। paśvādīnāmityarthaḥ । aṅguṣṭhamātratvamityetat vipariṇāmevānuvartate । ana virodhaḥ'; iti virodhasūtrādākṛṣṭe pade । tathā ca aapi'; tattadaṅguṣṭhaparimitatvāṅgīkāre apītaraprāṇināmaṅguṣṭhābhāve api na viṣṇoraṅguṣṭhamātratvasya virodhenāṅguṣṭhamātratvokterasambhavaḥ । kutaḥ? aṅguṣṭhamātratvokteretadvidyāyā amanuṣyādhikāratvāt'; manuṣyānadhikṛtya pravṛttatvāt । tadapi kutaḥ? vedavidyopāsanasya amanuṣyādhikāratvāt'; manuṣyamātrādhikāratvāditi yojanā । sūtre bhāṣye ca manuṣyāṇāmadhikāro yasmin athavā - adhikriyate atretyadhikāra upāsanaṃ śāstraṃ vā, manuṣyāṇāmeva adhikāro manuṣyādhikārastasya bhāvasatasmāditi vigrahaḥ । amanuṣyādhikāritvāt'; itipāṭhe manuṣyā adhikāriṇo yasmin tattathoktam । tathā ca manuṣyādhikārikatvādityarthaḥ । manuṣyapadaṃ ca vakṣyamāṇanyāyena mananādiśīlacetanaparam । tena devānāṃ jaritāryādīnāṃ vakṣyamāṇanyāyena vedavidyādhikāriṇāmetadvidyādhikārasiddhiḥ । tatra jaritāryādīnāṃ svasvāṅguṣṭhaparimitatvena bhagavadupāsanāsambhavāt, teṣāmetadvidyotpannavākyārthajñāna evādhikāro, nopāstāvapi । ata eva ṭīkāyāṃ manuṣyāṇāmeva vedavidyopāsanādhikāritveneti manuṣyatvaṃ vyāpakatvenoktam । na cānadhikāriṇāṃ paśvādīnāṃ dehasthitasya bhagavato aṅguṣṭhaparimitatvābhāve parimāṇāntarānukteradravyatvāpattiriti vācyam । paśvādidehagatasya paramātmanaḥ tattadākārayuktatvena tadanusāriparimāṇavattvāt । yathoktamaitareyabhāṣye - saṅkarṣaṇaśca pradyumnastadākārau nṛṣu sthitau । nārāyaṇāniruddhau tu paśvākārau paśusthitau ।।

anena - sūtre tuśabdo apyarthevadhāraṇe ca । tatrāpyarthasyobhayatrānvayaḥ । aṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ yujyata iti śeṣaḥ । taditi pradhānasūtrādanuvṛttasyeha vipariṇāmenānvayaḥ । na virodhaḥ ityasyākarṣaḥ । atasya manuṣyādhikāritvāt'; ityāvartate । tathā ca atu'; api sarvagatasyāpi atasya viṣṇoraṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ'; taduktiryujyate । yato atra ahṛdyapekṣayā tu'; hṛdyavakāśāpekṣayaiva aṅguṣṭhamātratvamucyate, na tu paricchinnatvāt । tacca mūrtiviśeṣe tanmātratvasya sattvādupacāreṇa vā yujyate । na ca nāṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ viṣṇoryuktaṃ, yatkiñcidaṅguṣṭhamātratvoktervyarthatvenāsambhavena ca tattadaṅguṣṭhamātratve vācye tasya ca paśvādīnāmaṅguṣṭhābhāvena tadantargataviṣṇāvayogāditi vācyam । yataḥ atu'; api itaraprāṇināmaṅguṣṭhābhāve api na viṣṇostattadaṅguṣṭhamātratvasya avirodhaḥ'; asambhavaḥ । kutaḥ? aṅguṣṭhamātratvavacanasya yadbodhakavidyāyāḥ amanuṣyādhikāratvāt'; manuṣyānevādhikṛtya pravṛttatvāt । tadapi kutaḥ? atasya'; vedavidyopāsanasya amanuṣyādhikāratvāt'; manuṣyamātre adhikāratvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।। iti vāmanādhikaraṇam ।।

।। devatādhikaraṇam ।।

manuṣyāṇāmeva vedavidyādhikāra ityuktam ।

asminnadhikaraṇe devānāṃ brahmavidyādhikāraḥ samarthyate । prāsaṅgikatvānnādhyāyapādasaṅgatī mārgaṇīye । śrutyādisaṅgativiṣayasaṃśayatadbījāni darśayati - manuṣyāṇāmiti ।। auktaṃ'; pūrvasūtre । tuśabdārthāvadhāraṇasya samāsapraviṣṭamanuṣyapadenāpi sambandho astīti bhāvena manuṣyāṇāmevetyanuvādaḥ । netareṣāmityevaśabdārthaḥ । avedavidyādhikāro'; vedavidyopāsanādhikāraḥ । anena - devatādhikārābhāvamukhena aviśve devā upāsate'; ityādipūrvodāhṛtaśrutyupalakṣitāśeṣaśrutiprāmāṇyasyākṣepātpūrvādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiḥ vedavidyādhikārākhyo viṣayaścokto bhavati । aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ'; iti śrutimūlāyāḥ amanuṣyāṇāmeva'; ityukteḥ aviśve devā upāsate'; iti śruteśca koṭidvayopasthāpakatvena sandehabījatvāttaduktyaiva devānāmadhikāro asti uta nāstīti saṃśayo, nāstīti pūrvapakṣaśca sūcitaḥ ।

tiryagādyapekṣayaiva manuṣyatvaviśeṣaṇamuktaṃ, na tu devādyapekṣayetyāha -

tataḥ kimityatassaṃśayabījaṃ vighaṭayan siddhāntayituṃ sūtramavatārayati - tiryagādīti ।। viśiṣṭabuddhyādirahitatiryagādivyāvṛttyarthamityarthaḥ । manuṣyatvaviśeṣaṇaṃ sāvadhāraṇatvenābhipretam । manuṣyapadam auktaṃ'; prayuktaṃ, tatreta śeṣaḥ । pūrvasūtra iti tadarthaḥ । svaprayuktaivakāravyāvarttyaṃ darśayati - na tviti ।। adevādyapekṣayā'; devādivyāvṛttyartham । tuśabdo viśeṣārthaḥ । na tu devādyarthamapītyapiśabdārtho vā । aityāha'; ityabhipretya sūtrakāro devānāmadhikārabhāvamāhetyarthaḥ ।

sū - oṃ ।। taduparyapi bādarāyaṇaḥ sambhavāt ।।

tadupari manuṣyāṇāṃ satāṃ devāditvaprāptyupari । sambhavati hi teṣāṃ viśiṣṭabuddhyādibhāvāt ।

tatsūtraṃ paṭhati - taduparīti ।। atra taduparīti sādhyadharmisūcakaṃ padamanūdya teṣāṃ tasmāttasyā iti vigrahāśrayeṇa vyācaṣṭe - taduparīti ।। vedavidyākāra ityanuṣajyate । na kevalaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ satāṃ, kintu taduparyapītyaperarthaḥ । tathā ca ateṣāṃ'; manuṣyāṇāṃ satāṃ devatāpadayogyānāṃ jīvānāṃ padaprāpteḥ pūrvaṃ manuṣyaśarīraṃ prāptānāṃ satāṃ atasmāt'; manuṣyatvāt aupari'; manuṣyaśarīrāpagamena atasyā upari'; devopadevādipadaprāpteruparitanakāle api devabhāvamāpannānāmapi vedavidyādhikāro astyeveti yojanā । kuta ityatastaddhetutayā sambhavāditi hetuṃ vyācaṣṭe । ahi'; yataḥ । avedavidyādhikāraḥ'; ityatrāpi sambadhyate । ateṣāṃ'; devānām । adhikārasambhavo api kuta ityato atrāpi sambhavādityetadevāvṛttya hetutayā yojayati - viśiṣṭeti ।। teṣāmityatrāpyanvīyate । tathā ca ateṣāṃ'; yogyamanuṣyāṇāṃ vidyākarmabhyāṃ devāditvaprāptimatāṃ asambhavāt'; viśiṣṭabuddhyādibhāvādarthagrahaṇānuṣṭhānopayuktabuddhiviśeṣādisadbhāvādityarthaḥ । arthitvasāmarthye ādipadena grāhye । na cārthitvābhāvaḥ ityatrāpi teṣāṃ sambhavati hītyeva hetuḥ । vidyābhisteṣāṃ mokṣasiddhiḥ sambhavati hīti tadarthaḥ । anena - sūtre tadityāvartate । manuṣyaparāmarśi cedaṃ buddhisthaparāmarśi ca। apiḥ samuccaye । adhikāra iti buddhyā vivicyātrānveti । anadhikārādhikārābhidhāyakajaiminibādarāyaṇoktirūpavipratipattisūcanāya bādarāyaṇapadam । tattvapradīparītyā tātparyajñāpanārthamadhikārādhikyajñaptidārḍhyārthaṃ ca bādarāyaṇaḥ svayameva vaktītyāha iti vā । sambhavāditi cāvartate । tathā ca yato na kevalaṃ devādipadayogyajīvānāṃ padaprāpteḥ pūrvaṃ bhūmau kiñcitkālaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ satāṃ tasyāṃ daśāyāmeva adhikāraḥ, kintu ataduparyapi'; tasmānmanuṣyatvādupari tadatyayena tābhyāṃ vidyākarmabhyāṃ tasyāḥ devāditvaprāpteruparitanakāle api devabhāvamāpannānāmapi vedavidyāyāmadhikāro astyeva । na ca tatkāraṇābhāvaḥ । asambhavāt'; adhikāropayogino viśiṣṭabuddhyādesteṣu sambhavāt । na ca devādīnāṃ viśiṣṭabuddhisāmarthyasadbhāve apyarthitvābhāvādadhikārābhāva iti vācyam । kutaḥ? asambhavāt'; vidyāsādhyajñānamokṣayorarthitvasambhavāditi bhagavān bādarāyaṇo manyata iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

tiryagādīnāṃ tadabhāvādabhāvaḥ । teṣāmapi yatra viśṣṭabuddhyādibhāvastatrāvirodhaḥ ।

nanu na devā vedavidyādhikāriṇaḥ, tathā sati sūtre amanuṣyamātravyāvartakamanuṣyapadaprayogena tiryagādivadamanuṣyatvānna devā vedavidyādhikāriṇa ityanumānasūcanāttadvirodhāpatterityata āha - tiryagādīnāmiti ।। ādipadena sthāvarāṇi mūḍhamanuṣyā vā gṛhyante । atadabhāvāt'; viśiṣṭabuddhyāderabhāvāt aabhāvaḥ'; tasya vedavidyādhikārasya । anenādhikārābhāve viśiṣṭabuddhyādirāhityasya prayojakatvoktyā paroktāmanuṣyatvahetoḥ sopādhikatvaṃ sādhyavyatirekasādhakopādhivyatirekākhyapratipakṣagrastatvaṃ coktaṃ bhavati । sautramanuṣyapadaṃ ca mananādiśīlaparaṃ sat viśiṣṭabuddhyādirahitameva cetanaṃ vyāvartayati, na tu martyabhinnamātramiti na tadvirodha iti bhāvaḥ । nanu viśiṣṭabuddhyādirāhityamupādhiḥ । tiryakṣu adhikārābhāvarūpasādhyāvyāpakatvāt । ata eva na tadabhāvo api sādhyavyatirekaheturityata āha - teṣāmapīti ।। apirubhayatrānveti । tatrādyassamuccaye । adhikāra iti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca na kevalaṃ devānāṃ, kintu ateṣāṃ'; tiraścāmapyadhikāre api na virodhaḥ nanu kathamavirodhastiryakṣu sarvatra vedādhikāre mānavirodhāpātādityata āha - teṣāmapīti ।। tiraścāṃ madhye apītyarthaḥ । ayatra'; yeṣu viśiṣṭabuddhyarthitvākhyarāgādibhāvaḥ tatsattvaṃ tatraivādhikāre aavirodho'; mānāvirodhaḥ । bādho na sarvatretyarthaḥ । anenāpinā sautro apiśabdo jaritāryādisamuccāyakaśceti sūcitam । yadāha tattvapradīpikākāraḥ - ateṣāmapītyādirapipadavyākhyā'; iti । ānandamālākāro api - atiryañco api kecidapiśabdagṛhītāḥ'; ityāha । tathā ca manuṣyabhinneṣvapi tiryakṣvadhikārasadbhāvādvyabhicārādadhikārābhāve nāmanuṣyatvaṃ hetuḥ, kintu viśiṣṭabuddhyādirāhityamevāvyabhicārāt । ato bhavatyeva sa upādhiḥ । ata eva sautramanuṣyapadasya vyāvarttyasaṅkoco api yukta iti bhāvaḥ ।

niṣedhābhāvāt । dṛśyante hi jaritāryādayaḥ ।।

nanu kathaṃ tiraścāmapyadhikāre apyavirodhaḥ । teṣāmadhikāraniṣedhasya taddarśanasya vā virodhitvādityāśaṅkya nādya ityāha - niṣedheti ।। teṣāmityatrāpi sambadhyate । adhikāre ityādau saṃyojyam । tena niṣedharāhitye sati viśiṣṭabuddhyādimattvamevādhikāre prayojakam, na kevalaṃ yena śūdrādau vyabhicāraḥ syāditi sūcitam । na dvitīya ityāha - dṛśyante hīti ।। vedādhikāritayeti śeṣaḥ । hiśabdo bhāratādiprasiddhisūcakaḥ । ata eva bhārate - 
evamukto bhrātṛbhistu jaritārirvibhāvasum ।
tuṣṭāva prāñjalirbhūtvā yattacchṛṇu narādhipa ।।

ityādinā jaritārisārisṛkkastambamitradroṇākhyeṣu pakṣiṣu madhye jaritāriragrajaḥ svabhrātṛbhirasmānmocayeti prārthitaḥ aayamagne jaritā'; ityāgneyasūktenāgniṃ stutvā khāṇḍavavanadahane svabhrātṝnagnidāhādamocayaditi pratipāditam । yata ityarthe vā hiśabdaḥ । atra jaritāryādaya ityeva pāṭho yuktaḥ, na tu jaritaryādaya iti hrasvayuktapāṭhaḥ, bhāratavirodhāt, tattvapradīpavirodhācceti dhyeyam । dṛśyante hītyanena - devā vedavidyādhikāriṇaḥ niṣedharāhitye sati viśiṣṭabuddhyādimattvāt tādṛśamartyavaditi siddhāntyabhimatānumāne manuṣyatvopādhirnirasto bhavati । jaritārau ādiśabdagṛhītasārisṛkkādau ca sādhyāvyāpaktavāt ।

sū - oṃ ।। virodhaḥ karmaṇīti cennānekapratipatterdarśanāt ।।

manuṣyā eva devādayo bhavantīti taduparītyuktam । tatra yadi manuṣyāḥ santo devādayo bhavanti tatpūrvaṃ devatābhāvāddevatoddiṣṭakarmaṇi virodha iti cet - 

devānāṃ vedavidyādhikārasiddhyarthaṃ taduparītyanenoktaṃ sāditvamākṣipya samādadhatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā'kṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe - virodha iti ।। manuṣyā eveti । devādipadayogyā jīvāḥ pūrvaṃ bhūmau kiñcitkālaṃ manuṣyāḥ santa eva atha devādayo bhavantītyarthaḥ । na tu manuṣyabhāvaṃ vinetyevaśabdārthaḥ ।। atroktamityanantaraṃ tadayuktamiti śeṣaḥ । kuta ityatastatpakṣe bādhakoktiparaṃ virodha ityaṃśaṃ sahetukaṃ vyācaṣṭe - tatrayadīti ।। yadītyārabhya bhavantītyantaṃ pūrvavākyārthānuvādastasyāpādakatvapradarśanārthaḥ । tatretyavyayaṃ tarhītyarthakaṃ bhavantītyataḥ paraṃ yojyam । yadvā - manuṣyā eva devādayo bhavantītyantaṃ pūrvavākyārthānuvādastasyāpādakatvapradarśanārthaḥ । tatretyavyayaṃ tarhītyarthakaṃ bhavantītyataḥ paraṃ yojyam । yadvā - manuṣyā eva devādayo bhavantītyuktyā prāptābhedaśaṅkāṃ vārayituṃ manuṣyā evetyādisvapadāni varṇayati - tatreti ।। yadvā - tatra devatoddiṣṭakarmaṇīti sāmānādhikaraṇyam । atra pakṣe yadīti śravaṇāttarhīti labhyate । bhavantītyanantaramityuktamityasti । ubhayatrādipadenopadevādayo gṛhyante । karmapadaṃ śabdasyāpyupalakṣakam । tathā ca yadi pūrvaṃ manuṣyāḥ santo apyatha devādayo bhavantītyuktamityucyate, tarhi atatpūrvaṃ'; tebhyaḥ pūrvaṃ teṣāṃ devādipadaprāpteḥ pūrvaṃ sādhakatvāvasthāyāṃ adevatābhāvāt'; devatāyā asattvāt yena karmaṇā devāditvaṃ sādhyamityuktam, atatra'; tasminneva adevatoddiṣṭakarmaṇi'; pūrvakalpe devatoddeśena pravṛttakarmaṇi devatāvācakaśabde ca avirodhaḥ'; tayorvaiyarthyamiti yojanā । uddeśyābhāvādvācyābhāvācceti bhāvaḥ ।

na, anekeṣāṃ devatāpadapratipatterdarśanāt । ate ha nākaṃ mahimānassacante । yatra pūrve sādhyāssanti devāḥ'; iti ।।
